worldes ere tyme comend men seyn al wysedom wryte dulleth ofte mannes wytte hym shal al ay rede thylke cause yf ye rede wol goo myddel wey wryte book bytwene twey somwhat luste somwhat lore lasse man may lyke wryte fewe men en dyte oure en glysshe make book englondes sake yere xvj kyng richard shal byfalle afterward god wote vpon tyde man see world euery syde sondry wyse dyuersed wel nygh stant al reuersed al speke tyme goo cause chaungeth nedeth nought specyfye thyng open ye euery man may behold netheles dayes old whan bookes leuer wrytyng byloued euer hem vertuous erthe among v noman wryte stode pry hem good shold sayth grete partye lost magnyfye worthy prynces tho bookes shewen wherof world ensampled tho dyden ne amys though tyrannye cruelte ryght u stonden degre wa wrytyng werk thus whiche borell clerk purpose wryte book world whylome toke long tyme old dayes passyd men seyn lassed wers plyght tho thenke touche also world whiche neweth euery daye may though sekenesse haue vpon hond long haue yet wol fonde wryte besynesse som partye gesse wyse man may aduysed prologue assised wysedome al bylongeth wyse man vnderfongeth shal drawe remembraunce fortune worldes chaunce whiche noman persone may knowe god allone whan prologue dispended book shal afterward ended loue whiche doth many wondre many wise hath put vnder wyse thenke trele toward grete betwene vertu vyce whiche longeth vnto offyce wyttes ben smale telle euery mannys tale book vpon amendement stond commaudement whome myn hert acorde send vnto myn owne lord whiche lancastre henry named hyghe god hath hym proclamed ful knyghthode al grace wold werk embrace hoole trust hoole byleue god graunte mote wel acheue empus preteritum presens fortuna beatum liquit antiquas vertit vrbe vias progenuit veterem concors dilectio pacem dum facies hominis nuncia mentis erat legibus vnicolor tunc temporis aura refulsit iustici plane tunc que fuere vie nunc que latens odium vul tum depingit amoris pace que sub ficta tempus ad arma tegit instar ex varijs mutoble cameliontis lex ge rit regnis sunt noua iura noius climata que fuerant solidissima sic que per orbem soluuntur nec eo centrum qi etis habent e statu regno que vt dicunt secundnm temporalia videlicet tempore regis ricardi secundi auno regni sui sextodecimo shal drawe mynde tyme passed fynde world stoode al welthe tho lyf helth plente tho ry chesse tho fortune tho prowesse tho knyghthode pry name wherof ye wide worldes fame wryte cronycles yet withhold iustyce lawe tho holde pryuelege regalye fast al baronye worshiped astate cytees knewe debate peple stood obeysaunce vnder reule gouernaunce pee rightwysenesse keste charyte tho stood reste mannys hert courage shewed thenne vysage word lyche conceyte wtthout semblaunt deceyte tho ther vnenuyed loue tho vertu set aboue vyce put vnder foote stant crop vnder rote world chaunged oueral therof moost specyal loue falle discord take record euery lond partye comyn voys whiche may lye nought vpon one vpon alle men clepe calle seyne regnes ben deuyded stede loue hate guyded werre wol pee purchace lawe hath take hyr double face iustyce oute way ryghtwysenes gone awey thus loke euery halue men seen soore without salue whiche al world hath ouertake ther reygne al take euery clymat hath dyele tornynge whele whiche blyude fortune ouerthroweth wherof certayne noman knoweth heuene wote done duelle vnder mone stond world vppon namely power hem ben worldes guydes good counseylle euery side ben kept vpright suche wyse hate breke nought thassise loue whiche al chyef kepe reygne oute meschyef al reson wold vnto hym whiche heued membres buxom shal bo sholde eke trouth alowe al hert make hem chere good counseyl good al though man wyse hym selue yet wysedom tivelue yf stonde one thenne anone god grace wold sende make thylk werre ende whiche euery day groweth newe gretely rewe specyal cristes sake whiche wold owne lyf forsake amonge men yeuen pee men tellen netheles loue world departed stant pee vneuene parted hem lyuen dayes loke al assayes hym wold reson seche comon worldes speche wonder thylk werre none wote hath yt werre lond hym self deceyueth dysese parte receyueth yet take men kepe thylk lord whiche al may kepe whome counseyl may hyd vpon world whiche tyd amende wherof men pleynen trewe hertes pleyne reconsyle loue ayene whiche kyng souerayne al worldes gouernaunce hygh purucaunce afferme pee bytwene londes take cause hondes world may stande appesed godbeede also plesed quas coluit moises vetus aut nouus ipse iohannes hesternas leges vix colit ista dy sic prius ecclesia bina virtute rokta nunc magi inculta p llet vtra que via pacificam petri vagus nam mucro resumens horruit x verba cruoris iter nuc tamen assiduo gladium de sangiune tinctum vi rat auaricia bege repente sacrum sic lupus pastor pater hostis mors miscrator prede que largitor pax orbe timor estatu cleri vt dicunt secundum spiritualia videlicet tempore ro th gilbonensis qui nomen clemetis tus est sibi tunc antipape thynk vpon dayes old lyf clerkys hold men seyn yt tho ensample wle al tho wysedom vertue souyten vnto god fyrst bysoughten substaunce scole ne shold fole witte vpon none erthly werkes ayene astate clerkis yt myghten flee vyce whiche symon hath offyce wrerof takyth gold honde thyke tyme vnderstode lumbard made none exchaunge bisshopryches chauge ne yet letter send dignyte ne prouende curyd without cure chirche kay aduenture armes brigantaylle stode thyng thenne vpon bataylle fyght make cheste yet thought hem honeste symplycyte pacyence maden thenne defence court worldly regaille hem thenne bataylle veyne honour nought desyryd whiche hath proud herte fyred humylyte tho withholde pryde vyce holde holy chirche largesse yafe thenne dyde grete almesse poure men nede eke chast word dede wherof peple ensample toke lust al vpon boke preche pray wyse men ryght waye suche stoode trouth vnlered lo thus petrus barge stered hem ylke tyme thus cam fyrste mannys ere feyth cryst al good thurgh hem ware good sobre chast large wyse men seyn wyse symon cause hath vnder take worldes swerd hond take wonder netheles whan crist hym self hath bode pee set testament holy chirche went lawe posyzyf hath set make werre stryf wordly goodes may laste god wote cause last euery ryght wronge also whyle lawe rewlyd clerkes werre intende shal amend woful world thynges make pee bytwene kynges lawe charyte whiche propre dewte belonged vnto preesthode thynketh make manhode heuen world nyghe vayne glorye eke sleygh whiche couetyse hath withhold none thynge behold myghten wynne thus werres begynne wherof holy chirche taxed poynt axed dysme goth bataylle though crist myght auayle hem ryght waye swerd chirche kaye torned holy bede cursyng euery stede whiche shold stonde vpon feyth cause ere leyth astonyd quarell shold worldes heele men sayn pestyle nce whiche hath expellyd pacyence fro clerge specyal shewyd oueral euery thyng whan greuyd yf gregory beleuyd bokes wryte doth v somdele wete cause thylke prelacye god nought companye euery werke foundyd shal stonde el confoundid cristes sake desyreth care take nought pryde thylk astate bere name prelate shal reson proufyte holy chirche vpon plyte hath set coscyence worldes reuerence ther suche many gladde whan sylke astate made nought meryte charge wold hem self discharge pouerte become grete pompe beyete scry e eke pharysee moyses vpon see chayre hygh ben sette wherof feyth ofte lette whiche bytake hem kepe crystescause al day slepe world nought foryete wele hym maye gete offyce court honouryd strong coffre hath al deuouryd vnder kaye auaryce tresour benefyce wherof poure shulne clothe ete drynke house bothe charyte goth al vnknowe greyne pyte knowe slouthe kepyth lybrarye whiche longeth sayntuarye study vpon worldes lore suffisith ght without delycacye swete tothe hath suffryd fordoth abstynence al ther loken ouer ethna brenne clergye al openly mannes eye auynyon peryence therof hath youen euydence men seyn hem deuyded yet cause nought decyded sayd euer shal bytwene twoo stole lyth fall whan men wenen best sytte holy chirche suche flytte rewe vnto v alle god graunte mote wel byfalle towardes hym whiche hath ye trouth ofte seen mochel slouth whan men ben drynke cuppe doth moche harme wha ye fire vppe yf somwho flamme stauche speke vpon brauche proud enuye hath made spring scysme causeth bringe newe secte lollardye also many heresye among clerkes hem selue better dyke delue stonde vpon ryght feyth knowe al yt byble sayth erre som clerkes vpon hond sho set vpon foote gloue acordeth behoue resonable mannes vse men bebelden vertuse crist erthe taught hyere sholde suche maner among hem hold wyse papacye desguyse vpon dyuers electyon whiche stant thaffection sendry londes al aboute whan god wol shal weve oute f trouthe mote stande atte last yet argumenten fast vpon pope astate wherof fallen grete debate cl rk sayd ye nay thys ey dryue forth daye eche hem hym self amendeth worldes good none entendeth whiche comyn proufyte seyen god myghty shal ordeyne wylle ther make none skylle peryll feyth euery clerke herte leyth kepe world specyal cause general whiche vnto holy chirche longeth none hem vnderfongeth shapen ony resystence thus ryght hath noo defence ther loue ther hold thus broke cristes fold wherof flok withoute guyde deuoured euery syde lak hem vnwar shepeherdes wyttes beware vpon world halue sharp pryk stede salue vsen wherof hele hurte shold hele shepe ful wulle vpon bak tose pulle whyle ther ony thyng pylle though none skylle wold wynne leue nought whan begynne vpon hir acte procede whiche good shepeherdes dede vpon also men seyn fro lese whiche pleyn breres forcatche wolden lache suche duresse bereue shal vpon thornes leue wolle whiche brere hath tore wherof shepe ben al tore herdes make hem lese feynen chalk chese though speke teche well done em self therof dele yf wolf come wey goostly staf thenne aweye wherof shold flok defende yf poure shepe offende ony thyng though lyte ben alredy smyte thus euer tale stroke falle vpon smale vpon ben grete hem lacketh hert bete vnder clerkes lawe men seen merel al mysdrawe wol saye general ther somme specyal whome al vertue duelleth tho ben thappostel telleth qiu vocatur deo tanquam aaron god electyon hath cleped perfectyon maner aawn nothyng thylk caas symon whiche foldes gate hath lete goth gate gone ryght weye ther ben also somme men saye folowen symon atte heles who carte goth vpon wheles couetyse worldes pryde holy chirche goth besyde whiche weth ward vysage nought courage yf men loke holy chirche bitwene word werche ther ful grete difference prechen v audyence noman shal soule empeyre al chery feyre worldes good telle also fayen ther helle whiche vnto mannys synne due bydden v therfor eschewe wykked good wordes vnderstode thenketh wold yet bytwene ernest game ful oftyme torned wyse holy tale deuyse merytory thylke dede charyte clothe fede poure folk parte worldes good departe noo thyng nought haue also feyn good saue penaunce abstynence chastyte contynence pleynly speke ylke body fat whiche deynte mete kepe leyen softe slepe whan hath elles al wylle chastyte shal stonde stylle netheles say aunter myssay touchend thishow euer stonde wyl nought vnderstonde therof haue nought done made fyrst mone highe god goodnes ther cause redresse ony man accuse may reson trouthe excuse vyce hem ben vngood repreef good euery man owne werkes shal bere thus clerkes good men ben comende al god amende worldes eye myrrour examplarye reulen taken hede bet wene men godbede vulgaris popul regali lege subact dum iacet vt mitis digna subibit si caput extollat lex sua frena relax vbi sibi velle iubet rigridis instar habet ignis aqua dominans duo sut pietate carentes ira tamen plebis est violenta magi destatu plebis vt diaint secudu actidencia mutabilia speke yt comune drede fortune hath bifalle sodry lo de ofte defaute bondes al sodenlyche wyst tonue whan lye aryst breken ronne al aboute whiche endles shold nought gone eke ful ofte lytel skare vpon bank men ware ete ye streme grete peyn euery man shal restreyne lawe faylleth errour groweth wyse ne troweth hath proued ofte er thus comyn clamour euery lond peple duelleth eche compleynt telleth world myswent therupon iugement yeueth euery man sondry wyse man wold hym self auyse conseyence nought mysuse may wel fyrst excuse god whiche euer stant one hym ther defaute none must stonde vpon v elue nought vpon ten ne twelue plenerlyche vpon v alle men cause shal byfalle nota contra hoc qd aliq sortem fortune aliqui influenciam planetaru penunt per quod vt dicitur reru euentus necessario contingit sed pocius di cendum est qd ea que no pro er aduersa hoc mundo vocamus secu dum merita et demerita hominum dig der iudicio proueniunt netheles somme men wryte sayn fortune wyte som men holde oppinion constellacion whiche causeth al man dothe god w te bothe whiche sothe world propre kynde euer vntre w blynde inproperlyche demeth fame blameth nought blame preyfeth nought preyse thus whan shal thynges peyse ther deceyt balaunce al varyaunce v shold v better auyse falle ryse world aresteth fallith al man ouer al owne cause wele wo fortune clepe soo man hym self groweth otherwyse troweth beholde peple israel euer whyle dyden wel fortune hem debonayre whan dyden contrayre fortune contraryende proueth wele ende world wonderful may whyle stande ful though seme wel beseyn euery worldes thyng vayne euer goth whele euer stant man doute fortune stant stylle hath ther man wylle al fer ony man maye knowe ther lasteth noo thyng throwe boecius qm dul edo humane vite multa amaritudine aspersa est world stant euer vpon debate may syker none astate ther fro vp doun world goth euer hath done euer shal wherof fynde specyal tale wryten byble whiche must nedes credible conclusyon seyth vpon deuysyon stant noo worldes thyng maye laste til dryue laste fro fyrst regne al daye soo befall regnes meuable man hym self hath culpable whiche gouernaunce fortuneth al worldes chaunce prosper aduersus obliquo tramite versus inmudus mud decepit oe genus mudus euentu versatur vt alea casu qua eler ludis iactat auara manus sicut ymago biri varia tur tempora mundi stat que nichil fir mu preter amare deum hic pro ogo tractat de statua illa quam rex nabugodonosor viderat sumpnis cuius caput aureu pectus argenteum venter eneus tibe ferree pedum vero quedam par ferrea quedam fictilis videbatur sub qua brorum diuersitate secundu danielis exposicionem huius mundi variacio fi gurabatur hygh almyyty purueauce who eterne remembrauce fyrst euery thyng present hath prophecye sent suche wyse thou shalt danyel mater yt world shal torne wede til byfalle vnto ende wherof tale telle shal whiche bytokned alle nabugodonosce slepte sweuen toke kepte til morowe aryse therof sore agryse til danyel dreme told prayd hym fayr wold rede tokene may seyd bedde lay thought syghe vpon stage stood wonder strauge ymage hede al neck also fyne gold bothe two breste shulders armes al syluer tharmes wombe al doune kne bra vpon see legges made al steel foot also somdele somdele part hem take erth men myyt pottes make feble meged strong myght stande long hic narrat vlteri de quodam lapide gradi vt dicto sompnio videbatur ab excelso mote super statua corruens ipsam quasi nichilum penitus contriuit thought yt syghe grete stone hylle hyghe fylle doun sodeyne anenture vpon foot figure whiche stone al broke gold syluer erthe styel bra pouder brought forth torned nought hic loquitur de iterpretacioe sopnij mo dicit de significacione capitis aurei sweuene whiche danyel anone rad seyde hym fygure straunge betokeneth ye world shal chauge wax lasse worth lasse til nought al ouer passe neck hede gold sayd betoken shold worthy world noble ryche whiche none shal lyche de pectore argenteo syluer ouer forth shal ben world la se worth de bentre eneo wobe bra token wers world whiche steel sawe afterward world bytokeneth hard de tibeis ferreis bvt yet werst euery dele last yt whan erth steell sawe foot departed bytokeneth moche woo de significacione pedum que ex duabus materijs disco dantibus adinui em diuisi extiterunt whan yt world deuyded mote algate fare amys erth menet steel gydre may laste w ell one waste mo e nedes falle laste de lapide statua cofringente ston fro ye hully stage saw donne falle ye ymage bath poudre broke sueuene hath danyel vnloke sayde goddes myght whiche whan men wene moost vpriyt stonde shal hem ouer caste world last newe shal begynne shal neuer twynne al payne al pee world shal last endles h scribit qualiter huius seculi regna var mutacionib prout dictum statua figurabatur secundum temp distinctioes sensibiliter hat di nuuntur thus expowned danyel kynges sueuen fair wel babyloyne cyte wysest chaldee n uden wyte mente told al hool entent partye byfalle gold fyrst regne alle de seculo aureo quod capite statue designatum est tempore ipsius nabugodonosor regis caldee v que regnum ci regis persarum kynges tyme tho last many dayes while monarchye al world partye babyloyne subgette held hym styll pliyt til world bygan dyuerse yt whan kyng perse whiche cyrus hight ayene pee forth sone cambyses babyloyne al empyre ryght wold hem self desire put vnder subiection toke possession slayn baltazar kyng whiche lost regne al thyng de seculo argenteo quod pectore designatum est tempore ipsi regis ciri v que reg um allexandri regis macedonie thus whan wone world siluer bigone gold passed wyse goth aboute regne darius felle perse thus ther alysander put hem vnder wrouyt ar e many wo der monarchye lefte g eces astate vp lefte persiens gone vnder foote suffre nedes mote de seculo en quod ventre desig natum est tempore ipsiue allexandri v que regnum iulij romanoru imperatoris tho world bigan brus siluer ended tyme thus last til befelle laste kyng whan day come strength deth ourcome netheles yet dyed shope hi regne deuyde knyghtes whiche hym serued haue deserued yaf conquestys wan wherof grete werre tho bygan among hem regnes thorugh proud ennye whiche hem lad til bifell ayene hem thus noble cezar inlius whiche tho kyng rome ond grete bataylle strong hond al grece perse chaldee wan put vnder al thoryent al marche thoccydent gouerne h vnder empyre lord syre held thorugh chyualrye al world monarchye fyrst honour whiche taketh name emperour de seculo ferreo quod tibeis de signatum est tempore iulij cesaris v que regnum caros magni regis fran orum rome wold assaylle ther myyt thyng contreua e euery contrey must obeye tho goth regne bra aweye comen world steel stode aboue vpon whel steel hardest kynde aboue al men fynde metalles suche rome tho myghtyest last longe tyme among romayns tyl bycome vyleyns fals emperour leo constauce sone also pat mon rychesse whiche syluester pure almesse fyrst constantinus lefte fro holy chirche refte adryan whiche pope sawe meschyef caas goth frauce playne prayth grete char emayne suche wyse ther wrought holy chirche ayene brought fraunchyse thr restore pope lust yaf hym thus whan god hath serued toke hath wel deseruyd dyademe orouned rome thus abandouned thempyre whiche cam neuer agayne hon romayn long tyme oode stylle vnder frens kynges wylle til fortune hir whele lad afterward lumbardes nouyt ye swerd ye suffrauce hym kyng fraunce whiche carl caluu clepyd resygned caas thempyre rome vnto lowys cosyn whiche lumbard last yere alberte berenger de seculo nou ssimis iam temporibus ad similitudinem pedum discordiam lapso et diuiso quod post decessu ipsius carolus cum begynne walle cyte withynne stand ruyne decaas feld paleys tonne wast ouer behold thylke astate whiche whylome ye romayns knyghthode cytezeyne peyse byforne chaf ke corne speke rome myght vnnethes stant ther ought vpryght worship worldes good byfore tyme stode worship away man sothe say cause hath ben deuysyon whiche moder confusyon comyth oueral nought mporal spyrytual also dede proueth ie hath many day thorugh venym medled holy chirche erthely thynge cryst hym self maketh knowlechyng noma may geder serue god world bnt swerue froward one stond vnstable crystes word may falle thyng open eye nedeth nought specyfye speke ought mater wyse man may tere world gone aboute whiche wel nyghe wered oute forme fygure whiche danyel scupture expowned fore told bra syluer gold world passed gone vpon old tone stant brutel erthe stele whiche acorden neuer dele mote nedes swerue syde thyng whiche men seen deuyde hic dicit secundu aplm no sum quos fine seculi deuenerunt thappostel writeth vnto v alle saith yt vpo v falle thende ye world may knowe ymage nyghe ouerthrowe world sygnefyed whysome magnyfyed old feble vyle ful meschyef perylle stant deuyded eke also lyche foot told statue aboue thus men seyn lak loue lond deuyded algace fare amys loke euery syde man may see world deuyde werres enso general among crystene oueral euery man secheth wreche yet clerkes alday preche seyn good dedes may none whiche stant nought vpon charyte charyte shold stonde dedely werre taken honde al wo cause man whiche wytte reson tokne wytnesse eche ymage bare lykensse man none beeste fro fyrst vnto mannys heste euery creature ordeyned afterward restreyned whan felle fellen eke whan seke wexen seke man hath passyon sekenes comparyson suffryn creature lo fyrst heuenly fygures hic scribit quod ex diuisionis passione singula creata detrimentum corruptibile paciuntur sonne mone eclypsen ben mannys synne wroth purest eyre synne alofte hath corrupt ful ofte ryght ye highe wyndes blowe anon ben lowe cloudy clere maye wel prouen mannes synne hate whiche maketh welken debate see properte euery thyng degre bynethe among v al stant lyche mater see ebbeth floweth lod welketh groweth tree leues grene bare nothyng sene ther lusty somer floures ther stormy wynter shoures dayes nyytes stant ther thynge vpryghtes lyght derke thus stant al worldes werke disposicion man condycyon thy gregory moral seyth man specyal lasse world properly proueth redyly man soule resonable angel resemblable lyche beste hath felyng lyche tree hath growyng stone ben thus propre qualyte man tellyth clergye world partye whan world mystorneth rete world al ouertorneth lond set fyrmament axen alle jugement ayene man make hym warre ther whyle hym stant al harre remenaunt wold nought acord wyse record man cause al woo world deuyded dyuysyon gospel sayth one hows vpon lay h tyl reygne ouerthrowe thus many man doth knowe dynysyon abouen alle thyng whiche maketh world alleand euer hath syth began may fyrst proue vpon man quod ex sue complexionis mate diuisus homo mortalis existat whiche coplexyon made vpon deuysyon colde hote moyst drye mote verray kynde deye contrarye estate stant euermore suche debate tyl part ouercome ther may fynal pee nome therwyse yf man made al geder one mater withoute jnterupcion ther shold corrupcion engen dyr vpon vnyte ther dyuersyte within hym self may last ne dyeth last man yet ouer ful grete dyuysyon ther thorugh euer strif whyle hym last ony lyf quod homo ex corporis anime condicione diuisus sicut saluacionis ita dampnacionis aptitudinem ingredituz body soule also among hem ben deuyded thyng body hateth soule loueth debateth netheles ful ofte sene werre whiche hem bytwene feble bath vyctorye draweth memorye qualiter adam statu innocen cie diuisus paradiso voluptatis terram laboris peccator proiectus est hath bifalle old new may werre sore rewe whiche fyrst byga paradys ther proued dysese ther wrought thylke werre tho forth brought vyce al dedly synne thorugh whiche dyuysyon cam ynne qualiter populi per vniuersum orbem cultura dei diuisi noe cum sua sequela duntaxat exceptis dilu io interierunt amonge men erth cause ye mater god grete flodes sende al world made ende noe felauship whiche sauf shyp ouer thorugh synne come nembroth syth thempyre nome qualiter edificacione turris babilonis quam dei contemptum nembroth erexit lingua prius hebreica varias lingua celica vindicta di uidebatur whan ye toure babylon hyyt lat make yt wold fiyt ayene ye high goddes myyt wherof deuyded anon ryyt langage suche eutent ther wyst none ment myght nought procede thus stant euery dede synne taketh caas hond may vpryght long stonde synne hir condycyon moder al deuysyon qualiter mundus qui statu diuisionis quali cotidianis presenti tempore vexatur flagellis lapide superuenien te id est diuina potencia v que ad resolucionem omnis carnis subito contere tur tokne whan world shal fayle sayth crist without nyle nyghe worldes ende pee acord wey shal wende al charyte shal seace among men hate encrece whan tokenes falle al sodenly stone shal falle danyel hath byknowe whiche al world shal ouerthrowe euery man shal aryse ioye elles iuise shal euer duelle streyt heuen streyt helle heuen pee al acorde helle ful suche discorde ther may loue day thy good whyle man may echone sette pee louen owne broder may wynne worldes welthe afterward soule helthe hic narrat exemplum de concordia et vnitate inter homines pro uocanda et dicit quida arion uu citharista ex sui cantus cithare que consonam melodia tante virtutis extiterat vt ipsum non solum virtum cum viro sed eciam leonem cum cerua lupu cum agno canem cum lepore jpsum audientes vnanimiter ab que vlla discor dia ad inuicem pacificauit wold god yt one another suche aryone whiche harp suche temp ire therto good mesure songe bestes wylde made note tame mylde hynde pee lyon wolf pee moto hare pee stood houd euery man vpon ground whiche aryon tyme herde wel lord shepeherde brought hem al good acord comon lord lord comon also set loue bothe two put wey melancolye lusty melodye whan euery man louz yf ther suche one nowe whiche coude harpe dyde myght auayle many stede make pee hate whan men thynken debate thyng good yt wysedom wa eth wood reson torned rage mesure vpon outrage hath set world drede bryngeth comon drede whiche stant euery mannes dore whan sharpnes spore hors syde smyteth sore greueth ofte speke matere whiche none god may stere good tyde euery man vpon syd besought prayd pee whiche cause al encrees worship worldes welthe hertes reste soules helthe withoute pee stond nothyng good thy cryst shed blood pee byseketh alle men amen amen amen amen explicit prologus incipit liber primus naturatus amor nature legib orbem subdit vnanimes co tat esse feras huius enim mundi p n eps amore esse vide ur u eget diues pauper et omnis e sunt agone pares amor lebis ad insidias vertit ta est amor egra salus vex uies pius error bellica pax vul du ce suaue malum rologo tractatum bat nu existit qualiter hodierne condicionis diuisio cari dis ctionem superauit intendit ad rsens libellum suu cuius noi c fessio amantis nuna patur de illo amore quo non solu manum genue sed et cuncta anima naturaliter subiciuntur j may stretche vnto ye heuene myn hod set al euene world euer balauce stat suffysauce grete thynges compasse mote lete ouer passe treten vpon thynges thy style wrytynges fro day forth thenke chaunge speke thyng strauge whiche euery kynde hath vpon honde therupon world mote stonde hath done syth began shal whyle ther ony man loue whiche mene trete shal sene whiche ther noman hym reule lawes loue oute reule moche lyte wel nyghe euery man wyte netheles ther man al world wyse loue temper mesure fallyth auenture wytte ne strengthe may helpe whiche elles wold hym yelpe rathest throwen vnder foote ther wyght therof bote yet neuer suche couyne couthe ordeyne medycyne thyng god lawe kynd hath sett ther may noman fynd ryght salue suche soore hath shal euermore loue mayster wylle ther lyf make skylle euer hym lyst sette ther myght whiche may hym lette shal fallen last wysedome cast falleth vpon chaunce yf ther euer balaunce whiche fortune gonerued may wel leue lerned loue hath balauce honde whiche wol reson vnderstonde loue blynde may see thy may certeynte beset vpon iugemente whele aboute wente yeueth grace vndeserued fro ye hath hym serued ful ofte wey hath taken fee playeth dye therupon shal byfalle tyll chauce falle shal lese shal wynne thus ful ofte men begynne yf wysten ment wolde chaunge al jugement hic quast persona alioru quos amor alligat fingens se auctor esse amantes varias eorum passiones varijs huius libri distinctionibus per singula scribere proponit preue self one tho whiche scole vnderfonge soth go longe speke mater may yow telle yf ye wol wonder hap whiche befelle hard felle touchend loue fortune whiche lyketh comune pleynly tellen oute hem louers aboute fro poynt poynt wol declare wryten woful care wofnl day woful chaunce men may take remembrauce shal rede good feyth wold rede euery man ensample take wysedome whiche hym bytake wote good appryse teche forth suche empryse preyse therfor wyll wryte shewe al openly hou loue gedre mette wherof world ensample fette may whan go thylke vnsely iolyf wo r ule stant wey glad gladnes awey yet may withstonde ought men may vnderstode non ego sampsonis vires non ulis arma inco sum sed vt hij victus amore pari discant alij docet experiencia facti rebus ambiguis que sunt henda via deuius orde ducit tep tata pericula sequentem instruit ter go simul ille cadat quibus er go venus casus laqucauit amantem orbis exemplum scribere cendo pal hic declarat materia dicens qualiter cupido ignito iaculo sui cordis memoriam graui vlcere perforauit qd genius percipiens jpsum vt dicit quasi mortis articulo spasmatum ad confitendum se genio sacerdoti super amoris causa sic semiuiuum speciali ter commendauit vpon poynt byfalle loue whiche yt j falle thynke telle matere herkne wol fortune hath ferde endyrday j forth ferde walke telle maye moneth maye whan euery ryd hath chose make theketh myrthes make loue hath acheued nothynge releued forther fro loue erthe heuene aboue speke ony spede wyst none rede man fare nto wode gan fare synge byrdes whan j ye wode amyddes fonde soote grene pleyne gan wo compleyne wysshyng wepyng al myn one myrthes made none hard ylke throwe ofte sythes ouerthrowe ground withoute breth euer wysshed deth whan oute peyne awoke cast vp many pytous look vnto heuene sayd thus thou cupyde thou venus thou god loue thou goddesse pyte mekenesse doth playnly lyue dye certes suche maladye haue long haue myght make wyse man mad shold long endure venus quene loues cure thou lyf thou lust thou mannes hele behold cause quarelle yeue sompart thy grace may fynde place thou gracious none word saw anone kyng loue quene kyng eyen wroth chere aweyward fro cast forth passed last netheles forth went fyry dart thought sent threwe thorugh myn hert rote hym fonde none bote benger hym lyst duelle whiche source welle wele wo shal betyde hem louen tyde abode allen cast uoo goodly chere thus netheles sayde art thou sone abrayde ryght man doth oute slepe therof took ryght good kepe bad nothyng adrad al nothyng glad ne sawe cause efte axed sayde caytyf lyeth wolde ye lady dere shal hool elles deye sayd telle thy maladye thy soore whiche thou pley nest ne hyde nouyt yf thou feynest medycyne madame man thyne thy court haue long serued aske haue deserued som wele long wo bygan loure thoo sayd ther many yow faytours may thou art ryght suche one feyntyse seyst thou hast seruyse netheles wyst wele word stode whele withoute ony feyterye algate maladye bud telle say trouthe madame yf ye wold haue routhe quod thenne wold telle yow sey forth quod telle hou thy sekenes euery dele madame wele lyf therto wol last loke cast sayd aunter yf thou lyue wylle fyrst thou shryue netheles wote self al vnto preest whiche cometh anone wol thou telle one one bothe thy thought al thy werk genius myn owne clerk come forth mannes shryft quod venus tho vplyft hede gan beholde self preest whiche wolde redy set hym doune confessyon confessus genio si sit medicina salutis experiar morbis quos tulit ipsa venus lesa quidem ferro medicantur membra saluti raro tamen medicum vulnus amoris habet ic dicit qualiter genio pro confessione sedenti prouolutus amas ad confitendum se flexis genibus incuruatur supplicans tamen vt ad sui se sus informacione confessor ille dice dis opponere sibi benign dignaretur worthy preest holy spekend thus began seyde benedicite sone felycyte loue eke wo also thou shalt shryue bothe two thou loues sake hast felt lete nothyng forsake telle pleynlyche byfalle aud yt word gan doun falle knee deuocyon ful grete contrycyon sayd domiuus myn holy fadre genius thou hast experyence loue who reuerence thou shalt shryne tyme pray lete mystyme shryfte dystourbed al myn hert conturbed ne may wyttes gete shal moche thyng foryete yf thou wolt synne oppose fro poynt poynt suppose ther shal thyng left behynde wyttes blynde ne self teche tho bygan anone preche wordes debonayre sayd softe fayre place set thy shryfte oppose venus goddesse aboue touchend who preest loue sermo genij sacerdotis super confessione ad amantem bvt netheles certayne skylle mote algate nedes wylle nought make spekynges loue thynges touchen cause vyce bylongeth thoffyce prestes who ordre bere wol nothyng forbere eche vyces one one shal shewe euerychone wherof thou myght take euydence rewle thy conscyence conclusyon fynal conclude wold specyal loue who seruaunt cause cam thynke bothe two fyrste myn ordre longeth vyces telle rewe next abouen al shewe loue wol propyrtees stond degree disposicyon veuus who condycyon must folowe hold loue al withholde lesse wyte though ne conne lyte thynges wyse taught suche wyse nought comyn vse speke vyces vertuse al loue lore venus bookes nomore techen nether text ne glose moche suppose syt preest wel wyd aud shame yf lewed presthode forme wol thy shryfte enforme last thou shalt vyces thy matere loue shal hem remeue yu shalt knowe meue man shal axe seyne touchend shryft mote pleyne nedeth nought make queynt trouth wordes wol peinte wol axe thy sone shal pleynly thou shalt knowe vnderstonde poyntes shryfte stode vi et audit fragiles sut ostia metis que viciosa man claudere nulla pt est ibi largo via graditur qua cordis ad antrum hostis ingrediens fossa talenta rapit hec michi confessor genius pamordia profert dum sit extremis vita remorsa mali nunc tn vt potent feminina loquela fateri ver ba per o timide conscia mentis agam hic confessio amantis cui de duobns precipue quin que sen b hoc est de visu auditu confessor pre ceteris opponit byytwene lyf deth herde prestes tale er asuerd prayd hym say wyl wold obeye forme appryse tho spak suche wyse bad shold shryue couchend wyttes fyue share amended hem myspended tho properly gate thorugh whiche herte algates cometh al thyng vnto feyre whiche may manys soule empeyre mater brouyt ynne sone thynk fyrst begynne wyce thyn eye hath stonde whiche vnderstonde moost princypal alle thorugh whome ye perylle may befalle speke loues kynde ful many suche man may fynde whiche euer cast eye loke yf myght aspye ful ofte thyng ne toucheth herte soucheth hyndrynge another wyght thus ful many worthy kynyt many lusty lady bothe hath ful ofte sythe wrothe eye theef loue doth ful grete meschyef also owne part ful ofte ylke fyry dart loue euery brenneth thorugh hym hert renneth thus mannes eye first hym self greueth alder werst many tyme knoweth vnto owne harme groweth sone herkne thy tale ware therby thyn eye kepe warde see passe nought warde hic narrat confessor exemplum de visu ab illicitis preseruando dicens qualiter acceon cadmi regis thebarum nepos dum quadam foresta venacionis causa spaaretur accidit vt ipse quendam fontem nemorosa arborum pulcritudine circu uentum superueniens vidit enim dia nam cum suis nimphis nudam flu mine balncantem quam diligencius intuens oculos suos muliebri nudita te nullatenns auertere volebat vnde indignata diana ipsum cerui figuram transformauit vyde sayth booke ensample touchend mysloke sayth whilome ther one worthy lord whiche acceone hote cosyn nyghe hym be fyrst hyghe vpset whiche kyng cadme hyght acceon wel myght aboue al cast chere vsed yere yere houndes grete horne among wodes thornes make huntyng chace hym best thought euery place fyude game way ther rood hunte play hym felle vpon tyde huntyng cam ryde forest one sawe vpon grene gras fayre fressh flonres sprynge herd among leues synge throstel nyghtyngalc thus er wyst dale cam wher lytel pleyne al round wel beseyn bnsshes grene cedres hyghe ther within caste eye myddes pleyne sawe welle fayr ther myght noman telle whiche dyana naked stood bathe play hyr flood many nimphe serueth eye awey ne suerueth fro whiche naked al wonder wroth al hym whiche goddesse forshoop anone lykenesse made hym take herte whiche fore houdes sterte ronne besylyche aboute many horne many route maden moche noyse crye last vnhappelye hert owne houdes slough hym vengeauce al drough lo sone man caste eye amys whiche acceon hath dere abought beware thy nought ofte hede toke better wynke loke proue ouyde poete also tale whiche matere acordeth sayth al thou shalt hic ponit aliud exemplum de eo de vbi dicit quidam princeps nomine phorce tres progenuit filias gorgones vulgo nuncupatas que vno partu exorte deformitatem monstrorum serpentinam obtinuerunt qui bus citra etatem peruenerant talis destinata fuerat natura quicum que ea aspiceret lapidem subito mutabatur et sic plures incaute respicientes visis illis perierunt fed perseus mile clipeo palladis gladio que mercu rij munitus ea extra montem athelantis cohabitantes auimo audaci ab que sui periculo interfecit methamor telleth thus yt lord phorche w hote doughters thre bnt vpon natyuyte suche constellacyon mannes nacyon fro kynde myswent lykenes serpent bothe one hem cleped stellybone suster snryale thyrd tellyth tale meousa hyght netheles comon name gorgones euery countrey ther monstres whiche men doute men clepe hem one eye among hem thre poure partye whiche myght see hath hath cause nede lad throwes eche hem wonder thyng yet amys ther wherof telle al man hem chere cast hem byhelde al fast oute man stone shape thus many one deceyued wolde mysloke ne sholde perseus worthy knyght whome pallas grete myght halpe took hym sheld therto eke god mercurye also lent hym swerd felle beyonde athlans hyghe hylle monstres foughte ther fond dyuerse men thylk lond thorugh syght hem mystorned standed stone whiche wysedome pro wesse god goddesse sheld pallas gan embrace whiche couerd sauf face mercurius swerd oute drough bare hym slough dredeful monstres al thre confessor sone auyse thou thy syght mysuse case thyn eye vpon meduse thou torned stone wyse man neuer none yf wol eye kepe take foule delyte kepe lust ny ofte nome thorugh streugthe loue come myllokyng hath ferd haue told hast thou herd good sonne take good hede ouer yet vede thou beware thyne heryng whiche hert tydynge many wnyte hath brought tarye mannes thonght netheles good thyng wherof man maye lere vertu accordaut toward al remenaunt good torne ere fro es yf man soo hym may ful ofte mysbefalle rede ensample amonges alle wherof kepe wel ere ought put man fere hic confessor exemplum narrat vt non ab auris exaudicione fatua animus deceptus inuoluatur et dicit qualiter ille serpens qui aspis wcatur quendam preciosissimum lapidem nomine carbunculum sue frontis medi gestas contra verba cantantis aure vnam assigendo promit et aliam sue caude stimulo firmissime obturat aserpent whiche aspydis cleped kynde hath stone noblest alle whiche carbucle calle bereth hede aboue hight whiche man sliyghte stone wynne hym daunte corecte hym wold enchaute anone perceyueth leyth doune one ere al plat vnto gronnde hold fast eke tother al faste stoppeth taylle sore wordes lasse ne enchauntement ne heveth wyse hym self skyeveth hath wordes wayued thns ere nought deceyued aliud exemplum super eodem qualiter rex vlixes cum bello troiano versus greciam nauigio remearet et prope illa monstra maximum sirenes nuncupata angelica voce canorano ipsum ventorum aduersitate nauigare oporteret omnium nautarum suorum aures obturari coegit thyng yt recordeth lyche vnto sample acordeth whiche tale troye fynde syrenes wonder kynde ben monstres bookes bellen greete see duellen body bothe vysage lyke woman yong age vp fro nauyl highe doune bynethe men may see bere fysshes fygure oner suche nature swete steuene lyke melodye heuene woman wy synge note grete lykyng suche mesure suche mysyke wherof shippes beswyke passen costes whan shipmen lay ere vnto wyce advyce wene paradys whiche hem helle reson may hem duelle whan grete lustes shippes stere besylyche vppon note herkene suche wyse assote hyr ryght cours weye foryete ere obeye saylen tyl byfalle perylle falle shippes drawe monstres slawe fro perylle netheles wysedom kyng vlyxes escapeth ouer passeth fore hyr hand compasseth noman companye hath power vnto folye ere lust cast hem stopped al fast none hem maye hem syng whan forth come saylyng suche gouernauce honde monstres haue withstod slough hem grete partye thus saut nauye wyse kyng thorugh gouernauce confessor wherof sone remembrauce thou myght ensample take haue told thou wel ware yeue credence yf thou see euydence yf thou woldest take kepe wysely couthest warde kepe thyne eye ere haue spoke haddest thou gate stoke fro suche felye comyth wynne thyn hertes wytte whiche within wherof thy loue excedeth mesure many peyne bredeth yf thou couthest sette rewle tho two thre ethe rewle thy thy wyttes fyue wol shryue ylke two tel therfor yf hast thou thyne eye ought myschrow amans fader ye bekuowe haue hem cast vpon meduse therof may nought excuse myn hert growen stone lady therupon hath suche prynte suche graue nought self saue opponit confessor sayst yu sone thyn ere fader gyltyf whan may lady wyt hath lost steve nought ulyxes dede falle anon vpon stede see lady stonde ther yow vnderstonde pulled thought reason leueth nought wherof may defende confessor good sonne god amende thynketh thy spech thy wyttes ryght seche thyn ere thyne eye wol specyfye wol axen ouer thynges celsior est aquila que leone forcior ille quem tumor elati cordis ad alta mouet sunt specie quin que quibus est superbia ductrix clamat et multis mundus adheret eis lauando faciem ficto pallore subornat fraudibus ipocrisis melle verba suis sic que pios animos sepe ruit muliebres ex humili verbo sub latitante dolo hic loquitur septem sunt peccata mortalia quorum caput superbia vanas specie habet et carum prima ipocrisis dicitur cuius proprietatem secundum vicium confessor amanti declarat sone shal enforme ther ben yet another forme dedly vyces seuen applyed wherof herte ofte plyed thyng shal hym greue fyrst hem thou shalt byleue pryde whiche princypal hath hym especyal mynystres syue ful dyuerse whiche shal reherce fyrst sayd ipocrysye thou art compauye telle forth sone shryue clene amans iwote fadre ye mene bnt wold yow beseche ye somwey teche ben ipocryte yf wyte wol beknowe sone ypocryte man whiche feyneth coseyen though al innocence withoute within doth wold wynne desyre wyne astate anone whan come ther weth corne torned gras rose thorne lambe byforne wolf thus malyce vnder colour iustyce peple telleth ordres wyten duelleth counseyll thylk world whiche forsaketh drawen ayene cloteth ryches men seyn vnder symplest pouerte doth seme grete deserte thyng whiche lytel worth within seyth open fy synne secreet ther vyce whiche ny noryce euer chere sobre softe goth blessyd ofte wherof blynde world dretcheth yet al ne stretcheth rewle vpon relygyon next condicyon suche clepe hem holy chirche sheweth eke worche among wyde furred hodes gete hem worldly goodes hem self thylke setten moost world blame yet contrarye lore ther nothyng louen semed lyght werke dedes whiche inward derke thus double ypocrysye whiche deuoute apparancye byser set vpon face wherof toward worldes grace semeth wel ryght thewed yet herte al beshrewed netheles stant byleued hath purpoos ofte acheued worship worldes welthe takyth sayd stelthe thorugh couerture falla ryght semblable caas vyce hath eke offycers among seculeres grete men sinale accompte set tale passe comune suche hem lyke comune sayth wold socoure peple wol deuoure day many one whiche speketh peter iohn thynketh iudas hert ther shal worldes good astert hand yet geueth almesse fasteth ofte hereth messe mea culpa whiche seyth vpon breste ful ofte leyth hond case vp ward eye though crystes face syghe soo semeth syght alone al myght rescue holy dede yet hert stede among bedys moost deuoute goth worldes cause aboute myght waryson encrese coparyson hic tractat confessor cum ama te super illa jpocrisia que sub amoris facie fraudulenter lat tando mulieres ipsi ficticijs credulas sepissime decepit innocentes ther louers suche sort feyne hem huble port al ypocrysye whiche deceyte flaterye hath many worthy wyght begyled whan hath tonge fyled softe speche lesyng forth fals pytous lokyng wold make woman wene gone vpon fayre grene whan fallyth myre may haue desyre falleth remenaunt halt word couenaunt tyme helspede ther sloygthe thylk deede whiche ony lones faytour may ne put assay hym belonged done colour reyny mone medycyne vpon face set axeth grace whiche hath sykenes feyned whan vysage desteyned eye vp cast syketh many contenaunce pyketh bryngen hyr byleue thyng whiche wold acheue wherof bereth pale hewe wold seme trewe maketh seke wha heyle whan berest lowest seyle swyfeest begyle woman whiche ylke whyle set vpon hym fayth credence sone yf thou thy conseyence entamed hast wyse shryfte thou myght auyse telle yf amans myn holy fadre certes feyne suche sykenesse nedeth nought wytnesse take god courage hath seke vysage eke thus wel may auowe lowe couthe neuer bo feyne humylyte withoute lyst better loute al thoughtes myn herte thyng shal neuer sterte speke lady dere make hyr ony feyned chere god wote wel ther lye nought chere hath suche thought good feith leueth wele wyll better thousand dele ony chere couthe syre haue yougthe done otherwyse place put therof grace excusen ne shal haue elles oueral loue companye pleyne withoute ypocrysye ther one whiche ser e al though may thank deserue whome yet neuer vnto daye sayd onlyche ye nay yf thought touchend say nought somdele wyte ye clepe ipocryte confessor sone syt wel euery wyght kepe thonyt trouth vp ryght towardes loue al wyse wolde hym wel aduyse hath byfalle matere shold nought feyned chere deceyue loue degre loue enery hert fre deceyt thou feynest therupon thy lust atteynest thou hast wonne thy wyle though lyke whyle thou shalt afterward repente proue myn entente fynde ensample crony que hem loue beswyke quod ipocrisia sit amore pericu losa narrat exemplum qualiter sub reg tiberij imperatoris quidam mile nomine mundns qui romanoru dux milicie tune prefuit dominam paulinam pulcherrima castitatis famosissimam mediantibus duobus falsis presbiteris templo isys domini sui se esse fingens sub fic e sauctitatis ipocrisi nocturno tempore vicia vn idem dux exilium presbiteri mortem ob sui criminis enormitatem damp nati extiterant byfesse old dayes thus whylome emperour tiberius monarche rome thus lad ther worthy romayn wyf pauline hyght whiche euery mannys syght al cyte fayrest men sayden eke lest hath ben euer yet strong man wyt whiche thurgh beaute ne may drawe loue vnder lawe thylke frele bore kynde whiche maketh hert eyen blynde reson may comuned wyse fortuned tale whiche wol mene wyf whiche lustes grene fresshe tendre age may let courage hym wol hyr assote ther duk hote mundus whiche bayllye lede alle chyualrye rome worthy knyght nought suche myght strengthe loue withstode ne brought honde maulgry wold yong wyf loueth hath put al assay wynne thyng whiche ne may gete hyr graunt maner yefte gold ne prayer whan sa mede toward loue myght spede sleyght feyned wrought therupon hym bythought ther cyte temple suche auctoryte whiche grete deuocyon noble woman toune comonlyche pylgremage gone pray thylke ymage whiche goddesse chyldyng cleped name isys temple rewle mynystre lawe whiche tho abouen al prestes two duk whiche thouyt loue gete vpon day hem two mete hath bede come haste ryche feste mete preuy place lord whiche wold thank pur chace eche hem gaf gift spak soo waye shryfte drough hem couyne helpe shape paulyne lust deceyue myght trouthes plyght nyght shold wynne temple therynne shal haue hyr al entent thus acorded forth wente lyste thorugh whiche ipocrysye ordeyned trecherye wherof lady deceyued prestes hadden wel conceyued grete holynesse counterfeyt symplenesse whiche hyd fals courage feyned heuenly message come sayd hyr thus paulyne god anubus hath sente v prestes sayth wol appere nyghtes tyme hym self allone loue hath thy persone therupon hath v bede isys temple stede honestly purueye thou nyght seye hym shalt take vysyon vpon thy condycyon whiche chast ful feyth suche pryce v tolde leyth wol stonde thyn acord bere herof record send v hyder bothe two glad innocence tho suche wordes herd humble chere thus ansuerd seyd goddes wylle al redy fulfylle housbondes leue wold isys temple eue vpon goddes grace abyde seruen hym nyght tyde prestes gone home tho ageyne goth souerayne goddes wylle told hym al pleyne ca wherof deceyued eke bad shold meke al hoole vnto goddes heeste thus whiche honeste god ward hyr entent nyght temple went fals prestes receyuen hyr suche tokue holynesse though sawen hyr goddesse al within preuy place softe bed large space made enterc rteyned afterward engyned whiche al honour supposeth fals prestes opposeth axeth obseruaunce myght moost plesauce god nyghtes reule kepe hyr bydden slepe lyggend vpon bed lofte sayden al stylle softe god anubus wold awake counseylle wyse take preestes fro lady gone wyst gyle none maner sayd tho slepe vpon bed leyd hope shold acheue thyng stood vpon bileue fulfylled holynesse hath fayled gesse closet fast duk hyd pryuely myght perceyue thought deceyue hath suche aray vpon nome whan wold vnto hyr come shold seme hir eye though veryly syghe god anubus suche wyse ypocryyte queyntyse awayteth euer tyl slepte oute place crepte stylle nothyng herde aud bed stalkynge ferde sodenly wyst beclypt armes hyr kyst wherof womannysshe rede wooke nyst rede softe wordes mylde comfort sayd child wold make suche kynde al world shal haue mynde worship ylke sone shal goddes wone ben hym self god also wordes moo whiche feyneth speche ladyes wytte al seche whiche al trouth weneth al vntrouthe meneth blynde tale lad al wyl whan hym thouyt ynouy agayne day hym withdrough pryuely ne wyste bycome lyste oute temple goth waye bygan bydde praye vpond bare ground knelend made offrende prestes yeftes grete yafe home ward strete dnke met sayd thus myghty god whiche annbus hote saue paulyne thou art disciplyne holy mannes myght may hath nyght thyng whiche thou hast euer esche ued grace haue pursued made lyeutenaunt thy way couenaunt fro day ward thyne yf lyke myne stond vpon thyne owne wylle herd tale bare stylle home went bifelle chambr ther fille hyr bed wepe crye sayd derke ypocrysye thorugh who dissimulacyon fals ymagynacyon wykkedly thus deceyued haue apperceyued thanke vuto goddes alle though thus byfalle shal neuer eft while lyue thylk auowe god yeue thus wepend compleyneth hyr fayr face al dysteyneth woful teres eye vpon agonye housbond come sawe ouercome sow axeth hyr hyr ey leth yt hir self bewei eth wel dyde therfore sayd allas wyfhode love whiche whysome honeste beeste defouled two myght speke tho ashamed pytous onde told vnto housbonde sothe al hole tale speche dede pale swouneth wele nyghe laste hyr armes faste vphelde ofte swore othe hyr nothyng wroth wel wote maye ther nouyt netheles within thought hert stood sory plyght sayd wold despyte auengyd euer falle sente vnto frendes alle whan comen fere told hem vpon matere axed hem done auysed sone sayd thought hem best set wyf fyrst rest pleyne kyng vpon mater thyng tho woful wyf comforted al wayes disported tyl somdele amended thus day tuo dispeded thyrd day goth pleyne many worthy cytezeyne many cytezeyne themperour herd seyne knewe falshede vyce sayd wold iustyee fyrste lete prestes take shold forsake put hem question suggestion ne coude one word refuse bnt wold hem self excuse blame vpon duke layd ther ayene couseyl sayd nought excused one two two haue wytte one thylke excusement none ouer sayd hem eke whan men wold vertue seke men shold prestes fynde hir ordre hyghe kynde tuterers weye thy yf ony man forswey thorugh hem excusable thus lawe resonable among wyse inge prestes bothe dampned preuy trecherye hyd vnder fals ypocrysye openly shewed many hem hath beshrewed whan prestes dede temple thylke horryble dede thoughten purge thylk ymage who cause pylgremage drouen also fast fer tyber cast ryuer hath defyed thus temple puryfyed haue thylke horryble synne whiche tyme therynne poynt thus aduyse duk otherwyse loue bestad dome nought hard lad loue put reson awey nought see ryght wey cause respyted deth hym acquyted al exybed loue begyled shal neuer come ayene trouthe vnpleyne may faylen vengeaunce taken remembraunce ypocrysye hath wrought halue men shal nought lyghtly leue al shold wyseman stere shyp suche wyndes blowe fyrst thouh begynne lowe ende nought meuable al broke mast cable shyp sodeyne blast whan men leste wene ouer cast fuloften man may see old tyme hath fynde grete experyence wherof take euydence good war also perylle hym wo hic vlterius ponit exemplum de illa ecia ipocrisia que inter viru viru decipies periculosissima consistit et narrat qualiter greci obsidione ciuitatis troye cum ipsam vi apprehendene nnllatenns potuerunt fallaci animo cum troianis vt dicut perpetuo statuebant super hoc quendam equm mire grossionis de ere fabricatum ad sacrificandum templo minerue confingentes hem yt ben derk wit troye also begyn ipocrysye hath bytrayd whan ye grekes al assayed fonde bataill ne syege myght auayll toune wynne thurgh pro wesse vyce feyned symplesse thorugh sleyghte calcas cryse wan suche maner wyse hors bra lete forge suche entaylle suche forge world neuer man suche another werk began crafty werkman epius made telle thus grekes thoughten begyle kyng troye thylke whyle anthenor enee bothe cyte counseylle wysest rychest myghtyest pryue place trete fayr byhestes yeftes grete gold haue engyned gedre whan couyned feynen make pee vnder yet neuertheles shopen destructyon bothe kynge towne thus fals pee take hem grece vndertake therupon fonde awey strengthe myght awey sleyghte shold helpe thanne ynche large spanne colour pee made telden glade stonden acord shal ben record vnto kyng troye sayden way loue thus pra yden wold thank deserue sacryfyce vnto myuerne pers kepe good entent must offre went kyng counseyled ca anthenor eneas therto hath youen assent pleyne trouthe blent thorugh counterfete ypocrysye sholden sacryfye grekes vnder holynesse anone al besynesse hors bra lete fayr dyghte whiche seen wonder syghte trapped hym selue smale wheles twelue vpon whiche men ynough craft toward ye town drough goth glystrend ayenst sonne tho ther ioye ynough begonne troye grete denocyon came also procession ayenst noble sacryfyse grete honour wyse vnto gate broughte entent whan soughte gate al smale therupon many tale worship mynerue whome comen serue towne whiche vnderstode al thyng goode pee wherof glade gate neptunus made thousand wynter ther fore haue anon broke tore strong wally doune breke large strete hors grete solempnyte brought within cyte offred grete reuerence whiche troye euydence loue pee euermo gregoys token leue tho al hole felauship forth wenten ship crossen sayle made hem yare anone though wolden fare whan blak wynter nyght withoute mone sterre lyght bederked hath water stronde al pryuely gone londe ful armed oute nauye symon whiche made efpye within troye cospyred whan tyme tokne fyred theyr wey holden comen ryght wolden gate broke purpoos ful take spoke er ony man may take kepe whyle cyte slepe slowen al within token myght wyn suche good suffysaunt brenden vp remenaunt thus come oute trecherye whiche vnder fals ypocrysye hyd wened pee tho myghten fynde relees thylk swerd whiche al deuoured fulofte thus swete soured whan knowe tast spylleth many worde wast shal suche peple trete whan weneth beyete shape leese ryght yf woman chese vpon wordes hereth som moste trewe appereth forthest fro trouthe yet fulofte routhe speden vntrewe louen euery day newe wherof lyef loth loue hath cause wroth man luste desyreth loue therupon conspyreth weedes feyned deceyue shal fayle receyue peyne ofte sene confessor thy sone mene fyt wel take hede thou eschewe thy manhede ipocrysye semblaunt thou ne nought deceyuaunt make woman byleue thyng whiche thy byleue suche feynt ipocrysye loue al trecherye thorugh whiche loue deceyned ofte feyned semblannt softe vnnethes loue may beware sone wel dare charge fle vyce many woma hath made nyce loke thou dele al iwys fadre nomore shal confessor sone kepe thou hast swore thou hast herd byfore sayd fyrst poynt pryde next vpon syde shryne speke ouer touchend pryde yet ther poynt second behote whiche inobedyence hote flectere fragi meli reputatur olle fictilis ad cacabu pugna valere neqit que ne lex hoim ne lex diuia valebit flectere multocies corde reflectit amor que non flectit amor non flec tend ab illo sed rigor illi plus ele phante riget ded gnatur amor poterit quos scire rebelles et rudib sorte prestat habere rudem sed qui spote sui subicit se cordis amore frangit aduersis omnia fata pius hic loquitur de secuda specie subie que inobediencia dicitur et primo illius vicij natura simpliciter declarat et tractat cosequente super illa obediecia que curia cupidinis exosa amoris cam ex sua ibesillitate sepissime retardat ti vyce inobediencie ageyne reule coseyence al yt huble disaloweth toward god ne boweth lawes heste man beste whiche goth vpon lustes wylde goth proude vyce vnmylde dysdeyneth al lawe felawe serue may pryde led euery syde selue whome speke whiche wol bowe breke yf loue myght hym plye elles iustyfye hert myght duayle thy sone suche entayle thyn hert disposed telle oute lete nought glosed yf thou vnbuxome loue degre thou shalt thy good world acheue amans fadre ye shal wel byleue yong whelpe whiche affayted hath mayster better wayted couche whan seyth go lowe anone may knowe lady wylle ne bowe grutche sore som thynges doth wherof tha wol telle soth two poyntes bethouyt wold myght nought obeye vnto lady hest dar make byhest sauf ylke two vnbuxome mo confessor opponit ben tho two telle quod fader one comaudeth mouthe close aud shold nought oppose loue whiche ofte preche preuelyche suche speche forbere suffre pee ne myght netheles al world obeye wy though tale nought alowe ayene hir wyll yet mote bowe seche yf myght haue grace thynge may embrace ought speke yet ful ofte speke wroth sayth stylle heest shal fulfylle therto ben obedyent cause fully shent speche le maye noman spede wote rede certes may nought obeye ne mote algates seye somwhat wold mene euer alyche grene grete loue whiche haue wherof saue speche obedyence thus fulofte sylence breke fyrst poynt wherof oute poynt yet pryde vpon syde telle disobeysaunce ful sore stant greuaunce may synke wytt oftyme bytt leue hyr chese newe sayth yf soth knewe fer stonde oute grace shold loue place therof wol disobeye also wel myght seye go take mone sytte bryng wytte neuer roted tre stood fast degre ne stonde fast vpon hyr loue may cast myn hert awey though wolde god wote though neuer sholde seen hyr eye daye yet stont ne maye hyr loue oute brest renue wondre retenue maulgre wol none myn hert euer one none chese whether wynne lese mote hyr loue tyl deye thus breke weye hestes commaudynges trulyche none thynges thy fadre touchand ylke lore yow byseche forme ye pleynly wold enforme myght myn hert reule loues cause reule murmur aduersis ita cocipit ille superb ena quod ex bina sorte pur get eum bina fortune cum spes amore resistit non sine mentali murmure plangit amans h ic loquitur de murmure plac tu qui super oes alios inobediecie secreciores vt ministre illi deseruiant toward vyce trete ther twey thilk estrete name murmur copleynt ther noman chere peynt set glad seblaunt therinne though fortune make hem wynne yet grutche yf lese weye chese wherof myght stonde appesed comonlych dysesed may welthe ne pouerte attempren hem deserte buxomnesse wyse oftyme despyse good fortune badde mannes reson hadde thorugh pryde wherof blynde ryght suche maner kynde ther louers though haue loue al wold craue yet wol grutche somme weye wold nought loue obeye vpon trouthe doo sholde hem lakketh wolde anone shal suche peyne euer vnbuxomly pleyne vpon fortune curse crye wold hertes plye suffre tyll better falle thy yf thou amonges alle hast vsed condycyon sone thy confession telle pleynly thou art fadre knowe wel part ye telle aboue murmur compleynt loue see spede comende ageynst fortune compleynende sayth euermo eke fuloftyme also whan see heuy word heuy chere lady grutche anone wordes dar speke none wherof myght displesyd myn hert dysesed many murmour god wote thus drynke myn owne swote though make semblaunt myn hert al disobeysaunt wyse confesse ye clepe vnbuxomnesse telle counseyl confessor sone rede byfalle weye thou loues lust obeye fer thou myght suffyse fulofte syth suche wyse obedyence loue auayleth al mannes strengthe fayleth wherof yf thou lyst wyte crony que wryte grete ensample thou myght fynde whiche comen mynde ic contra amori inobedientes ad comendacione obediencie confessor super eodem exemplum ponit vbi di que qdam regis sealie filia sue iuuentucis florib pulcherrime ex eius nouerce incantacionibus vetulam turpissimam transformata excitit flo rencius tunc imperatoris claudi nepos mile armis strennuissimus amorosus que legibus intendens ex sua obediencia pulcritudinem pristinam reformauit ther whylom dayes old worthy knyght men old neue perour court courteour wyfles florent hyghte man mochel myght armes desyrous chyualrous amerous fame worldes speche straunge auentures seche rood march aboute felle tyme whan oute fortune whiche may euery threde breke knytte mannes spede shope knyght rood pa strengthe take castel hym ladde fewe frendes hadde felle ylke stoude dedely wounde frghtend owne handes slayn branchus whiche capytayn sone heyre wherof ben wroth fadre modre knyyt branch hode worthyest al londe seyn wold vengeaunce vpon florent remembraunce toke worthynes knyghthode gentylnes stood cosynage themperour toke assuage durst sleyn hym fere grete despute son among hem self best lady slyest al men knewe tho old myght vnnethes go grandame vnto dede bygan rede said wold bring ynne shal hym deth wynne al owne graut thorugh strengthe veray couenaut withoute blame ony wyght anone sent knyght sone aleyde deth thus hym seyde florent hou thou wyte branchus deth men shal respyte take engement thou stonde iugement vpon certeyne condycyon thou vnto questyon whiche shal axe shalt ansuere ouer thou shalt eke swere yf thou soth fayle ther shal none thyng auayle thou ne shalt deth receyue men shal deceyue thou therof myght aduysed thou shalt haue day tyme assysed loue saufly wende thy dayes ende thou come ageyne thyn auyse knyyt worthy wise lady prayeth may wyte haue vnder seales wryte question shold whiche shal degre stonde lyf ieopardye feyneth companye sayth florent loue longeth al myn axyng longeth al woman moost desyre wol axe thempyre thou hast knoulechyng take counceylle axyng florent thyng hath vndertake tyme set day take vnder seal wrote oth suche wyse forth goth home emes court ageyne whome auenture pleyne told hym byfalle vpon alle wysest lond assent netheles one assent myght acorde plat one sayde another disposicion natural complexyon somme woman plesauce another greuaunce suche thyng specyal whiche hem al general plesaunt moost desyred aboue al moost conspyred suche one fynde constellacyon ne kynde thus florent withoute cure must stonde vpon auenture al shape vnto lyere defaulte ansuere knyght hath leuer dye breke trouthe lye place swore shapith hym gone ayene therfore whan tyme come toke leue lenger wold byleue prayth eme wroth poynt oth sayth noman shal hym wreke though afterward men speke parauenture dye thus went forth weye alone knyght auenturous ryght curyous wyte best rode alone cam nyghe ther wold forest ther vnder tre sawe sate creature lothly womannyssh fygure speke flessh bone foule yet sawe neuer none knyght byheld hyr redely wold haue passed cleped hym bad hym abyde hors hede syde tho torned hyr rode houed abode wyte wold mene bygan hym mene sayd florent thy name thou hast honde suche game yf thou better auysed thy deth shapen deuysed al world ne may saue yf thou counceyl haue florent whan tale herd vnto old wyght ansuerd counseyl prayd ayene hym thus sayd florent yf shape thou thorugh thy deth escape take worship thy dede shal haue mede thyng qd yt thou wold axe byd neuer better taxe quod fyrst thou sped thou shalt leue suche wed wol haue thy trouth honde thou shalt myn husbonde nay sayd florent may ryde forth thy wey quod yf thou go forth withoute rede thou shalt sekerlyche dede florent behyght good ynough lond rent parke plough al compteth nought tho felle knyyt mochel thouyt goth forth cometh ayene best seyne thought rode fro chose mote one two take hyr wyf elles lese lyf cast auauntage grete age may lyue whyle thought put ile noman shold knowe tyl deth ouerthrowe thus yong lusty knyght vnto old lothely wyght tho sayd yf none chaunce may make delyueraunce thylke speche whiche thou eyst thou shalt teche haue myn hod shal ye wedde thus trouth leid wedde yt frouceth vp yt browe couenaunt wol alowe sayth yf ony thyng thou hast techyng fro deth thy body may respyte wol thy trouthe acquyte elles none weye herken shal seye whan thou art come place maken grete manace vpon thy comyng abyde wol anone tyde oppose thyne ansuere wote thou wolt thyng forbere thou wenest thy best yf thou myght fynde rest wel ther elles shal lore thou shalt say vpon molde al woman leuest wolde souerayne mannes loue woman aboue sayth sayth al wylle elles may nought fulfylle thyng leuest haue ansuer thou shalt saue thy self otherwyse nought whan thou hast thy ende wrouyt come ayene thou shalt fynde lete nothyng oute thy mynde goth hym forth heuy chere e manere may worldes ioye atteyne yf dye hath peyne yf lyue mote hym bynde suche wytche old kynde woman vnsemelyest thus wote best hym lyef hym loth vnto castel forth goth ful ansuere yeue dye lyue forth counseyll cam lord thynges stonden record send vp lady sone forth cam old mone presence remenaunt strengthe al couenaunt tho reherced openly florent bad par dy shal tellen auys wote pry florent sayth al euer couthe suche word cam none mouthe yefte byheste myght ony wyse deth areste thus taryeth long late tyl lady bad algate shal dome fynal yeue ansuere specyal fyrst opposed hath truly supposed hym may nothyng yelpe yf tho wordes helpe whiche woman hath hym tauyt wherof hath hope caught shal excused told oute pleyne wylle tho whan matrone herd maner knyght ansuerd sayd treson wo hast thus told pryuyte whiche al woman desyre wold thou fyre netheles suche plyght florent ausuer quyt tho bygan soro newe mote gone vntrewe whiche trouthe whiche al shame drad goth forth stede penaunce taketh fortune chauce trouth affayted olde wyght hym hath awayted place lefte florent woful hede vp lyfte sawe sytte lothest wyghte euer man cast eye nose baa browes hyghe hyr eyen smal depe sett hyr chekes ben teres weet ryuelyn empty skyn hangyng doune vnto chyn lyppes ben shronken age ther grace vysage hyr front narwe hir locke hore loketh forth doth neck short shulders courbe myght mannes lust distourbe body grete thyng small shortly descryue hyr hath lyth withoute lak lyche vnto wolle sak profereth hyr vnto knyght bad hym behyght bath warrant hyr helde couenaunt brydel hym seseth god wote yt hym pleseth suche wordes speketh hym thynketh wel nyghe hert bre keth sorowe may fle yf wold vntrewe loke seke man hele taketh baldemony canele myrre sucre ryght suche maner lucre stant florent dyete drynketh bitter swete medleth sorowe lykyng lyueth sayth deyng thought shal cast awey vpon suche one wey old lothly oueralle nede mote nede shalle wold algate trouthe holde euery knyght therto holde hap euer hym falle though foulest alle honour womanhede hym thought shold take heede pure gentilnesse couthe hyr best adresse ragges tore set hir hors fore forth taketh weye softe wonder though sygheth ofte oule fleeth nyght al byrdes syght ryght knyght dayes brode close hym helde shope rode nyghtes tyme tyll tyde come ther wold abyde pryuely withoute noyse bryngeth foule grete coyse castel suche wyse noman myght shap auyse tyl chambre came preuy counseylle name suche men trust told hem nedes must beste wedde vnto wyf elles lost lyf pryue woman assent shold assent ragges anone drawe tyme lawe bath rest arrayed best craft combes brode myght esse locke shode ne wold shore counseyl therfore suche tyre tho vsed ordeynen excused crafte lyche aboute noman myght seen hem oute whan fully arrayed tyre al assayed tho fouler vnto se yet may none wedded nyght wo begone neuer knyght maryage bygan playe rage sayth wel ynough therof nothyng ne lough toke chere honde clepeth hym husbonde sayd lord go bed entent wedde thou shalt worldes blisse profereth hym kysse lusty lady body myght wel thought memorye hert purgatorye strengthe matrimonye myght make none essonye mote algate plye gone bed companye whan abed naked withoute slepe awaked torneth syde wold eyen hyde lokyng foule wyght chamber ful lyght curteyne sendal thynne newe bryd whiche lay withynne though nought acord armes beclypt hyr lord prayd torned hir fro wold hym torne ayeneward tho sayd one lay stylle ony stone euer one spak praide bad hym thynke sayde whan toke hyr honde herd vnderstode bonde set penauce man traunce torneth hym al sodenly sawe lady lay hym eyghtene wynter age whiche fayrest vysage euer al world syghe wold haue take hyr nyghe put hande loue besought hym wold loue sayth wynne lese mote one two thynges chese wol haue suche nyght elles vpon dayes lyght ye shal haue bothe two bygan sorowe tho many wyse cast thought al yet coude nought deuyse hym self whiche best wold hert rest prayth shold chese algate tyl last long late sayd ye lynes hele saye ye lyst quarele ansuer shal yiue euer lyue wol ye maystresse self gesse whiche best vnto choys thus graunte yow myn hole voys chese v bothe yow praye euer ye saye ryght ye wol wol lord sayd graunte mercy word yt ye sayn ye haue made souerayn destyne ouerpassed neuer shal lassed beaute whiche haue tyl take graue nyght day shal alwey suche yow kynges doughter cecyle felle syth whyle fader late stepmoder hate whiche ward hath bygonne forshope tylle wonne loue soueraynte knyght degre al passeth good name men seyn ye dede proueth thus youre euermo tho plesaunce ioye inough echone playd lough lyue long wel ferde clerkes chaunce herde wryten euydence teche obedyence may wel fortune man loue set hym lust aboue byfelle vnto knyght thy sone yf yu ryght thou shalt vnto thy loue obeye folowe hyr wylle weye amans myn holy fader wylle ye haue told suche skylle ensample fore shal euermo therfore myn obseruaunce loue obeysaunce better kepe ouer pryde yf ther ought elles wherof shryue shal thyng specyal fadre axeth pray confessor lest sone shal saye yet surquedrye whiche stant pryde companye wherof thou shalt anone knowe yf thou haue gylt none vpon forme thou shalt vnderstonde wel matere omnia scire putat sed se presumpci nescit nec sibi consimile quem putat esse parem qui magi astutus reputat se vincere bellum laqueos veneris forcius ipse cadit sepe cupido virum sibi qui presumit amatem fal lit vacuas spes redit ipsa vias h ic loquitur de tercia specie super bie que presumpcio dicitur cuius naturam primo secundum vicium confessor simpliciter declarat vrquedrye thylk vyce pryde ye third office hath court knowe trouthe til outhrowe vpon fortune grace cometh wyst ful ofte place doth al thyng gesse voydeth al sykernesse none couseyll good hym semeth suche hym self demeth suche wyse compasseth wytte al passeth pryde thurgh sought al thre set nought weneth hym seluen suche ther nomo thus wold bere pryce fayre semely wyse abouen al nought thy sayth one graunt mercy god whiche al grace sendeth wyttes dispendeth vpon hym self though god whiche myght auayle al vpon owne wytte stant tyl falle pytte ferre may aryse h ic tractat confessor cum amante super illa saltem presumpcione ex cuius superbia plures fatui amantes cum maioris certitudinis amore spe sibi promittunt inexpediti cicius destituuntur nd ryght thus wise vyce vpon cause loue proudely set hert aboue doth hym pleynly wene louen ony quene hath worthynes suffysaunce withoute purueannce ful ofte heueth vp hyghe chyppes fallen eye eke fulofte weneth nought byloued loued al ther best sone telleth lest haue told amans ha fader nought trowe ther noman lesse ony maner worthynesse halt hym lasse worthy byloued thy saye excusyng al men loue fre certes may noman werne loue hym self derne luteth mannes herte shal asterte wene worthy louen mercy syre ye wold mene shold otherwyse wene byloued beknowe ca confessor good sone telle amans lest wol telle good fadre ful ofte hath byfalle thorugh hope certeyne wenyng hath set veyne truste thyng helpe nouyt onlyche myn owne thought semeth belle lyke wordes men telle ansueryth ryght nomore ne lesse yow fadre confesse suche wyl wytte hath euer set hope behet ful many tyme wene sothe fynally spede dothe thus may telle wenyng begyleth many man hath ryght wel wote yf man wol bote whiche withoute botome ro must nedes onerthrowe ryght wenyng hath ferde whan wende next haue wenyng cast forthest last foole bowe vnbende whan al fayled wende thy fadre wenyng hath gone amys touchend snrquedrye yeue penaunce dye yf ye wold ony forme mater tale enforme whiche ayene vyce set shold fare wel bet hic ponit confessor exemplum co tra illos qui suis viribus presume te debiliores efficiuntur et narrat qualiter ille capane mile armis probatissimus de sua presumens audacia inuocacionem ad superos tempore necessitatis ex vecordia tamen et non liter primitus prouenisse asseruit vnde obsidione ciuitatis thebarum cu ipse quodam die coram suis hostibus ad debellan dum se obtulit ignis de celo subito superueniens ipsum armatum totaliter cineres conbussit sone al maner wyse surquedrye despyse wherof fynde write thus proud knyght capane suche surquedrye thorugh chyualrye vpon hym self mochel truste goddes hym ne lust quarelle beseche sayd ydel speche whiche cause pure drede lak herte nede vpon suche presumpcion held proud oppynyon tyl lastvpon day aboute thebe lay whan syege beleyne knyght cromy que seyne al mannes syght whan proudest gere nothyng myght hym dere ful armed sheld spere cyte wold assaylle god toke hym self bataylle ayene pryde fro sky fyry thonder sodenly sende poudre hym smote thus pryde whiche hote whan strengthe wende brent lost withouten ende proueth wel therfore strengthe man sone lore yf wel gouerne ouer man may lerne eke ful oftyme greueth man hym self beleueth though shold hym wel beseme al men deme hath foryete owne vyce tale hem nyce feynen hem self wyse shal telle suche wyse wherof thou shalt ensample take thou suche thyng vndertake hic loquitur confessor contra illos qui de sua sciecia presumentes aliorum condicioues udicantes indi screte redarguut et narrat exemplu de quodam principe regis hungarie germano qui cum featrem suum pau peribus publico vidit humiliatum ipsum redarguendo contrarium edocere presumebat sed rex omni sciencia prepollens ipsum sic incaute presumentem ad humilitatis memoriam ter ribili prouidencia micius castigauit fynde vpon surquedrye yt whilom hugarye old dayes kyng wyse honest al thyng byfel vpon daye moneth maye thylk tyme vsance kyng noble purueannce hath hym self chaar arrayed wheryn wold ryde amayed oute cyte playe lordes grete arraye lusty folk yonge somme pleyd somme songe somme gone som ryde somme pryke hors syde brydlen hem oute kyng eye cast aboute tyll atte last ware sawe comend ageyne chare two pylgryms grete age lyche vnto drye ymage pale fade hewed busshe whiche besnewed berdes hoore whyte ther kynde lyte ne semen fully dede come kyng bede somme good pur charyte grete humylyte oute chare grounde lepe hem bothe armes kepe kyst hem bothe foote honde byfore lordes lond yaf hem good therto whan hath dede goth chare ageyne tho murmour tho dysdeyne tho compleynt euery syde sayden owne pryde echone oure kyng hath thynge amys abesse royalte euery man myght se humbled hym suche wyse hem none empryse thus spoken fro hem hym tho al pryuely behynde bak hym self noman spak kynges broder presence thylk tyme grete offence toke therof abouen al blame vpon lyege lord hath leyd hath vnto lordes seyd anone tyme fynde shal nothyng left behynde wol speke vnto kyng felle vpon thyng mery fayr ynongh echone playd lough fellen tale newe fresshe floures grewe grene leues spronge loue among yonge bygan hertes wake euery byrd hath chose make thus may day thende lad home aye ne wende kyng sone come whan chambre nome broder ne redy brought tale vnto ere suche shame hyndeyng owne name hym self wold dretche vyle pouer wretche hym deyneth shewe suche symplesse ageynst state noblesse sayth shal vse mote hym self excuse toward lordes euerychone kyng stode stylle onystone tale ere leyde thought seyde netheles herde wel curtoysly ansuerde told shold amended thus yt tale ended al redy bord cloth kyng vnto souper goth among lordes halle souped alle leue forth go kyng bythought hym seluen tho hou broder may chastye thought surquedrye took vpon hond dispreyse humylyte whiche preyse therupon yaf suche counseylle toward kyng vnheyle wherof better lered hym thynketh make hym afered felle thylke dawe ther ordeyned lawe trompe sterne breth whiche cleped trompe deth court ye kyng certeyne man trompe bra hath kepyng therof serueth whan lord deth deserueth shall dredefull trompe blowe fore gate make knowe jugement yeue deth whiche shal foryeue kyng nyght anone man assent bad hym gone trompen broders gate whiche mote done algate goth forth doth kynges heste lord whiche herd tempeste fore gate blewe tho wyst lawe knewe sekerlyche dede helpe wyst rede sende frendes alle told hem byfalle hym axe cause soth thy ne wyst ther sow tho stode thylk tyme trompe suche sentence ther ayene resystence coude ordeyne weye ne mote algate deye yf may purchace gete lyege lordes grace wyttes therupon cast len appoynted last lord worthy lady vnto wyf whiche also drad lordes deth childre fyue bytwene hem two lyne yong tendre age stature vysage ryght fayr lusty see tho casten forth childre morowe full sorowe al naked smok shyrte tendre kynges herte grace shold go seche pardon deth biseche thus passen wofull nyght erly lyght gone hem forth suche wyse thou fore hast herd deuyse naked hyr shyrtes one wepte made mochel mone hyr hanged aboute hyr eres sobbyng sory terys lord goth humble pa whylome proud noble wherof cyte sore flyght hem sawen ylke syght netheles al openly suche wepyng suche cry forth child wyf goth pray lyf vnto court whan thry come men therin hath hyed nome wyght yf hem syghe water myght kepe eye sow maden tho kyng supposyth wo feyneth nought ne wyst netheles vpryst men told hym ferde whan wonder herde hast goth halle al attones doune falle ony pyte may founde kyng seth hem fell groude hath axed hem fere ye dispoylled broder sayd lord mercy wote none cause nyght ful late trompe deth gate tokene shold dye thus come preye ye worldes deth respyte ha foole thou thou art wyte kyng vnto broder seyde thou art lytel freyd trompes soune hath gone dispoilled thorugh ye toune thou thy wyf suche manere forth thy child ben syght men aboute thou sayst thou art doute deth whiche stant vnder lawe man man may withdrawe may per chaunce faylle shalt thou thy meruaylle doune chare alyght behelde fore syght hem grete age myn owne deth thorugh ymage god hath set lawe kynde wherof may bote fynde well wote suche ryght suche degre flesshe blood shal deye thus though lawe obeye whiche kynges put vnder ought wel lesse wonder thou whiche art withoute nede lawe lond suche drede whiche accompt iape thyng thou myyt ouerscape thy broder rede sethyn thou canst drede man sore drede god al thyne hert al shal dye al shal passe wel lyon asse wel begger lord toward deth one acord shal stonde wyse kyng wordes wyse broder taught al foryeue confessor thy
