sone yf thou lyue vertu thou must vyce eschewe lowe hert hublesse sewe thou surquedous amans fadre amerous wherof wold beseche ye ensample teche whiche myyt loues cause stonde confessor sene thou shalt vnderstonde loue thynges alle surquedrye falle may hym wel tyde whiche vseth thylk vyce pryde whiche torneth wysedome wenyng sothfastnesse lesyng though foule ymagynacyon thyn enformacyon thou thre vyce rede esche shalt tale rede whiche felle whilome dayes olde clerk ouyde tolde hic specyaali tractat confessor amante contra illos qui de propri formositate presumete amorem mu hen dedignantur et narrat exemplum qualiter cuiusdam principis fili nomine narcizus estiuo tempore cum ipse venacionis causa quendam ceruu selue cu suis canibus exagitaret gra uem sitim incurrens necessitate copulsus ad bibendum de quodam fonte pro mi inc nauit vbi ipse faciem suam pulchirrimam aqua percipies putabat se per hoc illam nimpham quam poete ekko woont flumine coram suis oculis conspeyisse de cuius amore confestim laqucatus vt ipse ad se de fente extra haberet pluri blandicijs ad sabatur sed cum illud nullatenus perfi ere poit pre nimio languore deficiens cotra lapides ibidem adiacentre caput exuerferans cerebru effudit whilom lord sone pride vice wo ne hath caught yt worthy lyche sechen al ye worldes riche woman loue ghe set hym self aboue stature beaute bothe hym thought al woman lothe comparyson toward condycyon yong lord marcizus hyght strengthe loue myght hert whiche vnafyled last begyled goddes purueaunce felle hym day per chaunce al proud fare vnto forest gan fare among ther hunte disporte hym whan cam place wold make chace houdes within throwe vncoupled horne blowe grete hert anone founde swyfte foot set grounde spore hors syde hym hasteth fast ryde tyl al men left behynde wod vnder lynde besyde roche telle sawe sprong lusty welle day wonder hote alle thurst hym falle must dye drynke doune lyeth brynke tyde hors vnto braunche leyd hym lowe staunche thurst cast look welle heed took sawe lyke vysage wende ymage suche nymphe tho say wherof loue hert assay bygan sene stoye made hym wene woman syghe welle cam nyghe ner cam hym ageyne wyst neuer seyne whan wepte sawe hyr wepe cryed toke good kepe word cryed also thus bygan newe wo whilome hym strauge tho made hym loue herte eschaunge set herte begynne thyng myght neuer wynne euer among gan loute praith hym come oute goth ferre whyle draweth nerre euer fond place wepeth cryeth axeth grace myght gete none ayene roche stone knewe none rede smote hym self tyl deede wherof nymphes welles ther elles vnto wodes bylongend body whiche dede lyggend pure pyte haue vnder graue graue oute sepulture sprong anone parauenture floures suche wonder syght men ensample take myght vpon dedes whiche dede tho sene stede wynter fressh fayre floures ben whiche contrayre kynde folye whiche felle surquedrye thus whiche loue disdeyn werst al byseyn set pryce hyghe lest worthy loues eye beiaped wyt wherof remembraunce yet thou myght ensample take eke al sake amans fadre touchend vyce thynke flee whiche wenynge euer tro weth namlich thing groweth loues cause wel wo yet pryded neuer wold grace sende toward lady wende towardes hyr wene loue shold bysene ther shold go pryde place fer fro thylk grace speke tyme mote suffre praye yow ye wo axe syde ther ony poynt pryde wherof nedeth shryue confessor sone god foryeue yf thou haue thyng mysdoo touchend euermo ther another yet pryde whiche coude neuer wordes hyde ne wold hym self auaunt may nothynge tonge daut ne clappeth belle wherof yf thou wolt telle behouely thou myght thy tonge stere toward world stande grace whiche lakketh ofte many place hym sytte stylle whiche elles shold haue wylle magnilo que propria minuit iactancia lingue fama quam stabilem firmat honore alens ipse sui laudem meriti non percipit vnde se sua per verba iactat orbe palam est que viri culpa iactancia que rubifactas muliere reas cansat habere genas hic loqitur de quarta specie super bie que iactancia dicitur ex cui natura causatur vt homo de se ipso testi monium perhilens suarum vtrtutum merita de laude culpam transferre et suam famam cum extollere vellet illu proprio ore subuertit sed venus amoris causa de isto vicio maculatos sua curia super omnes alios abhotrens expellit vt eorum multiloquiu verecundia detestatur vnde confesso amanti opponens materiam pleuius declarat vyce cleped auauntauce pryde hath take acque intauce owne pryce la seth suche mesure ouerpasseth owne herauld fyrst wel amys thak worthy blame thus worship name thorugh pryde auauntrye wineth vylonye vede pronde vyce hath thylk wynde offyce thorugh ye blastys yt b weth man name ouerthro weth vertu whiche shold elles sprynge vnto worldes knoulechynge fordeth al sore ryght suche manere lore ther ben louers thy yf thou art one hem trlle say hou whan thou hast take ony thyng loues ryght ouche ryng take vpon colde goodly worde w tolde frendly chere tokene letter wherof thyn hert better sent gretyng hast thou pryde thy lykyng made thyn auannt lyst wold fadre ye wyst conseyence lyeth yet neuer suche matere wherof myght myn hert amende moche sende mouthe said grete hym wele thus ther delo wherof make myn auaunt reson accordaunt may neuer lye loue make auauntrye wote shold haue encheson ye haue sayd many one fonde cause neuer none dauger whiche welny slough therof couthe telle ynough none auantaunce thus nedeth repentaunce axe fadre forther lyf thewf gyltyf confessor sone wel payd al wyto wel specyal loue vevay iustyce louen al ayene vyce al tymes debateth al hert hateth eke al maner wyse auauntrye despyse ensample thou myght wyte whiche fynde bokes wryte hic ponit confessor exemplum contra illos qui de sua armis probitate vel de suo amous causa de siderio completo se iactant et narrat qualiter albinus primus rex longo bardorum cum ipse quendam alium rege nomine gurmundu bello morientem triumphasset testam capitio de functi au ferens aphum ex ea gemmis ouw circumligatum sue victorie memoriam fabricari constituit insuper ipsius gurmundi filiam rosemu dam vapiens maritali thoro coninge sibi copilauit vnde ipso albino postea coram regni sui nobilibus suo regasli con sedente dicti gurmudi aphu infuso bino ad se inter epulas ferri iussit quem sumptum vxori sue regiue porrexit dicens bibe cum patre tuo qd ipsa huiusmodi operis ig nara feat quo facto rex statim su que per prius gesta fucrant cunctis au dientibus per singula se iactauit regina vero cum talia audisset animo celato factum abhorrens mordem dni sui regis circumspecta induseria conspiraint ipsum que auxiliantibus glodesida helmege brew subsecuto tempore inter fecit cuius mortem dux rauenensis tam corpus regine quam suorum fautorum pestea vindicauit hem lubardes calle albinus first alle bare croun lubardie grete chyualrye werre ageynst dyuers kynges fell among thynges tyme werre gurmud geptees lad myghty kyng also netheles felle hym albinus slough hym felde halpe hym notherspere ne shelde ne smote heed wherof toke awey panne whiche sayd wold make cuppe gurmundes sake kepe drawe memorye bataylle vyctorye thus feld wone lond anone ouer ronne sesed owne honde gurmundes doughter foude whiche mayde rosamund hyght euery man syght fayre fressh lusty one hert fylle hyr anone suche loue hyr cast hyr wedded last tyme long reste hyr dwelte beste loue eche wondre wel kepeth ye blynde wheel venue al hottest loue hyr whele torneth felle maner shal telle king stode al welth pee worship helth felt hym syde greued hath world acheued tho thought fest wold make wyues sake lordes feste obeysaunt heste may knowe therupon lete ordeyne sent anon lettres messagyers warned al offycers euery thyng wel arayed grete stedes assayed iustyng tornement many perled garnement embrouded ageyne day lordes best aray comen tyme set one iusteth wel another bet whyle torney thus cast care awey toke lustes vpon honde thou shalt vnderstonde mete kynges halle comen beden alle set serued deserued hem worthy knyghees seten pryce spoke youe oute among herawdes al aboute thus bynethe eke aboue al armes loue wherof aboute boordes men many sondry wordes myrthe whiche made kyng hym self bygan glade within hert took pryde sawe cuppe stonde syde whiche made gurmudes hede ye haue herd dede gold ryche stone beset bounde none stood vpon foote hyghte borned gold grete sleyghte werkemanshyp bygraue suche werke shold haue polysshed eke clene sygne sculle sene grypes eye kyng bad bere cuppe aweye whiche stood byfore hym boord fette thylk vpon word sculle fet wyn therin wherof bad wyf hegynne drynke thy fadre dame seyde byddyng obeyde toke sculle lyst drynketh nothyng wyst cuppe al oute kyng audyence aboute hath told hyr fadres sculle lordes knowe shulle vataylle soth wytnesse made auaut thorugh prowesse hath wyues loue wonne whiche sculle hath bygonne tho pryde mochel alofte speken softe thynkend thylk vnkynde pryde hyr lord nygh syde auaunath hym slayn pyked oute hyr fadres brayn sculle hath made cuppe suffered tyll vppe tho hath sekenesse feyned goth chabre hath copleyned vnto mayde whiche trust none wyght wyst mayde glodesyde hote whome lady hath byhote sadyshyp al auenge hyr vpon man dyd hyr drynke suche pliyt among hem al despyte hyr hyr fadre bothe wherof thoughtes ben wrothe sayd shal glad hym hath bestad hat nomore make auaunt thus felle couenaunt hat acorden last suche wyles cast wol gete hyr acord som orped knyght slee lord sleyghte begynne helmege myght wynne whiche kynges botyler proud lusty bachiler glodesyde loueth hote make hym assote loue graunted nyght shape gedre myght bedde mete done nyght quene hyr self nyght seconde went stede fonde chambre derke withoute lyght goth bedde knyght kepe obseruaunce loue doth obeysaunce weneth glodesyde lay syde hym axeth hath told hym tho sayd thy quene shal thy loue wel beseen thou hast thy wylle wrought shal sore ben abought thou shalt worche saye yf thou wolt suche waye plesaunce hold stylle euer shal ben thy wylle bothe al myn herytage anone wyld loue rage whiche noman hym gouerne hath made hym werne felle al hool assent thus whele al myswent whiche fortune hath vpon honde euer stonde shope among hem suche wyle kyng dede within whyle slyly come aboute ne ben discouered oute thought hem best flee rest thus tresour kyng tsxy trusse moche thyng certeyne felauship fled went awey ship hel hyr cours thenne tyl come rauenne duke helpe sought hym besought place graunteth duelle whan herd telle maner haue duk lete shape hem poyson whiche drunke hadden haue beswuke al made auauut pryde good therfore man hyde owne pryce yf speke may lyghtelyche thanke breke armes lyeth none auauntage hym thynketh name auaunce renomed dede also thynketh spede loue may hym auaunte man thylk vpce haunte purpoos shal ofte faylle armes wol trauaylle elles loues grace attryne loue tonge mote restreyne whiche beryth honoure keye thy sone al weye take ryght good hede matere thanke yow fadre dere scole gentyl lore yf ther ought elles pryde whiche shal esche axe forth wol shewe thyng ye wol enforme confessor sone yet forme ther vyor prydes lore whiche lyche hawke wyl sore fleeth vpon hygh delyces lykyng vyces wol nomans reson knowe tyl doune falle ouerthro vyce veynglorye hote wherof sone byhote trete speke suche wyse thou myght better auyse gloria perpetuos pregnat munda na dolores qui tamen est vanus gaudia vana cupit eius amiciciam quem gloria tollit inanis non sine bla dichis planus habehit homo merbis compositis qui sit stagulare fauellum scandere sellata iura valebit eques sic amore magi qui blanda subor nat ore merba per hoc bra um qd nequit alter halebit et tamen ornato cantus varios que paratus let que corda suis legibus optat amor hic loquitur de quinta specie superbie que inanis gloria vocatur et eiusdem vicij naturam primo delscubens super eodem moris causa confessor amanti consequenter opponit proud vyce veinglorye remebreth purgatorye worldes ioyes grete hym thynketh heuen beyete lyues pompe al pe yet shal deye netheles therof thynketh lyte al lust delyte newe thynges proud veyne ferforth may atteyne trowe yf myght make body newe wold take newe forme leue olde thyng may beholde whiche comon vse straunge anone old guyse chaunge wol falle therupon lyche vnto camelyon whiche vpon euery sondry hewe behold mote newe colour thus vnauysed fuloftyme stant desguysed ioylyf vytd may maketh hym euer fessehe gay doth al aray desguyse hym newe guyse lusty folk al take eke carolles make roundel balade verelay al yf may ue ge e hym auauntage none waxt corage ouer glad end thynketh ther deth comend hath al tyde loue suche maner pryde hym thynketh ioye endeles confessor shryue sone good pee thy loue telle pleyn yf thy glorye hath veyn amans fadre touchend al may wel ne shal veyne glorye excuse ne haue loue better dressyd arayd also haue ofte assayd roundel balades vyrelay hy loue whome myn hert lay tho make also peynte rollys wordes queynte set purpoos alofte yus long hem forth ofte balle eke chambre aboute made mery among oute yet ne ferd bet e glo ye veyn set oye made wold hyr glade er loue songes make sayd hyr sake e songes n wyten wordes fo speke myn arraye yet coude neuer gay e wel make song loue wherof myght ben aboue haue encheson glad rather ofte adrad sorowe sayth nay netheles wol say glad syde ame nothyng hyde al day wol brynge vnto myn ere men speken lady beryth pry fayr wyse womanlyche chere al thynge may wonder thaugh feyn eke may seyn tydynges lady hele al though may hyr dele yet wonder glad wote hyr good estat tyme dar wel swere none sorowe may dere thus gladed wyse fadre youre lore wyse whicho ye fully taught telle yf ye thynke ought thewf wyte ther acquyte sone sayd thy good wol thou vnderstood thynke vpon matere telle tale thou shalt ageyne proud vyde hyghe god iustyce wrothe grete vengeaunce doth herken tale soth though nought loues kynde grete ensample thou shalt fynde veyne glorye flee whiche ful vanyte hvmani generis cum sit sibi gloria maior sepe sub esse solet poox imis ille dolor men elata graues descensus sepe subibit men humilis stabile molle que firmat iter motibus innumeris volutat fortuna per orbem cum magi alta petit inferiora time h ic ponit confessor exemplum contra vicium inanis glorie norrans qualiter rex nabugodonosor rex caldeorum cum pse omni magesta ti sue gloria celsior extitisset deus eius superbiam castigare olens ipsum extra formam hominis estiam fenu commedentis transmutauit et sic perseptennium penitens cum ipse potenaorem se agnouit misertus den ipsum sui regni um restituta sanitate emendatum graciosius collocauit ther king yt moch miyt whiche nabugdonosor hyght yt spak fore yet byble name bore al world thoryent hoole commaundement kynges lyche none myghty ne ryche empyre lawes sayth thylke dawes obeysaunt trybute bere though god erthe strengthe put kynges vnder wrought pride many woder ful vayne glorye ne memorye ony god pryde pro peryte tyl hyghe kyng kynges whiche seeth knoweth al thynges who eye may nothyng asterte pryuyt e man herte speke sowne ere though oude wyndes toke vengeaunce pryde wold abyde loke yf wold hym amende hym afore token sende slepe nyght proude kyng wonder yght sweuen lay hym thought vpon mery day byhelde world abou tre growe sawe ther whiche world amyddes euen who heyght strauyt vy heuen leues fayr large fouyt ere rype c arge al men myght fede sawe also bowes sprede aboue al erthe whiche kynde al byrdes eke thought sawe also kynde al bestes go vnder tre aboute rounde fedden hem vpon grounde wonder stond syghe thought herd wy hyghe cryend sayd aboue alle hewe doune tre lete falle leues lete defou e hast doth feuyt destroye wast lete shreden euery braunche rote bete staunche whan al pryde cast grounde rote shal fast bounde shal man hert bere euery lust shal forbere man lyche oxe te gras shal purchace ete tyl water heuen haue wasshen hym tymes seuen thorugh knowe aryght heuenlyche myght made humble wylle hym whiche maye al saue spylle kyng sweuene abrayd vpon mow sayd vnto clerkes whiche none hem soth arad none sweuen couth vndo stood thylk tyme kyng subiectyon iudee affectyon bouen al one danyel loueth couthe wel dyuyne none couthe hym al thynges couthe goddes grace byfore kynges face sente oden sholde vpon poynt kyng tolde fortune sweuene expounde shold afterward founde whan danyel sweuene herde stood long tyme ansuerde made wondre beuy chere kyng toke hede manere bad hym telle wyst whome mochel yse sayd wold wroth danyel wonder loth sayd vpon men alle syre kyng thy sweuene myght falle nethelce touchend wol tellen dysese shape god wote yf thou shalt escape hyghe tree whiche thou hast sene whiche leues f uyt wel besene whiche stood ye world amyddes beestes byrdes gouerned hym alone syr kyng bytokeneth thy persone whiche stote aboue al erthely thynges thus regnen vnder kynges al peple vnto lovoteth al world thy persone douteth veyne honour deceyued thou hast reuerence weyued fro hym thy kyng aboue thou hast yt thou drede ne loue wolt nothyng kno god yu hath made rod thy veyne glorye thy folye grete peynes chastye voys thou herdest speke whiche bad bowes breke bewe felle doune tr word ongeth vnto thy regne shal ouerthro thou dyspoylled athro rote shal stonde thou shalt wel vnderstonde ther shal abyde thy regne tyme ageyne thou shal regne eke thou herdest say take mannes hert away set bestyal lyke oxe shal pasture reyned tymes seuen sore peyned tyl kno goddes myytes shal stonde ageyne vprightes al bytokeneth thyne estate whiche god debate thy mannes forme shal lassed tyl seuen yere ouer passed lykenes beste gras shal thy royal ste wether shal vpon rayne vnderstonde al payne whiche thou shalt suffre thylk tyde shape al thy pryde veyne glorye ynne whiche thou hast long stonde ynne vpon condycyon thy sweuene hath exposicyon thyng befalle dede amende wold rede yeue departe thyn almesse mercy forth ryghtwysenes beseche pray hyghe grace thou myght thy pee purcha god stonden good acord pryde loth lose lord wol suffre humylyte hym stonde deg e whan shyp hath loste stere none wyse may hym stere ageyne wawes rage proud kyng courage humylyte hath forlore sweuene sawe fore ne yet al danyel hym hath counseylled euery del lete passe oute mynde thorugh veyne glorye blynde seeth weye hym wo felle within tyme babyloyne wente vanyte pryde hym hente hert aroos veyne glorye drough memorye lordship regalye wordes surquedrye whan hym moost auaunteth lord whiche glorye daunteth al sodenly sayth trey stood paleys took hym men syght none hem war myght set eye bycome thus kyngdome wyld st drawe myghty goddes lawe thorugh power dyd transforme fro man bestes forme lyke oxe vndre foote graseth nedes mote geten lyues fode tho thought hym cold gras goode whilome ete hot spyces thus torned delyces wyn wonte drynke took thenne welles brynke pyt slough thought hym good ynough stede chambres wel arayed busshe wel payed hard ground lay vpon pylowes non stormes raynes falle wyndes blowe vpon hym alle tormented day nyght suche hyghe goddes myght tyl seuen yere ende toke vpon hym self tho gan loke stede mete gr trey stede handes long cleys stede man beste lyke sawe gan syke cloth gold perrye whiche hym wonte magny ye byheld cote here wepte woful teres vp heuen cast chere wepend thought manere though wordes may wynne thus sayd hert spak withynne myghty god al hast wrought al myyt brynge ageyne nouyt knowe al world hath prosperyte thyn aspect ben al alyche poure man eke ryche withoute ther may wyght thou aboue al myght myghty lord ward vyce thy mercy medle iustyce wol make couenaunt lyf remenaunt shal grace amende thy lawe dispende veyn glorye shal eschewe bowe vnto thyn heste sewe humylyte vowe thenkend gan doune bowe though hym lacke boy speehe gan fete areche wenend beestly steuene made pleynt vnto heuene kneleth wyse brayeth seche mercy assayeth god whiche made hym nothyng strauge yt saw pride chage anone huble tame fond toward god twynkelyng look mannes forme ageyne took reformed reygne wont reygne pryde veyn glorye euer afterward oute memorye lete passe thus shewed ben pryde vnthe wed ageyne hyghe goddes lawe whome man may felawe thy sone take good hede lede thy manhede thou lyke beste yf thy lyf shal honeste thou must humblesse take honde myght thou syker stonde speke wyse proud man assise thouy woma wold hym please pryde ben ease ther may noman mochel blame vyce whiche blame thy men shulden nothyng hyde myght falle blame pryde whiche worst vyce alle wherof byfalle tale thynke crony que telle yf may lyke thou myght humblesse sewe eke vyce pryde eschewe wherof glorye fals veyne god hym self hath dysdeyne though mounte athrowe shall falle doune ouerthrowe est virt humilis per quam deus altus ad yma sed tulit nostre viscera carnis habet sic humibis superest et sibi subditur omnis cuius habet nulla sorte superbus opem odit eum tetra celum defecit et ipsum sedibus interm stat que receptus ibi hic narrat confessor exeplum contra superbiam et dicit nuper quidam rex famose prudencie cuidam militi suo super questionibus vt inde certitudinis responsione daret subpena capitalis seutencie terminum pre fixit primo quid minoris indigencie ab inhabitantib orbem auxilium maius obtinuit secundo quid maioris valencie meritum continens minoris expense reprisas exigut tercio qid oia bona diminuens ex sui proprietate nichil penitus valuit quarum vero que stionnm quedam virgo dicti militis filia nomine patris solucionem aggredi en taliter regi respondit ad prima dixit quod terra nullius indiget qua tn adiuuare cotidianis laborib omnes intendunt ad secundam dixit humi litas omnibus virtutibus preualet q tamen nullius prodegalitatis expensis mesuram excedit ad terciam dixit subia omnia tam corporis qm anime bona deuastans maiorum expensarum excessus inducit aking whilom yog wise wit set grete pryce depe ymagynacyos straunge interpretacions problemes demaudes eke wysedom fynde seke wherof wold sondry wyse opposen hem wyse none hem myght vere vpon word yeue ansuere taken one whiche knyght hym euery thyng lyght also sone hem herde kynges wordes ansuerde thyng kynge axe wolde ther anone trouthe tolde kyng somdele enuye thouyt wold wyttes plye set som conclusyon whiche shold confusyon vnto knyght name wysedome hyghe fame ward hym self wold wynne thus al wyt wynne kyng bygan study muse straunge mater myght vse knyghtes wyttes confounde last hath founde knyght anone sent shal telle ment vpon poyntes mater question thou shalt fyrst poynt al thre thyng al degre al world hath nede lest yet men helpe alther mest second worth costage lest put forth thyrd whiche coste lest worth goth loste kyng thre demaudes axeth knyght lawe taxeth shal gone come ageyne thyrd weke telle hym pleyne euery poynt amounteth yf myscounteth make ansuere faylle ther shal none thyng faylle kyng sayth shal dede lese goodes hede knyght sory thynge wold excuse hym kyng ne wold hym forbere thus knyght ansuere goth home take auyfement entendement cast wytte aboute therof stant doute tho wyst wel kynges hert deth ne shold astert suche sow hym take gladship hath forsake thought fyrst vpon lyf vpon wyf vpon childee eke also whiche doughters two yongest hem age fourtene yere vysage ryght fayre stature lyche heuenlyche fygure maner goodly speche though men wold al londes seche shold haue founden lyke sawe hir fadre sorowe syke wyst cause cam hym pryuely yt made mone within gardyn al hym one vpon hyr knee gan doune falle humble hert hym calle sayd good fadre dere make ye thus heuy chere wote nothyng wel ye knowe fadre auenture yow felle ye myght saufly telle haue ofte herd sayd ye suche trust haue layd suster ne brother al world ne none ye durst haue told pryuete wel fadre thy fadre praye ne casteth nought hert awaye wold kepe honour wepe hyr eye may forbore wyssheth ben vnbore er fadre mystryst tellen hyr wyst euer among mercy cryede ne shold counseylle hyde hyr wold hym good nyghe flesshe blood wepyng laste chere vpon child caste sorowfully prayde told tale thus sayde sorowe doughter whiche make al sake alle suche chaunce befalle shal thyrd day lese al euer lese may lyf al good therto therfore sorowe cause ala quod fadre ye sholden deed destroyed suche wyse bygan poyntes deuyse whiche ye kyng told hym mouth sayd hyr pleynly couth ansuere poynt hereth hyr counseyl yafe sayd tho fadre syn ye none weye ye must nedes deye wold pray thyng late go yow kyng ye shal make hym vnderstonde hou ye wyttes fonde haue leyd ansuere vpon telle hym suche degre vpon word ye wol abyde tho lyue deye betyde yet per chaunce maye purchace som good word ye kynges grace lyf eke good saue ofte shal woman haue thyng yt man may areche fadre herd doughters speche thought ther reson ynne sawe owne lyf wynne reuthe done hym self cure better hym thought auenture put hym al good maner stood lyf certeyne lese thus thynkend bygan chese counseyll mayde eke purpoos whiche saide day come forth gone vnto court come anone kyng iugement set hath knyght asent arrayed best wyse mayden wordes wyse hyr fadre led honde place fonde kyng whiche wolde kyng knelend tolde enformed fore prayth kyng therfore daughter wordes wol take sayth wol vndertake vpon wordes stonde tho ther grete meritayl honde whiche soo wyse knyyt lyf vpon yong wyght set wold ieopardye many helde folye last neuertheles kyng commaunded pee mayde cast chere seyd wold hyr tale bad hyr speke bygan lyege lord quod poyntes whiche herde shal reson ansuerde first vnderstond thyng al world whiche men moost helpe lest nede lyege lord wold rede erthe whiche euermo mannys labour vego wel wynter maye mannes honde maye helpe forth make ryche thy men delue dyche eren strengthe plough hath hym self ynough nede lest euery man byrd best flour gras rote rynde euery thyng wey af kynde shal sterue erthe shal bycome oute erthe nome shal erthe torne ageyne thus may reson seyne therthe nedeles men helpe netheles lord touchand haue ansuerd poynt vnderstood whiche worth good costeth man lest kepe lord yf ye wol take kepe say humylyte thorugh whiche hyghe trynyte deserte trewe loue vnto mary aboue knewe humble entent owne sone doune sent aboue al hyr chese vertu whiche bedeth pee maye reson calle humylyte worthyest alle lest costeth mayntene al word sene hath humblesse vn hende bryngeth wer e londe desyreth best set euery man rest thus youre hyghe reuerence thynketh euydence poynt suffysaunt touchend remenaunt whiche thyrd askynges lest worth al thynges osteth telle pryde whiche may heuene abyde luafer hym felle bar pryde hym helle ther pryde grete cost whan pryde hath heuen lost paradyse adam pryde lost pryce myddel erthe eke also pryde cause al al world may suffyse stant pryde repryse pryde heed al synne whiche wasteth may wynne pryde euery mys pryk pryde worst al wyck costeth lest worth place hath forth thus haue sayd wol sey myn ansuere yow prey myn lyege lord offyce ye shal grace suche iustyce ordeyne fadre men world therof may say good kyng whiche reson vnderstood hath al herd whiche hath said inly glad wel payd al wrath ouer go bygan loke tho vpon mayde face whiche founde mochel grace al pryce eyde audyence thus seyde fayre mayde wel ye thyne ansuere eke lyketh thou wylt foryeue thy fadre gylt yf thou suche lygnage thou parage thy fadre pere bachylere thou sholdest wyf syker haue lyf say netheles wol shape thyn encrees worldes good thou wolt baue axe yeft yu shalt haue kynges wordes wyse knelyng thanked wyse lyege lord god mote yow quyte fader hath lyte waryson wende al lost amende ye may wel thorugh noble grace yt kyng ryght place none forth fressh hete erldom whiche eschete late falle honde vnto knyght rente londe hath youe chartre sesed thus al noyse appesed maide sate vpon hir knee byfore kynges charytees comen deth sayth euermore lyege lord ryght fore ye sayde record yf fadre lord pere vnto grete ye wolden elles lete ne shold wyf thus wote enery worthy lyf kynges word mote holden thy lord yf ye wolden grete charyte fulfylle god wote wel wylle whiche bachilere fadre made pere euer cam erles doughter yong kyng whiche plesyd alle hyr beaute hyr wyt alle wae loue hente none therto yaf assente myght mayde asterte ny lady herte took hyr wyfe holde whyle hath lyfe thus ye kyng toward knyyt acordeth hym ryght ouer good wyte cronyes wryte noble kyng whome tolde spayne tho dayes olde kyngdome gouernaunce aud book maketh remembrauce alphons propre name knyght also yf shal name dom petro hyght men telle doughter wyse petronelle cleped whiche ful grace sene thylk place hyr fadre oute tene hath breuyt made hyr self quene hath wel disclosed poyntes wherof opposed confessor lo sone thou myght al thyng matere one take pryde whome grace may betyde heuene felle oute stede paradys hym forbede good men erthe hym hate helle mote algate euery vertu shal weyued aud euery vyce receyued humblesse al wyse whiche moost worthy noo repryse taketh ageyne softe fayre ony thyng stant contrayre humble speche redressed thus yong mayd blessyd whiche spak fore fadre lyfe gat therfore wanne al kynges loue thy sone yf thou wolt loue sytt wel loue pryde take humblesse thy syde grace thou shalt gete amans fadre wol foryete yt ye haue told yf ony suche manere humble port may loue appaye afterward thenke assaye ouer beseche ye shryfte seche confessor good sone shal herkne lay ere tonchand pryde fayre al ferforth declare cause vyce cause loue thou hast pleyne herd aboue nomore seye touchend weye touchend enuye thynk telle whiche hath propre kynde helle withoute cause mysdo toward hym self mo afterward vnderstonde thou shalt spyces stonde explicit liber primus liter secundus pryde second ther many wo ful stoud wardes beryth boute within hym self withoute thought brenneth euer whan wote another leuer vertuous whiche passeth hym degre wherof taketh maladye vyce cleped hoote enuye thy sone yf ye art hast ben one tho speke loues ca yf euer yet thyn herte seke mennes hele god auannce quarele fadre ye thousand sythe whan haue sene another blythe loue goodly chere ethna whiche brenneth yere byyere hoote thylk whiche pryuely myn hertes thought within brenneth ship whiche wawe renneth forstormed blowe payned athrowe whan se another whiche passeth fortune loues yefte fadre telle shryfte place seche fynde grace stede may nought greue ye may ryght wel byleue toward lady serue though wyst sterue myn hert ful suche folye self may chastye whan court see cupyde approche vnto lady syde hem lusty ben fresshe though auayle hem resshe ben speche sorowe seche whan rownen ere groweth al fere namely whan talen long sorowes strong se hem wel ease telle dysease syre lady selue though haue wowers x twelue mystrust haue hire greueth nonght certes syre trowe al world seche ny woman dede speche wol better auyse hyr doth ne better sey soth kepe hyr honour al tyde yet gete hyr thank besyde netheles knowe whan see ony throwe elles yf may make ony man good chere though therof haue done thought wol entermete sone though self straunge enuye maketh myn hert chaunge sorowfully stad se another glad hyr alle loue may byfalle fayle spede therof take lytel hede haue sayd fader alle poynt specyal ferforthly haue wyst axe fadre yow lyst confessor sone axe ony thynke somdele thy lore telle example mater touchend enuye thou shalt though houndes kynde wryte cyuyle fynde ete chaf yet wol werne oxe whiche cometh herne therof take ony fode thus vnderstode stant loue many place oute loues grace wold another shold faylle may hym self auaylle yf may put ony lettr deth al may lette wherof fynde thou shalt wyte purpoos tale wryte hic ponit confessor exemplum contra istos saltem qui amoris causa aliorum gaudijs inuidentes ne ua quam per hoc sibi ipsis proficiunt et narrat qualiter mundus mile noie acis quem galathea numpha pulcherrima toto corde peramauit cum ipsi sub quadam rupe iuxta litus mari colloquium ad inuicem habuerunt polophemus gigas concussa rupe mag nam inde partem super caput acis ab alto percipiens ipsum per inuidiam terfecit et cum ipse super hoc dictam galatheam rapere voluisset neptun gigantem obsistens ipsam inuolutum salua custodia preseruauit sed et dij miserti corpus acis defuncti fonte aque dulcissime subito transmutarant ther ben suche mo xij able hem selue gete loue enuye vpon al aspye hem lacketh wolde kepe none sholde touchend loue cause spede wherof grete ensample rede whiche vnto mater acordeth ouyde book recordeth polyphemus whilome wrouyt galathe bysought loue whiche may latche made hym waite watche al weyes ferde tyl last knewe herde another leue loue mote leue speke ony spede knewe none rede wayten vpon alle tyl may see chaunce falle hyr myght greue whiche hym self may acheue galathe seyth poete aboue al vnmete beaute men knewe lusty loue true bachyleer degre ryght suche another whome hath hyr hert set myght nought let yefte ne byhest ne al hest yong knyght acis hote whiche hyr ageynward also hote al loueth mo herof polyphemus wo thorugh pure enuye euer aspyede wayteth vpon euery syde geder myght se yong acis galathe long wayteth fro tyl last founde hem two pryue place stood speke haue wordes good place hem syghe vnder bank nyghe grete see aboue stood byhelde lusty loue whiche eche hem made goodly wordes glade al hert hath set fyre pure enuye fyre whiche flyeth oute myghty bowe awey fled throwe loue wood whan sawe stood polypheme geaunt sawe soth ca galathe hym hath forsaken acis loue taken hert may forbere ne roreth bere wylde beste whome reson myght areste ran ethna helle aboute neuer yet fyre oute fulfylled sorowe grete dysease sawe acis wel ease tyl last hym bythought whiche al enuye sought torneth banke ageyne galathe hath seyne acis whome thought greue though hym self may releue geaunt rude myght part bank shoof doune right whiche euen vpon acis fylle fallyng hylle polyphemus acys slough wherof made sorowe ynough fled lond neptunus toke hyr hond kepte hyr fast plac fro polypheme manace fals enuye ne myght atteyne hyr companye galathe whome speke hyr self may wreke withouten ony semblaunt feyned hath hyr loues deth compleyned hyr sorowe hyr wo hath goddis moued pyte grace haue acis place lay deed vnto welle transformed bokes telle fressh stremes clere whilome lusty chere fresshe lust queme rude polypheme enuye hate wrothe thus algate confessor sone thou myght vnderstonde yf thou wolt grace stonde loue thou must leue enuye thou wylt thy partye toward thy loue stonde fre must thou suffre another byfalle vpon thy chaunce vnwyse vengeaunce whiche none mannes lefe vnto hym self grefe amans fader ensample good euer stood polyphemus lone tho shal stonde worchen ony felonye loue none suche enuye thy yf ther ought elles axe forth degre shal confesse shryfte vnto youre holynesse orta sibi solito mentalia gaudia liuor du videt alteri dampna doloris agit inuidus obridet hodie fletus aliorum fletus cui pro pri o crastina fata paret sic amore pare stat sorte iocos ama te cu vidit illusos inuidus ille quasi sic licet iuua uum speret tn ipse leuamen alterius casu lapsus ipse simul hac quitur confessor de secunda specie die que gaudium altr u de oris diatur et pumo eiusde vicij materiam tractans amantis consciam super codem vlterius inuestigat good sone yet ther vyce reuers vnto nuye taketh glad sse seeth heuynesse men welfare wot another care another hath fall thynketh hym self aryse alle suche gladship enuye worldes thyng partye ful oftymes eke also toues cause stant ryght thou sone hast ioye thou another sawe vnglad shryue thero fadre yi vysrno wen yo w louers lotten streyte fo poynt coucite ben pursuaunt yere yere soues court may fxr clymbe vpon whele wene al shal wele ben doune throwe last fed fast laughe see hem loure thus thatthey brewe loure drynke swete wel sed wote ben dysesed whiche telle lady dere none knowe reheth ouerthrowe ne stonde loue vpryght squyer nyght whiche lady ward pursueth leseth seweth thynke wynne glad withynne wote hym sorowe endute euer vpon suche auenture comfort men seyn see another peyn may compleyne hem wo beseyne self may auayle sene another mannes trauayle ryght glad let though fare let hie sow myn hert game whan knowe whiche lady stant enclyned hath loue termyned ryght ioyeful thought suche enuye greueth nought e knowe culpable ye wyse resonable fadre telle youre aduyse confessor sone enuye pryse suche forme vnderstonde ne myght reson stonde enuye hath suche kynde wol set hym self behynde hynder another wyght gladly lese owne ryght make another lese knowe tale lyche matere thenke telle yf thou wolt shewe propyrly vyce ennye malyce hic ponit confessor exemplum co tra illum qui sponte sui ipsius de trim tum alterius penam maic ein patitur et narrat cum iupiter gelum suum forma hominis vt homi num condiaones exploraret ab exce terram misit contigit ipse angel duo homines quorum vnus cupid alter inuidus erat itinevando spacio spacio quasi vni di committabatur et cum sero factum esset angelus corum se ipsum tun manifestans di quidquid alter e rum ab ipso dona ri sibi pecierit illud statim obtinebit socio suo secum comutanti affixmat duplicadu super quo cupidus impedit auaricia sperans sibi diiucias carpere duplicatas primo petere recusauit od cum inuid animiaduerteret naturam sui vicij concernens ita vt socius suus vtro que lumine pr uaretur se ipsum mo notulum fieri constanter primus ab angelo postulabat et sic vnius inui alteriu auariciam maculauit iubitex thus find write whilo wold wite vpon pleynt herd among men yt ferd wrong condycyon iustyfycacyon cause doune sent aungel whiche aboute went soth knowe may byfelle vpon day angel hym shold enforme clothed man forme ouertook vnderstonde two men wenten ouer bonde thorugh whiche thought aspye cause goth companye aungel wordes wyse opposeth hem sondry wyse lowde wordes softe made hem desputen ofte eche hem wason thus tale hem lad good examynacyon tyl knewe condycyon men bothe two sawe also wel last tho one hem coueyt u fe lawe enuyous thus whan hath knowlechyng anone feyned departyng sayd mote algate wende herken fell ende made hem vnderstonde goddes sonde sayd kyndeship haue done hym felauship wold som grace ageyne bad one hem shold seyne thyng hym leuest craue shal yefde haue ouer eke forth al sayth haue shal double felawe axeth thus grace taxeth concytous wondre glad man seyth fyvst ax sholde supposeth wolde make axyng worldes good knewe wel stood hym self double wyght shal take thus sleyght cause wolde wynne ad felawe fyrst begynne enuyous though late sawe mot algate make axynges fyrst thought worship proufyte sought shal double fere wold chese manere sheweth toward enuye vnto angel thus seyd yef e thus preyd make hym blynde owne eye felawe thyng syghe word sone spoke owne eye loke felawe forth also blynde eyen two tho glad ynough one wepte ough set tye cost wherof two hath lost thylke ensample whiche felle tho men telle ful ofte world empeyreth comonly yet wote none cause acordeth nought kynde myn owne harme che fynde shal brother greue myght neuer wel acheue yst thou sone folye fadre yf shold ly vpon poynt whiche ye haue sayd yet myn hert neuer layd wyse haue told ouermore yf ye wold ought elles shryft saye touchand enuye wold praye die par est detractio p ssima pestem qne magi infamein fla bue agit ingua venenato sermone reper utit aures sic vt alteteris scandala f volat morsibus rge quos inficit ipsa fideles vulneris ignoti pe salute carent sed ge ne sue amor nguam coseruat vt ei erbum qd loquitur nulla sinistra ge hic tractat confessor de tercia spe iuiudie que detractio dicitur sus viperos lesa qm sepe fama de langit ton hend enuyo brood wote one al good netheles yet ther one yt whiche l ped detractyon conferme actyon hath holde male bouche whoos tonge neuer crosse ne crouche may prouounce pleyne good word withoute frouce behynde man bak though pr yse fynt som lak whiche tale ay last al pryce shal ouer cast though ther cause yet wol iangle thy yt hath yt herauldye hem vsen lye nettle whiche vp renneth fresshe rede rose brenneth maketh hym fade pale hewe ryght fals enuyous hewe euery place duelleth fals wordes whiche telleth torneth preysyng blame worship worldes shame suche lesynges compasseth good ne passeth byt wene teth bakbyted thorugh fals tong endyted lyke sharnebyrdes kynde who nature fynde hotest day comen mery may spret wynge vp fleeth vnder al aboute seeth fayre lusty floures spryng therof hath lykyng seeth ony beste filthe maketh feste therupon wold alyghte lyketh hym none syghte ryght iangler enuyous though man se vertuous ful good condycyon therof maketh mencyon elles ly e wherof may see wyte renneth open mouth behynde man maketh couth al vertu whiche wol hyde euery man openly vyce telle whiche scole helle taught fostred vp nuye houshold companye hath propre offyce set euery man vyce mouth comly word euermore syt wry seyth werst may wyse nowe day loues court man may ful ofte pleyne matere many enuyous tale stered may ansuered yet ful ofte byleued many worthy loue greued thorugh bakbytynge fals enuye thou haue made suche ianglarye loues court sone hic amoris causa huins vicij men ad memoriam reducens cofesfessor amanti super codem plenius opponit shryue therof fadre yi wyte ye openly priuely whan dere lady mete thynke mete vnto hyr hyghe worthynesse ese see hyr besynesse al yong busty route whiche al day pursueth aboute eche tyme wayteth eche tale affayteth al deceyue innocent whiche wol assent men seyn vnknow n vnkist hyr thombe helde hyr fist close n hyr owne hond may wynne noman lond leueth al hereth thus ful ofte hyr self skereth al ware wyst al myn herte aryst comon louers see wold holde hem thre welny louen oueral myn hert enuyous al euer adrad gyle aunter yf within ony whyle myght innocence enhaunte thy wordes ful ofte haunte behynden hem dare wherof lady may ware say euer cometh mouth wers wold yf couth come vnto speche al may enquere seche suche deceyte telle al ay worst specyal fayne wolde wyst lytel ben tryst wold met double encent thus toward hem wykked mene wykked word euer grene netheles soth telle certeyne yf byfelle der trewest man bore chese among thousand score whiche al fully tryst lady loued wyst yet rather shold spede wold suche tale sprede lady yf myght wol al peyne vnryght therto wold al peyne certes though shold feyne telle neuer thought al world myght nought suffre another fully wynne yet begynne good bad wold none lady maketh fnlof e aspye vsen wordes enuye make bere blame thylk fame whiche vnto lady drawe euer renne gnawe hynder hem al euer may sothly saye lady selue celle nought twelue therof wol wel auyse speke iangle ony wyse toucheth lady name ernest game wold saue lady deth leuer lakke breth speke hyr name amys haue ye herd touchend sndre confession therfor detraxyon loue haue myspoke tesse howre wylle shal wroke al redy bere peyne also lere thyng ye wol allowe hounden must bowe wol bowe vnto youre best dar make byhest yow haue nothyug hyd told ryght betyd otherwyse myspeche conseyente seche enuye fynde myspoke haue ought behynde wherof euer myspayd haue ye herd haue sayd wol ye fadre sone euer kepe thy tonge stylle thou myyt haue thy wille thou seyst thy seluen lady suche manere wyse ware al thynges nedeth bakbytynges thou thy lady mys enforine knoweth al forme thy self art enuyous thou shalt gracyous thou parauentur sholdest elles ther wol man drynk welles whiche wote poyson ynne aud ofte suche men begynne wardes suche fynde set hem ofte fer behynde wenen byfore good sone thou therfore ware leue thy wycked speche wherof hath fallen ofte wreche many man byfore tyme wol handes tyme must vncleue many mote shal sene wol elles eleue shold euery wyse man fere wol another blame sekyth ofte owne shame whiche elles myght ryght stylle thy yf thy wylle stonde vpon amendement tale grete entendemet thynke telle thy sake wherof thou myght ensample take hic loqiutur confessor contra istos amoris causa detrahentes qui suis obliquijs aliena solacia perturbat et nacrat exemplum de constancia tibe rij rome imperatoris filia omnium biztutum famosissima ob eius amozem soldanus tunc persie vt eam vxorem ducere posset cristianum se fieri misit cuius accepta caucione consilio pe lagij tunc pape dictum filia vna cum du ob cardinalib alns que procerib persia maritagij ca naiugio honozifice destinata fiut que tamen obloquenau postea detractionis varijs modis ab que sui culpa dolorosa fata multipliater pa sa est worthy knyght caste law grete rome ye saw ceptre ryyt tybery constatyn hyght who wyf cleped ytalye gedre progenye childre hadden mayde hyr god wel apayde al wyde worldes fame spake worship good name constance crony que seyth hyght ful feyth grettest barbarye hem whiche vseden marchandye hath conuerted come ther vpon tyme rome shewen suche thyng brouyt whiche worthely hem bought ouer suche wyse hath hem wordes wyse crystes feyth wel enformed therto ben al conformed baptysme receyuen al hir fals goddes weyuen whan feyth certeyne gone barbarye ayene ther soudan hem sent axrth hem eutent haue hyr fyrst feyth forsake whiche haue vndertake ryght feyth kepe holde mater tale tolde al hool cyrcumstaunce sowdan constauce vpon poynt ansuerde beaute grace herde whiche wedde al hast cause spedde send maryage ferthermore good courage sayth may hyr haue cryst yt cam world saue wol byleue recorded ben eyther syde accorded therupon make ende wdan hostage sende rome prynces sone twelue wherof ye fadre glad hym selue pope auysed two cardynallyz hath assised lordes many mo donghter shold go see sowdan conuerted qvaliter adueniente constancia arbariam mater soldanithuiusmo di nupcias perturbare volens filium fuum vna aim dictum constancia cardinalibus que alijs romani prima die ad conuiuium inuitauit et conues centibus illis mensa ipsuin soldanum omnes que ibidem preter constanciam romanos ab insidijs latitantibus subdola detractione interfeci procurciurt ipsam que constanciam qua dam na ab que gubernaculo positam oltum mare ventorum flatibuo agita dam exilium di gi solam constituit bvt neu wel herted enuye tho bygan trauayle dystourbaunce hyr spousayle pryuely none ware modre whiche souldan bare lyue thought vnto hyr self yf sone hym wedde manere haue lost ioyes myn estate shal lassed thynkend thus hath compassed sleyyte yt may begyle sone fylle ylke whyle bytwene hem two yt feyned wordes ere wyse gan saye sone double waye al myn hert glad blythe self haue ofte sythe desyre thou wolt men seyth receyue take newe feyth whiche shal forthryng thy lyf eke worshipful wyf doughter emperour wedde shal grete honour thy sone yow byseche yf myght suche grace areche may especyal doughter come shal thynketh honeste thylk whiche fyrst feste shal make vnto hyr welcomyng souldan graunteth hyr axyng therof glad ynoughe vnder anone droughe fals wordes spak couyne deth behynde bak euer vpon ordynaunce made constaunce comen forth romaynes clerkes cytezeynes ryche feste hem made hyr close enuye tho sprade al tho hadden apert pryue connseyll maryage slough hem sodeyne rage endelong bord set myght let owne sone quyte dyed vpon plyte hyghe god wol spare may perylle mysfare worthy maiden st de saith nygh dede ere see fest yt stood whiche al torned blood dysshe forth cuppe alle bled ouerable sawe dye euery syde wonder though wepte syde makyng many woful mone al slayn al one old fende sarazyn lete take anon constancyn al good thyder broughte ordeyned thoughte naked ship withoute stere whiche good hyr fere vitaylles ynough yeres fyue wynde wold dryue put vpon wawes wyld qualiter nauis cum constancia partes anglie que tune pagana fuit prope humber sub quodam castello regis qui tunc allee weabatur post triennium applicuit quam quidam mile nomine elda dicti castelli tuc custes et naiu lete suscipiens vxori sue hermyngylde custodiam honoryfice commendauit bvt al thinges may shild thre yere cometh londe hyr shyp stere hath take honde northumberlond arryueth happeth dryueth vnder castel stood whiche vpon humber bank stood kynges owne also whiche allee cleped tho saxon worthy knyght bybeuyd ryght castel castelleyne elda kynges chamberlayne knyghtly man lawe sawe vpon wawe ship dryuend alone also bad anone men sholden go see bytokene may vpon somer day shyp loked founde elda within lytel stounde wyst wyf anone ward yong lady gone founden grete rychesse wold confesse axen netheles vpon ca shyp grete worship take felauship hyr glade maner ioye made sow weth sore fond crystendodom thylk lond elles hath al hir wylle thus duellith stille dame hermegylde whiche wyf elda lyche owne lyf qvaliter constancia eldam cum vxore sua hermingylda qui antea cri stiana non extiterat ad fidem eristi mi raculose conuertit constaunce loueth felle spekyng al day bytwene hem two though grace goddes purueauce mayden taught creaunce vnto wyf parfytely vpon day fast presence husbond go walkyng stronde blynde man whiche cam ther lad vnto wyf cryend bad hondes vp prayde wyse sayde hermegylde whiche crystes feyth enformed constaunce seyth receyued hast yeue syght vpon word hir hert aflyght thynkyng best done netheles herd bone sayd trust crystes lawe done crosse slawe thou blynde man beholde se god vpon kne thankyng syght took anone wherof meruayle euerychone elda wondreth alle open thyng whiche byfalle coucludeth hem suche weye feyth nedes obeye qualiter quidam iuuenis mile amozem constancie exardescens pro co que ipsa consentice luit eam de mor te hermyngylde qm ipse noctant interfecit verbis detractorijs aceusauit sed angelus domim ipsum sic detrahentem maxilla subito percuciens non solum pro mendaci comprobauit sed ictu morta post ipsius confessionem penitus interfecit lest fel vpo thing elda forth vnto kyng morowe took weye rode hermegyld home abode forth constaunce wel ese elda thought kyng plese vnwedred constance al pleyne ca goodly couthe tolde kyng glad sayd wolde come thyder suche wyse hym myght auyse tyme appoynted forth al elda trust specyal vpon knyght fro childhode vp drawe manhode hym told al thought wherof hym forthought netheles ylke tyde vnto wyf bad hym ryde make redy al thyng ageynst comyng kyng sayth hym self fore thenketh come therfore hym kepe told hym whan knyght rode forth weye soth tyme passed al wyt compassed constaunce myght wynne sawe tho spede therynne wherof lust bygan bate loue hate honoure enuye vpon trecherye lesyng hert cast tyl come home hygheth fast doth lady vnderstonde message husbonde therupon long day setten thynges array al shold euery thyng degre cam nyght wyf hath bed dyght mayden lay fals knyght vpon delay hath taryed tyl slepe wol tyme kepe dedely werkes fulfylle bed stalketh stylle wyst wyf hond rasour knyf bare whiche throte cut pryuely knyf put vnder beddes syde constaunce lay besyde elda come home nyght stylle pr uy lyght wold awake wyf hath awey take chambre lyggende fonde dede wyf bledende constaunce fast falle slepe sodenly cryed aloude awoke forth al cast look sawe lady blede wherof swowned deed fere stylle ony stone lay elda therupon n castel clepeth oute vp stert euery man aboute chambre forth wente whiche al vntrouthe mente fals knyght among alle vpon thyng whiche byfalle yth constance hath dede bed yede falsh de speche made hym seche fonde knyf sayde cryed sayde lo see knyf al blody nedeth matere ye thus innocence laundreth audyence fals wordes whiche feyneth yet compleyneth elda ful credence toke har ed lay booke vpon whiche syghe knyyt hath swore sayd hyghe al men myght wyte book wryte constance gyltyf wel wote hond heuen hym smote token forswore hath eyen lore oute hede stoude stert founde wy herd felle whiche sayd dampned man helle lo thus hath god thy laudre wroke thou ageyn costance hast spoke knowe sothe thou dye told oute felonye starf forth tale anone ground al gone dede lady bygraue elda whiche thought honour saue al may restreyneth sorowe qualitrr rex e ad fidem cristi conuersus baptismnm recepit consta stanciam super hoc lew animo desponsauit que tn qualis vel vnde fuit al ui nullo modo fatebatur et cum infra breue postea domino su inpregnata fuisset ipse ad debellandu scotis iter ar ripuit et ibidem super guerras aliqut diu permansit second day morowe kyng cam acorded wh n hym recorded god hath wrouyt vpo chace took remembraunce thought sayde al hool hert layde vpon constaunce sayde sholde loue hir yf wolde baptysme take crystes feyth byleue ouer seyth wold hyr wedde vpon assured eche make shrot tale cam bysshop oute wale fro bangor lucye hyght whiche thurgh ye grace god almyyt kyng many mo crystned bytwene hem two hath fulfylled maryage lust ne rage told hym neuer netheles vpon ca kyng glad stood wel wyst vnderstood noble creature hygh maker nature hath vysyted thro openlyche knowe childe kyng wherof abouen al thyng thanked god ryght glad fel tyme bestad vpon werre must ryde shold abyde left home kepe wyf che knewe holy lyf elda forth bisshop eke power goth seke ayene scottes fonde werre whiche toke honde qualiter regina constancia infa tem masculum que baptismo mau ricium ocant rege absente enixa est sed inuida mater regis domilda super isto facto condolens mendacibus regi certificauit vxor sua demoniaci et non humani generis quondam monstruosum fantasma locum geniture ad ortum produxit huiusmodi que detracto ibus aduersus constanciam procurauit qd ipsa nauim qua prius venerat iterum ad exilium vna cum suo par tu remissa desolabatur tyme set kynde come lady hath hyr chabre nome sone borne ful wherof ioyeful delyuerd sauf sone bisshop done yaf hym baptysme morys calleth therupon byfalleth lettecs wryten record sent vnto lyege lord kepers quene shold go bytwene messager knaresburgh whiche towne shold posse thorugh rydend cam fyrst daye kynges modre laye who ryght name domylde whiche al cause spylde whiche thanke deserue wolde vnto lady goth tolde message ferde feyned ioye herde yafe hym yeftes largely nyght al pryuely took lettres whiche fro poynt poynt ouer rad yt thuruy oute vntrewe wryte newe stede hem thus speke prima littera commendacione n constancie ab episcopo regi missa per domildam contrarium falsata oure lyege lord beseke thou v ne wroth though suche thyng loth vpon oure trouthe certyfye thy wyf whiche fayrye suche child delynerd fro kynde whiche stant al amys shold seye haue kepte oute weye drede pure worldes shame power childe name thylke whiche mysbore took therto swore none thou shal knowe pryuete morys hatte thus men wene borne quene thy owne body gete thyng may foryete thou ne send v word anon thy wylle therupon letter thou hast herd deuyse counterfete suche wyse man shold perceyue whiche thought deceyue leyde toke messager awoke w st thynge oos ood grete pa hym leef hym loth al hast ageyne goth na sbu gh went vnto mod entent fond ward kynge told vpon thyng seyth shold abyde al nyght made hym fest chere aryght feyned though coude thok strog wyn drok forth
