couseyll two stonde poynt vndo whiche kyng deposed euery man hath supposed wyf constance faye yf feyne delaye put hyr oute companye worship regalye lore ouer telle child shal amog yow dwelle claymen ony herytage see none auauntage al lost yf abyde thy loke euery syde toward meschyef charge yow byd ye ship vytaylle whiche toke arryuaylle theryn putteth two hyr self forth hyr child also forth brought depe taketh hyr see kepe foure dayes tyme set ye thyng lenger let youre lyf forfete thus letter counterfete messagyer whiche vnware vpon kynges halue bare shold haue bytake hede take rad wryten withynne grete sorowe begynne owne modre seyen brenne fyre byfore theyr eyen wepyng ther wo fynally thyng vpon see haue brought cause wyst nought thus vpon flood wone lady yong sone handes heuene straught mylde steuene knelend vpon hyr bare kne sayd hyghe mageste whiche seest poynt euery trouth take thy woful woman routh thylk childe shal kepe yt word bygan wepe swouned dede lay whiche al thynges may comforteth hyr last loketh eyen cast vpon hyr child sayd maner charge sorowe suffre thynketh grete pyte yf sterue thou shalt deye mote nedes weye moderhode tendrenesse al myn hole besynesse ordeyne offyce whiche shal thy noryce thus strengthed stode th took hyr child honde yaf souke euer amonge wepte whyle songe rokke hyr child slepe thus owne child kepe hath vnder goddes cure qualiter nauis constancie post biennium partes hispanie superior inter sarayinos iactabatur quorum manibus deus ipsam conseruans graciosissime liberauit fel vpon auenture ylke yere hath made ende hyr ship mote wende stregth wynd god hath yine estward spayn dryue ryght fast vnder castel walle hethen admyralle lord afterward one thelons whiche al bad fals knyght renegate goth loke estate shyp comen fonde forth child vpon hyr honde lady al one took hede persone sawe worthy wyght thought wold vpon nyght demene hyr owne wylle ship kepte hyr stylle noman sawe hyr daye goddes wylle thus laye vnknowe shal betyde fel nyghtes tyde knyght withoute felauship hath take boote cam ship thought hir lust take swore yf hym daunger make certeynly shold deye sawe ther none weye bad hym comforte loke fyrst oute porte man nygh stede whiche myght knowe dede maye wolde ryght glad tolde port anon ferde prayeth god herde sodenly thro dreynt bygan blowe wynde meuable fro londe thus myghty goddes honde hyr hath conueyed defended thre yere ben ful dispended qualiter nauicula costancie quo dam die per altum mare vagans inter copio nauium multitudinem dilapsa est quarum ar ennius romanorum consul dux capitane ipsam ignotam suscipiens v que ad ro mam secum perduxit vbi equalem vx ori sue elene permansuram reuerenter associauit nec non et eiusdem filium mauricium omni habundanaa qua si propririum educauit hir ship dryue vpon daye grete nauye laye shyppes al world one god wold none hyr shyp goth among hem alle stynt byfalle hath vessel vnder gete whiche mayster al flete resteth abode grete ship anker rode tho lord come forth syghe lay borde nyghe wondreth myght bad men go se lady tho rope syde au wold seluen hyde ne wyst sought aboute hyr fonde brought vp hyr child therupon lord spere bygan fro whens cam quod woman wofully bestad lord thus forth ytr sone vpon wawes shold wone cause wote nought whiche al thynges wrought yet ay thanke hym myght child kepte vpryght sauf two lord xr axeth eu mo byleued seyth ue trust crystes feyth whiche dyed vpon od e thy name tho quod name cust hym sayde ferthermore nought prayde astate trouthe pleyne wold hym elles nothyng yne name whiche feyned al thynges restreyned word ne told lord axeth yf wold hym abyde companye sayd cam fro barbarye rome ard home w nte tho supposeth mente sayth wold hym wende duelle lyues ende yf plesaunce thus vpon acqueyntaunce told hyr pleynly stood rome gentyl blode barbarye bytrayed therupon hath assayed werre take suche vengeaunce none thylk allyaunce whome treson compassed swerd lyue passed constaunce couthe knowe noo bycam seyde hyr ere vnto word leyde forther made che e ne h le maner happed lke tyme lord whome wold go rome senatour fadre emperour broder doughter hath wyue whiche hath hyr fadre eke lyue salustes cleped tho wyf eleyne hyght also whome constaunce cosyne thus seke medycyne hath god ordeyned grace forthwith place senatour trouthe plyght euer whyle lyue myght kepe hir worship wele god wol gyue hyr hele lady whiche fortune hym sen ship thus forth saylende child rome brought wyf thus sought take hyr companye whiche couthe curtosye al good wyf shold conne ly glad wonne felauship good one tho twelue yeres gone emperours doughter custe forth doug ter saluste kept man redyly knewe thy though wel hyr estate hyghe degre euery lyf hyr loueth wele qualiter rex allce inita pace cum otis guerris rediens non inuenta vyore sua causa exilij diligencius pers rutans cum matre suam domi da inde culpabilem sciusset psam igue proiciens conburi fecit herke thylk vnstable whele whiche euer torneth wente aboute kyng alle whiche oute thou fore hast herd ca ceyued thoruh modre come home ageyne axeth chamberlayne aud bisshop eke also quene ansuerd bad haue hym thylk letter rad whiche hem warrant tolde hym pleynly stant seyn thought grete pyte see worthy one suche child bo e sodenly forbore axeth hem child hym sayd nowhere al world though men sought neuer woman forth brought fayrer child one axeth hem anone ne hadden wryten den sayd nay sayden yi letter shewed ad whiche forsoken euery dele tho vnderscond wele treson thyng messager fore kyng brought sodenly opposed whiche thyng hath supposed al wel bygan saye nowhere vpon waye abode stede cause dede went fro naresburgh nyght two kynges moder dyde hym du lle ye kyng herd telle within hert wyst fast treson whiche modre cast thought wold abyde forth ryght tyde took hors rood anone hym ryde many one knaresburgh forth wente yche fyre thoder hence suche rage yth book moder sodenlyche took sayd vnto wyse este helle gyse hast thou deserued deye thou thus hast put aweye treson thy bakbytyng trewest knowlechyng wyues honest wol make byhest shal auengyd go lete fyre make tho bad men cast ynne fyrst told oute al synne dede hem alle wyte lettres wryte fro poynt poynt wrouyt tho deth brought brunt fore sone eye wherof whiche syghe herden cause stood seyn ngement good sone hath serued wel deserued thorugh treson owne tonge whiche thorugh londe songe costace euery wiyt cople neth al wo dystreyneth sorowful kynge bys ad shal neuermore glad seyth eftsone wedde tyl wyst spedde whiche ben fyrst wyf aud thus yong vnlusty lyf dryueth forth may qvaliter post apsum duodecim anuozum rex allee absolucionis causa romam proficiscens vxorem suam constana vna cum filio suo diuina prouidencia ibidem letus inuenit tyl byfel vpon day werres acheued thought wold releued soule hele vpon feyth whiche hath take seyth rome pylgremage wold go pope pelage take absolucyon vpon condycyon made edwyn lyeutenaunt whiche heyr hym apparaunt bond absence shal rewle prouydence al thyng wel bygone took leue forth gone elda hym tho fully e rome sent fore purueye hys guyde vpon weye helpe herbeg hath ayed senatour name myght kenne ca odece sayd arcenne hyght worthy knyght hym goth elda forth ryght told hym lord tydyng prayd comyng wold assygne hym herbergage dyde good courage whan al done kyng hym self cam sone senatour come cust wyf home hath told suche kyng allee grete array cyte come cust vpon tale hert c se colour pale swoune felle meruaylleth sodenly thyng hyr eyleth caught hyr vp woke sygheth pytoue loke feyneth sekenesse see kyng allee ioye whiche felle thought god hym hath towne brouyt kyng hath spoke pope told al couthe grope greueth conscyence thought reuerence estate went make feest anon sente vnto senatour come vpon morowe sytte hym mete tale hath cust foryet morys hyr sone tolde vpon morowe sholde al euer couth myght present kynges syght kynge hym ofte syghe morys fore kynges ye vpon morowe sat ful ofte stood vpon kyng chere vpon hym cast face thought fast sawe owne wyf constance nature resemblaunce face hym lyketh clothe one suyte bothe kyng hath moeued thought yt sawe knewe nought childe loueth kyndely yett wote noo cause wel saw vnderstode toward arcenne stode axeth hym anone ryght yf child sone sayd ye hym calle wold byfalle al wyse tho gan deuyse childes modre fond vpon see euery lond within ship stereles lady speles orth hir child hath forth draw kynge hath vnderstonde saw childes name axeth tho modre hyght also hym wolde telle preyde moris child hote seyde modre hat cust maner name allee wyst wel ynough wherof somdele smylend lough cust saxon seyn constance vpon word romeyn couthe specyfye tho fantasye aud wytt aboute renneth vpon loue whiche brenneth wondre neyther ne clene oute hym self awey note thynk ne sey feyn wold wherof hertes pryuete bygan werre ye nay whiche suche balaunce lay contenaunce throwe lost tyl myght knowe soth memorye man whiche lyeth purgatorye desyreth heuen ne longeth also sore wyte hym shal betyde boordes syde euery man ryse aboute kyng hath weyued al route senatour al one spak prayd hym bone see cust duelleth home hym telleth senatour wel apayd kyng lenger delayd see cust goth kyng warned thyng eleyne forth cam ayene kyng tho nam good hede sawe wyf anone al hertes lyf caught hyr armes kyst neuer wyght syghe ne wyst man ioye made wherof al glad whiche herd telle channce kyng tho wyf costace whiche grete part wylle rome tyme stylle abode made hym wel case yet coud neuer please hyr estate trouthe pleyne wyf wold hym seyne conntre bore ne yet therfore al wyt dyde seke thus lay bed speke prayth hym counseyleth bothe worship hem bothe thought honest wold honourable fest make went cyte emperour shal graunted al hym prayd tyme men sayd thylk emperour day fyrst doughter went away neuer glad ony man hym bad grace doughter sake grace wold nought forsake aud thus ful grete almesse dede wher f many bede qvaliter constancia que antea per totum tempus exilij sui penis omnes incognitam se celauit tunc mum patri suo imperatori se ipsam per omnia manifestant qd cum rex allee sci sset vna cum vniuersa romanoru multitudine inestimabili gaudio admirances cuuctipotentem laudarunt emperour oute toune within ten myle e uyroune thought hym best hath sondry place rest fortune wold tho duellend one tho kyng allee forth thassent cust wyf hath thyder sent moryce sone taught themperour goth straught fadre halue sought whiche lordship sought tht hyghe worthynes wold grete mekenes owne towne come see yeue tyme cyte fadre myght hym gete wosd one hym ete ford hath graunted request day fest worship emperour kyng este senatour forth wyues bothe two many lord lady mo hors ryden hym ageyne tyl byfell vpon pleyne syghe comend constaunce anone preyend spak lord abyde may fore ryde ben vpon bien benu fyrst whiche shal hym salu thus hyr lordes graunt upon mule whyte amblaunt forth fewe rood qu ne wondred wold mene ryden softe pa lady comen themperour presence sayd aloude audyence lord fadre wel tyme se honour good le whiche helpe quarele thanke vnto goddes myght ye rt aflyght told remembraunce wyst constauce neuer fadre half blythe wepend kyst hyr ofte sythe hert al ouercome though modre come fro deth lyf graue myght wonder haue hath hyr syght hyr owne lord come nyght themperour obeyed comfort w eyed constaunce come aboute hard hert none oute pyte tho ne wepte arcenius hyr fonde kepte glad falle ioye among hem alle ryden rome gate emperour thought al late tyl pope come tho lordes sende pray hym wol hast cam forth al hast tale herd wonderly chaunce ferd thanked god myracle whome may none obstable kyng noble feste hem made thuo al glade parlement went setten vnto entent put rome ful espeyre morys apparent heyre shold abyde hym stylle suche al londes wylle qualiter mauricius cum impera e vt here imperij remansit et rex allee et constancia ang regres si sunt euery thing fully spoke soro queynt al yt smoke tho toke leue allee yt kyng ful many ryche thyng whiche themperour hym yeue hath glad lyf lyue constance hath hond whiche comfort lond come home ageyne tong myght seyne ioye ylke stoude whiche rst sent goddes sound whome mysbileue synne left crystes feyth cam ynne hem whilome blynde qualiter rex ang post bicnnium humane carnis resolucionem subiens nature debitum persoluit post cuius obitum costancia cum patre suo rome se transtulit moraturam hyndreth euery kind gold may forlouyt deth comyng besought toke kyng suche acqueyntauce al retenauce ne myght defende lyf thus parteth wyf whiche made sorowe ynoughe therupon hir herte droughe leue englond euer go leuer rome whens cam thus al lond nam hyr leue goth rome ageyne bokes seyne thro deth kynde hath ouerthrowe hir worthy fadre whiche men seyde bytwene hyr armes deyde ward yere suend god hath made end fro worldes fayrye hath take hyr companye moryce hyr sone coroned whiche ferforth abandoned crystes feyth men hym calle morys crystnest alle thus whele meuyng loue last set aboue thou hast herd fore fals tunges lore whiche vpon loue wold lye thy touchend enuye whiche longeth vnto bakbytyngr ware thou make lesyng hyndryng another wyght yf thou wold taught aryght meschyef bakbytyng doth weye tale soth myght thou anone sewend whiche vyce acordend hic ponit confesso exemplu co tra istos detractores qui afterius bitupeaum mendacia confingentes diffamacom fieri procurauit et natrat qualiter perseus philippi regis macedonij filius demetrio fratri suo ob eius provitatem inuidens composito detractionis mendacio ipsum apud patrem suum mortaliter accusauit dicens ipse non solum patrem sed totum macedonij regnu romani hostibus proditurie vendidisset quem super hoc iudicinm producens testib que judicibns auro subornatis quamuis falsissime morte condempnatum e cit quo defuncto eciam et pater infea breue postea mortuus est et persio successiue regnante de huius detractionis iuuidiam abhorrens ipsum cum bniuersa suorum pugnatorum multitudine extra dauubij fluuium ab emilio tunc romanorum consule euen tu bellico interfeci fortunauit ita ab illo die macedonij potestas penitus de tructa romano imperio subiugata de seruiuit eius detractio quam contra um conspirauerat sui ipsius diffamacionem pro perpetuo diuulgata consistit ina crony que thou shalt wyte grete ensample fynd wryte whiche shal telle vpon thyng phelyp macedonye kyng two sone wyf who fame yet grece ryf demetrius fyrst broder hote perseus demetrius sayden tho better knyght tho whome lond attendanut whiche heyre apparaunt regne fadre day thyng whiche water may quenche world euer brenneth broder hert renneth proud enuye sygh broder shold clynne hyg hym mote obeye may suffer wey strength durst thyng sto took lesyng vpon honde sygh tyme spak therto byfelle tyme fadre grete werres rome whiche streyt lad thorugh myyty strength mahod whiche hath yuough knygthod ofte h sore greued werre acheued vpon ordynaunce home grece felle par chaunce demetaus whiche ofte aboute rydend stood tyme oute perse absence whiche bare tonge pestylence fals wordes whiche feyneth upen owne broder pleyneth pryuete behynde bak fadre thus spak dere fadre holde wey kynde reson wolde fro yow shal thyng hyde whiche myght torne ony syde youre estate greuaunce thy myn hertes obeysaunce toward yow thenke kepe good ye take kepe upon thyng whiche told broder hath v al sold hem rome yow also behote hym tho shal regne pee thus hath cast encres youre estate shal go nought thus proue shal brought ferforth vndertake shal wel mow forsake kyng vpon tale ansuerd said yf thyng whiche herd soth may brought proue shal behoue whiche v hath shapen werst hym self shal ferst shal dede yf may thus afterward vpon day demetrius come anone fadre hath hym nome bad broder perse tale shal reherce thylk treson whiche told whiche al vntrouthe wolde counseylleth hyghe nede treted may spede comon place jugement kyng therto yafe assent demetrius put holde wherof perseus bolde thus stood trouth vnder ye charge falshede goth large whiche thou gh byhest hath ouercome grettest lordes preuelyche acord stond wytnesse record iuge made fauourable thus lawe deceyuable ferforth fronth fond rescouse none thus lond forth kyng deceyued gyliles dampned deyde vpon acusement suche fals conspyrement though preuy throwe god wold vnknowe yt ward wel proued hym whiche hath yt deth cotroued broder slayn perseus wondre fayn thattho apparaut upon regne expectaut wherof wax proud beyn fadre dysdeyn hath take set none acompte whiche thouyt hym surmoute fyrst de bonayr tho rebelle contrayre heyr kyng took vpon hym al thyng malyce tyrannye contempt regalye lyued fadre soo wrought fadre hym bethought sawe whedyr syde droughe anone wyst wel ynough perse fals tonge hath thenuyous belle ronge hath slayne owne broder wherof knewe none sodenly iuge nome whiche corrupt sat vpon dome suche wyse hath hym pressed soth hym hath confessed al hath spoke sory kynge tho neuer man vpon molde thought certeyne wold engeaunce take vpon wrong party strongr lawe statute may ryght execute vpon dyuysyon lond torned vp doun wherof herbe distraught pure sorowe hath caught maladye whiche nature queynt euery creature kyng passed thus fals tonged perseus regyment hath vnderfonge ther may thyng stond longe whiche vpon trouthe grounded god whiche hath al thyng bouded sawe falshede gyle hath set hym lytel whyle shal regne vpon depose sodenly rose sodenly doune felle thylk tyme byfelle newe kyng newe pryde strengthe shope hym ryde sayd wold rome waste wherof made besy haste hath assembled hym hoost al euer myght man myght wepen al wold none forbe myght nombred folk whiche encombred thorugh yt god wold ouerthrowe anone rome knowe pompe whiche perse lad romayns tyme consul whiche cleped thus name panle emilius noble worthy knyght alle whiche cheef alle werre hond hath vndertake whan shold leue take yong doughter whiche wepte cause axeth hym ansuereth perseus dede hereth wondreth mene wold vpon childehode hym told perse lytel hound dede withethat pulleth vp hede made ryght glad vysage seyd presage touchend vnto perse fortune hym shald aduerse seyth suche prenostyke moost hound hym lyke houndes kynde berke vpon man behynde ryght behynde broders bak fals wordes whiche spak hath slayn routhe whiche hateth al vntrouth hyghe god shal redresse doughter prophetesse forth hyr lytel houndes deth betokeneth thus forth geth conforted euydeuc romayns defence ageyne grekes comende perseus nought semende meschyef whiche hym abode al multitude rode prayd hym vpon thyng bycomen kyng royalme gete hath al ryght foryete whiche longeth vnto gouernaunce wherof thorugh good ordynaunce felle vpon wynter tyde hoost shold ryde oner dauubye thylke flood whiche al frorn stood hard wende wel passe blynde wheel whiche torneth ofte men beware thylk yee whiche hors men bare brak grete partye dreynt chyualrye rereward took awey cam none hem lond drey paulus worthy knyyt romeyn aspye herd seyn hasteth al may vpon day cam hoost byheld large feld baners ben displayed hath anone men arrayed enbataylled goth hath feld assaylled slough took al fonde wherof macedonye londe thurgh kyng alisader honoured long tyme stood deuoured perse al infortune wyte comune al lond heyre exyle dyspeyred whyle desguysed power wede rome goth ther nede aft whiche thylk tyme worken lawn bra lerneth sustenaunce suche sone purueaunce fadre sayd strong pryson layd albe dede honger defaulte brede hounde token prophecye lyche hound shold dye whiche lyche condycyon whan detractyon bark broder behynde coufessor lo proufyde man may fynde whiche hyndre wol another wyght thy al thyn hool myght sone eschewe thylk vyce amans fadre elles nyce ye therof wel haue spoke myn hert loke euer shal enuye ther baylye towardes loue say sone gyle vnder hat sleyghtes tregetour hyd enuye suche colour hath yet fourth deceyuaunt whiche cleped fals semblaunt wherof mater forme herkne shal enforme nil bilinguis aget nisi duplo conci tat ore dum que diem loquitur vox sua vota tegit vultus habet lucem tenebras men sermo salutem actus sed morbum dat suus esse grauem pox tibi quam spondet magi est prenostica guerre comoda si dederit disce subesse dolum qnod que patet esse fides eo frau est que positi p ncipium pacti finis habere negat qm condicio talis deformat amantein qui magi apparens est amore nichil hic tractat confessor super quarta specie inuidie que dissimulacio dicitur cuius vultus quanto maio ri amicicie apparenciam ostendit tato subtilioris doli fallacias ad decipien du men ymaginatur fals seblaut yf shall telle aboue al ye welle yt deceyt floweth man wyse knoweth thylkf lood whiche tyde ne shold hym self guyde take sauf passage yet wynd man ere softe semeth oute maketh clere weder al aboute though seme soo fals semblaunt hath euer moo counseyl companye derke vntrewe ipocrysye whoos word destroyeth thouyt thy gyder brought one couyne one houshold shal ward thus told fals semblaunt nedeth nought telle old ensamples ought al day experyence man may see thylk euydence fayre wordes whiche hereth yet barge enuye stereth halt euer londe whiche fals seblaut oore hond roweth wol arryue lete wawes dryue grete tempest grete debate wherof loue estate empeyreth therfore rede sone thou flee drede vyce seyn lete thy semblaunt trewe pleyn fals semblaunt thylk vyce whiche neuer withoute offyce enuye thynketh gyle shal byfore ylke whyle pryue counseylle messagere semblaunt clere derke thought though man hym se knowe hym nouyt sheweth glas thyng whiche theryn neuer sheweth vysage neuer courage thus doth al thyng sleyght laye thy conscyence weyght good soue shryue thou euer customere fals semblaunt ony wyse ought yet auyse good fadre certes loue haue axe wold pray yow elles wote neuer bow fals semblaut yt haue gy sone sethyn thou wylt shal axe gabbe nought telle yf euer thy thought fals semblaunt couerture wyte ony creature loue stad wery sory glad whan thou wystyst al rouneth thyn ere thou toldest forth place setten hym fro loues grace woman hym best lyst theryn man counseyll wyst thou whome deceyue loue purpoos weyued thoughtest dysturbaunce thyn owne cause shold auaunce seyth secrete may man pryuete beh led halue wel myn art thou sone suche engyn telle good fadre nay party say somdele byknowe thati may stonde thylk rowe among hem saundres vse wol therof excuse suche colour ne steyne best semblaunt feyne telle fela wote al counseylle cold hote cause make hym chere tyl loue knowe yf myn herte soucheth ought vnto lady toucheth loue wold telle anone renne vnto welle cast water fyre carte amyd fyre haue counseyll knowe ful ofte syth ouerthrowe weneth best stonde yow vnderstonde yf man loue elles lady nought telle wol hyde shal word escape asyde forth deceypt semblaunt hym breke none couenaunt lyketh place let man grace ne inquesyty knowe another man lyf loue loue nought toncheth thyng thouyt al passeth thorugh myn ere ryght thyng neuer foryete layd asyde yf toucheth ony syde lady haue er spoken myn eres nought loken certes whan tyt wyl myn hert al wyt ben fully set herken spere ony man wol saye thus haue feyned companye ful ofte wold aspye thyng ony man telle worthy lady two cause fyrst cause wherof myght herken seke ony man myspeke wol excuse hyr fully wyst veryly myn hope shold hane hyr thank euermore cause yow assure see couerture haue feyned semblaunt oftyme passen al day byme ben louers wel wene truly hem al none ne louen euerychone lady sothelyche leue durst sytten preue none wyse shold asterte lustles herte lady syghe vysage goodly eye loued went suche myn entent cause myn aspye feyne companye make folowe ouer al gladly wold knowen al hold couert alway fulofte ye nay ne lyst ansuere ony wyse feynyng semblaunt wyse herken tale tyl knowe lady louers al rowe haue wrought fare though herd nouyt word vnderstode thynge goode leueth wel soth knowe wol fordren hem lyte al werst endyte telle lady plat forthryng myn owne estat hyndre al maye al yet dar saye fynde vnto self bote al though myn herte nedes mote though loue al dyscouer vnto lady dere good feyth haue myght hele fro swete wyght toucheth ony thyng wote wel heuen kyng sythen fyrst world bygan vnto none strannge man ne feyned semblannt ne chere wyte axe matere though yt loueth x twelue nought lady selue yf wold axe ony rede al onlyche owne hede loue ferde tale myn eres herde myn hert cam nought ne sanke depper thought bnt helde counseylle bede told neuer stede lete pas come fadre saye thy dome thou wolt yt peyned fals semblant haue feyned sone yf reson wel peised may vertu vp reysed ne vyce none set pryse thy sone yf thou wyse vyser vpon face whiche wol thyn hert embrace yf thou within throwe another man shal knowe myyt thou lightely falle blame lese grete part thy name netheles degre ful oftyme thou myght se suche men day vyce sette assay speke man blame warne thy shame sone may talke euery place walke yf none many dayes gone fyrst herd telle fals semblaut hath comonly yere yere hem duelle among v suche lumbardes calle slyest alle men seyn towne aboute feyne shewe thyng withoute whiche reuers within wherof ofte wyn whan reson shold lese ben last yet chefe fyrst yet behynde gone shuld fynde proufyte owne lond thus gone fre withoute bond done proufyte al large men bere al charge lumbardes vnto couyne whiche al londes conne engyne may fals semblaunt especyal br lykened euer al thynken duelle among self telle fyrst ben enformed lere craft whiche cleped faucrere yf faucrere come aboute afterward stant doute voyde subtyle honde best goodes lond brynge chaf take corn faucrere goth forn al wey fynt let e none vssher shet whiche hym lyst take entre thus counseyll secre euery thyng faucrere knoweth whiche strauge place bloweth whiche wote may greue thus faucrere maketh byleue ful ofte hath deceyued er may ben apperceyued thus vyce drede old bokes rede suche ensamples ar hym ought war al tho feynen chere wherof thou shalt tale hic ponit confessor exemplum contra istos q sub dissimulate beniuolecie speculo alios amore defrau dant et narrat qualiter hercules c ipse quoddam fluuium cui vad non nouit cum deianyra transmeare proposuit superueniens nessus gigas ob amiciciam herculis vt dixit deianyram vlnas su suscipiens trans ri pam saluo perduxit et statim cum ad litus peruenisset cito currere pptuit ipsam tam quam propriam preiudicium herculis asportare fugiens conabatur per qd non solum ipsi sed eciam herculi mortis euentum fortuna post modum causauit fals semblaunt whiche beleued ful many worthy wyght greued long tyme bore sone wyl therfore tale telle fals semblaunt whiche falseth many couenaunt many fraude fals couseylle honged vpon seylle abouten gylteles bothe deyanyre hercules whiche grete dysese felle thorugh fals semblaut shal telle hercules within throwe al hath hert throwe vpon fayre deyanyre felle hym day desyre vpon ryuer stood passe wold ouer flood withoute bote hym lede loue drede tendrenesse swete wyght knewe forth aryght geaunt nyghe whiche nessus hyght whan syghe hercules deianyre within hert gan conspyre whiche thought trecherye hath hercules grete enuye whiche bare herte loke thought shal wroke ne durst netheles ayene worthy hercules falle debate fyght feyned semblaunt al sleyght frendship al good cometh stood maketh hem al chere sayth owne man al redy thyng may fel vpon semblaunt tryst axeth hem yf wyst thyng best done myghten sauf sont water passe whan nessus pryuete knewe hert ment double entent made hem ryght glad vysage herd passage hym hyr thought gyle feyneth semblaunt whyle thought al another wyse done hem plesaunce seruyce nessus wordes slyghe yaf counseylle fore eye whiche semed outward prouffytable within deceyuable bad hem stremes depe beware take kepe knowe compas helpe suche ca sayth hym self ease wold yf yt myght hem please passage water take lady vndertake bere hyr stronde sauf set vpon londe hercules may also weye knowe shold go therto acorden alle shal byfalle wel payd hercules geaunt also glad toke lady vpon lofte set hyr shulder softe flood bygan wade whiche grutchyng made bare hyr oner sauf soude stood drye gronnd hercules ferre behynde set trouthe al oute mynde ther lefe loth deianyre forth goth thought dysseuer companye hem euer hercules therof took hede fast euer myght hym spede hyeth throwe hapneth bowe whiche al hast bende wold arowe sende whiche fore venymed hath wel shot tymed hym thorugh body smet thus fals wyght let leste suche felonye whan nessus wyst shold dye took deianyre shert blood hert thorugh oute desteyned ouer al told kepe shal pryuely hir entent yf lord hert went loue ony place shyrt sayth hath suche grace yf may mochel make shyrte vpon hym take shal al lete veyn torne loue ageyn glad deianyre hyr hert hyr thought fyre tyl cofer loke therof word spoke dayes gone yeres passe hertes waxen lasse lasse hem loue vntrewe hercules hert newe hert hath set eolen therof speken al men eolen fayre mayde men thylk tyme sayde kynges doughter euryce made hercules nyce vpon loue assote hym clotheth hyr cote clothed ofte thus feblesse set alofte strengthe put vnder fote man therof doo bo e deianyre hath herd speche sorowe seche helpe wote none goth vnto hyr coufer anone wepeud eye woful herte took oute thylk vnhappy sherte wend wel brought hyr werke aboute hercules shert dede suche entent bede nessus sayd er therfore ye ner aud fortune may weyued fals semblaunt deceyued wende best haue wonne lost al hath bygonne thylk shert vnto bone body set fyre anone cleueth may twynne venym therynne wyld man vnto hyghe wode ran clerk ouyde telleth grete tree ground felleth strengthe owne myght made hughe fyre vpryght lept hym self therin one brente hym bothe flesshe bone whiche thyng cam thorugh fals seblat fals nessus geant made vnto hym wyf wherof hath lost lyf also euermo thy sone thou wo rede wel ware therfore grete man lore ought yeue grete conceypt warne al suche deceypt graunt mercy fader ware fer dare fals semblaunt take acqueyntauce rather wol penaunce haue feyned chere axe forth ther bylongeth shryfte sone yet ther fyfte whiche conceyued enuye clepend supplantarye thorugh who compassement gyle ful many hath lost whyle loue wel wyse shal deuyse inuid alte riu supplatator horis et tua quo vertat cultura subt arat est op occultu qi q latrt agis herba qd facit subita sorte nociuus adest sic subtilis amas aliu supplatat amat et capit occulte qd ne ipse palam sepe que supplatas plata platat amo quod pntat proprijs alter ha bere bo u hie tractat confessor de quinta spe cie inuidie que supplantacio dicitur cu ius cultor pr u que percipiatur aliene dignitatis officij multocies intrusor existens vyce supplantacyon many fals collacyon cospirethal vnknowe ful oftyme hath ouerthrowe worship another man wel lyf awayte ayene sleyght cast purpoos last ne hath withset moost al herte set court vpon grete offyces dygnytees benefyces thus goth sleyghte hyndre shoue another stonden slyghe compas seede another set hym self ynne r ebeth wynne another man shal l se thus ful ofte chalk chefe chaungeth ful lytel cost wherof another hath lost proufyt shal receyue fortune receyue chaunge vpon whele woo men wele another man auayleth astate thus vp hayleth taketh byrd beyete men busshes bete sone wyse louers suche empryse shapen hem relyeued wrong achyeued man ryght whiche hath take day nyght ty kepe owne store toward hym self euermore propre lawe whiche thynge axeth felawe worchen supplauut take part thylk plant whiche hath hym self set fulofte al vnknet som man weneth ryght fast supplaunt sly cast ful ofte happeneth mowe thyng another man hath owe maketh comon propyrte sleyghte subtylte men may seen yere yere thus cleymeth boot stere whiche another mayster thy sone yf thou hast ben suche professyon dyscouer thy confessyon hast thou supplanted ony man ought yow telle myn holy fadre dede withouten ony drede gilteles thought censcyence excuse nought wrong ryght lacketh thyng myght ne wold longe man loue wy wey supplantacyon haue made appropryacyon hold neuer bought though another man forthought al speke one whome lete al gone may ouerpasse ne mote alwey compasse e rought queynty e myght ony wyse fro suche lady serue hert make swerue withoute ony part loue thegoddes al aboue wold myght byfalle alone shold hem alle supplante welde hyr wylle yt thyng may nought fnlfylle yf shold strengthe make dar vndertake thongh alysander therof myght ryse sklaunder certes shal neuer good feyth yet lener ony symplesse dye worche suche supplantarye wyse wol say yf fond syker way wold conclusyon worche supplantacyon hyghe loue wynne fadre yf synne al redy redresse gylt whiche confesse sone supplant dar drede tant ne quant thyng haue herd thou hast mysferd thynkend lyketh nought god beholt man thought yf thou vnderstood soth loues cause doth man supplantour thou woldest thyn honour double way take kepe fyrst thyn owne estate kepe thy self wel thought thou supplanted nought eke worship thy name towardes suffre euery man haue netheles wayte al assayes supplant loue wayes leef ful ofte leuer forsaketh hath done euer ensample fynde therupon qualiter agameno de amore brexeide achille diomedes de amore cri seide troilum supplanta ut troye agamenon supplanted worthy knyghte achilles swete wyghte whiche named brexeyda also cryseyda whome troylus loue ches supplanted hath diomedes qualiter amphitriun socium suam geta qui almaenam peramauit seipsum loco alterius cautelosa supplanta cione substituit geta amphitryone whilome one frendship companye rede supplantarye loue betyd tho begyled hath one hem two geta whome mene whome lusty fayr almene assured wey loue best wende aboue sykerest cupido cause lad whyle oute weye amphytryon hast next weye hath take forme hath wrouy nyght vnto chambre sought lay within whyle counterfeted dyde fyle voys geet suche wyse made hyr hyr bed aryse wenend lete hym gyder bed armes fast geta cam last vndo dore sayd vndo ansuerd bad hym goo sayd bedde al warme hyr lyef lay naked hyr arme wende soth lo supplaunt loue doth get forth beiaped went yet ne wyst ment amphitryon hym hath supplanted sleyghtr loue enchautrd thus put euery man oute ship loue hath lost rother reson stere fo skepe matere touchend loue supplaunt tal whiche acordaunt vnto thyn ere thynke enforme herken forme hic amoris causa cotra fraude detractionis ponit confessor exe plum et narrat de quodam romani imperatoris fillo qui probitates armorum super omnia exercere affectans nescrente patre vltra mare partes per e ad deseru endu soldano super guer cum solo milite tam quam socio suo ignotu se transtul et cum ipsius mi ae fama super alios ibidem accreuisset centigit vt quodam bello contra aliphum egipti inito soldanus sagitra mortaliter vulneratu prius quam moreretur quendam anulum suum filie sue secretissunu isto romano tradi dicens aualiter filia sua sub paterne enedictianis vinculo adiurata est quam uicum que dictum anulum ei afferret ipsum coniugem pre omnibus susciperet defuncto autem sol ver sus ciuitatem que lroyre dicitur itinerantes iste romanus commilitoni suo huius mistrij secretum reuelaiut qui octater bursa domini sui anulo fur surripiens hec que audiuit vsui proprio falsissima supplatacone applicuit f thylk cyte cheef alle men ye noble rome calle er set crystes feith crony que seyth emperour whiche ladde pee werres hadde thyng dysobeysaunt whiche rome appertenaunt al torned rest som thought best som thought thyng vnto tho who herte stood vpon knyghthode moost al manhode worthy sone emperour whiche wold ben werryour chyualrous worldes fame desyrous bygan fadre beseche werres myght seche straunge march ryde fadre sayd shold abyde wold graunte hym leue whiche wold byleue knyght whiche tryst ryght euen thought lyst toke told hym courage purposyth vyage fortune hym stonde seyd wold fonde grete see passe vnknowe abyde throwe vpon werres auayle poynt withoute fayle knyyt hath herd lord swore stant acord bothe yong preny counseyl ben assented wende therupon make ende tresour ynough hem token whan tyme best loken sodenlyche galey fro rome lond wente wey londed vpon syde world felle ylke tyde whiche euer happes hath dyuerse grete soldan perse ayene calyphe egypt werre whiche hym beclypt hath marche costeraunt whiche pursyuaunt worship armes atteyne romayn anone lete ordeyne redy euery dele arrayed wele euery thyng hym bylongeth strauyt vnto kayre wey fong geth sowdan fond axeth within lond myght hym werre serue whiche wol thank deserue soldan ryght glad wel specyall wyst romayn elles incertayn myghte wyte wey thus knyght whome sey toward soldan left march eft dedely werres wrought suche knyghthode euery man spak hym good thylke tyme stood myghty soldan wyf doughter hath lyf men sayd none feyr shold hyr fadres heyr yeres rype ynough hyr beaute many herte drongh bowe ylke lawe fro lyf may withdra loue who nature set lyf deth noo mesure hem knyghthode vndertake lusty peyne hath ouertake h rte romayn sore knyghthode pro wesse auaunteth courage lyche lyon rage fro whome al bestes fbe suche knyght degre armed felde ther durst none abyde shelde grete pryce vpon werres whiche al chaunce lad fortune shope march thassent bothe two soldan calyphe eke batayll vpon day seke whiche suche awey set lenger shold let made hem strong euery syde drough toward tyde bataylle shold soldan grete prynete goldryng doughter toke made hyr swere vpon book eke vpon goddes alle yf fortune byfalle bataylle dye shal thylk man obeye take hym housbonde whiche thylk ryng honde hyr shold brynge deth hath swore forth geth al power lond vnto march fond enemy ful enbataylled soldan hath feld assaylled ben hardy sone assemblen wherof dredeful hertes tremblen one sleeth sterueth abouen pryce deserueth knyght romayn rode dedely swerd man abode ayene defence egypt fled presence perse vpon chace pursuen grace byfelle arowe oute bowe al sodenly ylke throwe soldan smote lay chaas left thylke day bore tent souldan syghe went sholde algate dy knyaht romanye hym tryst doughter rynge anone twyst took hym told hym al ca vpon othe token shold ben wyf sayd hertes lyf souldan departed sone therupon done dede body wel fayre carye tyl come kayre worthelyche bygraue lordes whiche wolden saue regne whiche desolate brynge good estate parlement set anone herkne fel therupon yong lord worthy knyght rome vpon nyght morowe trete shold vnto bachyler told counseyll ryng lle sheweth thurgh whiche yt shall seyth kynges doughter wedde soo rynge leyd wedde told hyr fadre honde man fonde shold ym toke vnto lord thus seyth stant record man wote hath ring bachyler vpon thyng ere entent l yde thought seyde feyneth fals vysage glad courage another wyse old philosophr wyse wryten vpon thylk whyle may best man begyle whome man hath credence byfelle euydence toward yong lord rome bachyler whiche nome lord nyght slepte ryng whiche mayster kepte oute purs awere dede put another stede morow court set yong lady forth fet whome lordes done homage maryage treten axen wylle whiche thought fulfylle fadre hest mater sayd openly men may charge whiche hyr fadre bad tho lord rome glad droughe toward purs anone al nought gone bachyler hath forth drawe axeth therupon lawe hym hold couenaunt tokne suffysaunt myght forsake netheles lord hath take quarelle ayene owne man thynge euer myght nought herd clayme vnansuerd hath purpos fayled bachiler soo counsayled wedded thylk empyre crouned lord syre al lond hym hath receyued wherof lord whiche deceyued sekenes thyrd morowe conceyued hath dedely sorowe lay vppon deth ther whyle hym lasteth speche breth sende worthyest al londe eke best told hem al soth tho sone heyre also themperour grete rome gyder come knyght ryght told hem al pleyne ca counseyll tolde al wolde hath fayled mede good taketh none hede sayth loue whiche wende haue aboue therupon letter wryte doth fadre wyte al mater stood bertely mood vnto lordes besought telle lady bought hyr loue whiche another gladeth aud word hewe fadeth sayd dieu lady swete lyf hath lost kyndely hete lay dede ony stone wherof sory many one none al fals knyght degre arested put hold openly told treson whiche falle thorugh oute lond sayden alle soth men suppose owne vntrouth hym shal depose seche euydence honour grete reuerence wherof myghten knowe ende themperour anone sende letter whiche sone wrote soth wote telle sorow endeles yet hast netheles vpon tale whiche herde styward perse ferde worthy romayns eke lyege traytor seke thyder come knyght hym hath confessid falsely hath hym bore wherof worthy lord lore tho sayden som shold deye yet haue fouden suche weye shal dede perse thus skyles dyuerse cause coroned lond habandoned hym al though werr vnryght peyne hym dyght poynt ende grauten wel yt shal wende romayns rome ageyne thus acorded ful playne quyk body dede leue take forth lede supplaunt hath iuyse wherof thou myght auyse vpon informacyon touchend supplantacion thou sone take hede also supplaut doth halue man fynde salue pleynly hele suche sore hath shal euermore pryde enuye ioynt suffreth man good poynt may honoure let therupon yf shal set ensample holy chirche fynde supplaunt behynde god wote yf crony que tyme go fynde tale concordable supplaunt whiche fable maner shal telle whylome thynges felle ponit confessor exemplum contra istos causa dignitatis adquirende supplantatores et narrat qualiter papa bonefacius predecessore suu celestinu papatu contractata circumuencione fraudulenter supplantauit sed qui potentes sede deponit hu iusmodi supplatacom fraudem non sus tinens ipsum sic sublime exaltatum postea profundi carceris miseriam proici fame que siti cruciari nec ab hu ius vite gaudijs dolorosa morte supplantari permisit rome hath ofte falle vyker generall alle hem yt lyeuen cristes feyth ists al whiche none seyth hath shett worldes eye who name yf shal specyfye hyght pope nycholas thus passed cardynals wold saue forme lawe conclaue gone chese newe pope couthe agrope hath eche hem sayd entent tyl last assent vpon holy good recluse whiche ful gostely vertuse pacyence symplesse hath set hym hyghe noblesse thus pope canonysed grete honour intronyced vpon channce falle name celestyn men calle whiche notyfyed bulle holy chirche fulle al londes magnyfyed euery worship enuyed thylk tyme sen pope whome mene chose set syde cardynal thylk tyde whiche papate hath long desyred therupon gretely hath conspyred syghe fortune fayled whiche long tyme trauayled ylke fyre whiche ethna breneth thorugh woful hert renneth whiche resembled enuye wherof supplaunt trecherye engendred netheles feyneth loue feyneth pe outward doth reuerence al within conseyence thorugh fals ymagynacyon thought supplantacyon therupon wonder wyle wrought thylke whyle fel lygnage clergyon yonge age whome chamber affaited cardynal tyme hath waited wordes sly queynt whiche couth lyghtely peynt shope clerk whiche telle toward pope duelle within chambre nyght lay preuy wyght toward pope nyghtes tyde may man flee shal tyde cardynal whiche thought gyle vpon day whan whyle yong clerk hym took made hym swere vpon book told hym wylle forth al trompe bra hath hym take bad hym shal saye tyme awayte take ryght good kepe pope fast slepe none man ny thou sly thorugh oute trompe ere fro heuen though voys sowne suche prolacyon medytacyon therof may make vnderstonde though goddes sonde wyse thou shalt sex thylk estate awey pope whiche stant honoured shal soule socoured thylk worship last heuen whiche shal euer last clerk hath herd forme ho pope shold enforme toke cardynal leue goth hym home tyl eue pryuely trompe hedde tyl pope bedde mydnyght knew pope slepte blew within trompe thurgh yt wal told maner shal papacye leue take fyrst estate thus awake holy pope hath made thryes wherof dyuers fantasyes vpon grete holynesse within hert gan impresse pope ful innocence conceyueth conscyence goddes wyl cese wyse may relese hye estate wote nought thus within hym self thouyt stylle memorye tyl cam consistorye presence hem alle axeth yf byfalle ony pope chefe sholde lawe suffre wolde seten al stylle herde none whiche poynt ansuerde purpoos ment man knewe entent whiche shope gyle cardyual whyle al openly wo de pleyne seyth yf pope wol ordeyne suche lawe wrought myght chese elles nought sayd done pope anone vpon ca papal auctoryte hath made youe decre lawe confermed due forme al affermed innocent whiche deceyued papacye anone hath weyued reuounced resygned eke thyng seke vndernethe suche iape hath hym self shape hou euer hym seme myter dyademe hath thorugh supplantacyon confyrmacyon vpon fortune grace name cleped boneface vnder vyser enuye lo hyd trecherye whiche hath begyled many one suche counseyll ther may non whiche treson conspyred ny lyke spark fyred vp roofe whiche throwe lyeth hyd tyl whan yt wyndes blowe blaseth oute euery syde boneface whiche hyde trecherye supplaunt hath openly made auannt papacye hath wonne thyng wrong gonne may neuer stonde wel ende pryde shal bowe bende sheteth ful ofte oute weye thus pope whome seye stode hyghe whele suffre hym self wele enuye whiche loueles pryde whiche lawebes suche tempestes made hym erre charyte goth herre vpon mysgouernaunce agaynst lowys kyng fraunce toke quarel oultrage sayd shold done homage vnto chirche bodely wyst thyng shold doo grete seruyce world suche wyse withstood wrong demaud nought pope may commaund kyng wol pope obeye pope tho al weye may worche vyolence hath sent bulle sentence cursyng enterdyt kyng vpon wrongful plyyt kepe regne fro seruage counseyled baronage myght shal withstode thus cause take honde sayden papacye honoure magnyfye al euer spyrytual pryde temporal boneface persone ayene ylke wrong allone wolden stonde debate thus man nought state frensshe shopen myght greue fel ther knyght syre gwilliam de langaret whiche vpon cause set therupon took route men armes rood oute long awayte laye aspyede vpon daye pope auynyon sholde ryde oute toun vnto ponniforge whiche castel prouynce vpon weye rood knyght whiche houed abood embuysshed vpon horsbak al sodenlyche vpon hym brak hath hym brydel sesed sayde thou whiche hast dysesed courte fraunce thy wrong thou shalt synge another song thyn enterdyte thy sentence ayene thyn owne conseyence afcer thou shalt fele grope pleyne nought ageyne pope thylk name honourable thou whiche hast deceyuable trecherours al thy werke thou boneface thou proude clerke mysl der papacye thy fals body shal abye suffre hath deserued lo thus supplatour serued hym lad fraunce setcen hym penaunce within toure hard bondes honger hondes ece dyed god wote whome wrytyng yet regystred man maye whiche speketh sayth manere thy entre lyke foxe slyghe thy regne also pryde hyghe lyche lyon rage last thy passage thy deth houndes lyke suche letter cronyke proclamed court rome wherof wyse ensample nome yet ferforth dare rede af men beware loke wel algate none owne estate translate holy chirche degre fraude ne subtylyte thylk aaron honour took shal none receyue seyth book becleped shal thynken ca day whiche may reson bothe nature helpe euery man cure kepe symon fro folde nota de prophecia ioachim quanti meranarij sunt ouile dei tuas aures mei narracionibus fedare nolo ioachym thylk abbot tolde suche dayes sholden falle comonlyche place alle chapman suche mercery fraude supplantary many sholden bye selle ne may shame teste foule synne man god forbede oure dayes seyth yf clerk ware feyth chapmanhode suche feyre remenaunt mote nedes empeyre al world bylongeth whan holy chirche wrongeth thyng shal netheles mannes owne eye enuye preferred hath conscyence dyfferred man loketh vyce whiche modre malyce thylk fals enuye whiche causeth many trecherye may another see gracious shal stonden myght yf hynder suche wyght wel nyghe oueral vyce general qualiter ioab princeps milicie dauid inuidie causa abner subdole inter fecit et qualit achitofell ab hoc qd cusy consilio absolon preferebatur attenso inuidia laqueo se suspedit enuye thylk vnhap drough ioab deceypt slough abnet drede shold kyng dauyd suche ennye also felle thylk fals achitofelle counseylle ach ued sawe cusy byleued absolon hym forsake henge hym self vpon stake senec wytnesseth openly enuye propyrly court comon wenche halt tauerne shence drynke whiche maketh hert brene doth wytt rene euery wey compasse myght al passe whiche thorugh vnkyndeshyp enuyeth euery falauship thou myght wel knowe see vyce suche fyrst toward god abhomynable mankynde vuprofytable ben worth fewe shal reson proue shewe inuidie stumilus sine causa ledit abortus nam sine temptante crimine crimen habet non est huius opus tempture cupdinis archum dum que facies veneris ethnica flamina vorat ab que rubore gene palles quies fustus obu brat frigida nature c mebra docet hic describit confessor naturain inuidie tam amore quam aliter secundum proprietatem vicij enuye yf shal deseryue shapely wyue erthe among woman hym matere wherof myght plesaunce fyrst heuy contenaunce semeth euer vnglad able eke brenneth withynne kynde may proufyte wynne wherof shold loue please thylk blode shold haue ease regne among moyst veynes drye thylk vnkyndely peynes thorugh whiche enuye fyred ay thus reson proue may toward loue enuye nought wyse yf besought vpon syde euer falle werst vyce alle whiche hym self hath malyce vnderstonde euery vyce som cause hath wherof groweth enuye man knoweth fro whens cam oute helle thus wyse clerkes telle spyryt malyce wey kynde vyce tempted suche waye enuye hath kynde put waye malyce hath sturyng wherof maketh bakbytyng hym self therof dyseased may ther kynde pleased ay enuyeth ayene hym self plenyeth thus stant enuyt good espeyr ben hym self deuels heyr whiche next lyche forthest heuen ryche may neuer wone thy good dere sone thou wold fynde syker weye lone put enuye aweye myn holy fadre reson wolde vyce esche shold yet strengthe courage ye wold auauntage therof set recouere grete desyre vyce myght flee vnderstonde sone see physyk seke vertues vyces eke vyces wold esche mote reson sewe vertues thylk weye may vyces done aweye gydre maye duelle water welle fyre abateth malyce ryght vertu fordoth vyce ayene enuye charyte whiche modre pyte maketh man hert tendre may malyce engendre hym incline therin courage tempred though myght hym self releue yet wold another greue rather plesaunce bereth hym self greuaunce fayne wold another case wherof sone thyn ease ne tale whiche rede vnderstond wel rede hic ponit confossor exemplum de virtute cartatis centrum inuidi et narrat de constantino e lene filio suo qiu cum imperij romani dig nitatem obtinuerat morbo lepre fectus medici pro sanitate recuperanda ipsum sanguine puerorum moseulorum balneare prepe suerant sed cum numera multitudo matrum cum filijs huiusmodi medicine causa circuitu palacij affuisset imperator que corum gemitus clamores percepisset caritate motus ingemiscens sic agit vere ipse est dominus qui se facit seruum pietatis et dictis statum suum cuncti potentis medele commuttens sui ipsi morbum pocius quam infancium mor tem benignus elegit vnde ipse quo pagan lepresus extiterat ex vnda baptismatis renat vtrins que materie ta corporis que anime diuine miraculo consecutus est salutem imong bokes latyn fynde wryte costatyn worthy emperour rome suche infortunes hym come lusty age lepre caught vysage forth ouer al aboute myght ryden oute left shelde spere myght hym bestere holde hym chambre close thorugh al world fame arose grete clerkes ben assent come commaaundement trete vpon lordes hele long geder dele vpon medycyne appoynten hem determyne maner stood wold hym bathe childes blode within seuen yere age sayen shold suage lepre al vyolence whiche knewe accidence wey kynde falle therto acorden alle fynal conclusyon tolden oppynyon themperour anone counseyl toke therupone letter seales oute send euery lond aboute yong child seche whoos blood sayd shold leche themperours maladye ynough wepe crye among modres herd wofully cause ferd netheles mote bowe thus woman ther come ynowe child soukend theyr tete many teres lete hem lyef hem lothe woman child bothe paleys forth brought many sory hertes thought hem whiche body bore child forlore within whyle shold see modres wepe degre many hem swoune falle yong babyes cryeden alle noyse arose lord herde loked oute ferde sawe sayd abrayd oute slepe thus sayd thou dyuyne purueaunce whiche euery man balaunce kynde hast formed lyche pore bore ryche dyeth wyse vpon fool vpon wyse seken esse hele enter comune may eschewe fortune whiche kynde hath lawe sett strengthe beaute ben set euery man lyche fre profereth degre dysposycyon bodely complexyon eke soule resonable pore child bore able vertu kynges sone euery man owne wone luste assaye vyce vertue chefe maye thus stand al men fraunchysed estate deuysed somme worshyp rychesse pouerte dystresse one lordeth another serueth yet euery man deserueth world yeueth yeftes certes hath grete matere good condycyon whiche hath subiectyon men ben semblaunce eke toke remembraunce made lawe kynde wolde euery man lawe bynde bad man suche wold toward hym self ryght suche shold toward another done also thus worthy lord al tho set balaunce owne estate hym self stood debate thought good see mochel man blood spylt cause hym alone sawe also grete mone moders vnglade wo childre made wherof hert tendreth suche pyte within engendreth hym leuer chese owne body lese see grete mordre wrought vpon blood gylteth nought thus pyte whiche toke al lech forsoke put hym oute auenture al goddes cure sayth wol mayster mote seruaunt pyte ferforth ouercome charyte hath nome counseyll offycers bad vnto tresorers tresour al aboute departe among pouer route wymmen chyldren bothe wherof myght hem fede clothe sothly borne home ageyne withoute losse ony greyne thorugh charyte thus dyspendeth good wherof amendeth pouer peple countreuayleth harme hem trauayleth thus woful nyghtes sorow ioye torned morowe al thankyng al blyssyng whiche erst wepyng cursyng woman gone home glad ynough echone ioye lough preyd lordes hele whiche hath relesed quarele hath owne wyl forsake charyte goddes sake thou shalt god hath wrouyt matere doth al equyte hym wrought charyte ayeneward charytous pyte pytous neuer knowe yet charyte geth vnaquit nyght leyd slepe hyghe god wold hym kepe seynt peter seynt poule hym sende whome wold lepre amende two hym slepend appere fro god sayd manere constantyn thou hast serued pyte thou hast pyte deserued thy thou shalt suche pyte haue god thorugh pyte wol sane thou shalt double hele fynde fyrst bodelyche kynde nd thy woful soule also thou shalt hole two thou shalt despeyre thy lepre shal empeyre tyl thou wylt sende therupon vnto mount celyon syluestre clergye gyder duellen companye drede whiche many day hast ben foo crystes lay hast destroyed mochel shame prechours holy name thou hast somdele appesed thy god good dede plesed thou thy pyte hast bywaryd vpon blood whiche yu hast spared thy thy saluacyon thou shalt haue informacyon suche syluestre shal teche nedeth none leche emperour whiche al herd graunt mercy lord ansuerd wol ye say one thyng wold pray shal telle vnto syluestre youre name estre hym told hyght forth al oute offhis syght passen vp heuen awoke oute sweuen clepeth men come anone told dreme therupone suche wyse hem telleth mount syluestre duelleth haue hast sought foude hem brouyt themperour whiche told sweuen elles wold siluestre hath herd ye king ryght ioyeful thyng hym bygan al wyt techen vpon holy wryt fyrst mankynde ore hyghegod therfore sone send aboue whiche born mannes loue owne choys toke deth vpon croys graue byloke hath helle broke toke hem yt lyeue make v ful byloue veray goddes sone ayene kynde mannes wone fro deth rose thyrd day wold wel may styghe vp fadres euene flesshe blood heuene ryght forme flesshe blood shal reforme tyme cometh quyk dede thylk woful day drede euery man shal take dome well mayster groome myghty kynges retenue day maye stonde value worldly strengthe defende euery man mote entende stonde vpon owne dedes leue mennes nedes day may counseyl auayle pledour ple shal fayle sentence ylke daye maye none appele set delaye may gold iuge plye ne shal soth trye fetten euery man vp ryght wel plow man knyght leud man grete clerk shal stonde vpon owne werk suche fonnde tho suche shal euermo may peyue relesed may ioye encresed endeles haue shal receyue one two thus syluester sawe ground al newe lawe grete deuocyon precheth fro poynt poynt techeth vnto emperour sayth hyghe creatour hath vnder fonge charyte wrought suche pyte child honde thus lord hath vnderstode al thyng ferde vnto syluestre ansuerde al hool hert seyth redy feyth vessel whiche blood made syluestre stood clene water welle al hast lete felle set constantyn therynne al naked vp chynne whyle begonne lyght though sonne fro heuen place come took crystendome euer among holy tale lyke fysshes scale fellen hym efte tyl ther thyng lefte al grete maladye wold hym puryfye hyghe god hath made hym clene left thyng sene hath hym cleused two body soule also tho knewe emperour dede crystes feyth drede sende anone lettres oute lete cryen al aboute vpon peyne deth weyue baptysme ne receyue moder quene eleyne send bytwene hem tweyne treten cyte al crystned forth al emperour whiche hele hath foud within rome anone lete found two chirches whiche dyd make peter poule sake whome vysyon yaf therto possession lordship worldly good wylle good toward pope franchyse yet hath proued wyse see worchyng dede crony que thus rede anone hath made yefte voys herd hyghe lefte whiche al rome adrad sayd day venym shad holy chirche temporal whiche medleth spyrytal stant degre yet may man soth see god maye amende wylle therto none skylle go ther bygan charyte may helpe man bothe worldes haue sayd yf thou haue ere layd sone thou myght vnderstonde charyte take honde foloweth mochel grace thy yf thou wolt purchace thou enuye fle acqueynte charyte whiche vertu souerayne fadre shal peyne e sample whiche ye told al myn hert haue withold shal euermore liber tercius ira suis paribus est par fu rijs acherontis quo furo ad tempus nil pi tati habet ira melacolicos ani mo perturbat vt equo ure sui pondus nulla statera tenet omnibus causis grauat ira inter amantes illa magi facili sorte grauamen agit esi vbi vir discors leuiter que repugnat amori sepe loco ludi fletus ad os venit hic ercio libro tractat super quin que speciebus ire quarum prima melancoli dicitur cuius confessor primo describens amanti super eodem consequenter opponit thou vyces lest knowe sone hath vnknowe fro fyrste men theyr swerdes groude ther none vpon ye groude vyce foreyn fro ye lawe wherof many good felawe hath dystraught sodeyn chau yet kynde plesaunce doth acheueth pur o kynde greueth whiche outr conscyence enemy vnto pacyence name one seuene whiche ofte hath set world vneuent cleped cruel ire whoos herte euermore fyre speke amys bothe seruauntes ben euer wrothe good fadre telle thyng ire sone oure englysshe wrath hote whiche hath wordes ay hote al man pacyence fyred vyolence hym hath euer fyue seruauntes helpen hym seryue fyrst hem melancolye cleped whiche companye honderd tymes oure wol angry best loure man wote cause sone shryue thy hast thou malencolyen fadre ye seynt iulyen vntrewe wordes vse may therof excuse al maketh loue wel wote whiche myn hert euer hote brenne doth glede wrath may spede thus ful ofte day nought sauf onlyche myn owne thought seluen wrothe game gothe men glade wel vnglade men game torneth pure grame thus self oppressed thought whiche haue impressed al wakyng dreme mete hyr alone mete prayd hyr som good ansuere wol gladly swere seyth nay withouten oth thus waxe within wroth outward al affrayed dystempered e ayed thousand tymes day sowneth myn eres nay whiche sayd fore thus wyttes forlore namely whan begynne rekne self within many yeres ben agone syth haue truly loued one neuer took hyr hede euer lyche spede fole hyr dele hap al hele thynketh ay lenger ferre bringeth gladship erre wherof wyttes ben empryred sayth al dispeyred fynally muse thynk wol refuse anger bestad al world myght glad lasteth al vp doune ioye casteth forther ne may lady se redy wrathe fo touchyng lathe tornyng sere wode doth wylde see melancolyous ther ny seruaunt myn hous ne none tho aboute eche hem ne stant doute wene wold raue anger see haue wondre lasse seen ouerpasse fadre yf betyde approche ony tyde place lady hyr lyketh wy speke goodly word vntome al gold rome ne couth wroth al myn anger ouer goth glad presence hyr al offence foryete though nought ouer glad thought netheles soth telle ene word yf soo byfelle thylk tyme syghe myscast hyr eye lyst nought loke therof good hede toke anone fyrst estate torne also mate euer asyche wycke thus myn hond ayen prycke hurte haue many day go forth goo may fulofte bytyng lyppe make vnto self whyppe whiche many chele woful hert bete al wyttes ben vnsofte wroth ofte al melancolye whiche groweth fantasye loue wol loute bere forth angry sno wte ful many tymes yere fadre ye sytten loues stede yow byseche som ensample ye teche wherof may self appese confessor sone thyn hertes ese shal fulfylle thy prayer thou myght better ler meschyef vyce stereth whiche angre forbereth wherof hym thynketh sobre hym thynketh vpon foly dede poynt tale rede hic ponit confessor exemplum co tra istos qcu vires amoris sut realiter experti contra al o amantes malen ol ueritate ad iracundiam vindicte prouocantur et narrat qualiter rex eolus filium nomine marcharium filiam nomine habuit qui cum ab infanci que pubertatem inui cem fuerant educati cnpi cum ignito iaculo amborum cordis desideria amo rose penetrauit que natura canacis cooperan fratre suo inpregnata parturit super quo pater intollerabilem uentutis concupiscenci ignorans ni miam que furoris malencolia preuent dictam filiam cum partu dolorosissimo c su interfeci diiudicauit kyng whiche eolus hote befel hym thus two child fayre sone cheped machayre doughter canace hyght day este nyght whyle yong comon wone chambre geder come shold pleyd hem ofte tyl growen vp alofte yongthe lusty age kynde assaylleth courage loue doth hym lowe reson allowe halt lawes nature whome loue hath vnder c blynd hym self ryghtso maketh lyent blynde also suche maner yow telle al day geder duelle broder myght asterte al hoole herte loue vpon suster cast soo fel hem last machayre canace preuy place cupyde bad hem fyrst rysse whiche maystrysse kynde techeth euery lyf withoute lawe posytyf whiche taketh maner charge kepeth lawes al large nature took hem lore taught hem soo ouermore hath hem suche wyse da saith enchau ed blynde another ledeth tyll falle nothynge dredeth ryght none insyght byrd whiche wol lyght seeth mete net e whiche deceyt hym set yong folk perylle syghe lykyng eye felle vpon chaunce wyt hath lore remembrauce long geder assemble wobe o gan tremble held hyr hir chambre cloos drede shold discloos come vnto hyr fadre ere wherof sone also fere feynend cause ryde long durst abyde aun et yf men wol seyn suster hath forleyn yet knowe who child thylke throwe machayre goth canace abyt whiche delynerd yet ryght sone lest herkne woful ca soth whiche may ben hyd last knowe kyd vnto kyng stood vnderstood anone melenoolye though frenesye felle whiche thyng couthe mayster ful loue yougthe loue straunge wold herte chaunge benigne fauourable loue vnmerciable bytwene wawe wode wroth doughter chambre goth sawe child late bore wherof hath oth swore shal ful sore abye bygan mercy crye vpon hyr bar kn prayde hyr fadre thus sayde haue mercy fadre thenke thy child thy blode cam mysdede yongthe made flodes bad wade sawe peryl tho hath byfalle mercy fadre wreche wtth yt word lost hyr speche felle swounend fote sorowe nedes mote horryble cruelte myght attempre py oute chambre forth went fnl wrath entent took counseyl herte shal deth asterte whiche melan lyen pacyence hath lyen wherof may wrath restreyne wylde wode peyne al reson vntame knyght leped name toke hym wey sonde naked swerd bere honde sayd hym shold go telle vnto doughter manere hym bad sharp swerdes blad receyue shold al wo shal forth message goth knyght vnto woful yong wyght sharp swerde hyr e took wherof al bodye al ad done dede herd euer synge rede suche thyng tho done whiche lad wrath ne hath knowe loue lyte al wyte thorugh sodeyn melanoolye grete felonye thy sone stond caas thou myght vnderston yf thou euer cause loue shal dem thou aboue thou myght lede thy wylle lete neuer thorugh thy wrath spylle whiche enery kynde shold saue syt euery man haue reward loue myght ayenst who streugthe may wyght syth heth ayen ful oftyme hath e seyne hath byfalle grete vengeaunce wherof fynde remembraunce h ic narrat qualiter tiresias quodam mote duo serpentes uenit parite commiscentes quos cum virga percussit ati dij ob hoc quam naturam imped uit ipsum contra naturam forma virili muliebrem transm tarunt ovyde tyme tho tolde ensample sayd soo whilom tiresias walkend goth par ca vpon hyghe mounteyn syghe two serpentes weye nyghe nature hem taught assembled tho caught yerde whiche bare honde thought wold fonde letten hem smote hem bothe wherof goddes wrothe hath dystourbed kynde nature vnkynde vnkyndelyche transformed whiche erst formed woman shape hym angry iape angyr wrought hys angyr angerlyche bought lo thus sone ouyde hath wryte wherof thou myght reson wyte man suche best myght neuer ben honest man wrathen hym sore another doth lore kynde whiche maly vy though man resonable yet kynde uable loue wol none thynke thou sone therupone melanoolye aweye loue hath lust pleye whiche wold lyf greue amans f dre may wel byleue ye telle skylle lete euery man loue wylle lady shal wroth ther wrath fare amys alone vpon self bothe loue kynde soo bestad fynde wey may asterte whiche stant vpon myn owne hert thyng couth telle spryngeth vp deth welle whiche may stumes hide renneth ou euery syde boylen vp foule sawes chest wote felawes syue kepeth ale ryght chest kepe tale al wote wol dy lose speke ony man oppose cyte withoute walle men may go oute oueralle withoute ony resystence croked eloquence speketh al wote withynne wherof men lese wynne oftyme chydyng bryngeth hous suche tydyng maketh werre beddes hede leueyn brede whiche soureth al past aboute men ought wel suche oue doute euer bo redy bent whome hyt telle hym shent maye perce hym tonge e e loude belle ronge noyse soune men feren al towne wel done thonder cause wondre ye wyndes bloweth ful syth ouerthroweth cytees polycye baue herd peple crye echone sayd degre ha wykked tonge woo men sayn hard bone al though hym self haue none tonge breketh al pyeces hath many sondry spy vyces may wel desc yue hem thousand dele cheste falleth ful many wondre thyng byfalleth ne thyng forbere lle sone thyn ansuere hath euer yd thou ony tyme hast chyd tothard thy loue fader naye suche chest yet vnto daye ne made neuer god forbede er syng suche crede le er lewed al beshrewed worthy put bak al sorowe vpon bak ony man ordeyne couthe spak neuer yet mouthe vnto chest myght touche durst ryght wel vouche vpon hyr self wytnes wote hyr gentylnes wold wel excuse suche thynges vse yf shold betyde algates must chyde myght loue yet neuer aboue al wyde world wynne durst ony word begynne myght haue amoued cheste also reproued rather yf myght hyr lyke best wordes wold pyke whiche couthe myn hert chese serue hem forth stede chose helpelyche defye wold wordes plye myght wrath chest auale tellyng softe tale thus dar make forward neuer vnto lady ward yet spak word suche wyse wherof chest sh ld aryse thuo say ful ofte n haue spak softe parcas sayd ynough wel halt man plough ne balketh whyle n wel man affyle tonge somtyme ia hym may som lyght word ouerscape yet ne meneth ch ste haue ay hyr hest ful ofte spoke byknowe hou wylle ye knowe tyme cometh aboute dar speke say al oute long loue whiche wote neuer one alyche hote greueth al dysese telle though er dysplese speke forth nought ne leue though bebesyde hyr leue hope trowe netheles ayene pee though telle hyr al thouyt wote wel chyde nought men maye hyghe god byseche wol man speche wroth seyth yeueth seyth maketh hardy th sey dar wel better lady whiche woman though telle seluen haue chid man couthe better chyde ben euery tyde selue allone forthan made preuy mon euery tale whiche spake lady thenke p yse balaunce drawe remembraunce yf fynde lak ony word myspak whiche moche ony wyse anone wyttes despyse maste chydyng myn herte ony word shold asterte whiche shold haue holden ynne begynne yf ther elles ought speke spak nought yf may seche fynde ony word l behynde whiche shold haue spoke wold vpon self wroke chyde self al wyt ouer goo noo man maye tyme lor recouer thus therfore ouer wroth thouyht self chyde al nought thus moche lyte ful ofte self wyte al may auayle cheste though trauayle oule stok stok oule tho man defoule men wote wel whiche hath werse ny worth erse torneth vnto myn wne heede though telle deede wold euer chyde suche wyfe loue yow deuyse fadre ye haue al herd manere haue ferd cheste dyssencyon yeue absolucyon confessor sone yf thou wystest al cheste doth specyal loue welwyllyng thou woldest fleen knowlechyng speke fayre lerne thou falle cheste whiche soure grete dystasice taste thy remembraunce thou myght ge e pacyence whiche seche al offence tellen v old wyse nought elles may suffyse strengthe ne man wyt pacyence ouer syt ouer cometh laste maye nen long sast whiche wol bowe brek take hede sone speke fadre goodly speche wytte whiche ye teche thanke yow al myn hole hert world shal neuer astert ne shal wordes holde pacyence ye tolde ferforth myn hert thynketh wrath forthynketh fadre yf ye forth al somme good ensample specyal wolden telle som c nyste shold wel myn hert lyke pacyence myght matere vnto loue obeye putten dysese aweye ic ponit confessor exemplum de paciencia amore contra tem habenda et narrat qualiter vxor socratis ipsum quodam die multis sermonibus tigauit sed cum ipse ab lla responsione omnia probra pacienter sustulit indignat vxor qmdam ydriam plenam aque quam manu tenebat super caput viri sui subito effudit dicens e gila loquere qui respondens tune ait bere iam scio expertus sum quam post ventorum rabiem sequuntur vmbres et isto modo litis contumeliam sua paciencia deuicit sone man bye hym pee behoueth suffre socrates ensample left whiche wryte thou shalt soth wy e ensample mene al though lytel sene among men thylk euydence yet vpon pacyence set hym self assay thyng whiche myyt hym moste myspay desyred wykked wyf wedded whiche sorowe stry agaynst easee contrayre spak euer softe fayre tyl byfelle tolde wynter day colde wyf fro welle come pot water nome hath ought howse sawe hat sely spouse set loked book nygh fyre whiche ease man age bygan wood ge axeth deuel thoug bare wey kynde whiche stormy men may fynde fyrst maketh wyndes blow within throwe tryneth water gate ondoth thus wyf algates whiche reson wel beseyn hath made wynde wyn season yere set hym ner fyre myght iugement name bere pacyent yeue ensample good pacyence stood men myght knowe sone yf thou ony throwe tempted ayenst pacyence take hede vpon euydence shal par lesse greue fadre byleue shal maner nede wol take good hede er falle suche assay thynke esche yf may yf ther ought elles wherof myght take lore pray yow dare telle may beware somme tale matere sone euer good lere wherof thou myght thy word restreyne er thou falle ony peyne counseyl hyde may fayle wo besyde whiche shal byfalle wy fynde bokes wryte hic ponit confessor exemplum de alterius lite intromittere cauen du est et narrat qualiter iupiter cum iunone super quadam questi one litigabat videlicet vtrum vir mulier amous concupiscencia ferue cius ardebat super quo tiresiam eorum iudicem constituebant et quia ille contra iunonem dicte litis causa smay diffiniuit irata ipsorum amborum oculorum lumine claritatis ab que remis sione priuauit yet cam ther neuer good seryf seche al man lyf though begynne pure game ful ofte torneth grame doth greuaunce som syde wherof grete clerk ouyde lawe whiche tho iupyter iuno maketh bokes mencion felle dyssencyon maner boorde bygonne woorde among hem self pryuete vpon degre whiche two amorous man wyf vpon myght acorde one took iuge therupon whiche cleped tyresyas bad hym deme caas withoute auysement ayene iuno gaf iugement goddesse vpon ansuere wrothe wold forbere took wey euermo lyght eyen two iupiter hurt hath sene another benefete ther ayene yafe suche grace hym doth wyst sayd soth soth sayer euer yet leuer haue lokyng eye word prophecye soth ment strxfe cause hent grete peyne bodely sone thou ware ther hold thy ton stylle cloos hath word dyscloos wote mene ful ofte nyhe tene leseth ful many tyme grace wold thak purchace ouer sone dere men yf thou myght pryuyte haue wrouyt holde counseyle dyscouer nought cheste counseyl hele wo wele take tale thy mynde whiche old ensample fynde hic ponit confessor exemplum centrum illos qui amoris causa al u consilium reuelare presumunt et narrat qualiter quedam auis tunc albissima nomine coruus consilium mine sue cornide phebo denudauit onde contigit non solum ipsam cor dem interfeci sed et coruum qui tam quam albus fuit piceum colorem pro perpetuo transmutari pheb whiche maketh yt dayes lyght loue whiche tho hyyt cornide aboue hem alle pleseth shal befalle loue ther noma yt knoweth fortune hyr happes thro weth byfel vpon chaunce yong knyght acqueyntaunce wolde fals byrd whiche hath holde kept chambre pu youthe scoueryth al euer couthe byrdes name tho coruus whiche also wel whyte ony swan shrewe al lady phebus sayde wrath swerd oute braide whiche cornyde anone slough hym woo ynough took ful grete repentaunce wherof token remembraunce hem whiche vsed wycked speche vpon byrd toke wreche snowe whyte fore euer afterward cole black therfore transformed weth many man yet hym beshre weth clepen hym day rauen yet whome men may take euydence cryeth som myshap sygnyfyeth beware therfore say best thou wolt thy self rest good sone rede hic loquitur super eodem et nar rat qualiter laar nimpha de eo iupiter iuturnam adulterauit unoni iouis vxori secretnm reuelauit quapropter iupiter ira commotus lin gua laaris prius abscisa ipsam post profundum acherontis exulem perpetuo man pauit another place rede thylk nymphe whiche laar hyght pryuete nyght iupyter lay iuturne hath told god made yr ouertorne hyr tonge cut hyr helle euer send duelle worthy ben loue chamberere counseyl couthe hele suche dayes fele loues court seyd lete tonges gone vnteyd sone thou none tho li ngle telle tale soo namely thou ne chyde cheste counseyl hyde wrath said neuer wele fadre soth euery dele ye teche wol holde reule whiche holde flee chest ye byd wel hym neuer chyd telle forth yf ther touchyng vnto wrathes lore demoui est odium quasi scrib cui dabit ira teriam scripti cordis ad antrum sui non laxa amor odij que frena restringunt nec secreta sui iuris adire sciuit hic tractat confessor de tercia specie ire que odium dicitur
