suffceth within gate cam loue pe wol make reles debate whiche byfalle speke yf thou art one alle vyce hast witholde yet ought ye tolde fadre good feyth sone yi fadre nay ye leue lest sone thou shalt ha wrath shewend loug tyme gaderend duelleth hert loken tyl see tyme wroken sheweth tempest sodeyn wylde best whiche wote thyng mercy sone art thou knowen good fadee wene wote sonidele ye mene dare saufly make othe lady neuer loth wol swere netheles hate gylteles lady plye fro day day mercy crye mercy leyth shrote wordes seyth though lady loue algate tho wordes mote nedes hate wold al dyspent fer oute londe went hereafter shold hem yet loue lady dere thus hate ye may see bytwene lady word word hate hyr loue shal betyde loue forthermore wol shryue haue hated al lyue ianglers whiche enuye ben euer redy lye fals compassement ful often haue made shent hyndred ful oftyme canse wyste yme onlyche hyr owne thought thus ful ofte haue bought lye dranke wyn wold happe suche myn shryue ne may foryeue tyl see debate loue myn estate myghten owne deme loke wel shold hem queme hyndre man loueth sore thus hate hem euermore tyf loue hem wol wreche shal al cy byseche vnto myghty cupydo moche wolde doo loue god smy rod whiche loue smyten myght knowe wyten hyndryng woful peyne hym loue wold yn thus euer hem wayte hope tyl may seen hem lepe lope halten sore whiche euermore wold myght stonden lyght ne sholden haue aweye wolden put aweye wold hem put oute st de fro loue ryght dede spoke mouth wold yf uth hem god saue al hate haue toward ianglers euery dele wold al ferd wele thus haue fader sayd wylle saye forth stylle sone thou hast sayd hold nought fully payd thou wolt hat n ony man acorden ne though haue hyndred fore telle therfore thou myght vpon benyson wel haten condycyon tho ianglers thou toldest forthermore yf thou woldest hem hyndre ony wyse suche ha euer despyse thy sone wold rede thou drawe frendelyhede thou ne myght hate myght thou gete loue algate set sone rest thou shalt fynde best ouer dare thou ryght ware men ha aboute whiche euery wyse man shold doute hate euer vpon wayte fyssher bayte sleeth seeth fysshes fast seeth tyme last may worche woo shal man torne hym ther fro hate nyl felonye fulfylle feyne companye yet netheles fal semblaunt toward hym couenaunt witholde vnder bothe preuy wrath hym clothe shal seme grete byleue ware wel thou ne loue al thou seest afore thyn eye gregoys whylome syghe book troye de maye fyude ensample dede hic ponit confesso exemplum tra illos qui cum ire sue odiu ate vindicare non possint ficta dissimu acione vindictam subdole assequentur et narrat cum palamides princep grecorum obsidione troye quibus dam suis emulis proditorie interfect fuisset pater que suus rex namplus patria sua tun existens huiusmodi euentus certitudinem sci usset greco sui cordis odium super omnia r llegit vnde contigit cum greci deuicta troia per altum mare versus greciam nauigio remeantes obscurissimo noctis tempore nimia ventorum tempestate iac tabantur rex namplus terra sua contra litus mari vbi ioca saxoru minebant pericula super cacumina mo cium grandissimos noctanter fecit ignes quos greci aspicientes saluum po tum ibidem inuenire certissime putabant et terram approxim ntes diru nauibus magna par grecorum riclitabatur sone destructyon troye al bete doun slayn ye king gregoys whiche al thyng ben cause tornen home ageyn may man hop wythseyn hath ben seen felt ful ofte hard tyme softe see forth homeward went rage grete tempest hem hent iuno lete bende party bowe derk ye wynd gan blowe fyry welken bygan thonder though ye world shold al sonder heuen oute water gate reyny storme fel doune algates al tacle made vnwelde noman myght hym selfbyheld may men shipmen crye stood aunter dye behynde sat stere may sterne ship arose ageyne wawes lodesman hath lost lawes see bete euery syde nysten fortune abyde setten hem al goddes wylle wold hem self saue spylle thylk tyme felle thus kyng whiche namplus hote sone troye whiche gregoys ad made prynce alle tyl fortune lete hym falle name palamydes thorugh hate netheles somme hem deth caste treson ouer caste fadee herd telle swore yf euer tyme felle wold hym venge yf myght therto auowe hyght thus kyng thurgh preuy hate abode vpon wayte algate suche empryse auengyn hym open wyse fame goth wyde maketh knowe yt ye gregois home al felaushyp fro troye vpon see shyp namplus vnderstood knewe tydes flood sawe wynd blowe lond grete deceypt anone fonde preuy hate thou shalt wherof telle al matere kyng weder gan beholde wyst wel moten holde cours endelong marche ryght aud made vpon derk nyght grete shydes blokkes gre fyre ageyne grete rokkes shewe vpon hylles hyghe flete grece syghe fel ryght thought flete whiche hauen sought tho bryght fyres sawe ferre aud hem drawen ner nerre wyste wel vnderstood al fyre made good shewe men shold aryue thyderward hasten blyue semblaut men seyn gyle proued thylk whyle ship wed hym self accroche droof al pyeces roche deden ten twelue myght man helpe hym selue wenden deth escape withouten help deth shape thus comen fyrst fore vpon rokkes ben forlore thurgh noyse theyr cry al ware therby whan began rowe tho myght soth kuowe wende frendes fynde fonde frendship al behynde lond sone weyued hadden de eyued took hem hyghe see therto sayden alle ye fro day forth haue assayed sone wherof thou myght auyse fraude stant many wyse among hem gyle thynke ryueyne ynke whiche half fraude wryte stant suche maner man thy wyse men ne demen thynges semen knowe fynde myrrour sheweth kynde hath al word withynne sothe thyng withynne fareth hate throwe tyl man hath ouerthrowe shal man knowe chere whiche auaunt whiche ar thy sone thynke confessor fadre wol iwys yf wrathe axe charyte bokes knowe soth shal knowe hic cohiberr nequit manum sic spe ius naribus hic populo se timendus erit sepius luctum ven sua gaudia transf rt cum que suis mu talis amicus adest est amor pl xu non vti que alliciend fraudis impetuosa manus hic tractat confessor super quar q unta specie ire que impetu ositas homicidium dicuntur sed primo de impetuositate specialiter intendit ius natura spm naribus gestando ad omnes ire meciones vindicta parata paciencia nullatenus obseruat sone thou shalt vnderstonde yet ward wrath stonde dedely vyces two telle name conte homicide geder euery syde contake bokes seyn foolhast hath chamberleyn whoos counseyl al vnauysed pacyence despysed tyl homycyde hym mete fro mercy al vnmete thus worst alle hem whiche vnto wrath falle dede bothe eke thought acompten theyr wrath nouyt yf ther shedyng blood thus lyche best wode knowen good lyf haue swerd knyf hyr dedely wrath wreke pyte lyst hem speke none reason ne songe haue mygh stronge ware hym wel place euery man behoueth grace trowe shal hym fayle whome mercy myght auayle wron hten vpon tyrannye pyte myght hem plye telle sone fader thou hast culpable fadre nay cryst forbede speke dede whiche neuer culpable cause resonable matere shryfte sytten set shryue loue begonne fyrst aboue netheles beknowe touchend loues throwe whan wyttes ouer wende myn hertes contek hath none ende euer stant vpon debate grete dysese myn estate tyme lasteth fortune ouercasteth hyr whele straunge see wol chaunge cast al world aboute thynke home doute haue al tyme veyne fpended see amended rather empeyred wel nyhe despeyred ne may thank deserue euer loue euer serue euer lyche nere thus stonde suche sayth oute herre thus vpon self werre brynge put oute al pee fulofte rees wery myn owne lyf contek stryf byknowe haue ansuerd ye fadre haue herd myn hert wonderly begone whiche counseyl wherof wyt e one whiche hath reson companye agayn whiche stand partye wylle whiche hath hope acord thus bryngen vp dyscord wytte reson counseylen ofte myn herte shold softe shold wel renue put retenue lles holde hym vnder fote seyne yf mote owne reule haue vpon honde shal wytte vnderstonde hope tellen ouer al set hert champartye wysshyng fantasye tr seyth hym feyth thus reson wyt auysed wyt hope al day despysed reson sayth sholde leue loue leue spede wyll sayth ag yn suche hert vyleyn whiche dar leue tyl spede lat hope serue suche nede seyth eke hert syt al gouerned wyt hath lyues lust lore aud thus myn hert al suche con ck make yet may wel forsake ny mayster thought spede speke nought thou dost sone ageynst ryght loue grete myght lawe may noo man refuse myght thou better excuse netheles thou shalt lerned wyl shold gouerned reson kynde wherof tale wryte fynde hic ponit cosessoz exeplu ois impetuosa volutas sit discrecionis moderamine gubernanda et narrat qua ter dyogenes qui motus sui ammiracione subiugauerat regem alexandrum sub isto facto sibi opponente plenins informauit phylosopher whylome men told whylome dayes old dyogenes hyght old ne myght worldes trauayll best shope take rest duellyth home suche wyse nyhe hous lete deuyse endelong vp extre set tonne suche degre myght torne wherof ende taken therin sytte shold torne hym self wold take eyer see heuene deme planetes seuene whiche couthe moche thus ful ofte sat muse philosophye sool withoute companye vpon morow tyde thyng whiche shold betyde set hym lyst loke vpon sonne vpryst wherof propyrtees syghe felle cam rydynge nyghe kyng alysander route cast eye aboute sawe tonne ment wold wyte thyder sent knyght whome myght know hym self ylke throwe abode houeth ther stylle knyght kynges wylle spore made hors gone tonne cam anone fond man age hym told message suche ye kyng hym bede axeth within thylk stede tonne stood whiche vnderstood ca sat stylle spak word ageyne knyght bad speke sayd vyleyne thou shalt telle goo thy kyng axeth soo kyng quod vnryght sayd knyght thy man say nought quod bythought mannes man thou lyest fals chorl iwys knyyt hym said ryyt wroth kyng ayene goth told hym man ansuerd kyng tale herd bad shold alle abyde hym self wold thyder ryde cam fore tonne hath tale thus bygonne al heyl seyth man art thou quod suche one thou seest kynge whiche wordes wyse age wold despyse sayth fadre praye thou wolt cause saye thy man man syre kyng quod yf thou wylt yes seyth kyng quod soth thyng syth fyrst reason vnderstood knewe euyll good wyl whiche body moueth who werkes god reproueth haue restreyned euer hym stant vnder lore reson who subiect may amys thus weye couenaunt wyll man seruaunt euer hath euer shal wyl thy pryncipal lordship thy wyt thou couthest neuer yet take day rest thy laboure conqueroure worldes good whiche may last thou hyghest euer lyche fast thou reason hast wynne thus thy wylle cause synne thy lord whome thou seruest wherof thou lytel thank deseruest kyng yt thus ansuerd thyng wroth herd hyghe wordes whiche sayde gooodly wordes thus prayde hym wold telle name quod thylk whiche men dyogenes calle tho ye kyng ryght glad alle herd ofte fore man therfore sayde wyse dyogene shal thy grete wyt sene thou shalt yefte haue worldes good yu wolt craue quod houe sonne lete shyne tonne thou bynemest thylk yifte lyeth thy myyt shyfte none good nedeth kyng whome euery coutrey dredeth lo thus enformed wherof sone thou myght lere thy wylle shal beleued wyt releued thou hast sayd thy self thy wyl thy mayster thorugh whiche thyn hertes thought within euer contak begynne gretely drede homycyde brede loue wondre kynde hath wyttes ofte blynde fro mannes reason falle whan byfalle wylle shal courage lede loues cause drede wherof fynde ensample wryte whiche behouely wyte ic amoris causa ponit confes sor exemplum contra illos qui sua dampna nimis accelerantes ex impetuositate ipsos multocies offendut et narrat qualiter piramus cum ipse tisbe amicam suam loco inter eosde deputato tempore aduentus sui promptam non inuenit animo impetuoso se ip sum pre dolore extracto gladio mortaliter transfodit qui postea infra breue te pu veniens cum ipsum sic mortuum inuenisset eciam et illa sui ipsi mortem impetuose festinans eiusdem gladio cuspide sui cordis intima per mediu penetrauit rede tale telle thys cyte whiche semeramis enclosed hath walle aboute worthy folk many route inbabyted among whiche two ther abouen al noble grete duellyug tho within strete nyghe gedre sene thyng hem bytwene wow wow walle wal one lord hath specyal sone lusty bachyler al towne none pyer bad doughter eke al towne seke men wysten none fayre felle shold fayre doughter nye sone geder wone cupyde hath thynges shape ne myght hand escape fyre hem ne cast felle last folowe lore sewe whiche neuer man myghte eschewe loue shaped whiche hath hyr hertes ouerthraped alle weyes seche myght wynne speche woful peyne lysse loueth wel maye mysse namely ther two one accord goo yf som weye fynde loue euer suche kynde hath folk wel affayted awayted may man purpoos let thus bytwene hem twoo set hoole vpon wal make thorugh whiche haue hyr couseil take al tyme myght fayre mayde tysbe hyght whome loued hote piramus name hote long lesson recorden tyl laste acorden nyghtes tyme wende alone oute townes ende welle vnder tree cam fyrst shold stylle abyde felle nyghtes tyde mayde whiche desguysed al pryue soft paas goth thurugh ye large town vnknow tyl cam within throw lyked duelle thylk vnhappy fresshe welle whiche also forest nyghe cemyng lyon syghe felde take pray hast fleeth away fortune shold falle feer lete hyr wympyl falle nyhe wel vpon therbage wylde beest rage best whiche found ther oute hath slayn blody snowte hath eten wold drynke stremes cold come vnto welle fond wympel whiche oute hond falle hath drawe bled aboute al gnawe straught hym drynke vpon fresshe welles brynke oute playne torneth wode agayne tysbe durst remewe byrd whiche mewe whiche busshe kepte hyr close styl arose vnto self playneth ay fell whyle lay pyramus cam sone vnto welle mone fonde hyr wympyl blody neuer yet mannes ere tydyng ne mannes syght meruaylle whiche sore fryght man herte tho dede hym whiche stede many woful compleynyng bygan handes wryng whiche demeth sykerly dede sodeynly swerd al naked oute breyde fool hast thus seyde cause thy felonye reson dye dede cause word vpon kne felle goddes alle vnto heuene gan calle prayd syn done may loue tho haue world hyr grace myght haue place wold abyde sayth shal betyde pomel swerd ground set hert wound made vp hard hylte wyse hym self spylte fool hast deth nam within whyle cam laye dede vpon knyf woful yet neuer lyf tysbe hym syghe myght one word hygh speke hyr hert shette hyr lyf pry sette dede swownyng dede fel tyl afterward byfel oute hyr trauns awoke many woful pytous loke hyr eye alweye among caste vpon loue laste caught breth sayd thus thou whiche cleped art venus goddesse loue thou cupyde whiche loues cause haste guyde wote nowe wel ye blynde thylk vnhappe fynde bitwene loue piramus whiche se bledyng hath deserued thyn hest hath kept serued yonge bothe also allas ye v soo yet set hertes fyre made v suche thyng desyre wherof noo skyl couthe thus oure fresshe lusty youthe withoute ioye al dispended whiche thyng may neuer amended wol seye leuer deye haue sorowful day word lay hyr loue armes embraseth hyr owne deth purchaseth wepte kyst tyl laste wyst grete sorowe falle whiche ouergoth hyr wyttes alle whiche myght asterte swerdes poynt ayenst hyr herte set felle doune therupon wherof dede anone thus swerd bledende founde dede lyggende yt sone hast herd tale beware thyn owne bale thou cause thy foolhast kepe thou thy wyt ne cast vpon thy thought auenture wherof thy lyues forfeture maye falle yf thou haue thought telle thy tale hyde nought fad e vpon loues syde conscyence wol hyde loue pure wo haue ful ofte moued wysshes yf myght thousand tymes yow plyght storuen day therof shryue may though loue fully ne slow wyll deye ynow wyl culpable yf mercyable whiche may yeue lyf hele lyst dele wote who counseyl hym wold long tyme yet wold euer shal sleen destroye especyal gold nyne kynges londes ne shold hym saue fro myn hondes power yf yet hym stant fere nought yt euer couthe manace hynderer grace tyl dede may spede mote nede taken hede shape aweye therto may fynde weye sone telle thy whiche mortal enemy thou manacest dede fadre suche quede come fore aud doth cause lore name daunger whiche lady counseyler neuer yet slyghe come place nyghe nyght day daunger ne redy ay whome speche ne mede yet myght neuer loue spede euer fynde soth al lady sayth doth daunger shal make ende yt maketh al world myswede euer aske helpe may wel cleped sauns pyte ay hym bowe lesse wol tale allowe hath lady englewed wol remewed euer hongeth seyl soo preuy counseyl euer haue ought bede fynde daunger stede myn ansuere hym haue mercy craue mercy neuer poynt thus daunger fortune lad worse myght neuer thus bytwene daunger euer werre tyl dye myght suche maystrye daunger myght ouercome al ioye come thus wold fonde noo synne ne yet al world wynne myght fynde sleyght laye al state weyght wold hym countre deseuer come ayene ward neuer therfore wysshe wold fayn som wyse slayn whyle stant thyl place ne gete lady grace thus hate dedely thylk vyde wold stood none offyce place lady yf doo wol wel outher shal dye within whyle thy lady ful e muse may self exa se yf dye suche plyght thynketh myght quyt ne homycyde yf shold betyde god forbede shold double wey pyte al wyl wyt haue yeue euer serued yet shold suche wyse towardyng seruyse dede thynketh routhe ferthermore telle trouthe euer hath wel named worthy blamed reson appeled one word myyt heled man suffreth hym deye sawe euer suche weye sawe euer suche dystresse withoute pyte gentylnesse withoute mercy womanh de wol quyte man mede whiche hath euer loue trewe good fadre yf ye vpon tale telle wol stynte herkne yow sone attempre thy courage fro wrath lete thyn hert assuage wol hym vnderfonge may grace abyde longe loue receyued eke also yf weyued myght mochel thyng byfalle shold make man falle fro loue euer afterward ne durst soke thyderward hard weyes men gone softe er clymbe auyse ofte men seen al day rape reweth wykked ale breweth ful ofte mote werse drynk bettyr flede synke better vpon brydel chewe yf fel ouerthrewe hors stykked myre cast water fyre better brenne vp al hows man whiche malycyous foolhasty ful ofte falleth selden loue hym calleth thy better suffre throwe wylde ouer throwe suffraunce hath euer best wysen hym secheth rest thus yf thou wylt loue spede sone suffre rede may mous ayene ca thylk cause aske may loue make werre ne hath hym self werre loue axeth pe euer shalle fyghteth alle shal lest conquere empryse tellen ben wise wicke seryue haue werse hasten nought worth kerse thyng man maye acheue maye wel done eue mote abyde tyll morowe ne hast thyne owne soro sone take thy witte hath lost wel abitte ensample falleth thus thou myght wel take piramu hast swerd drough poynt hym self slough loue tysbe pytously hye wymple fond blody wende beste slayn hym ought ryght fayn sauf ryght besyde wold abyde meschyef felle thy ware sone warne dare thyng suche rees sufferaunce wel pee though thou loues court pursewe yet syt wel thou esche thou court ouerhas thou myght thy tyme wast yf thyne hap therto shape may helpe rape therfore attempte thy courage foolhast doth none auauntage yf sett man behynde cause loue fynde old ensamples thou shalt touchend loue hic ponit confessor exemplum contra illos qui amoris causa nimia festinacione concupiscentes tardius expediunt et narrat qualiter pro quam phebus qmdam virginem pulche trimam nomine da hnem nimi amoris acceleracione insequ batur ra tus cupido cor pheb sagitta aurea ig nita dencius vulnerau et econtra cor daphne quadam sagitta plumbea que f igidissima fuit sobrius per orauit et sic quanto magts phebus dencior amorem daphnem per ecut est quanto magi frigidior phe bi concupiscenciam dedignabatur amayden whysom ther one daphne hyyt none beaute sayd pheb hio loue hath hir laid therupon hyr sought foolhast besought hym reste euer vpon hyr loue grad sayd euer vnto hym nay byfelle vpon day cupyde whiche hath euery chaunce loue vnder gouernaunce sawe phebus hasten hym sore hym shold haste yet sp den last dart thorugh oute hert cast whiche gold al fyre made hym many fold desyre loue dede daphne eke stede dart leed cast smote whiche al cold thyng hote thus phebus lou brenneth hast aboute renneth boke yf myght wynne thus euer begynne euer wey f hym fl neuer loue sped make hym ful byleue foolhase myght acheue gete loue suche degre daphne laurel tree torued whiche euer grene tokne yet happes faylen hast may auaylen fadre graunt mercy whyle see lady tre hold owne forme may man forme w edyr part fortune wende vnto lyues ende e wold hyr serue euermo sone syth say beware phebus nought ensample vpon lore ye wold telle wryte better myght wyte foolhast sho esche wysedome counseyl sewe sone thou myght enforme thy pacy nce vpon forme old ensamples felle vnderstond shal telle ic ponit confessor exemplum contra istos qui nimio furo attensi vindictam sue vltra quam decet con u effectant et narrat qualiter athemas et demephon reges cum b troiano ad propria remeass nt et u ibidem pacifice receptinon fruss congregatoru unde pug nat rum eratu regiones suas non solum vastare incendio sed oms e sdem habitantes minimo v que ad orem perpetuam vindicte memor gladis interficere feruore iracundie pro pesu run sed rex nestor qui sen sapiens fuit fractat inte ipsos reges eorum regna inita pace humsmodi impetuosita miciu pacifica noble troye byleyn ouercome home ageyn gregoys torned fro ye siege kynges fonde owne lyege many place men seyde hem forsoke dysobeyde among whiche fel ca demephon athemas kynges bothe two serued syeges wold hem receyue algates weyue seche lond place fond noo grace wherof token hem rede sough n frendes nede eche hem assureth helpe owne broder vengen hem thylk oultrage wynne oyene herytage thus ryde aboute fast geten hem helpe laste hadden power suffysaunt maden couenaunt shold lyf saue ne prest ne clerk ne lord ne knaue ne wyf ne child fynde whiche bereth vysage mankynde lyf shal socoured dedely swerde deuoured suche foolhast ordynaunce shape doo vengeaunce purpos wist knowe amog theyr hoost tho ther blowe wordes many speche aboute yong men lusty route tale glad ynough care plough foolhastyf ben acorded ryf seyn may grete vengen hem suche forfet thus sayth vnwyse wylde tonge hem yonge ne whiche old hore salue sawe fore sore counseyl wyse anone aduyse preuy counseyl e lordes geder come demephon anthemas purpoos tolden seten al stylle herde none nestor ansuerde bad hem yf wold wynne sholden see begynne ende set fyrst entent hem ne repent axeth hem questyon fynal conclusyon wolden egne kynges peple onde seyth wonder wyerd seen kyng bycomen hyerd lyf beste onder lygeaunce heste man kyng remenauut thyng seyth eke yf purpoos holde slee peple two wolde myght restore al grece shold abye ful sore see wylde lestes wone whylome duellyd man sone cause hem trete stynte manaces grete better wynne fayr speche seyth suche vengeauce seche man moost aboue hym nedeth moost gete hym loue whan nestor hath tole sayd arene hym word withsayd thought hem al sayd wel thus fortune hyr dedely wheel werre torneth pee forth wenten netheles countreyes herd seyn kynges beseyn suche power lad none told hym nedrad seche pee ryth sende prayd forthwith kynges ben esed euery mannes hert esed al forye recorded thus en geder acorded kynges ayene receyued pee take wrath weyued al thorugh counseyl whiche good hym reson vnderstood ensample bet lawe whiche set fadre byseche hem dedely werres seche worldes cause shed n lobod af suche homycyde good confessor sone vpon thy questyon trouthe myn oppynyon ale ferforth wyt arecheth pleyn lawe opus angelus term pax dixit vltima cristi verba nent pacem quam guerra fugat hic sequitur contra oto guerre que non solum homicidij sed vniuer se mnndi desolacionis mater existit hyghe god iustyce suche werres ledeth inne wynne fyrst acompte grete cost forth folk hath los worldes rekenyng shal fynde wynnyng yf purchace heuen mede suche grace speke netheles cryst hath commaunded loue pe worcheth reuers trowe mood ful dyuers sythen fynde werres owne kynde ben toward god deserte eke bryngen pouert worldes good merueyle among men maye eyle v pee ne conne set trowe synne let euery mede synne deth wote neuer geth one byleue among oure self world leue better pee chese double weye lese yf stonde man may vnderstonde old lokes redeth one couetyse whiche ledeth brought fyrst werres inne grece yf shal begynne proued stood perse whiche ful good maden werre especyal soo dyden eral grete rychesse lond left thyng stond n werred archade nota greci omnem terram de ellabant fertilem sed tantum archadia pro eo quam pauper et steri fuit pacifi dimiserunt werres made cause bareyn pouer wherof myght recouer thus pouerte forbore yt nought nought hath lore yet wondre thyng ryche worthy kynge lord wol axe clayme propyrte thyng whiche hath ryght grete myght may euery man wel wyte bothe kynde lawe wryte expressely stonde ageyn mote nedes somwhat seyn al though reson ynne whiche seche cause wynne demed al wel euer hym semed br may wynne ynough trewe man plough gaygnage entendeth ryght werryour dyspendeth tyme hath conscyence poynt euydence hem suche werres make thou myght grete ensample take declarat per exemplum co tra istos principe seu alios quos cum que illicite guerre motores et narrat de quodam pirata parti mari ni spoliatore qui cum captus fuisset iudicium coram rege alexandro productus de latricinio accusat dixit alexandre vere quia cum pau ci socijs spoliorum causa naues tantu exploroego latrunculus v oo tu aute q cum infinita bellatorum multitu dine vniuersam terram thou stonde seruyce stylle abyde forth al tyde hath hym lyf witholde shal beholde made hym knyght yaf hym lond whiche afterward hond orped knyght many stede grete prowesse armes dede cronyke recorden wyse acorden whiche one ndycy n sett vpon destructyon suche capytayne suche retenue see yssue kyng befallyth laste grete wondre men caste vpon suche wrong wynne e may inne deth dy se euery syde reson put syde wylle g nerneth courage fau n fleeth ramage suffreth thyng weye wherof may take preye set vpon rauyne ylk man whiche couyne hath set suche maner wyse al world ne may suffyse wyl whiche resonable wherof ensample concordable lyche poynt whiche mene vpon alysander sene whiche set al entent fortune hym went reson myyt hym gouerne wylle sterne al world ouer hym lyst took wan inde superyour ful conquerour wylful purpoos wonne al erthe vnder sonne kyng homeward macedoyne cam babyloyne wende moost empyre whiche lord syre honour receyued moost sodenlyche deceyued strong poyson dyscomfyte lo proufyte werre helpeth ryde couetyse worldes pryde slee worldes men aboute bestes whiche gone ther oute ony lyf whiche reson ought wel knowe man ne shold thorugh tyrannye lyche bestes dye tyl kynde wold hym sende myght amende whiche taketh awey euermore lyf may restore thy sone al weye wel auysed preye slaught thou culpable withoute cause resonable fadre vnderstonde ye haue sayd ouer pray telle nay ye passe oue grete see werre slee sarayyn lawe sone myn preche suffre feyth haue herd gospel seyth slee nought cryst owne deth hath bought al men made hem fre tokne parfyte charyte taught hym selue dede twelue apostle went aboute holy feyth preche oute wherof deth sondry place suffre god grace feyth cryst hath made aryse yf wold wyse werre haue bought creauce yet stonde balaunce may prouen dede man cronykes rede fyrst holy chirche hath weyued preche hath swerd receyued wherof werres begonne grete partye wonne crystes feyth stant myswent god doo therof amendement wote best sone yf thou wylt lyue rest conscyence wel assysed er thou slee wel auysed man tellen v clerkes hath god aboue al erthely werkes ordeyned pryncypal eke soule specyal made lyche godhede syt wel taken hede loke euery syde er thou falle homycyde whiche synne general wel nye stant oueral holy chirche elles al whyle wdorl mote nede fare amys whele pyte thorugh couetyse worldes good defouled shedyng blo remenaunt folk aboute vnnethe stonden ony doute werre eche slee al worth stre charyte wherof prechen thyng techen thus blynde conscyence pe hath lost thylk euydence whiche cryst vpon erthe taught may see mordre manslauyt lyche dayes olde whan men synnes bought solde grece afore crystes feyth rede cronyke seyth touchend af mater thus thylk tyme peleus owne broder phocus slough gold ynough synne dyspensed gold wherof compensed achast whiche venus pryest assoylled ca al repentaunce bokes make remembrauce tellyth med e also slough sone two egeus plyte hath made hyr hyr synne quyte sone eke amphyoras who ryght name almeus moder slough eryphele achylo prest bokes recorden certayne somme gold acorden thylk horryble synful dede assoylled thus mede worldes goode fallyth ofte homycyde set alofte lyf shal knowe hem suche thynges wyrche also holy chirche lete suche synnes passe quyte wol hem acquyte dedely werres make wold ensample take lawe whiche naturel weye kynde weth wel homycyde degre whiche werreth ayene charyte among men shold duelle foer bokes telle che al world ryche men shal fynde one lyche best wyl take preye syth kynde hath suche weye wondre man whiche kynde hath reson wol eyther lasse kynde reson ouerpasse slee hym semblable man resonable kynde honeste worse beste nota secundum solinum contra ho iadium de natura cuiusdam aius faci ad similitudinem humanam habentis qiu cum de preda sua hominem myta flauium occident vident que aqua sunile sibi occisum statim pro delo moritur among bokes finde solin speketh wodre kinde seith foules ther whiche hath face bloood bone whiche man resemblaunce yf falle hym par chaunce whiche foule pray man fynde way wold hym slee yf ward day hath eten al felle shal besyde welle whiche wol drynke take whiche visage seeth make hath slayne anone thynketh mysdede forthynketh gretely pure sorowe lyueth tyl morowe ensample may wel se men shal homycyde eschewe euer mercy good take yf lawe hath forsake iustyce ageyne fnl oftyme haue herd seyne amonges werres hadden som whyle cause ladden mercy myyt haue slayn wherof fayn sone yf thou wolt recorde vertu myserycorde thou syghe neuer thylk place vsed lak grace euery lawe euery kynde mannes wyt mercy bynde namely worthy knyghtes stonde moost vpryghtes ben myghty greue sholden thenne releue hym whome myyten ouerthrowe ensample may men knowe hic ponit confessor exemplum de pietate contra homicidium et narrat qualiter achilles vna cum thephalo filio suo contra regem mesee qui tunc theucer vocabatur bellum inicrunt et cum achilles dietum regem bello prostratum occidere voluisset thephal pietate motus ipsum clipeo cooperiens veniam pro rege patre postulauit quo facto ipse rex adhuc viuens thephalum regni sui heredem libera volu tate constituit may faylen mede hath mercy rede cronyke fynd thus whan achilles telaphus sone ward troye fel hem come ayene thoucer kyng mese make warre lese lond wolde regne theucer pnt oute regne thus march assaylle theucer yaf hem bata ylle foughten bothe sydes faste happeth laste worthy greke achilles kyng among al ches cruel felle swerd hond hym felle smote hym dethes woude vnhorced fel grounde achilles vpon hym alyght wold anone wel myght haue slayn hym place thephalus fadre grace hym besought pyte prayth wold late hym cast sheld bytwene hem two achilles axeth hym thephalus cause tolde seyth mochel holde whylome theucer stede grete grace socour hym dede sayth hym wold acquyte prayth fadre respyte achilles tho withdrough hond al power lond yt sawe hyr kyng thus take fled hath f ld forsake grekes vnto chaas falle moost part alle countre lordes grete took wonne grete beyete anone vyctorye kyng whiche memorye vpon grete mercy thought laphus toward hym wrouyt presence al londe took hym fayre honde wyse gan seye sone mote double weye loue desyre thyn encrees fyrst thy fadre achilles whylome ful many day shold fare amys rescouse dyd quarele kepte al myn estate hele ther falle dystaunce among v yet remembraunce haue mercy whiche dede thou stede gentylnes fraunchesse hast mercy gesse wol ony tyme lost thou hast byme fortune falle yet stant trust abouen alle mercy whiche fynde thou wolt e kynde suche myn espeyr sone myn yre receyue al lond yeue sese thyn honde wyse accorde cause myserycorde lordes obeysaunce thelaphus purueaunce made coroned thus mercy reguerdoned whiche theucer dyde fore loo ensample made therfore thou myght take remembraunce sone thou seest chaunce men passyon take pyte compassyon lete thynge leef whiche another man greef yf thou desyre stonde ayene vyce ire counseyl pacyence take thy conscyence mercy thy gouernour shalt thou fynde rancour wherof thyn herte shal debate homycyde ne hate cheste melancolye thou shalt softe companye withoute conteck foolhast elles myght thou long wast thy tyme thou haue thy wylle loue wedyr stylle men preyse blame tempestes fadre wol hestes poynt ye haue tauyt toward self better saught thenke bewayle whyle lyne moche shryne wrathe al circumstaunce yeue ye lyst penaunce axe forther lyf yf wyse gyltyf ony thyng toucheth synne sone departe twynne shal behynde thynge leue amans good fadre leue axe forth lyste haue suche tryste ye soule hele ye fro nothyng wol hele shal telle trouthe sone art thou culpable slouthe ony poynt whiche hym longeth fadre tho poyntes longeth wyte pleynly mene maye shryue clene herkne shal ye pointes deuyse vnderstonde wel myn appryse shryfte stant value hym wol hym vertue leue vyces folye wynd word maystrye man hym self defende thyng whiche comende wherof ben fewe daye netheles may make vnto thy memorye knowe poyntes slouthe yu shalt knowe explicit liber tercius incipit liber quartus dicut accidia fore nutri em viaoru corpet cunctis tarda que lenta bonis que fieri possent hodie transfert piger ceas furato que prius hostia clandit equo poscenti tardo negat emolumeta cupi sed ven c beri ludit amore viri quarto libro loquitur con fessor de speciebus accidie qua primam tardacionem vocat cuius diciouem pertractans amanti su hoc consequenter opponit bpon vyces procede cause ofemanes dede fyrst poynt slouthe calle lachesse chyef alle aud hath properly kynde leuen al thyng behynde myght taryeth al long yere euermore sayth morowe wol tyme borowe wyssheth god sende weneth haue ende forthest begynne thus bryngeth many meschief inue vnware tyl mescheued may releued ryght nother ne lesse stant ofloue lachesse somtyme slouteth daye neuer gete may sone ylke thyng thou haue ony knoulechyng thou loue hast done telle good fadre yi laches knowe may stonde vpon rowe clad sute thought pursute make therto set day speke vnto swete may lachesse bad abyde yet bare hond wyt ne tyme speke tho thus tale fro tyme taryeng drough ther tyme good ynough sayd another tyme better thou shalt sende letter par caas wryte pleyn thou mouthe durst seyn thus haue lete tyme slyde slouthe kept tyde laches vyce ful hath made wyt nyce thought speke taryeng eld tyl wold myght nought thyng thought drede shame euer ernest game wote ther long tyme passed yet loue lassed whiche vnto lady haue though tonge slouy ocaue al tyme haue bede myn hert stant euer one stede axe besylyche grace whiche may yet embrace god wote maulgre myn wote ryght wel afyn grace cometh selde aboute slouthe whiche doute al remenaunt whiche loue appertenaunt thus touchend lachesse haue told confesse yow fadre e byseche ferthermore ye wol teche yf ther matere som goodly tale lere may lachesse awey ye wold telle prey wysse sonne rede among tale whiche rede old ensample therupon herkne wol telle hic ponit confessor exemplum contra istos qui amoris causa tardantes delinquunt et narrat quali ter dido regina eartaginis eneam ab incendijs troie fugitiuum amo rem suum gaiusa suscepit qui cum postea partes italie cartagine bella turum se transtulit ninuam que ibidem moram faciens tempus redditus sui ad didonem vltra modum tardauit ipsa intolieravili gaudio concussa sui cordis intima gladio transfodit ageyne lachesse loues caas fynde whylom eneas whome anchyses sone greete nauye lad fro troye arryueth eartage fo herbergage took betyd soo hyr whiche quene tho cyte acqueyntaunce wan who name remembrauce yet dydo hote whiche loueth eneas soo hote vpon wordes whiche sayd al hyr herte hym layd dyd al holy wolde sholde fro goth itayle shyp thew arryuayle hath take shope hym ryde whiche may long abyde hote payne loues throwe anone within lytel throwe setter vnto hyr knyght hath wryte dyde hym pseynsy wyte made ony tarying dretche ayene comyng ne myght hym fele see shold stonde suche degree whylome stood swan fore hyr make ore sorowe fether brayne shoof hath hyr self slayn kyng menander lay soth hath fonde lay spraulend wynges tweye whiche shold deye loue hym make shal thy sake quene sayde wel wote lo enee thus wrote many another word copleynt thoughtes feint towardes loue ful slouthe tyme let routhe whiche loueth hym fore euer sawe hym tarye hyr hert ful wo compleynend manyfolde hath hyr owne tale tolde vnto self thus spack fonde euer suche lack slouthe ony worthy knyght wote wel deth dyght thurgh hym whiche shold haue yf stynten al stryf thus syghe none bote ryght euen vnto hert rote naked sword anone threste thus got hyr self reste remembraunce al slowe wherof sone thou myght knowe hou taryeng vpon nede loues cause drede hath dydo sore abought whoos deth shal euer bethought euermore yf shal seche maner another speche cronyke fynde wryte tale whiche good wyte loquitur super eodem qualiter enolope vlixum maritum suum obsidione troie diucius morantem ob ipsius ibidem tardacionem epistola sua redargiut twye kyng vlyxes vpon sege among ye pres hem ye worthy kniytes abode longe tyme stylle thylke tyme man may see hou goodly penolope whiche hym trewe wyf lachesse wa pleyntyf wherof troye hym sende hyr wylle letter thus spekende worthy loue lorde alsso hath euer soo woman alone maketh man persoue hardy wowe hope wolde bowe suche thyuge wylle werr whyle lord elles self telle long passed syth fyrste ye home went wele nyhe euery man went come whyle ye oute besyly eche hem aboute whiche loue loue secheth grete prayer bysecheth somme maken grete manace yf myght come place myght wyl haue thyng shold saue ne wold worche thynges somme telle tydynges ye dede somme seyn certeynly ye beseyn loue newe leue holle euer thanke vnto goddes alle yet ought byfalle may man chekes rede netheles drede lachesse contynuaunce fortune myght werke suche chaunce whiche noman shal amende loo thus thys lady compleynend letter vnto hyr lord hath wryte prayd hym wold wyte thynke al tarye wold loue acquyte ayeneward wryte come hym self al hast none paper wast soo kepe holde trouthe withoute let ony slouthe vnto lord loue lyege troye grete syege leyd letter conueyd whiche wysedom hath purueyd al reson belongeth gentyl hert vnderfongeth hath ouer rad part ryght inly glad eke part dysesed loue hert hath thorugh sesed pure ymagynacyon none occupacyon whiche gan take syde may flyt hert asyde wyf hym enformed wherof hath hym self conformed al wyl courage shape take yage homeward tyme may soo hym thynketh one day thousand yere tyl may see ysage penolope whiche desyreth moost alle tyme byfalle troye destroyed brent made delayment goth hym home al hyghe fond fore eye worthy wyf good estate thus seced debate loue slouthe excused doth gret harme bsed hyndreth many cause honest nota ad huc de quodam astrologo super eodem qui quondam op ingeniosum quasi ad complementum septennius perducens vnius momenti tardacione omnem sui operis diligenciam pe nitus feustrauit grete clerk grostest rede redy vpon clergyr hede bra make forge telle suche thynges befelle seuen yeres besynesse layde lachesse half mynute houre fro fyrst began laboure lost al whyle fareth soo loues cause slowe withoute vnder wowe nyght fue ofte stant colde whiche myght yf wolde tyme haue kept haue ben inne nota ad huc contra tardacionem de virginibus fatuis que ni iam mora facientes intrante sponso ad nupa cum ipso non introterunt slouthe may profyt wynne may synge carole late ware come dole good receyue myght proued wel nyght whylome maydens fyue thylk lord cam wyue oy e awey lyght lampes wey slouthe brought aboute fro hym shet oute wherof sone thou beware ferforth telle dare l u must awayted yf thou wel affayted loue esehewe slouthe sone telle trouthe thou myght thy self able wynne loue make stable though thou myytest loue acheue fadre may wel leue neuer assygned place yet gete ony grace e suche tyme appoynted wold vnioynted euery lyme haue ne shold hepe saue myn oure bethe eke seede lady de otherwyse auysed graut suche tyme assysed netheles lachesse hath defaulte gesse tyme lost yf myght yf lyketh alyght pon lure whiche fynde cast ay crye fast lesse lyketh speke matere seche may fynde hast euer behynde wote may amounte fadre vpon myn acompte whiche ye ben set examyne shryft diseyplyne say youre best counseyl sonne counseyl stonde tyme goo doo forth thy besynes soo lachesse founde slouthe myghty confounde speed euery man werke many vyce sayth clerke hongen vpon slouthes lappe suche maketh man myshappe pleyne telle wyst therupon yf lyst knowe slouthes cause specyal yet ouermore vyce ful greuable hym whiche therof culpable stant al wrtues bare shal declare qui nichi attempt nichil expedit ore que muto munus amicicie vir sibi caro capit est modus verbis sed et qui parcit amori verba referre sua fauet vllus amor hic loquitur confessor de quadam specie accidie que pusillanimitas dictum est cuius imaginatiua formido ne que virtutes aggredi ne que vicia f gere au det sic quam vtrius que vite tam actiue quam co templatiue premium non attingit ouchend slouth degre yet pusillanymyte whiche saye langage hath lytel courage dare man werke legynne may reson wynne dare nought vndertake ryght shal profyte take vyce nature dare thyug set auenture hym lacketh worth dede wherof sholde cause spede wol manhode vnderstonde euer hath drede vpon honde al peryll shal saye hym thynketh wolf way ymagynacyon maketh excusacyon feyneth cause pure drede euer fayleth nede tyl al spylt deleth hath sore whiche man heleth whiche cleped lak herte though euery grace aboute hym sterte wol one stew fote reson lese mote wol aunter wynne soo forth sone yf begynne speke loue seruyce ben truantes suche wyse lakken hert vhan best speken loue ryght fere wexen dombe dare telle withoute soune doth belle whiche hath claper chyme ryght tyme herteles withoute speche loue dare thyng byseche thus lese wynne nought thy sone yf thou art ought culpable touchend slouthe shryue therof telle trouthe sadee al beknowe haue ben one slowe telle loues myn hert yet euer though world shold breke ferful dar speke purpoos haue nome toward lady come lete passe ouer goo sone soo man pursueth loue fortune seweth ful ofte yeueth happy chaunce hym whiche maketh contynuaunce preyse loue byseche nsample shal teche hic moris causa loquitur contra et dicit amon pre timore verbis obtumeseere non debet sed concinuando sui amous dia onem tucius prosequ tur et ponit co sessor exeplum qualiter pigma ion pro quam preces continuauit quandam imaginem e urneam cuius puleritudinis concupiscencia illaque tus extitit carnem sanguinem ad latus suum transformatam sencijt fynd hou whilome ther one who iname pygmalyone whiche lusty man youthe werkes entayll couthe aboue al men tho though fortune fel hym whome loue shal trauayle made image entayle lycho woman semblaunce feture contynaunce soo fayre neuer fygure ryght alyues creature semeth yuor whyte hath hyr wrouyt suche delyte rody eheke rody vpon hyr lyppes eke wherof hym self begyleth goodly looke smyloth thurgh pure impressyon owne imagynacion al herte courage loue vpon faire ymage set hyr lone preyde word ayeneward seyde long day thyng dede image stede euer att mete wold hyr serue prayde ete put vnto mouthe cuppe boord taken vppe hath hyr chambre nome nyght come leyd hyr led al naked wepte wasted kyste colde lyppes ofte wyssheth softe ofte ronneth ere ofte arme yd wold hyr embrace euer among axeth grace though wyst ment thus hym self gan torment suche dysese loues peyne noman myght hym peyne penaunce made suche contynuaunce fro day nyght prayd long prayer vnderfonge whiche venus hyr grace herd nyght werst ferd say naked arme cold ymage felt warme flessh bone ful lyf thus wan lusty wyf whiche obeysaunt wylle yf wold haue hold hym stylle thyng spoke shold haue faysed hath word tra uayfed durst speke loue spedde al wold abedde went two man childe betwene hem two ga e whiche hyght aphus whome yet ful ryyt certeyne whiche paphos men clepe name aros ensample thou myyt fynde worde may worche aboue kynde thy sone yf thou spare speke lost al thy fare slouthe bryngeth inne al wo ouer loke also god loue fauourable hem loue stable many wondre hath byfalle wherof speke amonges alle ye lyst taken hede wherof solempne tale rede whiche shal telle remembraunce vpon sorte loues chaunce hic ponit exemplum super eodem qualiter rex ligdus vxo sue thela cuse pregnanti nabatur quam si pareret infans occidetetur que tamen postea aim filiam ediderat isi de patt tunc presens fi nomine fili iphi appellari ipsam que maseu educare admonuit quam pater fi credens ipsam maritagium fil cuiusdam principis e e slita copulauit sed cum iphis debitum sui co ugij vnde soluere non habnit deos sui ad iutorium interpellabat qui super hoc miserti femineum genus mascu n ob affectum nature ip e per omnia transmu runt kyng lyg vpon ryf spa vnto thelacuse wif chyld grete swore shold lete yf doughter ore n shold forlore slayn wherof sory soo vyfel vpon ca whan delyuerd shld isys nyght pryne e whiche childyng goddesse cam helpe dy r sse tyll lady al smal doughter forth al whiche goddesse al weye bad kepe shold seye sone thus iphys named hym vpon fadre made wene thus chambre qu iphis forth drawe tho clothed arayed ryght kynges sone sholde tyl fortu e wolde ten yere age hym bytake maryage duke doughter wedde whiche daun e hyght ofte bedde child lay whiche one age soo within tyme yere gede ben pley fer lyggend bed vpon nyght nature whiche doth euery wyght vpon lawe muse constreyneth hem vse thyng whiche hem al vnknow wherof cupyde thylk throwe toke pyte grete loue lete set kynde aboue lawe may vsed vpon lust e cused loue ha eth thyng thyng whiche stant ayenst ye ore nature kynde hath thy cupyde hath beset grace vpon auenture acordaunt nature sawe tyme best eche hem hath est transformeth iphe man wherof kynde loue wan lusty yongthe iante wyf tho led mery lyf whiche kynde none offence thus take euydence semeth loue wel wyllend hem contynuend esy hert pursue thynge whiche loue due wherof sone matere thou myght nsample taken thy gre e besynesse thou myght yne rych sse loue yf slouth dar wel say trouth fe wyt seche fadre lak speche se sh oof fore none tyme lore wherof ther myght obstacle let loue myracle whiche bys ch day nyght fadre ryght forme shryf e knowe thyng ngeth slowe faderhode wol prey ther forther ony weye touchend vnto ylk vyce sone ye offyce ther serueth one specyal whiche hath lost memoryal withholde thyng whiche kepe holde wherof hym self ful ofte agreueth moost vpon hym leueth wyttes en weyued may ful lytel deceyued mentibus oblita alienis labitur e que probat accidia meminisse fui sic amor incautus qui non memoratur ad horas perdit offendit quod pera e nequit hic tractat confessor de vicio obliuionis qua mater eius accidia ad virtutum memo ia nec non amo ri causa inmemorem constitu serue accidie offyce ther slouth another vice whiche cleped foryet ylness may hert impresse vertu whiche reson hath sette clene wyttes foryede tellyng tale hert male hath remembraunce thy k forme wherof shold wyt enforme yet ne wote thus purpoos nought thy forlore wold abyde scarsely yf seeth tyde loue ment thus many louer hath shent telle therfore hast thou one hem hath slouthe begone fader hath ofte lady fro thynke vnto ward drawe cast many newe lawe al world torne vp doune decorde lesson wryte memoral telle shal come haue al foryete wy thought telle vnnethes spelle wende alther best haue red sore adred man sodenly goost byhelde fare fere get wyt self foryete wo neuer n whether shal ne cam muse amased yche book whiche rased letter may thyng rad see ben wyttes ouer lad euer thouyt haue spo e oute fro myn hert stoken stonde sayth dombe deef al ny worth iuy leef wende wel haue say last make abrayd ast vp myn heede loke aboute ght man doude wote shal bycome thus oft al ouercome wende best stonde vnderstonde place alone make many woful mone vnto self speke soo fool thyn hert tho thou thy worthy lady syghe thou ferd eye hond drede wel knowe womanly de oul age child thre yere age hast thou drede good one whome al vertu begone vyolence goodlyhede innocence withoute spot e ony blame nyce hert fy shame coward herte loue vnlered wherof art thou sore afered thy ong thou suffcest frese wolt thy goodly wordes lese thou hast fonde tyme space sholdest thou deserue grace thou thy self darst axe none al thou hast foryete anone thus despute loues ore helpe fynde none stomble vpon myn owne treyne make akynge peyne euer thynk among ho al self along say fool al fooles thou farest bytwene two stole wold syt e goth grou ne neuer shal founde bytwene foryetylnes drede man shold ony cause spede thus myn holy fadre dere toward self ye may hare pleyne fo yetylnesse elles al besynesse may take man thought hert taketh thurgh sough thynken euer vpon swe withoute slouthe byhete falle wele wo thought foryete neuerm laugh loure nought half mynute oure ne myght lete oute mynde yf itho ght vpon hende therof ne shal slouthe lette tyl deth oute world fet e al though suche ryng moyses thorugh enchauntynge somtyme ethyope made tharbys wedded hade whiche ryng bare oblyuyon name reson fynger sate anone loue forya e neuer knowe fel ylke throwe tharbys hond knowlechyng hym fond al clene oute memorye men may rede storye thus went quyte aweye neuer thylk day thought ther suche one al foryete ouer gone good feyth soo may euer fast myn herte toucheth thyng yt slouthe voucheth may foryete leef ne loth oueral goth myn herte foloweth hyr aboute thus may say withoute doute e werse ouyt nouyt passeth neuer fro thought myn herte seyd somtym hyr sore adrad somtyme ouerglad reule e space see goodly face thynke vpon hyr hyghe pry though paradys uesshed syght speke vnto n myght tyme though welde ne may wyt vnfolde fynde one word men al forye clene though stonde ther myle al foryerte whyle tonge haue wordes none thus stond thynke alone thyng h lpeth ofte nought afore thought speke come fory nought ne stonde mased asso ed thyng haue noted note synge al oute knoulechynge thus ioye drede al forye e nede fader slouth haue sayd pleyn trouth ye may ye lyst redresse thus stant foryetylnesse eke pusyllanymy e saye forth ye lyke wol sone haue wel herd hou thou hast sayd thou must amende loue grace wol sende man whiche dare axe none knowen euerychone man thought withoute speche god wote yet men byseche wyl withoute bedys dothe grace fewe stedys man foryete hym selue among thousand twelue wol hym take remembraunce lete hym falle take chauce thy pul vp besy herte sone lete thyng aster e loue fro thy besynesses touchyng foryetylnesse whiche many loue hath set behynde tale grete ensample fynde wherof py e wyte maner wryte hic amoris causa contra obliuiosos ponit confessor exemplum qualiter demophon versus bellum troia num itinerando philli de rodepey gina non tantum hospicium sed ecia amorem gandio magno susceptus e qui postea ipsa tro descendens rediturum infra certum tempus fide s se compromisit sed qiua huiusmodi promissiones diem statutu oblitus phillis obliuionem demephontis lacrimis primo deplangens tandem cordula collo suo circumligata se mortua suspendit kyng demophon ship troye ward felauship seylend goth vpon weye hapneth hym rodepeyr eolus hym blowe l nd rested throwe feste ylke tyme thus daughter lygurgius whiche quene countre soiourned cyte within castel stronde demophon cam vp londe hylles hyght yong age bothe stature ysage al hyr best vesemeth demophon ryyt wel quemeth come made hym chere suche manere lusty knyght ne myght asterte ne hyr herte within day twoo thought euer go wold assaye fortune gan quene comune goooly wordes ere put hyr oute fere swore hath trouthe plyght euer hyr owne knyght thus hyr stylle abode whyle shyp anker rood bad ynough tyme space speke loue seke grace lady herd al sayde swore prayde whiche enchauntement innocent though trouthe feyth leueth al euer seyth fortune sholde graunteth hym al wolde thus tyme ioye tyl shold go e tho made mochel sorowe trouth leyd sorowe come yf lyue may ageyne within moneth day therupon kysten bothe hym leef hym loth shyp goth forth went troye first entet dayes gone monethe passeth loue encreseth lasseth hym lost slepe mete tyme hath al foryete woful yong quene whiche wote myght mene letter send prayd hym come sayd ouercome strengthe loue suche wyse long may suffyse lyuen presence put vpon conseyence trouthe whiche hath wherof loueth hym hote sayth yf lenger lette suche day hym sette shold ste en slouthe whiche shame vnto trouth letter forth vpon hyr fonde wherof somdele comfort honde took wold abyde wayteth vpon ylke tyde whiche hath letter wryte pyte wyte dyde erst forgate tyme eftsone forsate whiche myght tyde awayteth euermo cast hyr eye vpon se somtyme nay somtyme ye somtyme cam somtyme nought thus dysputeth thought wote thynke may fastend al long day derk nyght tho hath set vp lyght lanterne hyghe vpon toure goth ofte hope comyng shold see lyght brennyng wherof myght weyes ryght come nyght al nonght deceyued venus hath hyr hope weyued shewed hyr vpon sky day fast within lytel throwe dayes lyght myght knowe tho byhelde see large saw ther barge e shyp fer may kenne doune fro tour gan renne herber al hyr one many woder woful mone made lyf wyst whiche al ioye myst swouneth pleyneth face dyst yneth teres whiche welle stremes eyen felle myght euer one cleped vpon demephon sayd allas thou slowe wyght neuer suche knyght thorugh vngentylnesse slouthe foryetylnesse ayenst trouthe breketh steuene tho hyr eye vp heuene cast sayde thou vnkynde shalt thou thy slouthe fynde lyst come see lady dede loue shal selue spylle whome yf thy wylle thou myghtest saue wel inough vpon grene bough syle whiche ha knyt hyr self lad aboute hyr whyte swere hit dede henge hyr self wherof goddes amoued demephon reproued goddes prouydence shape suche euydence euer afterward ayene slowe hillis throwe shape note tre al men myght see afterward hyllys hyllerd tre cleped yerd yet demophon shame daye bereth name woful chaunce ferde anone demephon herde euery man speche sorowe tho seche gan slouthe banne al late thanne lo thus sone myght thou wyte ayene vyde hou wryte man may harmes gesse fallen thurgh foryetylnesse wherof thy shryft haue herd yet slouthe hou hath ferd wyse thenke oppose thou haue gylt suppose dum plantare licet cultor qui n cli git ortum si desint feuctus imputat ipse sibi preterit ista dy bona nec valebit illa secunda hoc caret exemplo lentus amore suo hic tractat confessor de vicijs necligencie cuius condicio idiam amplectens omnes artes sciencie tam mo cansa quam aliter ignominiosa pretermittens cum nullum poterit e mi nere remedium sui ministerij diligenciam ey post facto vacuum attemptare presumit fvlfylled slouthes exeplair ther yet one secretayr cleped necligence whiche wol loke euydence wherof may beware fore hath cause lore wyse hond helpe may maner bond fyrst wold bynde thus euermore stant behynde thyng may amende ware seyth ende wold god knowe wherof beiaped mowe goth grete stede stole taketh hede maketh stable dore fast thus euer pleyth cast al shal saye hath maner ke also hym lyst lerne wyse le sett vertu pryse hym lyketh whyle fayleth ful ofte gyle weneth seker stonde thus thou myght wel vnderstode sone yf thou art suche loue thou myght come thyn aboue thou woldest wel acheue amans myn holy fadre leue may wel sauf conscyence eycuse neglygence towardes loue al wise though e none wyse truly amerous euer curyous hem best enforme knowen wyten al forme falleth vnto loues craft yet ne fond nought haft whiche myght vnto blade acorde neuer herd man recorde thyng myght auayle wynne loue withoute fayle yet ferforth couthe neuer fynde man reson ne kynde conthe teche suche arte ne fayled parte toward myn owne wyt contryue couthe neuer yet fynde ony se yrnesse myght lesse loue make spede leueth wel withouten drede yf ther suche weye certaynly shal deye lerned long go wote wel none netheles may wel soo rude degre eke wyttes ben soo dul ne may nought ful atteyne vnto hyghe lo e dar seye ouermore al though wyt strong wyl along sy nyght day lerne al lern emay hou myght loue wynne yet begynne wold make ende hou shal wende moost sorowe dare take god borowe myn entendemet none wyse neclygent saye haue thy pur seynt charyte telle fadre yow semeth confessor good feyth sone wel quemeth thou thy self hast thus acquyte toward vyce whiche noo wyte byde may houre lost al may laboure long yere soo men seyne euer doth veyne thorugh slouthe neclygece neuer suche scyence ne vertue whiche bodely ny destroyed lost therby ensample hath soo bokes fynde wryte also hic contra vicium necligencie ponit confessor exemplum et narrat cum pheton filius solis currum pa sui per regere debuerat ad monitus patre vt equos ne deuiarent equa manu diligeci ipse co liu pris sua necligecia pret e equos curru nimis basse errare permisit vn de non solum incendio orbem inflammauit sed ipsum de curru cadendem quoddam fluuium demergi ad inte tum causauit pheb whiche ye sone hote shyneth vpon erthe hote causeth euery lyues helthe sone al welthe whiche pheton hyght desyreth modre conspyreth whiche cleped clemene helpe counseyl fadre cart lede myght vpon fayre dayes lyght thyng prayde vnto fadre sayde wold wel forth al thre poyntes bad specyal vnto sone al wyse hym shold wel auyse take weye lore first hors sore ne pryk told reynes fast hold also ryght ware maner ledeth chare mystake gate vp auysement algate shold bere syker weye lowe ne heye cart dryue ony throwe drede lest shold ouerthrowe thus phebus ordynaunce toke pheton goueruaunce sonnes cart whiche lad b suche veyn glory set vpon hygh owne estate ne sygh thorugh neglygence took none hede myght wel long spede hors withouten lawe cart lete aboute drawe hym lyketh wantonly last sodenly reson wold knowe fyry cart droue lowe fyreth al world aboute wherof al doute god helpe cryden suche vnhappes betyden phebus whyche sawe neglygence pheton ayene defence chare hath dryue oute weye ordeyneth fel weye oute cart flood drowned lo stood hym neglygent fro hyghe fyrmament wold goo lowe anone doune ouerthrowe hyghe estate vyce goo lowe seruyce greueth goo hyghe wherof tale eesye exemplum super eodem de icharo filio didali carcere minotau existente cui dedalus vt inde eu faret ala componens firmite imunxit ne nimis alte propter solis ardorem ascen deret quod icharus sua ngligecia post ponens cum alcius sublimatus f sset subito ad terram corruens expira fynde whylome dedal whiche sone icharus hyght though hym thought loth suche pryson mynotaurus aboute myghten nowher wenden oute bygonnen shape pryson myght escape dedalus whiche fro youthe taught many craftes couthe fethers thynges hath made flee dyuers wynges hym sone also whome yafe charge tho bad hym thynke therupon wynges set wax yf took flyght hyghe al sodenlyche myght make melte sonne thus haue hyr flyyt legone oute pryson fayre softe alofte icharus gan mounte good counseyl none acopte set whiche fadre taught tyl sonne wynges caught wherof melt rom hyght withouten helpe ony flyght felle hi destructyon lych condycyon fallen oftymes fele lok gouernaunce wele al wel loue weye n w good fadre yow preye ther matere f uthe myght sene thy dylyg nce whiche euery man comeyence reson shold reule kepe yf lyst take kepe trllen abouen alle vertu may befalle whiche yeueth vnto vyces rest sleuthe slowest ab que labore vagus vi inutilis plec eno nescio qui vita v bit ei non amor ta nusero get imme valoris qui faciut opera clamat habere su hic loquitur confessor super illa specie ue ocium dicitur auus condiao virtutum cultura nullius occupacionis diligenciam admittene cuiusaim que expe icionem cause non attingit among louthes kynde whiche al labour set behynde hateth al besynes yet one whiche idelnes cleped noryoe man kynde euery vyce whiche secheth case many folde wynter doth nought colde somer may nought hete soo whether feese swete oute wol ben ydel al aboute yf pley ought dye euer taketh fee thynketh worship deserue lord whome wol serue duelle seruyce suche wyse seeth parauenture lordship oeuerture may onde stylla vse idelnesse wylle ne wol trauaylle take ryde lady sake lyueth vpon al wysshes catt wold ete fysshes without wetyng clees wold netheles fayleth haue wolde confessor sone yf thou suche molde art made telle pleyne thy shryft amans fadre god yeue yift toward loue may wytt al ydel neuer yett ne neuer shal whyle may goo sone telle hast thou done besyshyp loue ladyshyp hyr whiche thy lady fadre euer yet euery place euery stede lady hath bede al myn herte obedyent haue therto dylygent yf byd nought thyng thought cometh fyrst may suffyse bowe profre seruyce sotyme chambre somtyme halle ryght see tymes falle goth masse tyme shal ouerpasse ne approche hyr ladyhede aunter yf may hyr lede vnto chapel ageyne al wey veyne somdele may better fare may fele hyr bare may lede hyr clothed myn arme afterward doth harme pure imagynacyon collacyon make vnto seluen ofte say lord softe round smal wold god hadde hyr al withoute daunger wylle syke sitte ful stylle see besy thought torned idel nought al lete ne may see tyme another day ne besynes vnto ladyes worthynes therto wytte affayte see tyme awayte done leue whan tyme hyr leue thyng bydde doo bydde go goo hyr lyst clepe come thus hath fullyche ouercome myn idelnesse tyl sterue soo mote hyr nedes serue men seyn nede hath lawe thus mote nedely deawe serue bowe lofte lowte myn eye foloweth hyr aboute wol wol wol syt knele stodeth wol stod taketh hir werk hod weuyng brouderye muse prye vpon hyr fyngers long smale thynke tale synge syke contenaunce pyke yf falle tyme lyketh nought abyde byme occupyeth hyr thynges make taryenges dryue forth long daye loth departe waye symple port feyne somme dysport play wyth hyr lytel hounde bed ground byrdes cage none lytel page ne yet symple chamberere ne make hem alle chere al shold speke wele thus may ye see besy whele goth ydelyche aboute lyst ryden oute stede come thus though bede take hyr myn arme alofte set hyr hyr sadel softe forth lede hyr brydel wold ben ydel yf lyst ryde chare may therof ware none shape ryde ryght euen chares syde may speke among otherwhyle synge songe whiche ouyde book made sayd sorowes glade woful prosperyte belongeth propyrte loue wol hym serue yet ther fro may man swerue ne mote lawe obeye thus ryde forth weye ryght besy oueral herte body al baue sayd yow fore good fadre telle therfore ydelnes yf haue gylt sone yf thou alle wylt ought elles may thou shalt haue penaunce netheles man may see dayes ther ful many suche hertes slowe wol besyen hem knowe thyng loue tyl last strengthe hem ouercast maulgre hem mote obeye done al ydelshyp aweye serue wel besylyche sone art thou none suche loue shal wel excuse otherwyse yf thou refuse loue thou myght par ca b n idel somtyme kynges doughter vnauysed tyl cupyde hyr hath chastysed thou shalt tal acordaunt vnto matere hic ponit confessor ex mplum o qui amoris occupacionem omit grauioris infortunij casus expectant et narrat de quadam armennie regis filia que huiusmodi condicionis anapio iuuentutis ociosa persistes micabili postea visione castigata amoris obseqiuum pre ceteris diligencior efficitur armenye rede thus ther kyng whiche herupus hote lusty mayde doughter men saide name rosiphele whiche tho grete renome bothe wyse feyre shold hyr fadre heyre one defaulte slouthe towardes loue routhe wel couthe noman seye whiche myght set weye loues occupacyon thorugh none imagynacyon seole wold knowe thus one slowe suche hertes besynesse tyl venus goddesse whiche loues court hath reule hath brought better reule forth cupyde myght meruayle suche wyght whiche tho lusty age desyreth nouther maryage ne yet loue peramours whiche euer hath ben comon cours among hem lusty shewed hye hertes loweth fyry dart whiche throweth cupyde whiche loue god chastysynge hath made rod dryue awey wantonnesse soo within whyle gesse suche chaunce sporned al moo ouertorned whiche fyrste slowe manere fel thou shalt come moneth may wold walke vpon day sonne aryst woman fewe wyst forthe went pryuely vnto park fast al soft walkend vpon gras tyl cam ther laude thorugh ran grete riuer thought hyr fayr sayd wol abyde vnder shawe badde hyr woman withdrawe stood alone stylle thynke wylle sawe swete floures spryng herd gladde foules synge sawe bestes kynde buk doo hert hynde male go femele bygan quarele bytwene loue hyr owne hert whiche couthe astert cast hyr eye aboute sawe clad one sute route ladyes come ryde long vnder wode syde fayre ambulend hors sete al whyte fat grete echone ryde syde sadeles suche pryde perles gold wel begone ryche sawe neuer none kyrtels cope ryche clothed al alyche departed euen whyte blewe al lustes knewe embroudred oueral bodyes long smal beaute fayr vpon hyr face none erthely thyng may deface corownes theyr hedes bere eche hem quene al gold cresus halle lest coronal hem alle myyt haue bought worth thus come rydend forth kynges doughter sawe yt tide pure abasshede drewe hyr asyde held hyr cloos vnder abough lete hem stylle ryde inough thought auyce hem suche pryce worthy axe fro come bnt leuer worldes good wold haue wyst stood put hyr hede lytel oute loked hyr aboute sawe comend vnder lynde woman vpon hors behynde hors rood blak al ene galled vpon back halted enc oyed wherof woman annoyed thus hors sory plyght al sterre lyght amyddes front sadel este wonder bad whiche woful woman sat netheles ther ryche brydel none gold precious stone cote somdele tore aboute myddel tweuty score hors halter wel mo ther hangen tyme tho thus cam lady nyghe thenne took better hede syghe woman fayr vylage fresshe lusty yong tendre age lady stood bethought hyr wel vnderstood whiche come rydend tho tydynges couthe telle tho whiche sawe fore ryde put hyr forth prayd hyr abide sayd suster lete ben ryden ben rychely arrayed woman cam esmayed ausuerde ful softe speche sayd madame shal teche ar tho whylome seruauntes loue trouthe bere theyr hertes sett fare wel may let madame go seruyor must hast al wyse thy madame yeue leue may long leue good suster yet preye telle ye beseye haltres thus begone madame whilome one fadre kyng slowe thyng lyst loue obeye ful sore obeye lome loue hors feble bad al tore myn array euery yere fresshe may lusty ladyes ryde aboute must nedes sewe route maner ye see trusse hyr haltres forth hors knaue none offyce ne haue hem thynketh worthy slowe loues lore able lere wold tale hem couthe loue teche trsse byseche fore ryche brydel serueth awey chere swerueth gan wepe thus told ryche brydel whiche ye behold ryche vpon myn hors hede madame afore dede lusty lyf felle myn herte stryf loue whiche ouercome therof hede nome thought wold loue knyght last wel fonrtenyght lenger myght last nyghe lyf last allas late ware ne hym loued deth cam hast vyme r therto ony tyme ne myght ben acheued al releued wylle good therto loue suffreth soo shal suche brydel haue ye herd al myn ansuere god madame yow betake warneth al sake loue nought ydel byd hem thynke vpon brydel word al sodenly passeth sky al clene oute lady syght tho fore hyr hert aflyght sayd hyr self allas ryght caas lyue daye shal amende yf maye thus homeward lady went chaunged al hyr fyrst entent within hyr hert gan bere haltres wold bere lo sone myght thou take hede idelnes drede namelyche lone haue wryte thou myght vnderstond wyte among gentyl nacyon loue occupacyon whiche kepe lustes saue shold euery gentyl hert haue lady chastysed ryght knyght may auysed whiche ydel wol serue longe may per caas deserue gretter peyne aboute lad hors haltres thy good ware ther loken abouen alle maydens hou falle shold take ensample whiche haue told forsothe lady venus whome serue wommen wol thank deserue may thylk loue eschelbe peramours mote sewe cnpydes lawe netheles men seyn suche loue selde pee ny euer vpon afpye iange lyuge fals enuye ful ofte medled dysese thylk loue wel ease whiche sett vpon maryage dare shewen vysage alle place openly grete meruaylle thy mayde wol lette tyme ne besette hast vnto thylke feste wherof loue al honeste men may recouer losse good wyse man yet neuer stood whiche may recouer tyme lore may mayden wel therfore ensample take straungeth hyr loue long chaungeth hyr herte vpon hyr lustes grene maryage sene thus yere two thre left wedded whyle charge myght bere child whiche wo ld forbere ne may yf sholde fayle mayden spousayle wold tarye take may shal per chaunce day let leuest wherof tale vnto thyn ere whiche culpable vpon dede thenke telle rede ic ponit exemplum super eode et narrat de filla iepte quc aim x sui patr voto holocaustum deo oc cidi offerri deveret ipsa pro eo quod virgo fuit prolem ad dayes old noble duc iepte hyght felle shold go fyght ageyne amon cruel kyng speke vpon thyng within hert made vowe god sayd lord yf thou wol graunte vnto men vyctorye shal tokne thy memorye fyrst lyf vnto peyne doth wold come ageyne fader herd doughter seyn therupon one assent maydens anone assent sholden mayden wende speke vnto ende gone dounes dale wepyng woful tale euery hyr maydenhode compleyneth vpon thilk nede childer bore wherof hath hyr youthe lore whiche neuer recouere may fel hyr last day come whiche shold take deth whiche may forsake thus deyde woful mayde thylk cause whiche ye speke hem wol trauayl seke cause loue vpon desert speke wordes couuert trauayl ye ment sone myn entent wol telle hou thought hou whilome men loues bought thorugh grete trauail strauge lode yt myght falle moche blood though ther shad fynde j wryten cryst bad man shold sle shold wynne ouer see lady left home passe salt fome whome cryst bad shold preche al world feyth teche rucken nest resten hem lyketh best al swetenes delyces thus defenden v vyces sytten hem self al amy de slee fyghte v bydde hem whome shold boke seith connerten vnto crystes feyth haue grete meruayle hou wold byd thyng nede fortune euery fame shal ende lere name ought yet befalle ydel man wol calle myn entendement vpon youre amendement myn holy fadre yen semeth reason cause demeth myn sone haue herde thou haste shryn n speke ydel fare semeth thou tharst thou myght spede therof sone wol rede abyde haste faste thy dye ben euery day caste thou nost chauce shall bety better wayte vppon tyde rowe ayenst stremes stronge though ye thynke long er caas reuolucyon heuene thy condicyon ne yet one acord dar make record venus whoos preest sythen thyder cam bad thy lyf wherof thou el gyltyf thou myght herof thy conscyence excuse greete dylygence whiche thou lone hast dyspended thou oughtest wel commended yf ther ought fay thou slouthest trauaylle armes absent thou makest argument thou saydest aboue hou achilles thurgh strengthe loue armes left throwe thou shalt tale knowe whiche contrayre thou shalt wi man maye fynde wryde knyghthode shal werred ust may nought thenne preferred bed mote forsake shelde spere hond take thing shal make hem glad worthy kynght wherof soo cometh honde tale thou shalt vnderstonde hou knyght shalle armes sewe hi ase eschewe hic dicit moris delectamento posi si mile arn sua preferre defet et ponit e emplum de v yxe cum ipse bello troiano prop r amorem e remanere domi voluisset na plus pater palamides cum tantis sermonibus allocutus est vlixes thoro sue coningis forth gone lamacus anone fett fore ylough euen sett fadre shold dryue sawe chyld blyue droof plough oute weye namplus tho bygan seye hath half iape cryed vlyxes thou art aspyed al thou woldest mene openlyche sene thou hast feyned al thyng whiche grete shame kyng lust ony slouthe thou wylt quarel trouthe armes thylk honour forsake duelle home loues sake better honour wynne loue whiche lykyng inne thy take worshyp vpon honde elles thou shalt vnderstonde worthy knyghtes alle grece whiche vnto calle towardes wol ryght wroth greue per chans whiche shal double shame moost hyundrynge thy name thou slouthe ony loue shalt thy lustes set aboue leue armes knyghthode whiche pryce thy manhode ought fyrst desyred whiche herte fyred vpon wyf herd nought one word ayeue ansuerd torneth hym haluyng ashamed within hym self tamed herte al soty loue chyualrye left hym leef loth troye hem forth goth myght excuse thus stant yf knyght refuse lust armes trauayle may worldes ease auayle yf worshyp al fatam sibi mortem portu troie prenunciauit sed ipse miliciam poa e quam ocia affectans troiam adijt vbi sue mortis pr c perpetue laudis troni ademit worthy kyng prothesalay passage lay toward troye letter syde e whiche tho maner hede took hyr wommans drede forth goth nought ne troye fyrst whiche ondeth took ar yuayle hym leuer bataylle seyth deyen knyght lyue al myght reproued name lo thus vpon worldes fame knyghthode hath euer yet beset whiche cowardye let adhn super eodem qua iler rex saul non obstante quam per samuelem phitonissa suscitatum et coniu atum responsum quam pse bello moreretur accepisset hostes tamen suos aggredens mi icie famam cunctis huius vite bla dimentis preposuit kyng saul also fynde samuel kinde thorugh yt ye phi ne hath lered samarye ed long tyme dede kyng saul hym axeth dede shal goo fyght none samuel hym sayd anone fyrst day bataylle thou shalt slayn withoute faylle ionathas thy sone also hou euer felle soo worthy knyght courage hath vndertake vyage wold achilles iuuentute animatus famosis sime milicie probitate post odum ad optauit loken ouermore hath shal le euermore knyythode yt prowesse grounded vpon hardynesse hym wol vndertake wold ensample take vpon forme knyghtes awe hou achilles forth deawe chyro whiche centaurus hyyt many wonder lere myght stood thylk tyme thus chyro centaurus within large wyldernesse lyon leone leopard tygre also hert
