batayle setten day chosen fesd knyghtes couered vnder shelde gyder come tyme sett eche one met fel foughten bothe fote stone rote whiche myght letten hem weye al voyde take weye smyten stroke fewe hercules whiche wold shewe grete strengthe none stert vpon hym al one caught hym armes strong geaunt wote may long endure vnder hard bondes thouyt wold oute hodes sleyghte som maner escape couthe hym self shape lykenesse adder slypt oute hond forth skypte efte fyght wole borneth hym bole gan belwe suche soune though ye world shold al go doune ground sporneth traunceth large horne auaun th cast hym aboute whiche stant hym doute wayteth wel cam hym bothe horne nam al one hym cast vpon grounde helde hym fast ne myght sleyghte hond gete heyghte tyl ouercome olde hercules hath wolde kyng hy graunted fulfylle axyng owne wylle whome serued hyr thought wel deserued thus grete deserte armes wan hyr lygge armes whiche hath hyr dere abought otherwyse shold e nought de pantasilia ama onie regina que hectoris amore colligata contra pireum achillis filium apud tro arma ferre eciam specialiter non recusauit ouer yf thou wylt vpon knyghthode matere hou loue armes ben acqueynted man may see bothe wryte peynted ferforth pantasile whiche quene femyne loue hector afore seke thonou armes eke troye cam spere shelde rode hyr self felde maydens armed al oute rescous towne al aboute whiche grekes byleyn nota qualiter pholipheme propter mi cie famam finibuo terre defensionem troie veniens tres puellas regno amaz nie quoli et anno perci piendas sibi et heredibus suis imperpetuum ea de causa habere promeruit fro paphagonye men seyn whiche stant vpon worldes ende tyme lyked eke wende polyphemus whiche kyng troye come vpon thyng helpe thylk noble towne al renoun worshyp worldes fame whiche wold bere name dede forth wan loue specyal fayr trybute euermo felle thylk tyme soo pirrus sone achilles worthy quene among pres dedely swerd sought oute fond slough hyr owne hond wherof kyng paphagonye pantasile amazo ie quene hym lad suche maydens hem left alyue shyp tyl aryue body bygraue wyth worshyp woman saue goodnes dede graunten hym lusty mede euery yere truage hym herytage maydens fayre shal haue thre wyse spedde e whiche fortune armes sought trauayle ease bought wyse shold baue fayled nought trauayled nota pro eneas regem tur num bello deuicit non folum amor auine sed et regnum italie sibi sub ugatum obtinuit eneas eke within itayle ne hadde wonnen bataylle done myght besyly ayene kyng turne enemy nought soueyne wonne hath hym ouer ronne gat p y wan hyr loue nsample aboue sone haue told thou myght wel see bold dar trauayle vndertake cause loue shal take cather vnto loues grace comonly worthy place wommen louen worthynesse manhood gentylnesse gentyls desyred fader inspyred thorugh low wote weye gentylnesse seye wherof telle yow beseche hic dicit generosi amoris se ius preferuntur super quo querit amans quid si generositas cuius veritatem questioni confessor per singula dissoluit th ground sone seche n dyffynycyon ldes constytucyon ath sei name gentylnesse n fortune rychesse whiche long tyme falle age hat man hyghe lygnage af r fortune thou myght thyng mat reson vnderstonde v ryches maye stonde thyng whiche fayleth ofte stant day alofte al world hath wones morowe fallyth al one oute ryches pouerte soo therof deserte whiche gentylnesse maketh abyde loke syde hou gentylman bore adam whiche al tofore eue wyf hem two al alyche gentyl tho generacyon make declaracyon maye gentylnesse bee reson yf se man byrthe mesure comon nature ueth euery man alyche wel poure ryche naked ben bore bothe lord hath clothe hym self ylk thro hath pourest rowe shal bothe passe hem whiche hath lasse worldes good charge lord charge shal compte hath lustes body whiche shal deye al though dyuers weye deth yet ther one ende whiche euery man wende wel begger lord one nature one acord whiche oure elder moder erthe bothe receyueth al alyche denoureth nother part fauoureth wote noo thynge kynde may gentylnes fynde lak vertu lak grace wherof rychesse many place men wene best stonde al sodenly goth oute honde vertu set courage may noo world saluage whiche myght take done aweye tyl bodye deye shal ryched soo may fayle neuermo may wel gentylnesse whiche yeueth grete sykernesse condycyon resonable intencyon whiche oute soule groweth vertu vyce knoweth wherof man vyce escheweth withoute slouthe vertu seweth gentylman thyng elles whiche ne whiche hath ne whiche maye al yet daye loues court taken hede poure vertu shal spede ryche vyce woweth selde loue alloweth gentylman withoute good though condycyon good yf man bothe two ryche vertuous also wel worth yet put hym self forth muse done besynesses nother good ne gentylnesse may helpen hem whiche ydel wo degre trauayle belongeth happeth ofte fongeth worship ease two euer yet hath loue honest sondry weye profyteth doth aweye vyce bookes seyn maketh curteys vyleyn coward hardyesse yeueth prowesse caused vpon loues reule hym manhood reule eke toward womanhede therof wold taken hede better affayted euery thyng men may see loue euer lustes grene gentyl folk sene whiche thyng ther may kynde arest trowe best loue shold acqueynte ne wold make queynte whyle last thus conclude last ben ydel semeth whiche vnto thyng loue demeth slouthen shold ouer sone also speke loue yf shal seke vertu moral eke among hooly bokes wyse fynde wryte suche wyse loueth dede loue aboue al hede whiche bath vertues lede al vnto mannes dede belongeth ydelshyp hateth al felaushyp slouthe euer despyse whiche dysdeyne hath al appryse acordeth man wyt reson syt hym wel trauayle vpon som thyng whiche myyt auaile ydelshyp comended euery lawe hath defended ensamples therupon noble wyse salamon whiche euery thyng insyght seyth byrdes flyght made man bore labour whiche nought forlore hem thynken thryue whiche alyue hem besy whylome wel scoles elles euery day ensample take yf make thyng whiche fyrst founden shold brought aboute lyues thenne longg wyttes grete myghtes strong vertues ful besynesse wherof worldes redynesse body bothe courage stant euer vpon auauntage drawe memorye name bothe storye vpon vertu hyr dede sondry bokes thou myght rede expedit manibus labor vt de cotidiams actibus et vita viue poseit homo sed qui doctrine causa fert men te labores preualet et merita perpetu ata parat hic loquitur centrum ciosos quoscu que et mayime cotra istos qui excelletis prudencie ingenium habetes ab que fructu operum torpescunt et ponit exeplu de diligencia predecessorum qui ad toci humani geneis doctrinam et auxi um suis centinuis laboribus studne gracia mediante diuina artes sci enc primitus inuenerunt euery wysedome parfyt hyghe god spyryt yafe men erthe vpon forme matere wolde make h wyse thus cam fyrst apryse goodes al good thorugh hem whylome vnderstode lore whiche hem yeue wherof lyue euery day lerne newe al tyme men sewe labour forth brought corn though souyt none al feldes oute wysedome cam aboute hem fyrst tho bokes wryte may euery wyse man wyte grete laboure e also thus none ydel two plough hath vndertake laboure whiche lond hath take took studye muse whiche wolde refuse labour wyttes alle wyse befalle labour bygonne ought conne besynes yet sene stant euer alyche grene al body deye name hem shal neuer aweye cronyke fynde cham who labour yet mynde whiche fyrst lettres fonde wrote bebrewe honde naturel philosophye fonde fyrst also clergye cadmus lettres gregoys fyrst made vpon owne choys theges thyng shal byfalle fyrst angnrre alle philemenon vysage fonde descryue courage cladius eldras sulpyces telmegis panulf frigidylles menander epyloquorus solius pandar iosephus fyrst endytours olde cronyke eke auctours heredot scyence metre ryme cadence fyrste whiche men note musyke also note man voys softe sharp fende iubal harpe mery soune whiche lyke fonde poli forth phisike zeuers fond fyrst portrature promotheus seulpture forme hem thought resemblaunce anone wronyt tubal yren stele fonde forge wrought wele iadael sayth book fyrst made nette fysshes took huntyng eke fonde chace whiche knowe many place tente cold cord stake set vp fyrst dydit make verconius coke ye fyrst made delycacye craft myn rae wolle fonde made clothe owne honde dellora made lyne tho woman grete engyne thyng yeueth mete drink doth labour swynk tylle londes set vynes wherof cornes wynes ben sustenaunce mankynde old bokes fynde saturnus owne wyt hath founde fyrst yett chapmenhode fonde weye eke coygne moneye sondry metal fyrst man hou metal cam place thorugh man wytte goddes grace route philosophres wyse contreueden sondry wyse fyrst gete myne trye fyne also grete dylygence fonde thylk experyence whiche cleped alconomye wherof syluer multyplye made eke gold also telle hou bodyes seuen specyal foure spyrytes ioynt al stant substaunce matere bodyes whiche speke planettes ben bygonne gold tytled sonne mone syluer hath part iren stond vpon mart leed saturne groweth inbiter ra be weth coper sette venus part mercurius hath quyk syluer falleth whiche book calleth fyrst hylk foure named spyrytes whiche ben proclamed spyryte whiche second sal armonyak found thyrd spyryt sulphur fourth sewend antimonium name hote blowyng fyres hote thynges whiche say wo dyuers way philosophre tolde gold syluer ben holde two pryncypal extremytees whiche al degree metalles ben acordyng thorugh kynde resemblyng man couthe awey take ruste whiche woxen blake sauour hardnesse sholden take lykenesse gold syluer parfytely worche sekerly bytwene corp spyryte ex metal parfyte seuen formes sett al yf one let remenannt may fayle otherwyse may auayle whome art foud euery poynt certayne bound ordeynen man may fynde craft wrouyt wey kynde noo fable nne man yt werk legynne mote awayte euery tyde thyng left syde fyrst dystyllacyon forth congellacyon solucyon dyssencyon kepe entencyon poynt sublymacyon forth calcynacyon approbacyon doo fyxacyon temporat letre fyre tyl parfyte elyxer thylk philosophres stone maye gete whiche many one philosophres whylome write yf thou wolt name wyte thylk stene ether two whiche clarkes maden bokes recorden kynde hem shal recorden nota de tribus lapidibus quos phi lcsophi compesuerunt quorum primus apis vegetabilis qiu sanitatem conser uat secundus dicitur lapis animalis que membra virtutes sensibiles fortificat tercius dicitur lapis minera que omnia metalla purificat et suum perfectum naturali potencta de ucit old phylosophres wyse weye kynde sondry wise stone made thurgh clergye fyrst shal specyfye lapis vegetabilis whiche propre vertu man bele serue kepe preserue body fro sekenesse alle tyl deth kynde vpon hym falle second stone behote apis animalis hote wh vertu propre couthe erc eye nose mouthe wherof man may see smelle taste degre fele go helpeth man bothe two wyttes frue vnder fongeth kepe hym belongeth thyrd stone fpecyal name cleped myneral whiche metal euery myne attempreth tyl fyne putteth hem suche weye al vyce goth aweye rust stynk hardnesse aud ben suche clennesse mynetal fynde transformeth al fyrst kynde maketh hem able conceyue thorugh vertu receyue bothe substaunce fygure gold syluer nature two ben thextremytees whiche propyrtees hath euery metal desyre helpe comfort fyre stone sayd whiche sonne mone layd rede whyte stone hath power profyte maketh multyplycacyon gold fyxacyon causeth habyte doth werke parfyte thylk elyxer whiche men calle alconomye byfalle hem whylome wyse stant al wyse speken fast thylk stone hou make knowe none soth experyence netheles grete dylygence setten vpon thylk dede spyllen spede alwey fynde lette whiche bryngeth pouerte dette hem ryche fore losse lucre lore gete pound spend fyu hou suche craft shal thryue manere vsed better refused worchen vpon wene thyng stat went thy knewe scyence hym self trewe vpon forme founded wherof name yet grounded hem fyrste founded oute thus fame goth aboute suche soughten besynesse vertu worthynesse whome yf name calle hermes one fyrst alle whome art applyed geber therof magnyfyed ortolan maryen among whiche auycen whiche fond wrote grete partye practyke alconomye who bokes pleynly stonde vpon craft fewe vnderstonde yet putten assay ben ful many day knowen lytel mene one wyte wene forme wordes trete yet faylen beyete moche lyte algate found wyte soo folowe lyne parfyte medycyne whiche grounded vpon nature wryten scrypture greke arabe caldee suche auctoryte fyrst founden oute weye al thou hast herd seye wherof cronyke lore shal stonde pryce euermore toward oure march latyns yf thou wolt hem whylome vertuous therto laboryous carment made engyne fyrst lettres latyne whiche tonge romayne cam wherof arystarchus nam forth donat dyndymus fyrst reule scole thus latyn shal compowued wyse shal souned euery word degre shal stonde vpon congruyte thylk tyme rome also tullyus cythero wryten vpon rethoryke men shal wordes pyke forme eloquence whiche men seyn grete prudence oute bre e ierome whiche langage knewe byble whiche lawe closed latyn hath transposed many another wryter eke oute caldee arabe greke grete labour bokes wyse ttanslateden another wyse latyns hem self also studye thylk tyme grete trauayl scole took sondry forme look may take euydence vpon lore scyence craftes bothe clergye among whiche poesye louers ouyde wrote taught loue hote maner shold akele confessor thy sone yf thou fele loue brynge tofore behold ouyde take lore fadre yf myght spede loue wold bokes rede yf techen restreyne loue ydel peyne lerne thyng whiche may lyche vnto grene tre men took rote aweye ryght herte shold deye loue withdrawe wherof touchend vnto sawe pursewe loue ydelshyp esche good sonne soth seye syker ony weye loue thou hast seyd best wol haue al rest doo noo treuayle nede reson spede loues cause wynne whiche dare thyng begynne thyng shold cheue ouer thou shalt byleue syt wel knowe ben vyces slowe whiche vnto loue done grete let thou thyn hert vpon hem set erdit homo causam linquene sua iu seperi et quasi dimidtum par su mortis habet est amore vigil venus et quam habet vigilanti obsequium thalamis fert vigilata suis hic loquitur de sompnelencia que ac idie cameraria dictum est cuius natura semunortua alicuius negocij vigi l obser seperi fero torpere recus r vnde quatenus amorem concernit confessor amanti diligencius opponit toward slowe progenye yet one copanye cleped sopnole ice whiche deth slouthe reuerence whiche chamberleyn many honderd tyme hath leyn slepe sheld wake hath loue tre e take wake wake wylle may couche deune bylle hath al hym lyst ofte goth bedde vnkyst sayth druerye wol leue sluggardye though yt noman wold allowe slepe leuer wowe maner thus nyghtes seeth lusty knyghtes len woman awey seulketh hare goth dde leyth hym softe sleuthe e dremeth ofte hou siyketh myre hou sytteth fyre claweth bare shankes hou clymeth vp bankes fallyth slades depe taketh kepe falle suche dreme ryght shyp ageynst streme routeth slepy noyse brustleth monkes froyse throwe panne whyle selde whanne may dreme lusty sweuene hym thynketh though heuene ye world holy speketh maketh exposycyon dysposycyon wolde suche wyse doth loue al seruyce thank shal deserue sone yf thou wolt loue serue rede thou good fadre certes noo leuer trouthe er set suche slouthe bere suche slepy snoute bothe eyen hede oute better fully dey suche sluggardye ony name god shelde modre chil e lay hyr wombe cloos wold rather antropos whiche goddesse deth anone ony breth fro moder cast thyng agast thanke god lachesys e cleto whiche felawe shopen suche destyne natyuyte werdes setten wold shopen shold eschewe slepe truandyse soo hope suche wyse loue ben excused sompnolence haue vsed certes fadre genius yet vnto hath thus al tyme yf befelle myght come duelle place lady slo e ne slepy dar wel vndertake hyr lyst nyghtes wake chambre carole daunce thynketh may auaunce may gone vpon hyr honde yf wynne kynges lond may h r hond beclyppe suche gladnes dauce skyppe thynketh touche floor roo whiche renneth moor nought lyght mowe ye wyten al thy tyme slepe hate fallyth gate soo lyketh daunce dye caste chaunce axe loue somme demaunde elles lyst commaunde rede troylus ryght wol thus alredy consente yf may hente somtyme among good leyser dar desyre telle part preye anone byddeth go weye seyth ferre nyght swere euen lyght falleth last may worldes ioye last mote nedes fro hyr wende watche make ende yf hede toke pytously hyr loke shal leue take ought mercy slake hir daunger whiche sayth euer nay seyth often haue good day loth take leue therfor whyle may byleue tary forth nyght long nought along slepe sone go tyl mote nede algate byd god hyr see doune knelend knee take leue yf shal kysse hyr goo forth al otherwhyle yf dore er come fully dore torne ayene feyne thyng though lost ryng somwhat elles wolde kysse hyr eftsones yf sholde selden spede see mote nede departe departe thanne al herte curse banne euer slepe made eye thynketh mote drye withoute slepe waken euer shold dysseuer fro hyr whome al lyght curse also nyght al wylle courage saye awey thou black ymage whiche thy derck cloudy face maketh al worldes lyght deface causeth vnto slepe awey whiche mote gone aweye oute lady companye slepy nyght defye wold thou lay presse proserpyne goddesse pluto helle kyng tyl see day spryng set slepe rysshe word syghe wysshe sey ne day yet lady may beholde though efte thynke forthermore somme man hou nyght doth ease hath thyng yt may hym please long nyghtes syde fayle goo besyde slepe wherof serueth whiche noman thank deserueth gete hem loue ony place hynderer grace maketh hem dede throw ryght stok ouerthrowe fadre wyse slepy nyghtes despyse euer myddes tale thynke vpon nyghtyngale whiche slepeth wey kynde loue bokes fynde thus last goo bedde yet myn hert lyeth wedde r bere cam fro though departe w l bock may shet hym oute hym nedeth nought gone aboute perce may hard wal thus e oueral hyr ef hyr bed myn herte goth softely taketh hyr arme feleth hou warme wyssheth also body tho fele felyth thus self tormente tyl dede slepe hente thousand score wel fore tormented slepe dreme shepe ne thynk wulle dretched fulle loue haue take kepe laugh wepe lese wynne ende begynne otherwhyle dreme te alone mete daunger left behynde slepe suche ioye fynde ne bede neuer awake heede take shal aryse vpon morowe al torned sorowe nought cause shal aryse mette suche wyse last bethought al wyne helpeth nought yet thynketh wylle wold haue ley slepe stylle meten euer suche sweuen slepy heuene confessor sone thou tellyst soo man may fynde tyme ago many sweuene hath certeyn al som men seyn sweuenes credence shewe euydence ful ofte soth thynges tokne thynk wrytynges telle tale therupon whiche felle old dayes gone hic ponit exemplum qualiter pre nostice veritatis quande que certitudine figurant et narrat cum ceix rex trocinie pro reformacione fratr sui dedalionis ancipit em transmutati peregre proficiscens ar lo giue patria dimersus fucrat uno mitten ridem nunciam suam partes chimerie ad domum sompni iussit ipse alceone dicti regis vxori hui rei euentum per sompnia certificaret quo facto al ona rem perscrutans corpus mariti suij vbi super fluctus mortu iactabatur inuenit que pro lore augustiata cupiens corpus amplec tere altum mare super ipsum prosi vnde dij miserti amborum corpus aues que ad huc alceones dicte sunt subito conuerterunt fynde wryten poesie ceyx kyng trocenye alceon wyfe whiche owne hertes lyfe hym loueth hath also broder whiche cleped tho dedalyon par caas fro kynde man forshape goshauk lykenesse wherof kyng grete heuynesse hath take thought courage gone vpon pylgremage straunge regyon hath deuocyon done sacryfyce preye myght ony weye wardes goddes fynde grace broders hele purchace myght reformed hath ben transformed purpos ende kyng redy wende whiche wold go shyp done hym felaushyp wyf vnto see hym brought al hyr herte hym besought tyme wold seyn thought come ageyne within sayth two monethis day thus al hast may took leue forth sayleth wepend hyr self bewayleth torneth ther cam fro monethes ago whiche set comyng herd tydyng care seche wherof goddes byseche tho bygan many wyse iuno sacryfyce aboue al dede lord hath bede wyte knowe hou ferd iuno goddes herde anone vpon matere irys bad h r messagyer slepes hous shold wende byd hym make ende sweuene shewen al caas lady hou irys fro hyghe stage whiche vndertake hath message reyny cope dede vpon whiche wonderly begone colour dyners hewe honderd mo men knewe heuene lyche vnto bowe bende cam donne lowe god slepe fond straunge lond whiche marcheth vpon chymery seyth poesye god slepe hath made hous whiche entaylle meruaylous vnder hylle ther caue whiche sonne may haue yt man may knowe ary poynt bytwene day nyght fyre spark dore whiche may chark wherof eye shold vnshet inward let speke withoute stant grete tre nyhe aboute wheron ther myght crowe pye lyght clepe crye cost crowe day ne best none whiche noyse may hylle al aboute round growend vpon ground popy whiche bereth seed slepe herbes suche hepe stylle water none rennend vpon smal stone whiche hyght ethes ryuer vnder hylle suche maner whiche yeueth grete appetyte slepe thus ful delyte slepe hath hous couche within chambre yf shal touche hebenus slepy tre boordes al aboute shold slepe softe vpon fether bed alofte lyeth many pylwe doun chambre strowed vp doun sweuenes many thousand fold thus come irys hold bed whiche blak goth therwith slepe spak wyse bede message iuno dede ful wordes reherseth er slepy eres perseth moche woo last slomerend eyen vpcast sayd hyr shal bedoo wherof among thousand tho within hous slepy specyal chese oute thre whiche shold dede fyrst hem rede morpheus who nature take fygure persone hym lyketh wherof therof entryketh lyf whiche slepe shal nyght ithecus hyght whiche hath voys euery soune theyr chere theyr condycyoun euery lyf thyrd sewend pantafas may transforme euery thynge ryght forme chaunge another kynde hem thre fynde sweuenes stant al thapparence whiche otherwhyle euydence whyle iape netheles shape morpheus nyght allone wereth vnto alceone lykenesse husbond al naked dede vpon stronde hou dreynt specyal two wen shal tempest blak clowde wode see wyndes loude met sawe hym dyen wherof bygan cryen slepend bedde laye noyse hyr affraye woman stert vp aboute whiche doute axen hou ferde ryght sawe herde sweuen hath told hem euery dele halsen al wele seyn tokne good tyl wyst hou stood hath comfort hyr herte vpon morowe vp sterte see met body lay withoute let drough whan cam nygh stark dede armes sprad syghe lord fletend vpon wawe wherof wyttes withdrawe whiche toke deth kepe anone forth lepte depe wold haue cauyt hym hir arm infortune double harme goddes heuen aboue beheld trouthe loue whiche worthy lady stood haue vpon salt flood hyr dreynt lord hyr also fro deth lyf torned soo shapen byrdes swymmed vpon wawe amyddes sawe hyr lord lyuend lykenesse byrd swymmend sort myght dysport vpon ioye whiche wynges anone sprad hym bothe may suffyse lypte kyst suche wyse whylome wonte doo wynges byr armes tho took lyppes softe hyr hard bylle soo ful ofte fondeth hyr byrdes forme myght hyr self conforme plesaunce wyf dyde lyf though hyr power lore hyr wylle stood fore serueth may wherof ylk day geder vpon see wone many doughter sone bryngen forth byrdes kynde men sholde take mynde alceon trewe quene byrdes sene alceon name bere lo thus may stere sweuenes take kepe oftyme man slepe may see shal betyde thy helpeth som tyde man slepe belongeth slouthe noo lyf vnderfongeth whiche loue appertenaunt fader vpon couenaunt dare wel make auo al lyf nowe ferforth vnderstonde yet took neuer slepe honde tyme wake though myn eye wold take myn herde euer ageyne neuertheles speke pleyne al haue sayd wakyng ye may toucheth lady swete otherwyse byhete straunge place go lyst thyng wake soo woman lyst playe see waye whome shold myrthe take lyst longe wake yf pure shame wold eshewe name ne shold haue cause none seye loo suche one hath forlore contenaunce thus among synge daunce feyne lust none fulofte syth fete thought whiche myn hert falleth nyght myn hert appallyth see hyr nought whiche waker thought thus tymelyche may ful ofte brood day take al heue goo wey byleue seen pe caas loues goo forth nought ne vnto bed alone may ther lygge syghe grone wysshen al long nyght tyl see dayes lyght yf sompnolence vpon youre conscyence myn holy fader demeth ye sone wel payd shepe thou sluggardye nyght loues companye esche west hast thy peyne thy loue dare pleyne loue vpon lust wakend euer wolde none ende therof long nyghte set wherof thou ware bett telle tale bethought loue slepe acorden nought hic dicit vigilia amantibus non sompnolencia laudanda est et ponit exemplum de cephal filio phebi qui nocturno silencio auroram amicam suam diligencius amplectens solem lunam interpellabat videlicet sol circulo ab oriete distanciori currum cum luce sua retardaret et luna spera sua longissima orbem circuiens noctem continuaret ita vt ipsum cephalum amplexibus amore volutum prius quam illa dy illucesceret suis deliciis adquiescere diucius permittere dignarentur loue lyst wake nyyt may ensayle take cephalus yt lay aurora swete may armes al longe nyght toward lyght herte sye day whiche morowe nyhe anone vnto sonne preyde lust loue thus seyde phebus whiche dayes lyght gouerneth tyl nyght gladest euery creature lawe thy nature netheles ther thyng whiche onlyche thy knoulechyngr belongeth pryuete loue dute whiche oxeth ben part sylence couert desyreth shadyd thus lyyt faded vesper weth hym alofte nyght long softe vnder clowdes derste stylle hath thyng wylle fo thy vnto thy myghtos hyghe thou whiche art dayes eye loue myght counseyl hyde vpon derk nyghtes tyde al myn herte byseche plesaunce myght seche hyr whiche syeth myn armes withdrawe baner thyn armes sete thy lyghtas ben vnborne sygne caprycorne hous appropred saturne preye thou wolt soiourne ben nyghtes derk longe loue haue vnderfonge whiche lyeth syde naked whiche wold ben waked lyst thyng slepe good take kepe tyme prayer lyke stere fyry cart ordeyne thou thy swyft hors restreyne lowe vnder erthe occydent toward thorrent scr le go long eke dyane preye whiche cleped art thy noblesse nyghtes mone goddesse thou gracyous eo thyn owne hous ayene phebus opposyte stond al tyme delyte byholde venus glad eye vpon astronomye due coustellacyon thou makeste profyfycacyon dost child begete whiche yf myght gete al myn herte wolserue nyght thy vygylle obserue loo thus lusty sephalus prayd vnto phebe phebus nyght lengthe drawe soo myght lawe thylk poynt loues heste whiche cleped nyghtes feste withouten slepe sluggardye whiche venus oute companye hath put awey thylk whiche lustles fer game chambre doth ful oft woo bedde falleth loue shold awayted slouthe whiche euyl affayted slepe hath made retenue thynge loue due al dette payeth none wote hou nyght gone ne hou daye come aboute slepe route tyl hyghe mydday aryse sephalus dyd otherwyse thou sonne host herd aboue amans fader hath loue bedde naked syde wolde eyen hyde slepe man certes touchend felle neuer yet whyle may catche slepe honde lyggend alone fonde dreme mery sweuene day yf falle may thought sweuen plese thynst somdele ese none comfort haue soo nedeth nought shal craue sonnes carte tarye ne yet mone carye cours long vpon heuene nought huene worldes good degre slepe yet see sowhat sweuene lyketh whiche afterward myn hert enteyketh fynde otherwyse wote seruyce sompnolence man doth sone certes thou sayst soth helpeth kynde somtyme physyk fynde whan take mesure whiche slepe mesure vpon reule belongeth ful oft sodeyne chaunce fongeth suche infortune hym greueth old bokes leueth sompnolence hou wryte maye man sothe wyte wold ensample take whyle good wake w rof tale poesye thynke specyfye hic loquitur amoris causa co tra istos qiu sopnolencie dediti ca que seruare tenentur amittunt et narrat cum yo puella pulcherrima iunone vaccam transformata argi custodiam sic deposita fuisset superuemens mercurius argum dormientem occidit vt ipsam vaccam pastura rapiens quo voluit secum perduxit ovyde thus telleth sawes hou iupiter olde dayes lay mayde whiche y cleped wherof iuno wyf wrothe goddesse yo torned lykenesse cowe goo ther oute large feldes al aboute gete hyr mete vpon grene therupon hyghe quene betook hyr argus kepe seldon wonte slepe yet honderd eyen al alyche wel sym herkne hou begyled mercurye whiche al affyled cowe stele cam desguysed pype wel deuysed vpon note musyke wherof myght eres lyke ouer affayted lusty tale awayted tyme thus felde cam argus beheld yo whiche besyde hym went pype anone hent gan pype manere thyng whiche slepy pypyng euer among told hym suche lusty song fool hath brought slepe none eye myght kepe hede whiche mercurye smote forth al anone fote hote stal cowe argus kept al fel slept ensample many mo mochel slepe doth ofte wo tyme wake yf man vyce take sompnolonce hym delyte men shold vpon dore wryte epytaphe vpon graue spylle nought saue shaped though dede thymy sone hold vp thyn heds lete slepe thyne eye englue reason due fader touchend ryght told ofte bedde sholde maye slepe though wolde loue euer fast byme whiche taketh none hede due tyme shal myn eye close none hert wol oppose hold scole suche wyse tyl day aryse selde slepe thus fro sompnolence kepe myn eye thy yf ther ought elles degre axe forth sone yi slouthe whiche moder forth drawer noryce man many dredeful vyce hath yet another last alle whiche many hath made falle myght neuer aryse wherof thou shalt auyse er thou thy self mysfare vyce wol declare nil fortuna iuuat vbi desperacid dit quo desiccat humor non viridesat humus magnanimus sed amor em ponit inde salutem cosequitur prospera fata fauent hic loquitur super vltima specie acadie que tristicia siue desperacio dicitur auus olstinata condicio tocius con solacionis spem deponens alicuius remed quo kberari poterit fortunam sib euenire impossible credit whan slouthe doth al yt may dryue forth long day tyl bycome nede last vpon dede laketh hou tyme lore woo begone therfore within thought conceyueth trystesse hym self deceyueth wanhope bryngeth inne comfort begynne euery ioye hym dylayed within herte affrayeth thousand tyme one breth wepend wyssheth deth fortune fynt aduerse wol happe reheree though world al forlore sayth allas lore shal lyue shal doo fortune foo wote wel god wol helpe shold ioye yelpe ther bote care ouer cast al welfare shapen al stryf allas neuer lyf fullyche ouertake thus wol sorowe make god hym myght auayle yet ne wol trauayle helpe hym suche nede slouteth vnder suche drede whiche affermed hert ryght myght nought asterte worldes woo whiche inne also falle synne hym thynketh fer culpable god wol mercyable soo grete synne foryeue thus leueth shryue yf man thylk throwe wold hym couseyle wol knowe soth though man fynde trystesse suche kynde mayntene fely hath hym obstynacy whiche within suche slouthe forslaketh al trouthe wol reson bo yet alowe owne skylle hede thus dwyneth tyl dede hyndryng owne estate man obstynate whan hope foloweth last whiche may longe last tyl slouthe make hym ende god wote whether shal wende sone ryght suche manere louers heuy chere sorowen nede whan torned theyr spede self rede lesen hope spede stynten loue pursewe thus faden hyde hewe lustles hertes waxe herof wold axe thou sone art one tho good fadre soo take poynt knowe elles ouerthrowe al euer ye haue seyd sorowe euermore vnteyd secheth oueral veynes counseylle peynes bote doo therto thus withouten hope goo soo wyttes ben empeyred sayd despeyred wynne loue thylke swete withoute whome behete myn herte bestad ryght may neuer glad trouthe shal lye pure sorowe whiche drye sayth wol nought dretchyng myn owne thoughe suche wanhope falle ne vnnethes calle speke ony grace lady grace purchace yet say nought al myn defaulte neuer yet stede tyme bede ne sayde dorst tolde neuer fonde wolde ought knewe myn entent speke goodly word assent netheles dar seys yf synful wold prey god foryeuenesse half grete besynesse haue lady lak axyng mercy sholde neuer come helle aud thus may sothly telle sauf ceye byd trystesse al amydde fulfylled dysperaunce therfor yeue penaunce myn holy fader lyketh sone thy herte syketh sorowe myght thou amende tyl loue grace wol sende thou thyne owne cause empeyrese tyme yt thou thy self dyspeyrest uot thyng auayleth hope herte fayleth suche soor ina rable eke goddes ben vengeable man may ryght wel feede old bokes rede thyng whiche hath byfalle ensample hic narrat qualiter iphis gi theucri filius ob amore cuuisda puelle nomine araxarathen quam ne que donis aut precibus vincere potuit de perans ante patris ipsi ianuas noctanter se suspendit vnde dij comoti dic tam puellam lapidem durissuuam transmutarunt quam rex theucer vna cum filio suo apud ciuitatem sala minam templo veneris pro perpetua memoria sepeliri locari fecit whylome old dayes fer mese ye kyng theucer knyyt son iphis loue e soo mastred hath set al courage regard lygnage vpon mayde lowe astate though potestate worldes good subgett loue put suche plyte excedeth mesure reson hym self assure nought prayd lasse loue hym layd loue vn wise costreyned reson streyned lustes herte seweth drede shame esche weth shold toke hede saue kepe hyr womanhede thyng stood debate bytwene lust estate yaue send spak mouth yet ought euer couth vnto spede fond weye cast hope aweye within hert gan dyspeyre fro day day empeyre hath lost al delyte lust slepe appetyte thurgh strength sone lasseth wyt reson ouer passeth whiche lyf ne tought deth vpon hym self sought nyght weye nam wyst none bycam nyght derk mone shone fore gate cam sone yong mayde woful word allas dedely pleyntes bygan stylle noman herde sayde thus thou cupyde thou venus fortuned whoos ordenaunce loue euery man chaunce ye knowen al myn hole hert ne may hondes asterte euer crye yet deyneth plye ne toward ere enclyne thus see noo medycyne make ende quarele deth shal stede hele ha thou woful lady dere whiche duellest thy fadre slepest thy bed ese thou wotest thyng dysese thou vnmete lord sweuene shalt thou mete dremes hast thou hond thou slepest stond though deth deserue shal thy loue sterue shal kynges sone deye loue felonye whether thou therof haue ioye sorow shalt thou see dede morowe hard hert abouen alle deth whiche shal falle thou wolt grace shal told many place dede loue trouthe thy defaulte thy slouthe thy daunger shal many mo ensample euermo woful deth recorde word took corde whiche vpon gate tre henge hym self pyte morowe cam nyght gone men come oute syghe anone yonge lord dede hous withoute dede noman knewe cause wepyng ther cry mayden herde sawe thyng hou mysferd auone wyst mente al cause hou wente al world told oute preyth hem aboute take wngeaunce cause thylk chaunce kynges sone spy taketh vpon hyr self gylt al redy peyne whiche ony man hyr wol ordeyne yf ony wold sayth hyr self shold doo wreche hyr owne hond thorugh oute world euery lod euery lyf therof shal speke hou hyr self shold wreke wepeth cryeth swouneth oft cast hyr eyen vp alofte sayd among ful pytously god thou wost wel iphis thus byseyn ordeyne many may seyn thousand wynter hou suche mayden dyd amys dyde ne dyde noo pyte hym whiche loue lore doo pyte therfore word felle grosid swoune lay astound goddes whiche pleyntes herde sawe hou wofully ferde lyf awey took anone shopen stone forme hyr ymage body bothe vysage meruaylle thyng vnto place cam kyng eke quene many mo wysten foo haue told aboue hou iphys dede loue refused helden al men excused wondren vpon vengeaunce kepe remembraunce fayre ymage mayden lyche companye noble ryche torch grete solempnyte salamyne cyte lede carye forth dede corp seyn shall besyde thylk image haue sepulture begraue corp image thus cyte venus goddesse temple geder bothe forth lad thylke image myracle sette vpon hyghe pynacle al myght knowe vnder maden lowe tombe ryche none marble eke iaspre stone wheryn iphys byloken euermore shal spoken men shal sothe wyte haue epytaphe wryte thyng whiche shold abyde stable lettres granen table marble sayd thys lyeth slouy hym self iphis loue araxarathen eusample tho woman suffren men dyen soo forme man may seen also hou torned flesshe bone fygure stone nesshe hard beware thy afterward ye men woman bothe two ensampleth tho loo thus sone seye greueth dyuers weye despeyr man falle whiche last braunche alle slouthe thou hast herd deuyse wherof thou thy self auyse good thou deceyued wherof hope grace weyued fadre hou stonde nou haue pleynly vnderstonde slouthes court propyrte wherof touchend degre euer thynk ware ouer dare al myn hert yow byseche ye wold enforme teche youre apryse loue al wel wyse may clene shryue confessor sonne whyle thou art alyue hast also thy ful mynde among vyces whiche fynde yet one suche seuene whiche al world hath set vneuene causeth many tymes wrong cause hath vnderfong wherof thou shalt forme matere expliat liber quartus incipit liber quintus stat auaricia nature legibus et que largue amor poscit strict e illa vetat omne est nimium vi c osum dicitur auru vellera sicut oues seruat auarus opes non decet vt solo ser abitur o sed amori debet homo lam solus habere suam first hyghe god bega world kynde man falle grete encrees worldes good tho prees al set comune speken fortune lese wynne tyl auaryce brought inne yt ye world woye man hore shepe oxe men knewen money tho went pee oute weye werre came euery syde whiche al loue leyd asyde comon propre made stede shouel spade sharp take honde wyse cam londe wherof men made dyches depe hyghe walles kepe gold whiche auaryce encloseth al lytel hym supposeth though myyt al world purchace thyng may embrace gold catel lond lete neuer oute hond gete hym halt fast though world sholde euer last lyche vnto helle bokes telle cometh ther lasse shal departe neuermore thus hath cofer loken shal ben vnstoken hym lyst haue syght gold hou shyneth bryght theron may loke muse wyse dare vse take part lesse power euermore hym lakketh hath inough oxe draweth plough hym self hath profyte shepe ryght plyte wulle bereth vpon day another taketh flees aweye thus hath yt nought ne hath therof part ne tath seye hou suche man hath good reson vnderstood inproperlyche sayd good hath hym halt hym taid ne gladeth nought alle vnto good thralle subget thus serueth shold mayster suche kyng thauarous sone thou art amerous telle yf thou farest loue soo fadre semeth auarous yet neuer ye setten caas ye tolden aboue ful possessyon loue yet neuer fore soo thynketh wel therfore may excuse wel dede wylle withoute drede yf tresour myght gete shold neuer foryete ne wold faste holde tyl god loue hym selue wolde deth v shold departe two leueth wel loue euen myn owne lyf swete lusty wyf myght one welden wylle wold holde hyr stylle wyse taketh kepe wold kepe yet frydaye wold fast though kepte holde fast fy bagges kyst ynough yf kyst certes yf myn leuer myn gold al worlde ryche ne myght make ryche inly good set nought good myght gete suche thynge tresour kynge though wold faste holde therto mochel byholde myyt pype lasse suffre ouerpasse wyll thus wold ben auarous yf shold fadre herd sey hou auarous hath yet somme wey wherof may glad may hym lyst tresour se grope fele al aboute ful ofte shet ther oute worthy tresour lyf lyche vnto tolden fore hou oxe yok hath bore thyng shold hym auayle wyse trauayle euer hath welfare wote wel haue care sayth loues knaue nought ne haue deme owne thought yf auaryce nought sone haue wonder thongh thou serue put vnder loue whiche kynde acordeth soo euery book recordeth kynde plesaunce man aboue sustenaunce vnto gold shal serue bowe may reason auowe auaryce netheles may geten encrees gold wold serue kepe taketh nought elles kepe fylle bagges large al hym charge ne parteth nought al kepeth seruaunt shal thus though multyplye gold withoute tresorye man nought amended gold yf dyspended man vse wherof rede tale take therof good heede byfelle old tyde telleth v c erk ouyde achus whiche god wyn acordannt dyuyn preest whiche cillenus hiyt fel nyght th preest druke goth straid rof men euyl apayd fryg ond went last chorle hym hent strengthe felaushyp vpon drunkeshyp bounden hym cheynes fast forth lad hym also fast kyng whiche hyght myde wold vyce hyde curtoys kyng toke hym hede bad men sholde hym lede chambre kepe e leyser slepe tho preest sone vnboud vpon couche fro ground slepe le softe inough woke yt kyng hym drouy presence dyd hym chere preest suche manere wh se yt hym lyketh duelleth al bachus telleth cam hym ageyne bachus herd seyn hou myde hath done curtesye hym thynketh vylony reward hym dede myght godhede vnto kyng god appereth clepeth hereth god myde thanketh fayre soo debonayre toward prest bad hym sey thyng wold preye shold haue worldly good kyng glad stylle stood axyng doute al world casteth aboute thyng best state hym self stood debate vpon thre poyntes whiche fynde ben leuest vnto mannes kynde fyrst hem delyte two ben worshyp profyte thought yf craue delyte though delyte may haue delyte shal passen age syker auauntage euery ioye bodely shal ende woo delyte thy wol chese yf worshyp axe world lordshyp occupacyon proude imagynacyon whiche maketh hert veyn within certeyne wynne lorde knaue al one weye bore deye yf profyte axe wolde maner sholde worldes good haue sykernesse euery theef vpon rychesse wayteth robbe stele suche ood cause harmes fele also though man one al world within wones tresour myght haue euery deele yet one man dele toward hym self thynke clothynge mete drynke oute take vanyte hath lord degre thus vpon poyntes dyuerse dyuersly gan reherce poynt hym thought best pleynly gete hym rest syker weye cast netheles yet last felle vpon couetyse gold sondry wyse thought haue sayd fore tresour may sone forlore inly grete desyre touchend suche recouer hou myght cause auayle gete hym gold withoute fayle within hert thus preyseth gold sayth hou peyseth aboue al metal gold sayth may lede hoost make werre ayene kyng gold put vnder al thyng set whome hym lyst aboue gold make hate loue werre pee ryght wrong long short short long withoute gold may fest gold lorde man beste may hem bye selle soo man may sothely telle al world gold obeyeth thy kyng bachus preyth graunte hym gold excedeth mesure hym nedeth men tellen maladye whiche callyd ioropesy resembled vyce weye kynde auaryce idropesye drynketh thyrsteth hym thynketh may drynke fylle soo may thyng fulfylle lustes appetyte ryght suche maner plyte stant euer auaryce euer stood hath worsdes good wolde kepe streyte euer coueyte ryght suche condicyon wythoute good discrecyon kyng auaryce smete al worlde myght wete bachus preyd wherupon honde leid sholde thorugh touche anone become gold therupon god hym graunteth bad tho kyng fryge glad put assaye al hast maye toucheth toucheth hond al gold stone tre leef gras floure fruyte al gold thus toucheth may last hongre att last hym took soo mote nede wey kynde hongre fede clothe leyd boord set alle forth byfore hym set dissh drink cuppe meet wold drynk ete mouth anone cam nyghe al gold syghe auayrce folye bygnne crye preyde bachus foryeue gylt suffre hym lyue suche fore soo nought forlore god whiche greuaunce herd toke routhe vpon repentauce bad hym goo forth redyly vnto flood fast whiche paceole hyght whiche sone euer myght sholde hym wasshe oueral said hym shal recouere hys fyrst astate ageyn kyng right herd seyn flood goth fro lond wesshe hym bothe fote hond forth al remenaunt hym set uendunt sawe meruayles strauge flood coloure gan chaunge grauel smal stone gold torne al attones quyte thus fortune chaunge lad sawe touche gone goth hym home ryght forth soone lyueth forth dyde er put al auaryce fer ryches gold despyseth seyth mete clothe suffyseth thus hath kyng experyence hou fooles done reuerence gold whiche owne kynde lasse worth rynde sustenaunce man fode made lawes goode al thyng set vpon skylle lede people tylle l nd lyue vnder lawe also shold forth drawe bestayl seche none encrees f gold whiche breche pee man may fynde wryte fere tyme gold smyte coygne men floren knewe wel nyhe noman vntrewe nother shelde ne spere ne dedely wepen bere toune withoute walle whiche closed ouer alle tho bro ge lond whiche taketh euery cause hod may yt man knowe hou floreyn moder fyrst malengyn brynger alle werre wherof world stant oute herre thorugh counseyl auary whiche owne propre vyce whiche helle wonderful may neuermore ful euer cometh therynne awey ne may neuer wynne sone myn thou late al suche auaryce go take thy part thou hast byd thou wast hold largesse mesure yf thou see creature whiche thorugh pouert falle nede yeue hym somme good rede hym wol yeuen peyne shal haue elles peyne among al bynethe helle whiche men calle woful peyne tantaly whiche shal redely deuyse hou theryn men stond helle thou shalt vnderst nd flood thylk offyce whiche serueth al auaryce man stonde shal therin stant vp euen chynne aboue hede also hougeth fruyt whiche peyne longeth fruyt toucheth euer one ouerlyppe therupon suche thyrst honger hym assayleth neuer appetyte ne fayleth wende hongar fede fruyt withdraweth hym nede though haue hede hyghe fruyt euer alyche nyghe honger wel also though hym thurst sore water bowe adoune flood suche condycyon aualeth drynke areche may loo whiche wreche mete drynk hym couthe yet ther comth none mouth lyche peynes flood stant auaryce worldes good hath inough yet hym nedeth scarcenes hym forbedeth euer honger trauayleth hym alyche sore peyned oueral thy thy goodes oueral sone loke thou dyspende wherof thou myght thy self amende bothe eke place also yf thou wolt purchace loued thou must vse largesse yf thou refuse yeue thy loues sake reson thou take loue thou woldest craue thy yf thou wolt grace haue gracyous largesse auaryce sekenesse esche aboue al thyng take ensample myde kyng flood helle also inough al wo though matere fynden men ought auaryce esche man thylk vyce sewe gete hym self lytel rest though body rest hert vpon gold trauayleth whome many nyyt drede assaileth though lygge bed naked herte euermore awaked dremeth lyeth slepe hon besy kepe tresour noo theef stele thus hath woful wele ryght wyse thou thy self wolt wel auyse louers suche inough wol vnto reason bough e come aboue maystres loue sholden glad loue ben moost bestad fayn wolden holden hir herte hir eye ouerall wenen euery man theef stele awey hem leef thus thorugh owne fantasye fallen ielousye hath shyp broke cable euery wynde meuable amans fader ye telle haue herde oftyme telle ielousye yet vnderstond neuer wherfore wold byseche ye wold enforme teche maner thyng myght sone hard netheles haue herd herkne thou shalt ansuerd nota de ielousia cuius fantastica suspicio amorem quentuis fidelissimu mul ciens sine causa corruptum imagina tur among men lak manhod maryage vpon wyshode maketh man hym self deceyueth wherof yt conceyueth ylke vnesy maladye whiche cleped ielousye whiche yf propyrte shal telle nyorte worcheth man feuer cotydyan whiche euery day wol come aboute man oute home yf man wol wone feuer comon wone moost greuous man eye maketh hym tote prye loue euer go shal hyr lytel mysteppe seeth al eye walkend oueral synge dauce seeth lest countenaunce loke man syde hym rowne ony tyde laugh oure eye euery houre draweth nyght soo withoute lyght anone al game shente set parlement speke cometh bedde sayth yf wedde wold neuermore haue wyf torneth stryf lust loues dute al vpon dyuersyte fresshe wel arayed sayth baner dysplayed cle e gestes fro weye yf wel beseye hyr lyst glad beryth hond mad loueth husbond sayth may wel vnderstond yf wold companye shold afore eye al plesaunce myyt daye ne nyght thyng best lyueth wel oute al rest euer hym lyst seyn dare speke one word ageyn wepeth hold hyr lyppes cloos may wel wryte saunce poos wyf whiche suche one maryed al woman waryed feuer jelousye eche dayes fantasye soro euer alyche grene loue sene whyle hym lyst home abyde wol oute ryde hath redy spye abydyng companye jangler euyl mouthed one ne may ther gone ne speke one word ne one loke ne wol wende croke torne owne entent though thyng honour ment lord comth home ageyn jangler must somwhat seyn withoute withynne feuer euer begynne cometh ende tyl deth hym hath made ende though ne ne see wyte manere al honoure womanhede therof ielous taketh none ede man loue vnkynde cast staf doth blynde fynt defaulte none dremeth stone hou leyd groneth ofte lyeth pylowe softe ther nought stryf chest loue shold make rest grete thyng yf kysse thuo hath loste nyghtes blysse suche tyme grutcheth euer beryth hond ther leuer wold another stede hym abedde tho wordes mo jelousye torneth fro lyeth vpon syde draweth hyr asyde ther wepeth al nyght peyne dyght thought hath beset bonde whiche may vnknet wote tyme ofte cursed euer gold vnpursed whiche leyd vpon book al forsook loue hym al late pleyneth algate mo e forbere hym owe though ne wold allowe man lord thylk feyre may woman empeyre speke ought ageyne thy wylle thus beryth peyne stylle yf feuer woman ke shal wel harde sha yf bothe see fynde matere dare self pleyne thus suffreth double peyne loo thus sone haue ryt thou myght jelousye wyte feuer condycyon whiche fal suspectyon wherof feuer groweth olde bokes weth may fynde hou v teche telle hou feuer jelousye somdele groweth sotye loue somdele vntrust sekeman left lust may sauoure gete hateth owne mete ryght feuerous maladye whiche caused fantasye maketh jelous feble plyght leue loue appetyt thorugh feyned informacyon imagynacyon fynally taken heede men may wel make lykelyhede bytwene hym whiche auarou gold hym ir u loue one degre stonde bothe semeth one wold haue bagges styl nought departen wyll dare theues slepe fayne wold tresour kepe maye wel glad euermore adrad louers gone aboute aunter yf put hym oute haue bothe lytel ioye wel loue moneye hast thou sone techyng ielousye knowlechyng thou myght vnderstonde fro cometh eke whome lyke beware thy thou syke thylk feuer haue spoke wol hym self wroke loue hateth thyng men may fynde lore hem whylome wy hou speke many wyse fader sothe ye seyn loke ageyn byfore tyme hou falle wherof myght ensample falle suche men ben ielous maner greuous ryght fayn wold ensample good sone thy prayere suche ensamples fynde soo comen mynde vpon poynt tyme gone thynke tellen one hic ponit confessor exemplum contra istos maritos quos ielousia la et narrat qualiter vul canus cuins vxor venus extitit suspicionem inter ipsam martem concipies eorum gestus diligencius explorabat vnde contigit cum ipse quadam vice ambo inter se pariter amplexantes lecto nudo inuenit et exclamas omnem cetum deorum et deatum ad tatum spectaculum conuocauit super quo tamen derisum pocius quam remedium tota cohorte consecutus est ovyde wrote many thynges among ye whiche wrytinges told tale poesie whiche toucheth ielousye vpon certeyne caas loue among goddes al aboue felle ylke tyme thus god af fyre whiche vulcanus hote hath craft forth assygned smyth iupyter fygure bothe vysage stature othly malgracyous yet hath within hous lykyng lyf fayre venus wyf mar whiche bataylles god eye vnto whiche chyualrous felle hym ben amerous thought grete pyte see soo lusty one coupled hard wyght peyne day nyght dyd yf wynne myght good insyght toward noble knyghtly lord loue fel acord lakketh nouyt tyme place ny syker grace two hertes fallen one wyse wayte neuer none somtyme ne mete thus fayre lusty swete mar hath ofte companye thylk vnkynde ielousye whiche euermore herte opposeth maketh vulcanus supposeth wel ouerall hym self sayde shal better yf may felle vpon day thyng slyghly ledde fond hem bothe edde al warme echone naked craft al redy maked strong cheynes hath hem bounde geder hem founde lefte hem bothe lygge gan crye tho vnto goddes al aboute assembled route come al one see none amendes bat rebuked hem loues frendes sayd blame yf ther felle hym ony shame thorugh mysgouernauce thus lost contenaunce god lete cause falle scorne owen e lo en mar oute hondes wherof erthely husbondes euer myght ensample take suche chaunce hem ouertake vulcanus wyf bewrayd blame vpon hym self ho layd wherof shame whiche ought lore euery man leueth reulen hym matere though suche hap loue asterte yet shold apoynte herte ielousye wrought feyne though wyst nouyt yf ete ouerpasse sklaunder shal wel lasse ese stonde thou myght wel vnderstonde man shal nedes le lasse harme chese ielousye vntryst maketh ful many harme aryst whiche elles shold aryse yf man wold hym auyse byfelle vulcanus hym ought reson thynke thus syth god therof shamed wel shold erthely man blamed take vpon hym vyce thy sone thyne offyce beware thou nought ielous whiche oftyme hath shent hous fadre ensample bard hou suche thyng heuen ward among goddes myght falle one god alle whiche lord heuene helle yf lyke telle hou suche goddes come place ye myght mochel thank purchace shal wel taught alle confessor sonne soo ouerall hem stonden mysbyleu suche fygures wherof may wel iustyfyed may deifyed taketh awey honour whiche due creatour yeueth creature doth grete forteture caldee netheles vpon feyth though le holde affermed creaunce helle penaunce folk whiche stant oute byleue shal ceyue byleue caldees loo wyse stant byleue oute assyse egypt worst alle feyth fals hou falle dyuers beestes honoure though goddes netheles yit forth al goddes
