thynke telle suche wyse shal hym pryse de hebreorum seu iudeorum secta quorum sinagoga coclesia cristi superueniente defecit flood fro whiche noe sauf ye world degre made seyth new agein flour fruit gras grein beest byrde mankynde whiche euer hath god vnkynde stondynge al fare world made bare afterwarde restored amog men nothyng mored toward god good lyuyng al torned lykyng flesshe foryete whiche yafe hem lyfe mete heuene erthe creatour thus cam forth grete errour hyghe god ne knewe maden goddes newe thou hast herd sayd fore man tyme bore ne bad choys god whome yafe voys wherof mysbyleue cam tyme abraham fond oute ryght weye men shold obeye hyghe god whiche weldeth al euer hath done euer shal heuen erthe eke helle thyng myght may telle patryarche lygnage forbad none image enclyne shold wyse offrend sacryfyse al hoole hertes loue vnto myghty god aboue shold hym mo thus thylk tyme tho bygan feyth vpon erthe whiche byleues ferthe ryghtwysenes conceyued must nedes receyued hym al ryght inne hyghe god whiche wold wynne people vnto owne feyth abraham ground leyth made hym multyplye grete progenye egypte al ouer sprad pharao wrong hem lad seruytude ayene pee tyl god lete sende moyses make delyueraunce peple grete vengeannce took whiche wonder kyng slayn ye lod put vnder god bad reed see deuyde whiche stood vpryght euery syde yafe vnto people weye foote passed dreye gone forth desert kepe hem couert dayes sonne brent large cloude hem ouer went wyssen hem nyght fyry pyler hem alyght hongre pleyn myghty god began reyne manna fro heuen doune grounde wherof eche hem hath fonnde fode suche ryght hym lyst shold vpon hym tryst right set tonne broche perced hard roche spronge oute water al wille man beste hath bronke wyll afterward yafe lawe moyses hem withdrawe shold fro bad wyse lad tyl took possessyon lond promyssyon caleph iosue march vpon suche degre departen lygnage eche hem herytage pourpartye hath vnderfonge thus stood byleue longe whiche prophetes gouerned eke peple lerned grete honour sholde hem falle moost nede alle fayleden cryst bore hou feyth haue lore nedeth nought tellen al mater soo general luafer best heuene ought moost haue stond euene towardes god took debate obstynate wold nought trouthe enclyne fel euer ruyne adam eke paradys stood moost al pry state innocence ayene god brake defence fell hye place wey ryght suche maner weye iewes best plyght shold moost parfyght haue stonde vpon prophecye tho fellen moost folye hym whiche fro heuen come mayde flesshe hath nome amonge hem born fed men wold nought sped goddes sone one voys henge slough vpon croys wherof parfyte lawe fro forth forth drawe stonde meryte bnt truage folk subgect withoute propyrte place lyuen oute goddes grace dyspers al londes oute thus feyth come whylome iewes stood whiche nonght parfytely good speke falle feyth abouen alle trouthe comprehended wherof ben al amended de fide cristiana qua perfecte le gi complementum summi isterij sacramentum nostre que saluacionis fundamentum infallibiliter consistere credimus hyghe almyghty mageste ryght wysenes pyte synne whiche adam wrouyt sawe tyme souyt sende sone fro ye heuene sette man soule euene whiche forfalle vpon poynt whiche byfalle ne myght hym self aryse gregorye sayth apryse helpeth nought man bore goddes sone vnbore thurgh fyrst synne whilom adam brouyt v inne sholden al men lost cryst restoreth thylk lost bought flesshe blood yf thynken hou stood thylk raunson whiche payd seynt gregorye wrote sayd al behouely man wherof woo bygan cause al welthe whiche welle helthe hyghe creatour lyf vpon nede suche stryf wold creature take hym self forfeture suffre man sake thus may reson wel forsake ilke synne orygynal ne cause specyal man worshyp last whiche shal withouten ende last cause godhede assembled manhede vyrgyne nome oure flesshe man become bodely fraternyte wherof man degre stondeth worthy haue told dyd erst thousand fold thorugh baptysme newe lawe whiche crist lord felawe thus hyghe goddes myght whiche vyrgyne alyght man soule hath reconsyled whiche long ben exyled stant feyth vpon byleue withoute whiche may man acheue gete hym paradys ageyn byleue certeyn ful grace vertu man clepeth ihesu clene lyf forth good dede may faylen heuen mede soo stonde vppon byleue euery man may wel acheue whiche taken hath ryght feyth elles gospel seyth saluacyon ther maye none preche therupone thus cryst bad apostle alle who power falle v holy chirche good dedes wirche feyth suffyseth nought good dede also wrought good thou thy whiche thorugh baptysme propyrly art vnto crystes feyth professed wa e thou oppressed antecrystes lollardye iewes prophecye set god auauntage ryght newe tapynage lollardye goth aboute sette crystes feyth doute sayntes v fore whome feyth first vp bore holy chirche stood releued oughten better byleued whiche men knowe holy though feyne blowe lollardye mannes ere yf thou wylt lyue oute fere suche newe lore rede eschewe hold forth ryght weye sewe thyn auncestres dyde thou byleue nought amys cryst wrought fyrst taught soo dede word araught yafe ensample persone wordes haue alone lyke tree leues grene vpon whiche fruyt sene nota cum anthenor palladium troie templo minerue abstulit tho ibidem summ sacerdos auro corruptus oculos auertit et sic malum quasi non videns scienter fieri permisit preest thoas whiche mynerue temple serue palladyon troye kepte vnder keye moneye anthenor whiche hath nome hath suffred antherior come palladyon stele wherof worshyp wele troians ben ouerthrowe thoas throwe anthenor iewele took wynkend cast awey look deceyte wyle shold hym self begyle hyd eyen fro syght wende wel myght excuse fals conseyence wote yf thylk euydence tyme estate excuse myght prelate nowend hou feyth dyscresyth al moral vertu cyth wherof keyes bere yet hem lyketh stere goo ly eye see world aduersyte wol labour vndertake kepe hem bytake cryst dyed hym self feyth oure ferful prelate seyth lyf swete kepeth feyth vnholpe slepyth vnder hyr ease entende lust syf dyspende euery man hym lyst thus stat world fulfylled mi noman seeth ryght weye wardes chirche keye thorugh myshandelyng mys wreynt worldes wawe hath ny dreynt shyp whiche peter hath stere forme kept matere transformed wyse yf gostly wyse prelate good old dayes stood lytel nede among men taken hede pseudo telle whiche come duelle sowe cokkyll corn tylthe nere hand lo n whiche cryst sewe fyrst hond stant cokkylle lond stood whylome good greyne prelate men seyne slouthen shold tylle tro skylle lak hem aboue peple straunged fro loue trouthe cause ignorance pnrueaunce lyght men arn derk yf prelate wolde werk vpon feyth whiche c men sholde nought weye seche withoute lyght vsed men see charge al day refused whiche holy chirche hath vndertake gregorius quando petrus cum iudea andreas cum achaia thomas cum iudea et paulus cum gente venient quid dicemus no moderni quorum fossum talentum pro nichi computabitur wold ensample take gregorye vpon omelye ageyne slouthe prelacye compleyneth hym thus seyth peter fader feyth domesday shal hym bryng iudeam whiche thorugh prechyng wan andrew achay shal come dette pay thomas este beyete ynde poule route grete sondry londes shal presente fulfylled lond rente whiche world holden voyde hondes shal appere touchend oure cure spyrytual whiche oure charge specyal thyng may amounte vpon thylk ende oure acompte cryst hym self audytour taketh none hede wyn honour offyce chauncellery kynges tresorye ne wryt ne wyll warant may auayle world wel row shal make v mowe soo passe withoute mede none otherwyse spede rede spedde whiche de besauntes dde therupon gat none en rees tyme netheles man thanke deserue world lusty serue hym ben al acorded wyst wel recorded thorugh oute erthe al londes late knyy e wynne hondes oure tonges shal stylle stonde vpon flesshes wylle trauayl preche feyth cryst teche folk paynem wol euery prelate holde see al suche may gete lusty drynk lusty mete wherof body fatt ful vnto gostely labour dull slough handel thylk plough elles swyft inough toward worldes auaryce sacryfyce whiche apostel seyth openly ayene feyth vnto idoles youe graunted netheles haunted vertu chaunged vyce largesse auaryce who chapytre mowe trete fader mater bete fer euer whyle lyue shal bet heed yeue vnto self many weye ouer wold prey wyte braunches auaryce hou fare al wel loue wyse sone shal deuyse suche maner stonde thou shalt hem vnderstonde agros iugit agris cupidus domibus que domos que possidea tam sic quasi solus humum solus innumeros mulieru spirat amores sacrum millenis sit sibi culta menu hic tractat confessor super illa specie auaricie que cupiditas dicitur qua amoris causa pertractans amanti super hoc opponit dame auarice nouyt soleyn gold capiteyn court sodry wise scole apryse hath seruauntes many one wherof couetyse one whiche large world aboute seche vauntages oute may profyte wynne auaryce bryngeth inne one halt draweth day whiche hem bedaweth nomore sonne mone ony thyng done namely couetyse stant oute al assyse resonable man fare h purposeth hym fare vpon lucre beyete smal pathe large strete furlong longe myle al one thylk whyle suche one holde dame auaryce hym hath withholde whiche pryncypal outward oueral purueon spye ryght hungry pye storue beestes ben awayted ryght c uetyse affayted loke may purchace wylle wold enbrace al wyde world beelyppeth euer somwhat ouer hyppeth may nought al fulfylle lustes gredy wylle falleth londe couetyse myghty hond ful hard fede taketh none hede may purchace gete conscyence hath al foryete thyng may amounte shal afterward c mpte luce degre tho lesse ben thanhe fysshes gretely deuoureth water hem socoureth ryght soo lawe may rescowe fro hym wol ryght allowe suche one myght wylle shal stonde ryght thus men destroyed ful ofte tyl grete god alofte ayene grete couetyse redresse owne wyse example altho fynde tale wryte soo whiche good lere afterward thou shalt hic ponit confessor exemplum co mognates pidos et narrat de sso romanorum imperatore qui qua speculum virgiln ro titerat dolosa circumuent ditate euertit vnde non solum sui erdicionem sed tocius ciuitatis intollerabilem dampnum cotingere cau sauit rome stode noble plite virgile tho parfite myrrour made cler set wnes eye marble vpon payler withoute thyrty myle aboute day eke also nyght beholde myght yr enemyes yf ony al ordynaunce whiche ayene cyte cast soo whyle thylk myrrour last ther lond whiche myyt acheue werre rome greue wherof grete enuye tho felle thylk tyme soo rome werres strong ageyne cartage stonde long two cytees vpon debate cartage sawe stronge astate rome thylk myrroure stonde thought al pryuely fonde ouerthrowe somme wyle hanybal thylk whyle prynce leder cartage whiche set al courage vpon knyghthode suche wyse worthy wyse none counseyled wherof world yet merueyled maystryes wrought vpon march whiche sought fel thylke tyme also kyng puyle whiche tho thought ayene rome rebelle thus take quarelle hou destroye emperour rome tho gouernour crassus whiche couetous euer desyrous golde gete pyllage wherof puyle eke cartage philosophres wyse grete begynneof mater trete last degre philosophres thre doo thys thyng whiche vndertake therupon hem toke grete tresour gold cofres rome thus philosophres gedre companye went noman wyse ment rome come pryuely duelt thoughten deceyne none myyt hem perceyue tyl sondry stedes haue gold vnder erthe begraue tresours holde sheld seme gold forth thenne vpon day al openly good array themperour presente tolden entente duelle vnder seruyse hem axeth wyse hym told suche plyte eche hem spyryt whiche sle end nyght appereth hem sondry dremes lereth world hath betyd vnder ground yf ought hyd olde tresour ony throwe shal sweuene knowe vpon condycyon theyseyn gold vnder toun hyd rome wol fynde shal nought left behynde soo haluen dele hem graunteth assenteth wele thus cam sleyghte duelle couetyse telle emperour bad redyly lodged fast owne bodye lay morow day one hem sayth mette whele gold hoord shold fette wherof emperour glad therupon anone nours goo myne hym self couyne goth forth al hond tresour redy fond sayd shold glad vpon day second haue another gold hoord found whiche second mayster took vpon sweuene vndertook thus sothe peryence themperour yafe suche credence al trust al feyth sekyrlyc e hem leyth fond hym releued parfytely beleued though goddes thre herkne subtylyte thyrd mayster shold mete whiche saiden shold mete aboue hem al couthe moost withoute noyse bost al pryuelycho wolde vpon morowe sweuene tolde themperour ryght ere said hym wist tresour soo plentyuous gold eke precious iewelles ryche stone vnto al hors one charge suffisaunt lord vpon couenaunt glade axeth maister saide vnder glas told hym eke myne wolde ordeyne suche engyne werk shold vndersett timbre withoute lett men maye tresour sauely delue soo myrrour hym selue withoute empeirement shal stonde thus maister vpon honde hath vndertake al weye lord whiche wit alweye couetise blent anone therto yafe assent thus myne forth tymbre sette vp oueral wherof pyler stood vp ryght til byfelle vpon nyght clerkes whan ware hou tymbre bare piler myrroure stood sleight man vnderstood go nyght vnto myne pitche sulphir syne cyte slepe wylde fyre depe cast among tymbre werk forth whyle nyght derk desguysed pouer array passeden towne day comen vpon helle sawen hou myrrour felle wherof made ioye ynough eche hem lough sayd loo couetyse may hem wyse proued afterward euery lond rome ward whiche subgett fore myrrour forlore wonder herd seye anone begonne dysobeye werres vpon euery syde thus hath rome lost pryde defouled oueral fynde hanybal romayns day hem oute away grete multytude slough gold rynges whiche drouy gentyle handes ben dede busshellys ful thre rede feld made brydge also myght ouer tyber goo vpon corp dede romayns whiche slouy speke iuyse whiche couetyse take vpon emperour destroyed myrrour wonder romayns made chayere set emperour therin sayden wold wynne gold superfluyte gold shold plente receyue tyl sayde ho gold whiche tho boylend hote within panne mouthe poure thanne thus ye thirst gold queint gold whiche ben atteynt wherof sone thou myght couetyse hath lost stere resonable gouernaunce falleth ofte grete greuaunce may werse thyng couetyse aboute kyng persone doth aduersyte yf inhis counseyl stond bryngeth al day meschyef hond comon harme yfit growe within court wol knowe shal kyng bepyled man whiche hath lond tyled awayteth nought redyly heruest gredely ne maken thenne warde watche profyte myyten catche yett ful ofte falleth soo men may seen among hem tho whiche moost coueyteth fast hath lest auauntage last fortune ther ageyne though coueyte veyne happes ben nought al alyche one made pouer another ryche court som doth profyte som ben euer one plyte yet alyche sore coueyte fortune vnto one part fauourable though nought resonable thyng may man seen al day wherof telle may ensample remembraunce hou euery man maye take chauce rychesse pouerte hou stonde deserte noughteuery thyng aguyte ofte man may see yet best doth lest shal haue helpeth nought worlde craue whiche oute reule mesure hath euer stand auenture wel court elles hou al dayes stood thynges felle thynke tale telle ic ponit xhemplum contra illos qui domibns regum seruientes pro eo quam ipsi secundum eorum cupidita tem promoti non existunt de regio ser uicio puis e nm defectu indiserete murmurant cronyke rede aboute kyng must nede therof knyghtes squyers grete route eke offycers som long tyme hym seruyd ano thouyten haue deseruid auauncement gone withoute som also ben route comen whyle agone auaunced anone old men vpon thyng durst ageyn kyng among hem self compleynen ofte thynge sayd softe ne cometh oute last kyng wyst al fast whiche hyghe prudence shope therfore euydence hem pleynen ca knowe who defaute al within owne entent noman wyst ment anone bete two cofres make one semblaunce one make lyche lyf thylk throwe one may fro knowe chambre brought noman wote brouyt netheles kyng hath bede set pryue stede yt wysedome sly therto tyme sygh al pryuelyche none wyst owne hondes one kyst fyn gold fyne perrye whiche oute tresorye take anone feld ful cofre strawe mull stone meuyd feld also thus ful bothe twoo erlyche vpon day bad within lay shold fore bed boord vp set fayre spred lete cofres fette vpon boord dyde hem sette knewe name wel tho whiche ayene hym grutched bothe chambre halle anone sente hem alle sayd hem wyse shal man hym despyse wote wel ye haue long serued god wote ye haue deserued yf long ye bnauaunced elles yf long yow soth shal preued stoppe euyl word loo two cofres boord whiche lyst bothe two wyteth wel one tho trosour ful bygone yf ye happe therupone ye shal ryche men euer chese take whiche leuer wel ware ye take one vndertake maner good therin wherof ye myghten profyte wynne goth gyder one assent maketh youre auysement day auaunce stant vpon youre owne chaunce al defaulte grace shal shewed place vpon alle wel ofyne defaute shal myn knelen al one voys kyng thanken choys vp aryse gone asyde hem auyse last acorde wherof tale recorde yssu befalle knyght shal speke hem alle kneleth doune kyng sayth vpon thyng wynne lese ben al auysed chese tho toke knyhht yerd hond goth cofres stond thassent eueryehone leyd yard vpon one seyth kyng hou thylk chese reguerden name preyth hym yt myyt haue kyng whiche wold honour saue hath herd comon voys hath graunteth hem owne choys toke hem therupon keye wold seye good haue suppose bad anone cofre vnclose fulfilled straw stone thus serued al one thyng stede anone cofre vndede sawen grete rychesse wel couthen gesse loo serth kyng maye ye see defaute thy self wol acquyte bereth ye owne wyte fortune hath refused thus wyse kyng excused left cuyl speche mercy kyng byseche nota hic de diuiciarum accidencia vbi narrat qualiter fredericus imperator romanorum duo pauperrs auditut litigantes quorum vnus dixit bene potest ditari quem rex vult ditare et alius dixit quem deus vult ditare diues erit que rex cum ad experimentum postea probata fuisset ille qui deum inuocabat pastellum auro plenum sortitus est alius vero caponis pastellum sorte preelegit somdele mater lyke fynde tale hou frederyk rome tyme emperour herde wente grete clamour twoo beggers vpon weye one hem bygan seye lord wel may man ryche whome kyng lyst ryche sayd thyng soo ryche wel begoo whome god wol sende wele thus maden wordes fele wherof lord hath hede nome dyde hem come paleys shal ete bad ordeyne mete two pasteyes whiche lete make capon one bake wynne floreyns al may within lete put grete rychesse euen lyche myght gesse outward bothe two begger commaunded tho whiche held hym kyng fyrst chese vpon thyng saw hem felt hem nought soo vpon owne thought chese capon forsoke whiche felawe toke wyst hou ferde seyth aloude men herde certaynly conceyued may lyghtly deceyued trysteth vnto man helpe wel hym god wol helpe stant syker syde whiche elles shold goo besyde see felawe wel recouer mote duelle stylle pouer thus spak begger entent pouer cam pouer went hath rychesse sought infortuue wold nought soo may shewe sondry wyse betwene fortune couetyse chaunce cast vpon dee yet man may ful ofte see inowe suche netheles whiche put hem self euer pres gete hem good yet faile speke entayle touchend loue thy matere good sone thon myght ryght tho men stood infortune worldes good thou hast herd telle aboue ryght ful ofte stant loue though thou coueyte euermore thou shalt haue noo dele whiche shape remenaunt iape netheles nowe tho ben coueyte soo woman see ye ten twelue though ther loue vnauysed beaute stant assysed mannes herte anone rouneth tale ere seyth loueth streyte thus sette hym coueyte honderd though sawe day sholde may grete couetyse sotye fool empryse eche hem fynt somwhat pleseth hym one whyte kyn one noble kyn one hath rody cheke one semeth meke one hath eyen greye one laugh pleye one long smal one lyte tal one pale bleche one softe speche one camused one hath vsed one dauuce synge thyng lykyuge fynt though fele hath lytel hele inough therfore hyr loue thus honderd score whyle newe wold whome forsaketh shal bad blynde man colour demeth al one ryght hym semeth soo hath lust iugement couetyse loue blent hym thynketh couetyse al world ne may suffyse wylle wold haue alle myght byfalle soo comon strete set nought beyete sone hast thou suche couetyse nay fader suche loue despyse whyle lyue shal done euer good feyth yet leuer coueyte suche weye ben euer tyl deye poure iob loueles taken one haules thankes noman lyue man shold al vnthryue ought wyseman coueyte lawe set streyte thy self al saue suche one ther wold haue noue al mo sone thou woldest soo nought wroth bnt ouer wol telle hou men whiche otherwyse ryght ouly couetyse see woman ryche wol al hyr loue affyche nonght beaute face ne yet vertu ne grace whiche hath elles ryght inough park plough thynges whiche therto lo geth none otherwyse ther longeth loue yf profyt fynde yf profyte behynde hyr loue euer lesse lesse hath rychesse loue proporcyon thou hast suche condycyon sone telle ryght myn holy fader nay iwys condycyon suche haue none truly fader loue one well al myn hertes thought certes though nought poure medea whiche exyled creusa wold hyr nought lesse loue ne though hyr aboue ryche quene canda e whiche deserue loue grace alysander kyng yofe many worthy ryche thyng elles pantasylee whiche quene femyne grete rychesse hyr nam loue hector cam troye rescous toune suche condycyon though lady hyr selue also ryche suche twelue couthe though better loue hyr loue pleyne wyse speke couetyse pouerte rychesse loue nouther ne lesse good feyth tro couetous man lady syghe thorugh lokyng eye ne sholde haue suche stroke withyn gold myght wyn shold nought hyr loue asterte yf lefte herte suche man coutheskylle woman men rude among woman come gone vnder protectyon loue affectyon ne shal take hem sleue ben oute byleue hem lusteth lady cheere euer thynkend gold cofte wol none loue profre wote loue amouteth reson trulyche acompteth may knowe taken hede al lust womanhede whiche may ben lady face lady hath eke grace men shold yeuen apryse maye wel seye hou wyse sobre symple contenaunce al good gouernaunce belongeth worthy wyght hath pleynly thylk nyght bore none nature set hyr al one beaute bounte byseyn maye wel afferme seyn sawe yet neuer creature comlyheede feture ony kynges regyon lyche hyr comparyson therto haue told yet hath thousand fold bounte shortely telle pure heede welle myrroure ensample good hyr vertues vnderstood thynketh ought ynough suffyse withouten couetyse loue suche one serue whiche hyr chere deserue byloued better ywys par ca rychest hath gold mylyon suche hath myn opynyon euer shal neuertheles saye nought haueles ny ryche wel ese hath inough plese worldes good whome hyr lyst one thyng wold wel ye wyst neuer worldes good myn hert vnto hyr ward stood ryght purr loue wote hyghe god aboue fader ye say therto confessor sone saye wel doo take ryght good byleue man wol hym self releue loue ony wyse shal wel fynde couetyse shal sore greue hym last suche loue may last men seyn oure dayes men taken fewe assayes yf cause rychesse thy loue wel lesse wold ensamples telle old dayes felle myght man wel vnderstond suche loue may long stonde herkne sone thou shalt grete ensample matere hic ponit exemplum contra istos qui non propter amorem sed propter diuicias sponsalia sumunt et narrat de quodam regis apubic senescalla qui non solum propter pecuniam vxorem duxit sed eciam pecunie come ci vxorem sibi desponsatam vendidit trete vpon ca loue soo tolden aboue fynde wryte woder thyng puyle whysome kyng man hyghe complexyon yong affectyon nature age yet falle courage lust woman knowe soo betyd vpon throwe lord felle grete sekenes phisyk hath done hesynes sondry cure many one make hym hoole therupon worthy mayster whiche ther yafe hym counseyl vpon ca yf wold haue parfyte heele shold woman dele fresshe yong lusty wyght done hym compauye nyght sayd hym redely shal al hole ther otherwyse knewe cure kyng stode auenture lyf deth medycyne assented couyne styward whome trusteth wel took told hym euery del hou mayster hath seyd therupon hath hym prayd charged vpon lygeaunce make purueaunce suche one couenable plesaunce delytable bad hym hou euer stood shal spare good wylle ryght wel paye styward seyd wold assaye bnt thou shalt wyte fynde bokes wryte couetyse loue doth styward telle soth amonges al men lyue lusty lady hath wyue whiche netheles gold took nouyt loue seyth book ryche marchaunt lond hyr fader hyr fond worthely suche rychesse worldes good suche largesse hyr yafe maryage thylk auauntage gold styward hath hyr take lucre nought loues sake stiward wel sene herkne wol mene styward owne herte sowe lord may asterte maladye haue lusty woman hym saue though wold yeue inough tresour wherof drough grete couetyse mynde set honour fer behynde thus whome gold hath ouerset trapped owne net gold hath made wyttes lame soo sechend owne shame rouneth kynges ere seyd wyste gentyl lusty one tho thyder wolde gone mote yiue yeftes grete yf thurgh grete beyete gold seyd shold spede kyng hym bad vpon nede take honderd pound shold yeue wolde worthy place thus stonde loues grace king gold hath habandouned tale ful rouned styward toke gold went within hert many went couetyse cast wherof purpoos last ayene loue ayene ryght toke sayd hou thylk nyght wyf shal lygge kyng goth thynkend vpon thyng toward inne tyl ca home chambre nome wyf told hyr al ca whiche rede shame hyr handes hath hym praid enelend wyse sayd reson skylle thyng bydde wylle redy done heste thyng honest gold shold selle tho wordes felle forth gastely contenaunce seyth shal done obeysaunce folowe wylle euery place thus thurgh strengthe nace innocence ouerlad wherof sore adrad wylle mote nede obeye therupon shape weye owne wyf nyghte hath oute al mennes syght pryuely none wist brouyt kyng hym list may doo hyr wolde sholde hym bedde vnder cloth styward took leue goth chambre fast hou slepte wote sawe cause ielousye whiche hath companye suche lusty one hym thought degre noman wel ese doth al may plese soo al hert thus kyng ioye lad tyl nyhe vpon day styward lay cam bedde wyse hath bede shold aryse kyng sayd nay shold go styward sayd ageyne nought soo mote gone er knowe swore ylke throwe fette kyng tale wold seyth hou hath hir bouyt thy shal departe nought tyl bryght day holde armes gan hyr folde whiche lyst pleye bad styward gone aweye soo dyd ayene wylle thus wyf bedde stylle lay king long nyght tyl hyghe sonne lyght knewe thyng tho cam styward kyng prayd hym withoute shame sauyng owne name myght leden home ayene lady told hym pleyne hou owne wyf kyng ere vnto stryf hath leyd herde wel nyhe oute wyt ferde sayd caytyf moost al euer byfalle ony coward wyse betoke wyf conetyse thou hast hyr begyled eke thyne owne estate reuyled wherof buxome vnto shal neuer auowe god make day yf take thou shalt honged drawe loke anone thou withdrawe soo see neuer styward drad hym sore al hast may fled awey day exyled oute lond loo nyce hysbond whiche thus wif hath lost euer netheles leuer kyng hyr weddeth honoureth wherof hyr name secoureth whiche erst lost thurgh couetyse hym lad hyr wyse hath hym self also forlore sone thou ware therfore thou shalt loue ony place thou couetyse embrace whiche loues kynde al man may fynde tyme thylk rage ful grete dysese maryage venym medleth sucre maryage made lucre lust hele man shal dele may fayle repente fader suche myn entente netheles good haue good may oftyme saue loue whiche shold elles spylle god wote hertes wille dar wel take wytnesse yet neuer rychesse sett maryage none al myn herte vpon one frely persone stant al worldes ioye alone axe nother park ne plough hyr inough hyr loue shold suffyse withouten couetyse loo fader touchend ryght shryfte knowe pleyn yf yr wol ought elles seyn couetyse yf ther loue agropeth oute sore fallere cum nequeat propria vir fraude subornat testis sic que eis vera retorta fides sicut agros cupidus du querit amans mulieres vult testis falsos falsus habere suos non sine vi dictum periurus abibit eis visu qui cordis intima cuncta videt fallere per iuro non est laudanda puella glori set falso condicionis opus hic tractat super illis auaricie speciebus que falsum testimonium et periurum nucupantur quorum fraudulenta circumuencio tam cupiditatis que amoris causa sui desiderij propositum quam sepe fallaciter attingit sone thou shalt vnderstonde hou couetyse hath yet hode specyal two couseyllours ben also procurours fyrst hem fals wytnesse whiche euer redy wytnesse thyng maister wol hym hote periure second hote whiche spareth nought swere oth though fals god wroth one shal fals wytnes bere shal thyng swere charged booke hepe croke make mayster ofte wynne wol know sinne couetyse thus men seyn make many fals bargeyn may trewe quarel aryse thylk queste thylk assyse two people enforme kepe euer one maner forme vpon gold conscyence founde take euydence thus fals wytnes othes wynne hem mete drynk clothe ryght hem knewe louers ful many vntrewe may woman fynde ynowe eche hem shal wowe anone wold hand doune leyn vpon book swere seyn wol feyth trouthe bere thus profereth hym swe e se uen euer tyl deye al trecherye soth hym self tryeth sw reth lyeth feyth maketh al ther st may woman truste hym lest tyl may wylle acheue l nger leue thus trouthe loue exyled good woman begyled eke speke fals wytnesse suche many g sse lyche vnto prouysours make hem preuy procura tour telle hou suche man whiche worthy loue al good man sholde conne soo lesyng hath bygone cause whiche wol procede also syker crede make knowen fals thus ful ofte aboute hals loue fals men embraced loue whiche purchaced come afterward lytel pryse thy sone yf thou wyse thou hast herd euydence thou myght thyne owne conscyence oppose yf thou hast suche one nay god wote fader none ne neuer men seyth man shal make feyth herte tonge must acorde yf dyscorde fals elles nought dare say thought loue dyscordable vnto word ordablo wyse fader may ryght wel swere saufly lady loue wel acordeth euery del nedeth nought soth sawe wytnesse shold drawe day neuer yett ne myght synke wyt counseyl shold seye ony wyght bewreye sechen helpe suche manere lady dere though thousand men wy loue em lyst swer witnesse yet fals wytnesse dare vnto trouthe dwelle loue telle thus fader gylteles ye haue herd nethele dome put al sone wyte specyal shal comonlyche fayle al though tyme faylle fals wytnesse cause spede vpon poynt falsheede shal afterward kyd wherof betyd ensample suche thynges blynde cronyke wryte fynde hic ponit exemplum de illis qui falsum testificantes amoris innocenciam circumu niunt et narrat qualiter achillem filium suum adolesce tem muliebri vestitum apparatu asserens esse puellam inter regis lichomedis filias ad educandum produxit et si achilles cepto rege filie sue deidamie socia et cubicularia effectus super ipsam pir um geniut qui poste mire probitatis miliciam assecutus mortem patris sui apud troiam polix ene tirannice vindicauit goddesse see thetis sone name achilles kepe warde whyle yong ward thought hym saufly take whiche drad sake sayd prophecye troy shold dye cyt byleyn thy bokes seyn cast hyr wyt sondry wyfe hou hym myght desguyse man shold body knowe byf lle ylke throwe whyle thou vpon dede kyng whiche lychomede hote wel begone fayre doughters many one duelt f r oute yle shalt thou wonder wyle quene whiche moder achilles vpon ca hyr e mayden lete cloth gere whiche longeth vnto womanhede yong toke hede suffreth al hat hym dede wherof hath hyr woman bede chargeth othe alle hou afterward byfalle dyscouer nought ng feyne make knoulechyng vpon counseyl whiche nom euery place come telle wytnesse hyr lady doughter ryght suche maner wise bad shold done seruyse achilles vnderfongeth yong lady belongeth honoure seruyce reuerence thetys grete dylygen hym hath taught affayted hou awayted sobre go tely contenaunce shold womanhede auaunce none soth knowe myght euery man syght shold seme pure maide suche wise hym saide achilles whiche ilke yong vpon hym smyle bigan besein thus bokes sein frette perle vpon hede al fresshe bitwene white rede whiche tho tendre age stood colour visage loke vpon cheke seen childy maner eke woman beholde moder tolde soo begone cause thought gone lichomede thilke tyde sayd shold abyde among doughters duelle achilles herd moder telle wyst nonght cause netheles ful buxo ly redy e bad wherof mode ryght glad lychomede forth went whe kyng knewe entent youg doughter cam vnto ere suche record suche wytnesse ryght grete gladnesse soth sawe herde wote hou ferde vpon counseyl nede al kyng lychomede hath toward hym doughter take thetys moder sake put hyr companye duelle deydamye owne doughter eldest fayrest comlyest al doughters whiche loo thus thetys cause lad left ther achilles feyned whiche hath hym self restreyned al euer may oute maner man took womannyssh chere wherof vnto bedfere deydamye hath nyght kynde wold hym selue yght philosopher seyn may wyght ther ageyn thylk tyme sene long nyghtes hem bytwene nature whiche may forbere hath made hem bothe stere kyssen fyrst ouermore hyghe wey loues lore gone al done dede whorof lost maydenhede aud afterward wel know byfel ylk throwe troye syege lay vpon cause menelay quene dame eleyn greg y hadden moche p yne al day fyght assayle myght nought auayle soo noble cyte wynne pryue counseyll begynne sondry wyse tret last among grete fellen vnto acord phor eu record whiche astronomyen eke grete magycyen shold calculacyon serche constellacyon hou cyte myghten gete whiche nought foryet belongeth clerk study set vpon werk long aboute wytte cast tyl fond oute last yf hadden achylles werre shal endeles oner told hem pleyn manere byseyn place shal founde soo within lytel stounde vlyxes forth dyomede vpon poynt lychomed agamen geder sent vlyxes forth went whiche one moost wyse ordeyned hath suche wyse moost rychest aray wherof woman may gay hym took manyfolde ouermore told harnoys lusty knyght whiche burued syluer bryght swerde plate eke mayle though shold doo batayle took also hym shyp thus geder felaushyp forth dyomede hope tyl myghten see place achylles wynde stood mys euery topseyle cole blewe tyl vlyxes march knewe lychomede regne styresman wel hym lad comen sauf londe gone oute vpon stronde burgh foud kyng whiche hath facounde vlyxes dyd message counseyl courage cam told nought vndernethe bethought maner myght aspye achilles deydamye fro ful many lusty lady pleyd day two fortuned fel tyme suche wyse bachus sacryfyce yong ladyes shold make straunge mennes sake come fro syege troye maden wel ioye reuel daunsyng euery lyf whiche couthe syng lusty woman route fresshe carolle hath songe aboute al netheles grekes vnknowe achilles degre outhen wyte whiche ne voys ne paas vlyxes vpon caas thyng high prudence hath wrouyt thylk aray whiche hath bouyt yeue among woman let fetten al gere forth knyghtes harnoys eke al countre seke men sholden nought fay er see euery thyng degre endelong vpon boorde leyde lychomede preyde euery lady ches sholde thyng al wold take wey yefte hem self shold shefte sayde owne wylle achylles stood nought stylle bryght hel e beheld swerde hauberk shelde hert felle therto anone al wold none knyghtes ge e vnderfongeth thylk array whiche belogeth vnto woman forsoke wyse seyth booke knowen whiche goth forth grete paas chambre lay anone made delay armeth hym knyghtely wyse better man deuyse fortune sholde falle cam forth fore hem alle whiche tho glad inough lychomede thyng lough sawe ferde wyst wel herde doughter forleyn ouerseyn wonder ouergoth wyt cronyke wreton yet thyng whiche shal neuer foryete hou achilles hath byge e pyrrus vpon deydamye wherof cam oute trecherye fals wytnes sayde hou achylles mayde thyng sene tho syege go forth vlyxes dyoinede loo thus proued dede fully spoke thylk whyle one woman another begyle ony sekyrnesse thetys whiche goddesse deydamye hath beiaped hou shal ben escaped tho woman who innocence al day thorugh suche credence deceyued ofte sene men suche vntrouthe mene ben slye suche wyse sleyghte queyntyse fals wytnesse bryngen inne doth hem ofte wynne worthy therw thy sone doo soo fader fals wytnesse trouthe maner expresse touchend loue hou bath ferd ye haue told haue wel herd ye sayden otherwyse hou thylk vyce couetyse hath yet periure acord thou lyst som record telle another tale also loues cause tyme ago thyng forswore wolde preye therfore wherof myght ensample take good sone thy sake touchand shal fulfylle thyn axyng thyne owne wylle matere shal declare woman deceyued tender herbe men swere cometh thassay ther fynde fals another day iason dyde medee whiche stant yet auctoryte tokne memoryal wherof tale specyal book troye wryte whiche shal wyte hic amoris causa ponit exemplum contra perinros et narrat qualiter iason prius quam ad insulam col chos pro aureo vellere ibidem conquestando transmearet amorem couiugium regis othonis filie iuramento firmius se astrinxit sed suo postea completo negocio cu ipsa secu nauigio grecia perduxisset vbi illa senecta patris sui esonis floridam iuuentutem mirabili sciencia reformauit ipse iason fidei sue ligamento alijs que beneficijs post positis dictam medeam pro quadam causa regis creontis filia periurus dereliquit grece whylome kyng fame knoulechyng byleueth yet peleus hyghte felle hym thus fortune hyr whele lad chylde owne regne decesse broder netheles who ryght name eson hath worthy knyght iason bygoten whiche euery lond al passed hond armes best named worthyest sought worshyp oueral herkne telle shal auenture sought whiche afterward ful dere bought ile whiche colchos cleped therof awos grete speche londe aboute suche meruayle none oute al wyde world nowhere tho ile shepe told whiche flees bare al gold goddes sette ne myght wey fette power worldes wyght yet ful many worthy knyght assayed dorst euer fel hem worst wold nought forsake knyghthode vndertake doo thyng therto belongeth worthy iason sore alongeth see straunge regyons knowe condycyous march went cause hoole entent set colchos seke therupon dyde speke peleus eme kyng wel payd thyng shope anone passage suche lygnage knyghtes whiche chees hym toke hercules whiche ful chyualrye iason wente companye moneth may colde stormes away wynd good ye shyp yare took hyr leue forth fare toward colchos weye hem byfelle long seye hou lamedon kyng troye whiche ought wel haue made hem ioyr rest whyle hym preide oute lond hem congeyde felle dyssencyon whiche afterward destructyon cyte men may matere thus worthy folk gregoys fro kyng curtois fro land seyl vpdrawe thene went hem forth many sawe made many grete manace tyl last place whiche sought arryue stryken seyle forth blyue senten vnto kyng tolden wolden oetes whiche kyng herd tydyng iason whiche comen thought done hem grete worshyp anone come oute shyp strayt vnto kyng went hand iason hent paleys gate fer kyng cam gate toward iason done hem chere lakketh manere kyng sawe presence yafe hym ageyn suche reuerence kynges state belongeth thus kyng hym vnderfongeth iason arme caught forth halle straught sat speke thyngis iason told hym tho tydyngys come fayre hym prayde haste tyme kyng sayde iason thou art worthy knyght lyeth man myght done thou art come fore hath many knyght forlore wolden assaye iason hym wold esmaye seyd euery worldes cure fortune stant auenture parauenter wel parauenter woo hou euer goo shal myn hond assayed kyng tho helde hym wel paid grekes sore dredde aunter yf iason ne spedde myght therof blame tho al worldes fame grece speke armes thy drad hym harmes gan preche hym preye iason wold obeye sayd wold purpoos holde ought ony man hym tolde kyng wordes herde sawe knyyt ansuerde yet wold make hym glad medea gone whiche doughter cam iason whiche good hede nam hyr sawe ageyn hyr goth hym nothing loth welcomed hym londe softe took hym honde doune seten bothe herd spoke name grete worthynes thy gan hyr eye inpresse vpon face stature aud thought hou neuer creature welfarend iason ryght suche degre nc myght withholde look good hede hyr took hym ne thouyt vnder heuene beaute saw neuer hyr euene al felle womanhede thus eche took hede though word record hertes bothe one acord ben set loue tho myghten wordes mo kyng hym made grete joye fest al men yaf hest wol thank deserue sholde al iason serue whyle wold duelle thus day shortely telle many myrthes dyspent tyl nyght come tho went echone took leue lenger myghten leue hou iason nyght slepe wel wote shepe whiche cam yle thought lytel whyle al medea thought soo many wyse thought wyt wakend daye somtyme ye somtyme nay somtyme thus somtyme styred fro loue eke conquest holde heste thus roos vp morowe took hym seynt iohn borow sayd wold fyrst begynne loue wynne flees gold whiche come thus hym good hert nome medea ryght wyse tyl day cam must ryse lay bythought hyr al nyght hou noble worthy knyght ony weye myght wedde wel ne wist yf ne spedde thyng whiche vndertake myght hyr self noo purpoos take yf deyde bataylle algate fayle geten hym dede thus vygan sette rede torne aboute wyttes al loke hou myght falle hym bad leyser speke telle desyre soo felle day iason swete may gyder sette hadde space speke besought hyr grace tale goodly herd afterward hym ansuerd seyd iason thou wylt thou myyt sauf thou myyt spilt wyte wel neuer man yf couthe ne myght fortune acheue whiche thou comest loue thou wolt holde couenaunt loue al remenaunt shal thy lyf honour saue thou flees gold shalt haue sayd al owne wylle madame shal truly fulfylle youre hest whyle lyf may last thus long prayd last graunteth hyght hym nyyt cometh tyme wold hym sende certeynly suche one shold hym pryuely lone hyr chambre brynge thanketh hyr tydyng grace hym begonne hym thynketh al thinges wone day made ende lost lyght comen derk nyght whiche al dayes eye blent iason took leue forth went cam prees took cound hercules told hym betyd praid hym shold wel hed wold loke whyles shold thus stood hede name mayden fro medea came chambre iason ledde fond redy ledde fayrest wysest eke symple cheere meke hym sawe al ashamed hyr tale nowe entamed sykernesse mariage set forth ryche ymage fygure iubites iason swore said also wy god shold hym help yf medea dyd hym help purpoos myght wynne shold neuer parte twynne euer whyle hym last lyf wold hir hold wyf word kyssed shold hem vnclothe come maide hyr wyse dyde hem ful seruyse tyl fed naked wote nyght wel waked loth wold loyser hym told gan fro poynt poynt enforme batuyle al forme whiche shold fynde ybe come said entre paas god armes hath set two ox sterne stoute casten fyte flamme aboute al month na soo syttin al bbose passeth hem bytwene fer ore vppon grene goth gold kepe serpent whiche may neuer slepe thus shold wyn fire stoppe must begyn whiche fyers beestes cast daunce mote hem last may yokke dryur therupon must bylyue serpent suche strength assails may slee hym bataile whiche must ye teeth outdraw longeth lawe must ox yoke til yt haue plowe broke forowe londe whiche iowe teeth serpent muste shall arise knyghtes armed wel al ryghtes hem nought take hede eche hem hasty hede shalle slee dethes wounde thus leid groude go forthe take pray must goddes pray faile ony wyse haue herd deuyse may sette none weye ne must algates deye haue told perille yow telle forth al quod medea iason tho ye shal knowe er ye goo ageyne venym fyre shall recouere nygh day arise vp soo may delyuer yow thyng haue maye youre lif honoure saue loth rise bothe wyse vp rysen last iason clothes hym cast made hym redy ryght anon hir serke dyde vpon cost hir mantee close withouten aroos tooke forth ryche tye made gold perrye oute whiche took ryng stone worth al thyng said whyles wold myght perylle hym dere water maye drenchyd cometh ye fyre quenchid ouercometh also cruel beste may none aduersite yt man areste soo see londe hath rynge vppon honde ouer gan seyne yf man wylle beseyne within honde close stone maye inuysyble gone ryng iason ytaught forth hym taught sacryfice shold make gan oute hyr cofre take hym thought heuenly figure whiche al charme coniure wrought also ful writ name whiche shold wyt hym taught rede bad hym wold spede without rest ony whyle londed yle shold make sacryfise de carecte wise hym tauyt knee doun bet th e si he toward oryent shold goddes plese wynne hym self mochel ese whan thryes radde open boxe hym adde toke hym present ful suche oynement fyre ne venym none shold fasten hym vpone anoynted thy taught hym shall enoyn e arines al aboute shold thyng doute took hym maner glu whiche huge vertue n wolde caste shold bynd anone faste man myght doo aw bad al wey shold mowthes throwe two ox fire blowe therof stoppe malyce glewe shal serue se yce ouer hyr oynement hyr ryng hyr enchauntement ageyne serpent shold hym tille hym slewe sheld spere may sau ly ynough ox yoke plough teeth sowe suche wyse tyl knyghtes see aryse chone doune layd suche maner haue said loo thus medea iason ordeyneth prayeth therupon thyng forgete shold also prayd hym wold al armes done grounde knele thonke anone goddes forth ese flees gold shold seese sesed sone go withoute ony taryeng seid vnto wepyng felle yt thorugh nom loue forth ouercomen world hym te sawe bette ne must nedes parte fro took hym armes two honderd tymes gan hym kysse said al worldes blisse tryst lust lyf hel thy help thy quarele praye vnto goddes alle yt word gan doune falle swounyng hir vp name forthwith maiden came ther bed anone hyr brouht iason hyr besought hyr said manere worthy lusty ladyes dere comforteth yow trou h shall fayle slouthe ne wylle thurgh oute fulfille youre comaudement wille yet hope yow bryng within whyle suche tydyng whiche shall make v bothe ga wold kepe hyr name wyst nyhe day said adyeu swete may forth hym took ge whiche bad take hym streyght vnto chambre wet gothe ed slepe hym hen lay man hym awoke hercules hede hym toke tyl vnder day ganne syke sore sodenly abrayed slepe took hym kepe chamberleyns en soone make redy al gere awos vnto kyng went said thyng whiche cam wold go kyng therfore wonder woo wold hym fayn withdraw told hym many dredeful saw iason wold recorde last accorde wold abyde ote redy yde yt worthy knyyt gre ful armed vp euery pece batayle belongeth toke hond sore longeth till water passid whan cam set hym knee doun strauyl carecte taught rad made sacryfyce sythen anoynced hym wy medea hym hath ede arose hym fro glewe fi e qu ynt anone gan ateynt grete serpent hym slough erst sorowe ynough serpent made hym trauaile hard sore batayle stood felle long tyme felle th swerd ne spere myght serpent dere shelled al aboute spyld al edge tole withoute soo rude hard skyn myght thyng goo ther venym fire geder cast ason greued sore blast yf ben oynement rynge enchauntement whiche medea took hym beforn worm lorn thurgh ye vertu therof ca iason dragon ouercam anone tethe oute drowe set ox plowe whiche brake pece ond sewe hem owne ond myght grete merueyle see euery tooth degre sprag vp knyyt spere sheld whiche ryght anon feld echone slough iason medea forgat bothe knee gan doune fall ga thankyng goddes flees took gothe bote sonne shyneth bryght hote flees gold shone forth water glystered oueralle medea weped syghed ofte stode vppon wre aloft al pryuely within hir self herd ten twelf prayd said god hym spede knyght hath maidenhede dy loked toward yle sawe within whyle flees glisteryng geyn sonne said lord al wonne knyght feld hath ouereomen wold god comen lord god wold londe dare take honde wynges two wold haue flowen hym tho streyte vnto ote day w clere sonne hote grekes grete doute whyle hyr lord oute wise shold betyde waited vpon tyde see ende shold falle stood also noble alle footh comyn towne loked vp doune ware within throwe cam ye bote wel know saw ason brought prey gan al sey yden one sreuen euer vnder heuen noble knyght iason wel ny e al saiden iason fayre knyght neuer man myght e gold wynne thus talk begynne kyng forth anone sawe flees shone iason cam londe kyng hym self took honde kyssed hym greete ioyr made grekes wonder glade ye thyng right mery thought forth hym yt flees broyt euery man gan prece well hym myght wyn see propyrte thus passen cyte gone vnto place straught medea whiche forgate hyr naught redy sai anone welcome worthy knyght iason wold haue kyst hym woder fayne shame borned hyr agayne maner tho thy durst took hyr leue iason wen e chambre hym sente hyr maide see ferd whiche whan sawe herd faren oute stood wel al aboute told hyr lady wist ioye hyr mayden kyst bathe arrayd herbes tempred assayd iason vnarmed soon dyde befelle done bathe went anone wysshe hym clene ony one took soppe oute came best array name kempt hede glad goth hym forth al mery glad ryght streyght kynges hall pmg grete lordes alle made hym glad welcomyng hem told tythyng befelle wan shepes felle medea sent came soone parlement myght iason see none glad al ioye seche hym made euery man speche som men said one somme saide though goddes broder myght make fire thonder myght wonder hym cyde eche man taught hath power within al world myght wyn lo best al goode thus seid stood also walked vp doune bothe court towne tyme souper cam anone wysshen therto gone medea iason set tho many deynte fet set ore hem boord none soo lykyng word ther spoke amog hem two dorst speke tho though adden lytyl space yet acorden place iason shold come nyght euery torche euery lyght oute thynges speken loude supposynges hem stoden aboute loue euermore doute wysely gouerned hem loue lerned al doo dysshe cuppe clothe bord l vppe ake whyle hem lyst wake af r leue take gone edde reste hym thought beste euery man fast slepe iason wold tyme kepe forth stalkend al pryuely vnto chambre redyly mayde whiche hym kepte medea wook nothyng slepte netheles bed al hast hym spedde made hym naked al warme anone took hyr arme nede speke ese hem lyst eche plese soo hadden ioye ynough tho setten hou hym awey shal stele wordes fele al treded ende iason took eue gan forth wende vnto owne chambre pee wyst none hercules slepte w tyme fel toward pryme took ym suche tryste secre none wyste told hem counseyl sayde wylle shyp al thyng pryuelyche theuenyng noman myght dede aspye companye wol goo withoute leue enger wol nought byleue ne wold thylk throwe kyng quene shold knowe sayde al thys shal doo iason trust wel therto medea mene whyle whiche thought hyr fader begyle tresour whiche hyr fader hyr al pryuely lad iason tyme sett awey stal fonde let straught goth hyr shyp grece felaushyp anone drough vp sey e al nyght couseylle erly sonne shone men seen hou gon come vnto kyng told soth knowe wold axeth doughter word ala goo moder wepte fader wood man lepte gan tyme warye swore othe wol tarye calyphe galeye cours wey whiche iason took wold take myght hym ouertake sayden al yee anone see al sayd one word gone within shyppes boord seylle goth vp forth strauyt none exployt therof cauyt forth tornen home ayene al laboure eyn iason grece prey goth thorugh see ryght weye ther come men told made ioye yong old eson wyse sone comen hath acheued soughte home hym medea broughte al wyde world none glad man one geder ben louers tho tyl sone twoo wherof bothe glade olde eson greete ioye made seen encrees lygnage grete age men away n euery day shold gone away iasen whiche sawe fader old en medea made hym bold art magy e whiche couth prayth hyr fader youth wold make ayeneward newe toward hym trewe behyghte hym wold tyme sawe therto dede matere wonder thyng yet nouelrye ynke tellen grete partye n qiubus medica mentis esone n tute decrepitum ad sue iuuentutis adolescenciam prudens medea reduxit thus byfel vpon nyght nought sterre liyt banysshed ryght hyr lyst wyght hyr seluen wyst world stylle euery syde mydnyght tyde open xede foote al bare sprad gan fare vpon hyr clothes gyrt al specheles gras glode forth adder doth none otherwyse ne goth tyl cam fresshe flood whyle withstood thryes torned hyr aboute thryes eke gan doune loute flood w et hyr thryes water gaspeth dretchyng onde tho took hyr speche honde fyrst began clepe calle vpward vnto sterres alle wynde ayre see ond preyd held vp hyr hond echates gan crye whiche goddesse sorcerye seyde helpeth nede ye maden spede iason cam flees seche helpe byseche loketh ware doune fro sky cam chare whiche dragon aboute drough tho gan hyr hede doune bough vp styghe fayre wel drofe forth chare wheel aboue ayer among skyes lond crete tho partyes sought gan fast hyr hyghe therupon hulles hyghe othryn olymphe also eke hulles moo fonde gade eth herbes soute pulleth vp som rote many knyf shereth alle hyr chaar ere thus hath hulles sought flodes forya nought erydyan amphrydos eneye eke sperceydos hem went nome bothe water f fond eke smal stone whiche al chese oute none rede see part behouelycke hyr art took afterward aboute sought sondry sedes oute feldes many greues eke part took leues thyng myyt hyr aua yle fond crete thessayle dayes nyghtes nyne grete trauayl grete pyne purueyed euery pece torned homward grece byfore gate eson hyr chare lete awey gone took oute fyrst therin tho thought begyn suche thyng semeth impossyble made hyr self inuysyble pre enclosed myght man dysclosed took turues lond withoute helpe man honde aud heled grene gras whiche aulter made vnto echates goddesse art magyke sorceresse eft another iuuente whiche dyde hole entente tho took felwood berueyne herbes better tweyne whiche anone without ett aulters ben aboute set two sondry pyttes fast made hastely wether whiche blak ouy oute therof blood drough dyde pyttes twoo warme mylk put also therto hony meynt suche wyse gan make hyr sacryfyce cryde prayde forth al pluto god infernal quene proserpyne aud sought oute lyne hem longen craft behynd noman laft praid hem alle couth graunte eson fyrst youth old eson brought forth tho wey bad al goo vpon peryl myght falle word wenten alle leften two alone tho began gaspe gone made sygnes many one sayd hyr wordes therupone spellyng hir charmes took eson bothe hyr armes made hym slepe fast hym vpon hir herbes cast blak wether tho took hewe flesshe doth cook eyther aulter part leyde charmes seyde fyre doune sky alyght made brenne lyght medea sawe brenne anone gan sterte renne fyry aulters al aboute beste whiche goth oute wylde semeth aboute hyr sholders henge hyr though oute mynde torned another kynde tho lay certeyn wode clefte whiche peces efte made hem pyttes wete put hem fyry hete toke brond al blase thryes bygan rase aboute eson slepte efte water whiche kepte made cercle aboute hym thryes eke fyre sulphyr twyes ful many another thyng dede whiche wryten stede vp doune made wonder soune somtyme lyche vnto cok somtyme vnto lauerok somtyme cacleth henne somtyme speketh done menne ryght hir argon straugeth sondry wyse hyl forme chaungeth semeth fayre woman forth craft seith goddesse hyr lyst lesse dyde bokes fynde passeth ouer mannes kynde wol wondres thyng wrouyt matere make ende gan suche meruayle herd neuer man poynted newe mone tyme done sett cauldron fyre whiche al hoole tyre medycyne stood iuse water blood lete boyle suche plyte tyl sawe spume whyte tho cast rynde roote seed floure bote many herbe many stone wherof hath many one eke cympheyus serpent hyr hath al hyr scale lent ydre hyr yafe adder skyn boyle cast hem part eke horned oule whiche men nyghtes houle rauen whiche told nyne honderd wynter old took heed al bylle medy yue wylle took therafter bowele see wolf hele eson thousand mo thyngis tho caldron gyder blyue put took olyue drye braunche hem ster whiche anone gan floure bere weye al fresshe grene ageyn vertue herd f yn lete lest drope alle vpon bare flore doune falle droppe falle anone spronge floure gras waye anone al mede grene myght wel sene medea knewe wyst hyr medycyne tryse goth eson lay took swerd assay whiche wounde vpon syde made ther may slyde blood within whiche old seke trouble feble coldr tho took vnto vse herbes al best iuse poured wounde made beynes ful sounde tho made woundes close took hond vp wse tho yafe hym drynk drauyt whiche youthe agayn caught heed hert bysage lyche vnto twenty wynter age lyche vnto fresshe may hore here away passed ben cold shoures ryght recouereth floures loo myght ony man deuyse woman shewe ony wyse hertely loue ony stede medea iason dede fyrst made hym flees wyn alle kyth kyn grete tresour hym stal fader forth al elde hath torned youthe whiche thyng none man couth hou hyr uyt remembraunce duelleth yet kyng peleus eme deed iason bare coroune beede medea hath fulfylled wylle shold ryght fulfylle trouthe whiche hyr afore le colchos swore tho medea moost deceyued hath another receyued whtch doughter kynge creon creusa byght thus iason loue vntrewe medea left toke newe afterward sore abought medea hyr art hath wrought cloth gold mantel ryche whiche semeth worth kynges ryche vnto creusa sent name yeft present susterhood hem bytwene yong fresshe quene mantyl lappyd hyr aboute none therof fyre sprang oute brent hyr bothe flesshe bone tho cam medea iason sone hond sayd thou euery lond moost vntre creature loo shal thy forfeture bothe sone slough byfore eye oute drough swerd wold haue slayn hyr tho fare wel goo vnto pallas court aboue pleyneth vpon loue goddesse left grete dystresse thus myyt thou see sorow doth swere othe whiche soth loues cause namely sone wel ware thy kepe thou forswore whiche haue told tofore ouyde telleth euery dele fader may leue wele haue herde ofte seye hou iason toke flees aweye fro colchos yet herd nought fyrst thyder brouyt good thou lyst prayere telle wold byseche sone wol seche bokes may fynde wryte netheles yf thou wolt wyte maner thou hast preyde shal telle hou seyde nota qualiter aureum vellus pardes insule colchos primo deuenit athemas rex philen habiut coniugem qua faxum genuit et hellen mortua autem hellen athemas iunonem regis cadmi filiam postea vxorem dnxit que nouerce di tos infa te tantum recollegit odi que ambo mari proici penis regem procurauit vnde iuno compaciens quemdam arietem grandem aureo vestitum vellere ad litus natantem destinauit super cuius dorsum pueros apponi iussit quo facto aries super vndas regressus cum solo frixo sibi adherente colchos applicuit vbi iuno dictum arietem cu suo vellere prout alijs canitur coni sub ta custodia collocauit fame thylk shepes felle colchos bifelle al gold shal neuer deye wherof thynke seye hou cam fyrst ile kyng thylk whyle wardes grece athemas cronyke name wyf whiche phylen hyght whome fortune dyght chyldren yong two fay fyrst tho man chylde ryght fayre doughter eke whiche men call hellen hade wyf ther may man lyf endure vpon erthe worthy quene thou myyt er chyldren age took ende passage grete worshyp bygraue thyng lyketh god haue grete reason ben thy thys kyng grete suffrauce vnderfongeth afterward hym belongeth tyme wedde newe wyf toke bedde whiche iuo hyght mayde eke doughter men sayde cadme whiche kyng also holde thylke dayes tho iuo kynges make cast hou myght make chyldre hyr fadre loth shope wyle ayene hem vnto kyng vnknow yere two sete doo sowe lond soden whete aboute wherof corn may spryngen oute thus sleyghte couyne aroos derthe famyne thorugh oute lond suche wyse soo kyng sacryfyce vpon poynt dyserrsse cere whiche goddesse corne hath shape hym yeue loke yf may foryeue meschyef whiche lond whiche knewe fore hond cyraimstaunce al thys thyng ageyn comynge kyng temple hath shape soo hyr acord al tho whiche temple prestes haue sayd ful declared vnto kyng yf desyuer countre fryxus hellen bothe whome goddes ben wrothe whyle tho chyldre ben within suche tylthe shal man begyn wherof gete hym ony corn thus sayd thus sworn al prestes whiche causeth al fare seyd eke therto wolde euery man tolde soo quene hem preyd kyng whiche bath ere leyd leueth al euer herde vnto tale thus ansuerde seyth leuer hym chese chyldren bothe lese hym al remenaunt hem whiche apperdendunt vnto lond whiche shal kepe bade wyf take kepe manere best done delyuerd sone oute world anone two men ordeyneth gone fyrst made hem swere chyldren shold vnto see none knowe hem therin throwe child see ben lad wyse yuo bad men redy doo goddesse whiche iuno hote appereth stede hath vnto men forbede chyldren ne slee bad hem loke see taken hede syghen swam sheepe fore hyr eyen whoos flees burned gold al goddesse forth al comaundeth withoute let shold anone chyldre set aboue vpon shepes bak al ryght spak wherof men gone home ageyne felle bokes seyne hellen yong mayden tho whiche see wo bego pure drede hyr hert hath lore fro shepe whiche hath hyr bore swounend feynt felle hyr self deeynt frixus shepe forth swam tyl ile colchos cam iuno goddesse fond whiche toke shepe lond tte suche wyse thou fere hast herd deuyse wherof cam al wo iason forswore soo vnto mede spoke fader hath broke trouth ye haue told worthy loue ne beloued semeth euery loue ne quemeth hym whiche newe fangle netheles thou lyst taken hede vpon shryfte procede loues cause ayene vyce couetyse auoryce wold wyte sone fynde wryte yet one thylk brood whiche worldes good make tresoure moneye put al conscyence weye wherof thy confessyon name condycyon shal afterwarde declare whiche maketh one ryche another bare plus capit vsura sibi quam debetur et illud fraude colocata sepe latenter agit sic amoz excessus quam sepe suos vt cuarus spirat et viuus tres capit ipse loco hic tractat de illa specie auaricie que vsura dicitur cuius creditor pecunia tantum numerata plus quam sibi de iure debetur incrementum lucri ad auget pon benche syttend hyy auaryce vsure syghe ful clothed owne sute whiche good maketh chase sute brocours renne aboute lyche vnto ratch route suche lucre none aboue ground whiche ratch founde see beyete sterte shal hem wyse asterde dryue net lucre whiche vsure hath set vsure ryche duelleth al euer byeth selleth hath ordeyned sleyghte mesure double double weyghte outward selleth lasse maketh tasse wherof hous ful withynne retcheth nought soo wynne though lese ten twelue loue al toward hym selue none see may wynne suche thre shal ought yeue lene wol ayene ward take bene hath lent smal pese ryght ther many louers though loue lyte scarsely wold weye myte yet wold haue pound ageyne doth vsure bargeyn certes suche vsure vnlyche falleth vnto ryche al wel loue beyete vnto hem grete sayth symple pouer selden recouer yf thorugh greete deserte netheles men see pouerte pursute contenaunce ful ofte make grete cheuaunce take loue auauntage helpe brocage maken seme nought thus ful ofte loue bought lytel mochel take fals weyghtes make sone sayd aboue thou wost vsure loue telle thy thou wylt thou therof host ony gylt fader nay ought tho poyntes ye tolden wol trouth assure weyghte loue mesure hath large certeyn euer took loue ageyne yet couthe neuer sleyghte take ageyne double weyghte loue haue yeue also wy mote shryue haue remyssyon synne soo yet couthe neuer wynne ne yet soo mochel soth seyn euer myght haue half ageyn ful loue haue lent myn hop wel went hoole myght haue half thynketh goddesse half vsure wold haue double conscyence trouble byd neuer dele hole haluen dele none excesse thynketh netheles forthynketh wel wote wol euery day better see ho euer yeue lene loue place mene ought euer axe craue nothyng ayeneward haue wol lete befalle beyete ne shal yeue lene loue al thought soo clene toward shal nougt byleue yf hyr good leue rewarde wold nought ageyn wote last bargeyn shal stonde vpon grete lost may neuer cost recouer world tyl dye soo touchend partye may wel excuse shal speke forth al ouy brocour went poynt cam neuer myn entent soo meruayleth thyng lady eyleth al myn herte al tyme hath doo better byme haue herd sayd thouyt fre netheles pryuete fader ben myn hole shryfte dar myn hert wel dysclose touchend vsure suppose whiche ye tellen loue vsed lady may ben excused one lokyng hyr eye myn hool herte hath tyl deye al euer may hath wonne hyr man wherof thynketh good reson wolde somdele rewarde sholde yeue part hath al falle herafter shal yet dare seyne hyr lyst neuer yeue ageyne good word suche wyse wherof myne hope myght aryse greete loue compense hou hyr conscyence excuse wol vsure large weyghte grete mesure hath loue haue nought whiche haue dere abought myne herte haue payde al asyde layde go loueles aboute hyr ought stonde ryght grete doute tyl redresse suche synne wol al loue wynne yeueth lyue nought also moche graunt mercy hyr lyst seye whiche myght greete peyne alyght poynt lo thus fare payeth chaffare byeth dere yet hath none mote nedes pouer gone thus bye dere haue loue ne may come aboue wynne loue none encrece wylle neuer lese touchend vsure loue acquyte yf lady wyte pray god suche grace hyr sende tyme must amende sone thou hast answerd touchend vsure haue al herd thou loue hast wonnen smale thou tellest thy tale thy lady therof accusist thynketh thy wordes thou mysusist thyne owne knowlechyng thou saist one lokyng thy hole herte fro took may suche hyr one look worth herte many fold hast thou thy herte wel sold whan thou hast worthy also thou tellest thy hyr weyght loue vneuen maye thy semyng vnder heuen stonde euer euen balaunce stondeth loues gouernace suche statute lawe though thy loue drawe peyse balaunce thou may aske ageyn ther fore doubte grace loue lord euery place may lawe hym iustyfye eddour ne companye ne wylle wylle hym liketh spede spille loue man may wel begynne whether shalle lese wynne wote man till last therfore coueyte fast sone abyde thyn ende per c al may good wende thou hast told said one thyng ryght wel payd thou sleyghte ne gyle brocoure hast whyle engyned loue suche dede venged rede hic ponit exemplum contra istos marituss qui vltra id quod proprias habent vxores ad noue voluptatis crementum alias mulieres superflue lu crari non verentur et narrat qualiter iuno vindictam ecco lucris adquirendis de consilio mariti iouis diatrix exstiterat broker loue deceyuen woder though receyuen wrong deserue somtyme goo serue doo plesaunce whyle yet last owne gyle vppon hyr owne hede descendeth whiche god vengeace sedeth ensample tyme goo man may fynde hath felle somtyme sene hygh goddes quene iuno company mayden ful trechery euer one acord iubiter hyr lord gete hym loues newe thorugh suche brocage vntrew al wyse hym nedeth whiche shame dredeth queynt wordes slye blynded suche wise ladyes eye whome iuno tryst ther thyng wyst pryuely may thyng ne cometh knowlechyng thyng yt done derk nyyt knowen whan day liyt befelle last al slyghe mayden cast ouer cast ouerthrowen soothe must knowen iuno done vnderstonde manere hyr husbonde fals brocage hath taken vsure loue mesure whan took wyf wherof mayden gyltyf whiche hath ben as thus game shent suffred hym must nede broucore mysdede hir counceylle gaf therto hyr vengeaunce doo iuno hyr wordes bryg mayden whic e tito hyght reproueth saith wyse traitresse suc e seruyse hast thou thyne owne lady ser ed thou hast grete peyne wel deserued thy slygh wordes peynte flaterye queynt towards thy quene thorugh thou madest went housbond trewe loueth el al soo hym nedeth n ught vppon shall bought whiche arte pryue doynges ful oft thy besynges deceyued hast day whyle wel quyte may thou hast counceyled lord hath deled shalle set suche kynde euer vnto worldes ende al thou herest thou shalt telle clappe oute doth belle word shape may vyce mouthe escape man world cryeth withouten faile hecco replyeth word hym lust say word saith agayn thus somtyme leue large morow eue woodes hylles bothe suche brocage wyues lothe whiche doth lordes herte chaunge loue place straunge thy yf euer soo befalle thou herafter chambre hall wedded man hold thou hast thy al loue wast one wyf shal wel suffys yf tho couetyse loue wold aske thou sholdest done ageyne lod men trewe fader degre conscyence accused suche brocage haue vsed thorugh yt loue lust thy speketh forth ye begonne auaryce vppon shryft sonne shal braunches yft ordre ben set whome good wel beset par verbis verba munus pro munere reddi conuenit vt pondus qu statera ger preterea cupido non da sua dona cupido nam qui nulla eri gramina nulla metet hic tractat auctor super illa specie auaricie que parcimonia dicitur cuius natura tenax aliqualem sue substancie porcionem aut deo aut hominibus par ticipare nullatenus consentit blynd uaryce ly nage counceylle co nage withhold ageyne largesse h th one who name scarceness whiche kepat howe thorugh auarous good lete hond though god hym self shold fonde gyft shold thyng haue yf man wold craue must fayle nede wherof hym self may spede thus scarcenes euery place reason may thyng purcha egre aboue al priu aua stondeth se euermore wo estate offyce rewle vyce taketh lepis hoppeth blent lyght slee flent gede hym ne hard ne nesshe valewe resshe good helpyng another ne though owne broder gyft loue ndeth euery man hym aboue thynketh vnkyndeship hym nedeth noo felauship bagge acorde hym rekketh man recorde hym euyl good trust good allone falleth ofte best weneth stond lofd wel loue wyse loue euer somme repryse hym wol lone holde thy sone thou art holde tonchend telle thy shry hast thou searse large gyft vnto thy loue thou serues thou wel deseruest gyft thou myght bett f good wyl sette yt whiche thou myyt yu better fa thenne wysedom spare thus men seyn euery nede wyse fyrst made mede mede may spede helpeth dede ful faileth game wylle ydel hond reclame hawke many nyce man doth thy sone telle sooth saye outhe yf thou haue thy ue scorse fro fader hath sto den thus yf ou resus alle goood oc auian ryches indyan perles ryche stone al geder myn one set maner acounte wold bare sted amounde gyue hyr al day soo swete may myght lyke lesse thus cause largesse ye may vnderstonde leue shall better acheue purpoos whiche thought yf gaf hyr neuer nought ne therto durst profre make wel wote wylle take gyue wylle also escheweng bothe two thus trowe skylle towardes ne wylle cause haue hope nought moche drope toward may see gyueth taketh suche degre wey frendelyhede soo kepe hyr womanhede euery man speketh hyr wele wylle take dele yet wote wel wold gyue doo bothe shold pl se hyr al myght reson wote euery wyght may wey asterte mayster hert must mayster goode god wote wel al mode al good whyles haue ouyt al herte al thought frely god hath gyue shal hirs whyles lyue ryght hyr lyst hyr selue commade nedeth demaunde aske yf haue scarse loue parse wylle answere sey sone ryght wel doo tyme rcenesse hath ben sene fore lesse lost thou shalt e e tale lyke matere hic loquitur contra istos qui auaricia stricti largitans beneficium amo ri causa confundunt et ponit exemplum qua cer croseus largu et hilaris babionem auarum et tenacione de amore viole qui pulcherrima fuit dono largissimus circumuenit carcenes loue acord neuer ffor euery thyng wel yt leue yt hath bouyt dere speke matere sparyng lytel cost ful oftyme man lost large cote hode man scarse gode wylle gyue shall take gyfte man may vndertak hyghe god plese queme gyft man world may deme euery creature bore thou yeue hym glad therfore euery gladship fynd comfort vnto loues kynde cause man sped wise first gaf mede kepeth loue hows men ben couetou space gyue parte knowe cupides fortune apryse deceyueth al couetyse hateth al negardry loke party sooth ensample fynde wryten babeo loue menage fayter hyr age hyght vyota name whiche ful youthe game hyr seft large fre suche another chynche e men wise al londe afaited honde seruaunt whiche spodius called wise thus worldes good suffysaunce lykyng plesaun longeth ryc esse loue stood grete dystresse soo yong lusty wyght thyng felle lou right euer serued ouerall begone al tyl cupyde oenus e e medycyn seke ordeyne wold c ryght wyll gratchyng euer hym none fare pynche spare worldes mukke gete encrees goth wretche loueles beiaped scarcyte large free set herte dispend crocius hath bende venus took hold shot oft wold loo thus departeth loue al man wol felawe gyue spend telle worthy dwelle loues courte releued thy sone yf leued thou shalt large thy dispence fader conscyence ony thyng amys wylle amend toward loue namely sone wel redyly thou saist yt wel paid al ferthermore shall vnto thy shryft specyfye auary progenye vyce sueth thou shalt haue wonder hit among folk many regne suche vyce myght regne comune alle assayes men may fynde dayes cuncta creatum deus et qui cuncta c uit dampnant ingrati dictum quam facto viu non dolor longe stat quo si ami traxit et fine deserit esse suam hic quitur super illa aborta specie auaricie que ingratitudo dictum e cuius codicioni non lum creator sed cuncte creature abhominabilem detestantur vyce lyke vnto fende neuer yet ma frede cleped vnkyndeship couyne felauship auaryce witholde thynketh shold bolde vnto moder hym bare hym may neuer man wol haue meryte wold acquyte world moche vsed fewe ben excused telle hym endeles thus saye neuertheles vyce cometh sonde taketh thoke hode though al myghtes serue shall hem thyng deserue taketh ony man may gyue whyle hath one day lyue wylle nothyng reward ag yne grutcheth gyue ageyne hath berne fulle maketh kynde herte dulle sey trust suche frendship fyndeth kyndeship speke wordes pleyne thus many man compleyne dayes thou shalt fynde nede fewe frendes kynde thou hast done hem bifore forgeten lore bookes speken vyce tellen god iustice wey kynde also nature euery lyuynge creature lawe also dampne vnkynde man ar et natura cristus sit omnia iura dampnat ingratum lamentantur fore natum hit one vnkynde hynge done ageyne kynde kynde neuer stood man yelde euylle goode wold take hede beste glad goood dede loueth creature lawe nature whiche doth hym ese se mater auctoryte ful oftyme hath befalle w rof tale among v alle whiche old samplary thynke specyfye hic narrat quod bestie suis benefi n hominem ingratum naturaliter prece unt et ponit exemplum de rome senature qui quadam sta venacionis insistens dum predicta day per woode huntyng went happeth sodeyne went chase pursueth thorugh happe man escheweth felle vnware pyt myght let pytte depe felle lowe men none myght knowe bicame none nygh falle meschyef syghe thus alone lay clepend cryend day secoure delyueraunce til ageyne eue felle per chaunce whylo bicam nyght poure man bardus hyght come forth walkend asse gadred hym tasse grene stykkes drye selle whome wold hem bey lyuelode myght suche loode towne asshe carye felle hym tarye tyme nyhe pytte trusse fast knyt herd voyce cryed dymme ere brymme hath leyd herd man seid help adryan wylle geue al good poure man vnderstood wold gladly wyn lord within spak said yf saue sikernes shalle haue couenaunt afterward thow wilt gyue suche reward thou behyghtest beforne hath othe sworne heuen goddes alle myght bifalle hym oute pytt brought goodes ought shal haue euen haluendele bardus seid wold wele word asse anon vntrusse therupon doune goth co pyt whiche hath ende knyt staf wherby said wold adryan hym shold hold thenne per fallen pytte fallen ape whiche throwe whan rope doune cam lowe sodenly therto skypte bothe armes clypte bardus asse anon hym hath vpdrawen gone sawe ape wend ben iape fayry sore hym dradde adryan eftsones gradd help cryed fast eftsones cord cast whan come vnto grounde grete serpent hath bewound whiche bardus anon vp drough hym thought wel ynough hit fanton b yet herd voyce therto answerd arte thou goddes name quod adryan whiche good thou shalt haue euen half od bardus god half thyrd tyme assay shall caste cord forth pytte came hym lord rome nam therupon hym hath dressid hond ful ofte blessi bad bardus hale vnderstood tale bitwene hym asse al softe hath drawen set hym vp lofte without harme esyly said one graunt mercy forth hym went cyte lete poure bardu neuertheles symple couenaunt ca hath asked ye answerd said yf yt hym vp braide ought hath spoken done shall wroken hym soone hym better dede none rede asse ageyne cast trusse hyed hym homeward fast cam home bedde told wyf spedde fynally speke ought nto lord dradde hym sore one word durst sey vpon morowe ageyne maner recorde forth asse cord gader woode er goth cometh ther nto place wold gan ape anone behold whiche gadred al aboute stykkes rowte leyd hem redy hond wherof made isse bonde fro day day wyse thus profered seruyse woode ynough vpon tyme drough toward woode sawe beside grete gastly serpent glyde til came presence hir kynd reuerence hath hym done forth stone bryght castalle oute hir mouthe way lete doune falle went hir way shold adrad thenne poure bardus gladde end god stone goeth taketh vp anone hath grete wonder wytte beest hym hath quytte man hath failed whome moost trauayled put goddes honde torn home fond nto wyf hath shewde bothe lewd den shold selle l nger wold dwelle forthe anone vpon tale stone profereth sale ryght hym self sette wler anone hym fette gold made payement therof none delayement thus stone boyt sold homeward ioye many fold bardus goth came home hows nam gold oute purse within fond also stone therin wherfor ioye hert playd wyf thus said gold loo ston wyf wonder therupon asked hym myght trouthe quod dare swere vpon book marchaunt took went knowe entent thurgh god grace thy morow place wyl assay selle yf wol hym dwelle pe purse ageyne dare sauely swere seyn vertue stone morowe cam gone aboute stede stone selle dede left chapman whan cam e presence wyf home oute p r anone nome gold fond stone thus felle hym ral sold dyuerse place suche fortune grac wel maye thyng b hyd ne last kyd fame goth aboute rome ferforth wordes come emperour iustynyan lete send man asked hym bardus told hym serpent eke be al though made none biheste trauaylle wel quyt mannes wyt made couenaunt mouthe swore therto al couthe parte gyue halue good hath forgeten stood wold
