wodryng among p last neuerthelese party whiche hath pleyned lawe hath demed ordeyned hem auysed webe shall haue haluendel thorugh oute adryans good thus vnkynde blode stondeth memorye vnto day thorugh yt euery wyse may ensamplyn hym took mynde shame vnkynde ageyne whiche reson debateth euery creature hateth thy sone thy offyce rede thou flee ylke vyce right cronycle adryan feyth forgate worldes cou fys ful oft suche maner wy louers man may see ful many vnkynd wel promyse euyl la lyf last whan haue hir ylle done hir loue gone soone saist thou soone fader wol saye allas euer suche man borne hen hath trouthe sworn hath loue wold ony tyme shold euer berde fynd fals vnkynde fader touchend may stonde degre took neuer loue e may goo therby doo profi e el ony spede fynd may wel thynk al dare speke ou yf durst wold pleyn whome suffre peyn loue euer hyr lyche hot nother gyft nother byhote rewardyng seruyce hit lyst hyr maner wyse wylle sey kynde seye vnkynde dare god aboue whiche demeth e ry herte loue wote myn owne side shall vnkyndenes abyde shall lady dwell therof dare telle good fader telle ye thenke sone vnkyndeship whiche toward thy ladyship thou pleynest wyll nought thou arte blame thought may thy desyre though brenne euer doth fir r hir honoure mysset el tyme cometh yet whiche stondeth vpon thy destyne thy sone rede thynke wel euer bifalle man hath lustes alle thou toldest biforne thou loue art forsworn hast vnkyndenysse thou myght therof thy grace blysse leue thy contenannce forther may suche g uaunce loue vnkyndeship wherfore kepe thy worship olde bokes tale shalle telle dy tale en wel ware therby wyl openly hic ponit exemplum contra istos o amo ingratoe et narrat qualiter theseus cadani filius consilio suffultus adriane regis mynos filie domo qd orinthus dicitur minotaurum vincit vnde theseus adriane sponsalia certissime p omittens ipsam vna cum fedra sorore sua creta secum nauigio duxit statim postea oblito gratitudinis beneficio adrianam ipsum saluantem insula chion spretam post tergum reliquit fedra ni sibi sponsatam ingratis coronauit ynos telleth poete wiche sotyme kynge crete sone androche hyght befell nto athenis ere sent bare hym lygnage suche pryde tooke courage forgeten hath scoles ryote among fooles dyd many thynges wrong vsed lyf long til last wrought fond meschyef yt whiche souyt thorugh felle yt slayn fader whiche herd sayn wrothe euer myght men armes hym dyght strong power forth went vnto athenis brent pleyne countre al cytees stode hym doute defence hadde ageyne power ladde egeus kyng couceylle took vppon thynge cyte soo pee trete bitwene mynos egeus fele ben acorded thus kyng mynos fro yere yere receyue shal thou shalt oute athenys truage men myghty age persones nyne whiche shall wyll doo special vengeaunce sonnes deth none grace ne geth take iuyse done suche wyse whiche stood wonder ca tyme wherof men yet rede synge kyng mynos kepyng cruel monstre seith geste half man half beeste mynotaurus hote whiche bigoten ryote vppon phasyfe owne wyf while oute vpon strif greete syege troye lost hath al ioye sawe moustre bore bad men ordeyne another fore felle tyme thus clerk one dedalus ben hir assent hir world hath myswent made owne wyt wherof remembraunce yet mynotaure suche hows strong merueylous man within went soo many dyuerse went ne shall come oute go amasyd al aboute hows loke warde mynotaurus put warde lyf therm cam man beest ouercam slewe fedde hym therupon wise many one athenys truage deuoured rage euery yere shopen hem athenys go toward thylke woful channce set ordynaunce vpon fortune lot caste til theseus last whiche ye kynges sonne amonges felle lot vppon chaunce felle knyght worthy al whan sawe chaunce falle ferd though took hede al euer myght spede hym felauship forth grece goth ship kyng mynos sought profereth al hym ought vpon poynt hir acorde sterne kyng cruel lorde toke euery day one nyne put hym disciplyne mynotaure deuoured theseus fauoured kepte till last mene whyle cast mene thyng hym best felle adryane tho whiche douyter mynos herd worthy los theseus myght sawe lusty knyght hole herte hym layd also loue hir prayd ferforth alone ordeyned anone maner shold hym saue shope dyd hym haue clewe threde wiche withynne fyrst atthe dore shal begynne wold ageyn ward wende hym take one ende go wey ouer sey speche tooke hym pelot whiche shold throte mynotaure cast ryght suche wepen also hym dyght reson may fayle make ende batayle hym taught dyuerse wyse tyl conyng enpryse best shold kylle thus shortely telle mayden hym taught theseus monstre faught smote hede ye nam thred cam gothe ageyne til oute grete wonder al aboute mynos tribute hath rebeced werre al seced bitwene athenis hem crete speke swete who beaute withoute wane fayre mayden adryane saw theseus sounde neuer yet vppon grounde gladder wyght tho theseus dwellyd day two mayden spak rowned hym abandouned euer couthe hyr lusty youthe al pryuely bytwene hem twey first floure took awey fayre hyr behyght euer whyle lyue myght shold hyr take wyf owne hertes lyf shold hyr loue trouthe hyr bere myght forbere sore loueth hym ageyne euer wold seyne al hir hert leuyth thus purpoos acheuyth assured trouthe hym went routhe fedra hir yong suster eke lusty mayden sobre meke fulfilled al curtosye susterhode companye loue whiche hem bytwene see hir suster made quene hir fader lefte forth went hym al first entent forgate within litel throwe al ouerthrowe wend shold stonde ship blowen fro londe wherin lay sailend adryan mochel fere wyndo lowde blewe see ne knewe praid reste whyle felle vpoon yle nyght ben dreue hyr leue hath yeue shall londe take hir rest nothyng hir best londe brought whiche yt tyme thought nouyt al trouthe took kepe hath layd hir doune slepe long hath ben forwatched certes euyl matched fer loues kynde best vnkynde theseus whiche trouthe kept yonge lady slept fulfylled vnkyndeship hath forgeten al godeshyp whiche adryan hym done bad shypmen soone hale vp saile abyde forth gothe tyde toward athenys londe left lady stronde slepend til awoke whan cast vp hyf loke toward stronde saw wyyt hyr herte sore aflyght ne wyst thynke drowe hyr water bryncke biheld see large sawe ship sawe barge ferforth myght kenne lord said suche synne al world shal vppon woful woman worthy knyyt hath done wroyt wend loue bought deserued nede stode vppon drede also loue behyght grete wondre myght towardes vnkynde soo lete mynde thyng said owne mouthe whan couthe drawen worldes fame shalle hynderyng name wel wote soo wote gaf trouth bodyly honoure shold kepe word gan wepe sorowed ynough hyr fair tress drough hyr self took suche strif bitwene deth lyf swounend lay ful oft among hym long whiche loue vnkynd wherof wrong shall euermo stonde cronycle remembraunce also asketh vengeaunce vnkynde loues ca theseus al though noble knyght lawe loues ryght forfeyted hath alwey adryane putt awey whiche grece vnkynde dede rede fedra suster took stede hyr fel afterward mekel tene vyce whiche mene vnkyndeship whore falleth trouthe mannes herte palleth good dede acquyte may stonde meryte towardes god also men calle hym worldes soo fende vnto another mannes frende al toward hym self alone thy sone thy persone vyce aboue flee fader ye teche thynk doo matere ouer wold fayn wherof shal shryue good sonne thy lore reule couetyse shalle propyrte deuyse euery vyce herken wel ware thervp viribus ex clara re tollit luce rapina floris et iuncta virgine mella ca pit hic tractat super illa specie auaricie que rapina nuncupatur cuius mater extorcio ipsam ad deseruiendum magnatum curijs specialius commendauit lygnage audry sone yet vyce ryght name rauyne whiche hath route couyne rauyne among maystres dwelleth seruautes men telleth extorcion witholde rauyne mennes folde maketh lord payeth nought euer may sought hows ther shall thyng lack ful ofte abyeth pack poure men dwellen aboute thus stodeth comyn peple doute whiche doo none amendement whan hym fayleth payment rauyne maketh none skyle taketh strengthe ben wyse louers shal deuyse whan el may auayle anone strengthe assayle gete loue sesyne see tyme rauyne loue certes fader lady loue soo though pompey al world wold obey el suche alisandre wold suche sclaundre good man soo doth good feyth sone thou seyst sooth wol purueannce suche weye lust auaunce shal sore abye yf old example lye good fader telle one conne many one touchend loue matere lysten sone thou shalt hath befallen loues cause man take rauyne pray whiche femenyne hic ponit exemplum contra istos amoris causa raptores et narrat qualiter pandyon rex athenensis du filias progne aute regi tracie terres desponsata contigit quod cum tereus ad instanciam vxoris sue philomenam de athenis traciam sorore visitacionis causa secum quadam vice perduceret concupiscencia philoment tanta seueritate itinere dilapsus est quod non solum ipse violencia sue rapine virginitate oppressit sed et ipsiue linguam non factum detegeret forpice intulauit vnde imperpetue memorie cro nicam tanti raptoris postea vindicarut ther ryal noble kyng ryche al worldes thyng whiche propre enherytace athenis gouernaunce thynketh therupon name kyng pandyon two doughters wyf whiche loued lyf first doughter proygne hyght second wel myght called faire philomene felle moche tene fader purueaunce doughter proygne wold auance gaf hir vnto maryage worthy kyng lygnage noble knyght also honde kyd euery lond trace hyght thereus clerk ouyde telleth thus thereus wyfe home ladde lusty lyf hir hadde till felle vppon tyde proygne lay hym besyde bethought hyr myght hir suster myght see hyr lord hir wylle said goodly wordes hym praid hyr myghe goo yf lyked hym wold hym self wende el somme sende whiche myght hir sufter grete shape myght mete hir lord anone herd gaue acord thus answerd wille said youre sake wey youre suster take self bryng hir yf may lay igan hym hir armes clyppe kyssed hym hyr softe lyppe said syre graunt mercy sone redy tooke leue go sory tyme dyd soo thereus goth forth shippe hym felaushippe see right cours nam countrey til cam philomene dwellyng hyr suster tydyng told glade mochel ioye hym made fader moder bothe leue hir doughter lothe yf presence neuertheles reuerence hym wolde hym self trauaile wold shold faile praid gyue hir leue wold behynde leue al hast made hir toward hir suster fare thereus forth went hole entent fro hir frendes gone sottith hym hyr loue anone eyen myght witho ne must hyr behold sight gan desyre set owne herte fyre fire towe approchet hym anone strengthe rocheth till hete deuoured towe ne may succoured tiraunt rauener power therto sawe tyme space lose hath al grace forgate wedded man rage hir ran ryght wolf taketh pray bygan ye pray fader moder dere help ne myght lytel myght defence ageyne rude knyght make woode reson vnderstoode helde hir vnder suche wyse myght arise say oppressid dysesed yf goushauke seysed byrd whiche durst f remeue thus tiraunt aft suche thyng men seyn may neuer yolden ageyn vyrgyny suche auyn py self came meschyef hede name knewe maid woful herte thus said thou al men werse euer man ders doo suche dede thou hast day shall falle hope soo shalle telle oute fylle speche shall fulfille wyde world rede lengthe thou hast done str gth yf among peple dwelle vnto peple shall telle yf walle stone closed shalle vnto stone clepe telle hem al felonye yf wodes wende shalle le en crye byrdes oute shall al aboute lowde shall reherse voyce shall heuen perce shalle sowne goddes er fals man thy fere uel ony beest shalt thou hold thy byheste whiche thou vnto suster mades thou al loue vngladese arte ensample al vntrewe wold god suster knewe thyn vntrouthe stood lyon wode vnhappy hondes stronge caught tress longe whiche bond hir armes feble dede armes grounde anone hyr case oute clyppeth also fase hir tong payre sheres yt blode eres oute hir eyen hir mouthe made hir fayr fa e vncouthe lay swownyng vnto deth vnnethe ony birth yet hir tong reft lytel parte yet left word al may sowne chi e bird iargowne neuertheles woode hounde hyr body hent vp fro thr ground put towre strong right wronge pur osed alway shold abyde hir deyng day neuertheles taketh h felle mysdede al meschyef befalle thereus fowle hym befalle comen palays ner wyf anon mylde chere al reuerece honourably hym kept hit sawe anon wept dissey bigan oske streyte suster said dede quam igue ab id woful wyf stood bitwene hir deth lyf cause herd tydyng sawe hir lord wepyng wende al trouthe wel routhe perles forsaken hir black clothes taken gentil kyn e worship hir susters mynde made ryche entyerement found none amendement syghe sobbe sorowe gyle vnder gore leue kyng quene torne ageyne philomene bigan telle erste cam pryson ferst thought kyngis donghtet strauge make sodeyne chaunge fro welthe vnto grete wo began thynk tho though mouthe thyng praid within hir herte thus said thou almyghty iubyter bye sittest lokest fer thou suffrest many wrongful doyng yet thy wyllyng may thyng hid thou knowest betid wold ben borne forlorn speche vyrgynyte good lord whan thou therof wil vengeace shape delyueraunce euer among lady wept thought neuer kept worldes woman wysshed euermore vnto sufter dere hir speketh manere said suster ye knewe myn estate ye wold rewe trowe delyueraunce ye wold shap vengeaun hym fals man neuertheles wpf send somme tokenyng wherof ye shal haue som know bechyng thyng wote shal yow lothe whiche toucheth lothe within whyle wafe clothe sylke al whyte letter ymagery whiche al foly r u hir done lopped gedre sone set hir signet therupon sent proygne anon messager forth bare amounted ware neuertheles proygne goth pryuely taketh hir clothe went ageyne ryght cam courte hym herde nam proygne philomene herd wold knowe ford opened man brouyt wo ther hath wrouyt meschyef befalle swoune gan doune falle efte aroos gan stonde efte taketh clothe hond ld letter ymages last oute suche outrage said wepe bote swereth yf leue mote shall ven ed otherwise gan hir auyse fyrst myght vnto hyr wyn hir suster man swore shold knowe shope therfore thereus thyng wyst yet ryght hir seluen lyst hir suster delyuerd soone oute pryson mone proigne brouyt nyght syght chambre alone made many pit u mone proigne sorowe made whiche sawe hir suster pale fade specheles dishonoured ben de oured also vpon hir lord thought vntruely wrought spousede broken made vowe shold wroken word kneled doune wepyng grete deuocion vnto cupide venus praid said thus ye whome thynge asterde loue may euery herte ye knowe ye ben aboue god goddesse loue ye wyte wel euer yet wylle al wyt sith first ye shope wedde lay lord bedde haue ben trewe degre euer thought neuer loue place al kyng trace whiche lord wyf allas woful strif hym thus ageynward fynde vntre vnkynde euer lady armes lay well wote ne may amend wrong grete ful lytel lete myne owne suster tooke wyf forsoke loo thus venus cupyde praid ferthermore cryde vnto ollo hyhest said myghty god rest thou doo vengeaunce debate suster al hir estate thou knowest hath forlore hyr mandenhede therfore al world shall blame suster hath shame thereus hir sent wel thou knowest myn entet al worshyp good lord geuest lyues fode euery wyght pray woful susters ben late v lothe ben thyn owne woman lothe thus playneth proigne asketh wreche though hir suster tack speche hym al thyng wote hir sorowe lesse hote herd hem two hym ought haue sorowed euermo sorowe hem bitwene signes pleyneth philomene proigne seith shall wreke world therof shall speke proigne sykenes feyned wherof vnto hir lord pleyned praid myght hir chambre kepe hir lysteth wake slepe hir graunted thus gedre two wold hym lytell good herken herafter stood woful auentures felle susters ben bothe felle hem alonge grete wronge whiche thereus hem done purpose venge hem soone thereus proigne wyf sone lyf beloued hyght moder wyst wel myght reus greue slee child leue thus yt said madde wo whiche hath ouerladde withoute insight moderhede forgate pyte lost drede hir chambre pryuely child withoute noyse cry slewe hewe hym al peces dyuerse spyeces flesshe hewe taketh made therof sewe fader mete serued gan hym ete ne wist stood thus owne flesshe blood hym self deuoured ageyne kynde hym fore vnkynde vp ryse herte shold agryse shewe hym child dede philomene took vp hede bitwene two disshes al wrothe cam forth susters bothe setten borde proigne began word said werst wykke conseyence whome prykke may stere loo thou hast doo lo ben susters two rauener loo thy praye whome falsely way thou hast thy tirannye wrought lo somdele bought better shall thy dede world shall euer synge rede remembraunce thy defame thou loue hast done suche shame shall neuer forgete sterte vp fro mete shoue boord flore caught swerd anone swore shold hondes deye vnto goddes crye bigan lowde steuene herd vp heuene twynkelyng eye goddes meschyef seye formes chaunged al thre eche hem degre torned birdes kynde delyuerly men may fynde seate ynne formes set twynne telleth tale first nyghtingale shapen philomene whiche wynter sene leues falle naked en busshes alle byrde hir wylle euer hyd dwelle pryue place noman shold see hir face shame myght lassid thyng passid whan lost hir maydenhede euer vpon hir womanhede though god wold hir chage thynketh straunge holdeth hir cloos wynter day whan wynter goth awey nature goddesse wylle hir owne fre largesse herbis floures bothe tse feldis medowes clothe also woodes greues ben hylled grene leues byrd hir hyde may bitwene mar apryl may e wynter held cloos pure shame aroos whan sawe bowes thyck bare styck hyd leuys grene wode cometh philomene maketh hir playnte nyght day say ng euery man may ne yet mayde soo old wyse said whiche vnderstoode ment hir note ben suche entent eke said songe maketh grete ioye myrthe amog said bird face may hyd though haue lost maydenhede shal man see chekes rede thus medleth ioye wo hir sorowe myrthe also soo loues maladye maketh dynerse melo ye said loue woful blysse wysdom man wysse lusty feuer wounde soft note reherceth ofte hem vnderstond tale haue nyghtyngale whiche erst cleped philomene told al euer wold mene bothe hir forme hir note wherof men may story note hir suster proigne fynde torned oute kynde swalowe swyft wynge also wynter lyeth sowyng may thyng sene world woxen grene comen somer tyde flyeth forth begyn chyde chatereth oute hir langage falshede maryage telleth maner speche termes spouse breche wol woodes dwelle wold openly telle also spouse amog folkes cometh howse doo wyues vnderstonde falshede hir husbonde ware hem also many vntrewe tho thus ben susters byrdes asthe ben ward men lothe ne wylle pure shame man honde tame euer dwelleth hir mynde fond man vnkynde fals thereus suche one among v note condycyon men saye euery regyon within wne eke withoute regneth comonly aboute namely remembraunce wyll declare vengeaunce goddes hym ordeyned susters pleyned anoue chaunged owne kynde straunged lapwenche made thus hoppeth gras hede stondeth vp ryght crest token knyght yet vnto day men seith lapwenche hath lost feyth byrd ful est alle confessor ware sone ye falle yf thou suche couyne gete loue rauyne thy lust may falle thus befelle thereus amans fader god forbede leuer fortrede wyld horse drawe er ageyne loue lawe dyd ony thyng lowde stylle whiche ladyes wylle men seyen euery loue hath drede foloweth hir drede hir loue dredeth plese loue serue hym nedeth thus maye ye knowe skylle rauyn doo wyll ageyne hir wylle suche weye whyle lyue wylle obeye abydynge hir curtosye ony mercy wold hyr ply thy fader wote haue doo amys ferthermore shalle byseche thou som poynt ye teche asketh forth yf ought may better taught iu vt ex spolijs grandi quam sepe tumultum quo graditur p pul latro perurget iter sic amor ex su poterit quo carpere predam si locus est aptus cetera multa timet hic loquitur super cupiditatis specie quam furtum vocant cuius ministri alicuius legis offensam non metutes tam amoris causa qua ali r saam quam sepe conscienciam offendunt whan couetyse poure estate stondeth hym self vpon debate thurgh lack mysgouernaunce vnto sustenauce ne none wey fynde gete hym good blynde whiche seeth shalle falle ylke vyce yt calle robbery taketh honde thorugh water londe thyng men forswynke geteth hym clothe mete drynke hym retcheth begyn though theft soo may wyn thy make purchaas lyeth waytyng paas thyng yt seeth ther passe taketh paas lasse ought worth take pakkes wel rensake pryncly bereth none gold ne fyndeth oute ewel taketh propyrte wodes feldes eke thus robbery goth seke may purpoos fynde right kynde good sone thou myght speke loue matere make veray resemblaunce right thefe maketh cheuesace robbeth mennes goodes aboute woode feld goth oute ben louers wylde stedes come fynd woman able therto space couenable withoute let fare take parte chaffare ye though shepeherdesse yet wold lord wantonnesse assay though v mete mennes good swe therof wote nothyng wyf f whiche loueth hir lyf hir lord sytteth neuer dele e loue vntrewe e robbed pa tooke lust vnder shawe ageyne loue ageyne lawe thyng sene forbede vngoodly dede taketh robberye loue e may ustyfye cause ful oft sythe onye hath ben blythe shall sory thryes example suche robberyes fynde wryten thou shalt acordynge vnto matere hic loquitur contra istos amo causa predones qui cum suam furtiue concupiscenciam aspirant fortuna contra u operatur et narrat quod cum neptunus quandam virginem mine cornicem solam inxta dea bulantem opprimere suo furto voluisset superueniens pallas ipsam de manibus eius virginitate seruata gracius l bera rede whilome w id fairest ouyde said hir tyme tho chambre also allas goddesse wyfe mar whome prowesse gyuen worthy knyghtes grete myghtes gouerneth bataile withoute hym may auayle strong honde helpe maye knyght armes yelpe fyght vnder banere speke matere faire fresshe lusty may alone went day vpon stronde play cam neptunus way whiche hath see gouernauce herte suche plesaunce tooke maiden sygh hert aroos hyghe sodenly vnware beheld beaute bare cast anone herte shall hym wey asterte yf take auauntage mayden l ge broches ne thynges somme smale thynges thought haue parte yt wet hir bothe armes hent put hond toward cofre wherfor robbe made profere lusty tresour stele whiche passeth goodes fe called may enhede floure womanhede mayde c nyx name cleped dredyng al shame sawe myght debate wel wyst wold algate fulfylle lust robberye anone began wepe crye said pallas noble quene shewe thy myght late sent kepe saue myn honoure help lese floure whiche vnder key loken worde soone spoken pallas shope recouyre wylle desyre hir whiche mayden w sodenly vpon ca oute hir woman kynde byrdes lykenes fynde transformed forth neptunus thyng stall thyng wold haue stole federes black ony cole oute armes throwe flewe eyen crowe whiche hir delyte kepe hir maydenhede whyte vnder wede fethers blake perlys whyte forsake lyf may restore ageyne thus neptune hert veyn hath vppon robbery set byrd flowen let fayr mayde fro hym scaped euer le ei ed sco e hath ore sone e thou ware therfore thou maydenhede stele wherof men see dy fele al day befalle dyuerse wyse shal yet deuyse another tale therupon felle old yes gone hic ponit ex plu cotra istos causa virginitatis lese predonis et narrat qd cum calistona regis lichoantis mire pulcritudinis filia suam virginitatem ane conseruare castissima voluisset et luam que tegea dicitur inter alias hidem nimphas moraturam se transtulit ubiter virginis castitatem subtili furto surripiens quendam filium qui postea archas nominatus e ex ea genuit vnde iuno calistona semel eius pulcritudinem vrse tur pissime deformitatem subito transfigurauit kyn lychaon vpon wyf doughter goodely lif cleue mayden worthy fame calystona whoos right name cleped many lorde besought hyr acorde loue myght man wyn lust therin swore hyr herte said wold euer maid wherfor kepe hir self pee suche amadryades clexed maydens tho nymp e eke also vpon spryng fresshe welles shope dwelle nowhere ell thus cam calistona wode tegea vyrgynyte behyght vnto dyane therto plygh hir trouthe vpon bowes g ne kepe hir maydenhede clene whiche afterward vpon day pryuely stolen away iubiter thorugh queyntyse hir toke suche wyse sodenly forth alle hyr wombe aroos swalle myght hydde therupon betydde dyane whiche herd telle pryue place vnto welle nymphes al companye comen aragerye said bathe wold bad euery mayden shold hyr al naked bathe also began preuy woo c listona wex rede shame knewe game whome suche thyng befalle none made hem naked alle thyng wold hyde withdrewe hir euer asyde netheles flode dyana hir selue stood thought come vnperceyued therof deceyued cam lytell nyghe dyana wombe seygh said awey thou fowle beest thyn estate honeste chast water touche thon hast suche touche whiche neuer may hole ageyne thus goth forleyn shame nymphes fledde til nature hir spedde sonne hyght archas named delyuerd iuno wyf iubiter wrothe hastyf purpoos doo vengeaunce came forth vpon chaunce calistona spakke set vpon hyr many lacke said thou arte take thou thy werk may forsake thou vngoodly ypocryte thou arte gretely wyte thou shalt fnl sore abye ylke stelthe mycherye thou hast bothe take doo wherof thy fader lychao shall glad wote doughter soo hote hath broken hir chast vowe shall chastyse thy grete beaute shal torned thorugh whiche yt thou hast mystorned thy large fronte thy eyen gray shall hem chaunge way feture thy face suche wyse shall deface euery man shal forbere forth lykenes fer took forshapen anon within tyme therupon byfelle bowe honde hunte gamen fonde woode gothe playe hir sone archas waye happed came good hede name stood vnder bowe knewe hym well hym drowe though hir forme lore loue lost therfore whiche kynde hath set vnder lawe vnder woode shawe hyr child belhed glade hir armes sprade though womanhede toward hym come took hede bare bowe bente arowe sente gan tyse bowe none knowe beest wylde inpiter wold shylde moder sone also ordeyned hem bothe euer saue thus sone thou myght haue ensample flee robbe vyrgynyte yong innocent awey euer ouy wey old bookes rede sache robberye drede namely goode whiche euer woman goode desyreth kepe hold somtymes dayes old yf thou tale wel thou may somde old ensample take heede floure maydenhed tyme holden pry shall euer stonde thou shalt vnderstonde herkene tale next sewend maydenhede commend hic loquitur de virginitat comm dacione vbi dicit quod nuper imperatores obstanti status dignitatem virginibus sedebant via rome amog gestes old fynde valery told man euer emperour rome shold honoure vyrgyn weye hir mete shold obeye worshyp vyrgynyte grete dignyte woman tho chaste men also commended ouerall speke therof special hic loquitur qualiter phirinus iu uenu rome pulcherrimus vt ill sa sua virginitatem conseruaret ambo oculos ruens vulti sui decorem abhominabilem constituit touchend men ensaple fynd phirinus yt ma kynd aboue al fayrest rome also comlyest well hyr myght behold haue hym syght thus tempted ofte sore wold among woman coueyted beaute face streyted hath threst oute bothe eyen wymmen hym seyn afterward hym ne rought thus maydenhede bonght may proue wil thy aboue al vnder sky maydenhede preyse vertues wold peyse apocalipsis recordeth cast heuen best acordeth hij sequntur agnum quocumqy erit may shewe wel therfore haue told bere fore heuen erthe also except bothe two oute flesshe man leuen gregory hath ensample geuen carne preter carnem viuere pocius vita angelica est quam humana ierom seyth shall rather told lyker angel many fold lyf man kynde reson fynde thorugh grace aboue flesshe withoute flesshely loue man lyue chast neuertheles man may suche haue ben yet ben vertu selden wonne mater haue begonne thynke telle therof whiche sone thy lor lyst take hede trete vpon maydenhede vt rosa de spinis spineto preualet orta vt filij flores cespite plura valet c sibi virgiuitas carnis sposalia vin cit eternos fetus que sine lahe parit bookes seyn man lyf vpon knyghthode werre strif set among enemyes right freel flessh who nature ay redy spurne falle fyrst foman alle werre redy ay werreth nyght werreth day man hath neuer rest therfore knyght best thorugh myght grace god sonde whiche bataill may withstode wherof dwelleth memorye hem somtyme vyctorye dedely werre hadden hyhe prowesse ye hadd thorugh ye sowle stood amended vpon erthe yet commended hic loquitur qualiter valentinianus imperator ipse octogenarius plures prou ncias romano imperio belliger sub iugauit dixit se super onia magi gaudere de eo quod contra sue carnis concupiscenciam victoriam op nuisset nam et ipse virgo omnibus diebus vite sue castissimus permansit emperour old dayes al assayes worthy knyyt honde suche lod yet vassellage stood vn wedded al age cronycle told honderd wynter old men wold dedes peyse knyghthode armes preyse hondes kynges londes subiection put vnder pryce wonder set none acounte seid myght amounte ageyn one poynte hath nomen flesshe hath ouercomen virgyn sayde batayle pry laid lo sone auyse fader may wel al soo world men sone ag lawe men may fynde god man lawe kynde hath set world multyplye wylle hym iustyfye doo lawe neuertheles youre good sawe good kepe may wol ageyne seye nay sone take say maydenhede taken away withoute lawes ordynaunce may fayle vengeauuce yf thou wylt sooth wyten behold tale whiche wryten kyng agamenon cyte l sbon wonuen mayden fond fairest londe tyme men wyst hir hym lyst wherof daungerous ye thyng yt whiche precious fayre mayden cleped creseyde doughter crysys whiche tyme speciall tyme bisshop pryncipal phebus sacryfyce wel vyce agamenon way troyward tooke way mayden hym ladde grete lust hir hadde phebus yt whiche grete disdeyne yt maiden forleyn anone troye came mengeaunce vpon dede name aud sent comune pestylence sought hir euydence made calculacion knowe condicyon deth cam sodenly last redyly cause also man fonde forth stounde agamenon opposed whiche hath knowleched ye ca foly hath wrought therupon mercy sought toward god dyuerse wyse prayer sacryfyce mayden home sende gafe hir gold ynough spende euer whyles wold lyue thus syn forgyue pestylence seced loo encrecid loue whiche ylle wonne letter vnbegonne take thyng withoute leue whiche thou must nedes leue yet haue maugre forth thy robben ouerall loues cause yf thou begynne ease thou shalt wynne fader wyl wy sone wel ware youre examplarye loue cause robberye haue right wel vnderstonde ouer stonde yet wol wyte youre apryse thynge couetyse idiando latens tempus rimatur et horam fur quibus occulto tempore furta parat sic amor insidijs vacat et sub tegmine laudes predere furtiuos nocte fauente queat hic tractat super illa cupiditatis specie que secrum latrocinium dicitur cuius natura custodire rerum nesciente ea que cupit tam per diem quam per n c tem absqy strepitu clauculo fnratur wyth couetyse yf fynde seruaunt kynd steleth hote myche ye hym euer companye whome yf shall telle sooth stalketh pecok doth taketh pray soo couerte man wote aperte wote lord home wold stalke aboute come thyng fynt way sawe men away steleth goth forth al therof man knowe shal eke uf oft goth nyght withouten mone sterre lyght craft dore vnpykyth taketh therin hym lyketh yf dore shet entre lette wylle wyndowe crept whyle lord fast slepe steleth thyng hym best lyst goth wey wyst ful ofte also lyght day yet wold stele make assay vnder cete hond put knyf purs cut receyueth fynde therin thus auntreth hym wyn bereth horne bloweth man counceyll knoweth may gete mychyng al bylle vnder wyng hound goth fold hath taken wold mouth vppon gras wypeth feyned chere hym slyketh euer shepe strangle man therof shall iangle knowe dede ryght doth stelthe euery stede hym lyst pray take wel cause make wel feyne wel glose ne shalle man suppose innocent thus mannes eye blent craft may vse withoute helpe ony refuse ben louers degre hir lust pryuete sey geten al stelthe ther atteynen grete welthe tyme lasteth loue awayteth euer casteth may stele catche pray therto may fynde way nyght day taketh parte may yf may doo yet wol stele kysse two telle yf thou euer dydest ony wyse thy lady vnto fader sone thus thou haue stolen ony kus thyng therto longeth man suche theues hongeth telle thy sey trouthe fader nay routhe wylle thefe moost lef yet durst neuer pryuete mot one take byr kne stele hir yf durst wote wel netheles yf lye stelthe ne robberye loue whiche felle thought hir dyd neuer nought seyn herte fayled shalle castel assayled though hertes ten strong men myn owne man dare vsen may self recouere though man neuer pouere bere herte aud soo faileth wyt shold myn acorde seruaunt lede ayenst lord yf foote wold owhere go hondes wold el herte ageyne remenaunt veyne thus lacketh al weele yet ne dare steele thyng whiche longeth vnto loue eke hie aboue may wel therto areche tyme speche ful seld yf stele may word two go way betwyxt hir estate comparyson may none fele wel wote al heuy hote set hond withoute loue thus mote algate leue stele may take wyse mote forsake en thefe ageyne wylle thyng whiche may fulfylle serpent whiche neuer slepte flees gold wel ne kepte colchos tale told lady thousand folde bet er yemed bewaked clothed naked kepe hir body nyght day hath wardey dy ay whiche wonderful wyght hym man myght swerde ne wepen may daunte ne sleyghte charme enchat wherof myght made tame daunger right name whiche vnder lock vnder key man may hyr stele awey al tresoure vnderfonge vnto loue may longe lest lokyng hir eye mote stole yf seye grutcheth lyte wold sone set wyte hym wold stelle greueth wonder sore prouerbe euer newe straunge lokes maken trewe wolden stele pyke wel man syke hym nether mene whome daunger wold eue lene tresoure hath kepe though wold stalke crepe wayte eue eke morowe daunger shall thyng borowe stele wote wel may nouyt thus right wel bethought daunger stondeth offyce stelthe whiche clepeth vyce shall gylty neuermo therfore wold ago fet neuer hym hert afterward ferd myght afterward perca loue make somme purchaas stelth somme way stont fro fer away fader ye told aboue steleth goth nyght loue maye wele poynte forsake oftymes ne wake nyghtes slepe pray take kepe loked suche wyse nyght may aryse somme wyndowe loken oute see howsyng al aboute may chambre knowe whiche lady trowe lyeth hir bedde slepeth softe hert thefe ful ofte stonde behold long nyghtes ben cold thynk hyr lyeth wysshe wy nectanabus l protheus couthen nygromance lykenes semblauce ryght hem lyst hem self transforme yf suche forme saye wold flee hir chambre see ony grace wold falle myght vnder palle somme thyng loue pyke stele thus thynke thoughtes fele though therof thyng sooth yet case tyme doth last whan fynde falle mynde sce haue stond long haue profyte vnderfonge stalk bed within thynke begyn loue whan shall nyght wylle good myght lacketh bothe grace soo thought enbrace yet haue better ferde fader oo haue ye herde stelthe oue haue doo wylle hath therto worthy penaunce put vnto custodia virgo conseruabatur phebus eiue pulchritudinem concupis hen conclaue domus clara luce sub ntrans virginis pudiciciam matre absente deflorauit vnde ipsa inpregnata ratus pater filiam suam ad toward loue hath within hyr ward phebus loue hath constreyned withoute reste payned herte coueite mayde whiche warded streyte within chambre kepte cloos selden whan discloos goth hir moder play lenchoter men say mayden hyght orc anus hir fader befelle thus doughter kept dere ben bifore yere yere vnder hir moder discyplyne clene malden vyrgyne vpon whoos natyuyte comelyhede beaute nature hath set al may lyche vnto fresshe may eyther monethes yere sourmounteth withoute pere mayden feiture wherof phebus oute mesure hyr loueth euery syde waiteth yf may betyde thorugh ony sleygthe myght hir lusty maydenhede vnright whiche al worldes welth thus lurkyng vpon stelthe awayte longe lay till befelle vppon day thorugh hir chambre wall came al sodenly stalle thyng hym lyefe woo whyle yt thefe venus whiche enemy thylk loues mycherye discouerith playne caa befelle toward phebus concubyne lete couyne thylk loue dedely brothe pleyne vpo mayde goth told hir fader stood wherof sorowe well nyhe woode vnto hir moder thus said loo kepe mayd phebus dare thyng speke vpon shall wreke soo maydens mowe take ensample suffre maydenhede stole deth may thole bad go make pytte wherin hath doughter sette wold pyte haue al quyck graue deed anone presence phebus reuerence ben loue hath wrouyt thoruy power aboue sprong vp oute molde floure named gold whiche stonte gouerneth sonne thus loue euyll wonne ful ofte cometh repentayle fader meruayle counceyll wreyed oftyme loue hath pleyed stole many pryue game whiche neuer yet cam blame thynketh hydde youre tale betydde venus disturbed caas eke also brode daye phebus suche fylthe wrought wherof maide blame brought afterward fore ye seyden fore stelth loue goth nyght doth thynges oute syght therof lust also tale lyche matere wherof myght ensample take good sone thy sake befelle dayes olde poete told vpon nyghtes mycherye herken tale poesye hic ponit yemplum super eodem quod de notte contingit et narrat qualiter hercules cum eola quadam spelunca nobili thophis dictum sub mo te thimolo ibi silua bachi e hospicio pernoctarunt et cum ipsi varijs lectis seperatim iacentes dormi runt contigit lectum herculis vestimentis eole lectum qy eole pelle leonis contra hercules induebatur operari super quo fobnns silua descendeus speluncam subintrauit temptans si forte cum eola sue concupiscencie voluptatem nesciente hercules furari posset et cum ad lectum herculis muliebri palpata veste ex casu peruenisset putans eolam fuisse cubiculum nudo corpore ingreditur quem senciens hercules manibus apprehesum ipsum ad terra ita fortiter al lisit vt inpotens sui corporis effectus vsay mane ipsum requieuit vbi saba cum nymphis siluestribus superue niens ipsum sic illusum deridebat myghtyest men hercules eolen whiche ye loue courage geder whiche syde hath eolen loue thylk caue seid thought best three hir reste thylk day thylke nyght lusty wyght euery thyng hym obeyd lyketh hir al seide long day befelle caue vnder hylle thymolus whiche
