made vpon wey slough euer thus pley took grete mace also knytted hir gyrdel lyche man awyd hercules hath assayd clothen hym array thus iape forth day till hir souper redy hadden souped shopen hem goo rest thought hem best bad thylke nyght two sondry beddes shold dyght e geder lygge nold cause offre wold vpon morowe hir sacryfice seruaunte dyn offyce sondey beddes made anon rest gone eche hem self sondry place fair eolen hath set mace besides beddes bede aboue clothes hir loue hylled hir bedde aboute whiche thyng douts hir wympel wonde aboute chek hir kyrtel hir mantell eke abrode vpon bedde spredde thus slepen bothe bedde trauayle wyn seruaunt lyke dronken swyn bygan rowte fast fanus whiche stelthe cast comen caue fonde al saue withoute noyse went derk nyght syght blent yet happed hym god eolen bed tho leyd alone slepe wold take kepe whoos bed made assay lyon lay cote found eke feleth mace herte ke eth durst abyde stalketh vpon euery side sought aboute hond bed till fond lay wympled vysage tho glad courage hyr kyrtell fonde also eke hir mantell bothe two bespred pon ed oft made hym naked soft bed vnware crepte hercules tyme slept wende well thus stede eole anone profereth hym loue whiche felt man aboue hercules hym threwe ground sore haue hym fond lyggend therupon morowe tho lytel sorowe fanus hym self made nt el al glade loghen hym scorne aboute saba nymp route doune loke ferd sooth herde beiaped oueral sone thou ware al vse suche mycheryes yf thou haue better aspy aunture yf betyde fanus thylke tyde wherof thou myght shamed holy fader certes yf right good leue suche mycherye thynke leue myn faynt herte wol serue maugre wylle deserue thylke place loue ye tolden aboue couetyse pyllage lygnage whiche toucheth shuft pray therof ye wold assay may vyce eschewe sone thou hast herd shewe vyces stont rowe cou yse thou shalt knowe yet one whiche last sacrylege thou fast god hym self debateth wherof e henen hym hatet sacrilegus tantum furto loca sacrum prophanat vt sibi sint agri sic domus dei nec locus est quo temptat amans quod amat si que posse nequit carpere elle capit hic tractat super vltima cupidita specie que sacrilegium dicitur cuius fructum ea quam altissimo sanctificantur bona depredans lesie tantum spolijs insidiatu hyhe god good purueyeth hath man fode clothes mete drynke bade adam shold swynke geten hym sustenaunce eke set ordynaunce vpon lawe moyses though man haueles shall theft stele dayes ther fele wol labour vndertake maye stelthe take hold sykerlyche wonne thus lawe ouercome whiche god hath set namely hem soo vntrewe goddes robbe holy chirche theft whiche wyrch name cleped sacrylege ayene whome thynke allege condicion telle whiche rifeleth book belle forth remenaunt goddes hows appertynaunt shold ydd bede doth theft holy stede taketh fynt therin seeth may wyn wendeth cursidnesse ne briketh holynesse doth god reuerence hath lose conscyence though prest therfor corse seyth fareth worse speke otherwyse man lasseth fraunchyse taketh holy chirche pray note bede shall pray fro god hath yeue al propirte speciall whiche vnto crist hym self due bynemeth may wel eschewe payne comyng afterward hath made forward sacryl ge dwelle whiche hath herytage helle yf rede old lawe fynde wryte thylke dawe prynces thre comparable al degre one hem cleped thus prowde kyng antyochus nabuzardon hyght whiche enforced al myght temple destroye waste e dyde al hast thyrde whiche shamed nabogo donoser named ierusalem put vnder sacrylege many wonder holy temple wrought wiche balthasar heyre abought mane techel phares wryt walle thou myyt wyt byble hath declared spared yet day men pylle maken argument skylle sacrylege belongeth man therafter longeth taketh hede doth right telle sooth loues cause yf shall trete ben suche smale grete leyser fynde el wyll leten belle ne though see preest masse wol leten ouerpasse fond loue stande telle ere aske god none grace whyle ben hooly place go somme ananntage wylle haue pyllage goodly wordes byheste el take lest oute hir hond ryng gloue nyhe weder wyl shoue said shall forgete token hir gete thus halowe hye feste suche thefte may chirche areste al leful hem lyketh whome el myslyketh eke right self kynde grete cytees men may fynde lusty folk make hem gay wayte vpon holy day chirches mynstres eke gone woman seke suche one gooth sore fayrest al route sytten al rewe wylle body shewe croked keyned theron set ouche chapelet whiche late come greues el one grene leues shold seme fresshe thus loketh flesshe ryght hauke whiche hath siyt vpon fowle shall lyght fayrye weth hym fore ye hooly place sytte al make hir hertes flytte eye nowhere wol abyde loke pry euery side hym hest lyketh otherwhyle among syketh thynketh hem ther thynken two thre yet loueth none alle euer chaunce falle netheles sey soothe cause doeth stele herte two ouce chirche go said aboue sacrylege loue wel may steleth away neuer yelde may telle thy sone anon hast thou doo sacrylege none haue said manere fader matere wylle yow telle redyly haue doo bnt truly maye excuse myn entent neuer chirche went suche maner ye shryue man lyue cause haue last may vnto craft thyng able stele though neuer fele bnt yet wylle sey lady whome lyeth hooly quarelle chirche chappelle goo matens masse tyme wayte wel passe chirche come stonde though take look hond contenannce look bnt toward hyr al loke yf falle pray vnto god somwhat say pater noster crede al wold spede bede holy chirche myght somme myracle wirche lady berte chaunge whiche euer hath straunge deuocion al myn contemplacion al herte courage set hyr ymage euer wayte vpon tyde loke ony thyng syde maye hir auyse anone couetyse smyt leef holy chirche theef stele vestyment thyng talent wold stele yf myght glad word goodly syght euer seruyce profere namely goth offre lede yf may somwhat wold stele away beclyppe hir wast yet last stele tast whyle graunt mercy seith wynne therby lusty touche good word eke al remenannt seke fro purpoos wonder ferre may say said erre hooly chirche yf wowe conscyence yet wold allowe soo vpon amendement myght gete assignement wherfore spede place suche sacrylege hold grace thus fader sooth sey chirche right wey myght ought loue take suche hansell haue forsake fynally confesse holynesse whyle hir see ony stede yet onght euer dede sacrylege hyr took word looke el yf herd frede toward offryng hir lede take therof take may el ere nought away though wold ought l haue thynges ben saue kepte suche pryuelege may doo sacrylege god wote wylle netheles though must nedes kepe pee gree sone myn lete passe wyl therto lasse myght otherwyse awey thy fader yow prey telle thou thynkest therupon therof haue gylt none thy wylle sone blame remenaunt game haue told yet take lere thy wyt thyng hath tyme stede whiche serueth bede e chambre another speche yf thou wystest wreche sacrylege hath abought ow sholdest vse ryght nought thou shalt amende tale wol dispende hic amoris causa super istius vi articulo ponit exemplum et narrat pro quod paris pr ami regis filius nam menelai vxorem quada g insula templo veneris sacrile abduxit illa troye famosissima sidie per vniuersum orbis climita di nulgata precipue causabat ita qd huiusmodi sacrilegium non solum ad ipsius regis patriam omnium az suoru interitum sed ad perpetuam vrbis de solacionem vindicem fomitem ministrabat al men saith know ye world thoruy blow troye lamedon hercules iasen toward colchos oute gr see seylyng vpon pece londe troye reste preyde wrongfully conueyde found hym vyleyne cam grece ageyne power gete myght towardes troye haue hem dyght took suche vengeaunce wherof stant yet remembraunce destroyed kyng alle leften brent walle grekes troyes many slowe prysoners took ynowe among whiche one kynges doughter lamedone esyona fayre thynge whiche vnto lamon kyng hercules assent hole parlement wylle yeue graunted thus hath grete troye dannted hym torne suche manere shalt thou cause tale telle vpon chaunces bifelle kyng lamedon whiche dyed thus sone one priamus whiche thylke tyme home herd come fond cyte falle whiche bygan vpon walle made cyte newe whiche londes knewe tho se den lyme stone world fayre none one side towne kyng lete make ylyowne hye toure strong place whiche adrad manace quarell none engyne though men wold make myne man craft myght approche set vpon roche walles towne aboute hem stode al world doute proporcyon syx gate toun suche enforme suche entayle hem see grete meruayl dyches brode depe fewe men myght kepe al world semeth tho yf goddes foo grete prees vnto cyte drowe peple ynowe burgeys therin dwellen may man tong tellen cyte ryche good made wel stood kyng pry mu tho hym bethought grece whylome wrought hir swerd deuoured suster dishououred thelamon awey ladde thynkyng wex vnglad set anone parlement whiche lordes assent many wyse spoke myghten ben awroke last netheles seid al acord pee setten eyther party rest thought hem al best resonable amendement thus anthenor forth sent aske esyona ageyne wyte wold seyne passeth see barge grece sey charge whiche said redyly vnto lordes spak grece aboute herd wordes stoute namelyche thelamon mayden wold gone said maner thynge bad hym gone home kyng gate none amende ought couthe doo sende anthenor ayene goth home vnto kyng come told grece herd thelamon answerd hir aboue wol neyther pee ne loue euery man shall done best men seyen nyght hath rest kynge bythought hym ye nyyt erly day lyght took counceyll matere acord manere withouten ony let certeyne tyme shold set parlement ben auysed wyse anysed parlement set day moneth may priamus sight wyf hecuba hyght whome tyme sone fyue doughters thre beside two thyrty mo knyghtes al tho vpon wyt bygete el myght hem get whiche knowe suche world ylk throwe child ryche therof man hym lyche parlement day come ben lordes al tho prouounced purposed cause hem disclosed anthenor grece ferde sytten ay stylle herde tho spak euery man aboute alledged many doute many prowde word spoke also moost partye tho wysten best werre rest withoute fere hector among lordes tale told suche wyse said lordes ye ben wyse ye knowen wel aboue al moost worthy stant grete manhode worthynes knyghthode wel agrope hem bylongeth al europe whiche thyrd parte euen alle world vnder heuen folke fewe reson eschewe perylle falle therin better leue bygyn thyng whiche may acheued wyse fynde hym greued doth greue loketh fore wylle see behynde may ful ofte harmes fynde wyck strif haue worse haue encheson corse wote wel hate grekes debate hem ben suche myght ful good euery wyght hym self ryght wel bythought thus sey nought whyle lyf may stonde ye taken werre honde falle best werst shall seluen ferst greue hem euer may stylle one say nay thyng yt couceil demeth vnto wel quemeth werre certes pee say netheles belongeth say shape ye best way whan hector said deuyse next hym tho spak paryse whiche broder alyed hym best thought thus seid strong thyng suffer wrong suffre shame stronge haue suffred two al yet haue doo soo myght reforme wrong shame better forme sente anthenor ye wel knowe hir grete wordes blowe vppon hir wrongfull dedes eke wol hym self meke pee lyst reson take men seyn reson wyll hym forsake multitude men strengthe ten hath sene trewe quarele ayene honderd haluendele hath better goddes grace thus hath befalle many place yf lyke vnto yow alle wylle assay bifalle oure enemy yf may greue haue caught grete byleue vpon pleyne poynt wol declare yonder day gan fare hunte vnto grete herte whiche fore houndes sterte euery man went syde hym pursewe ryde bigan chase sooth say within whyle oute way rode nyst slope caught grasse beside welle leyd doune slepe vysyoun god mercurye came goddess thre hym name mynerue venus iuno hond appel tho held gold lettres wryte thus dyd wyte put hem vpon fayrest hem thre gold appel shold gyue eche hem shryue echone faire behyght venus said yf myght appel gyfte gete wold neuermore forgete said grece londe wold brynge honde al erthe fayrest thought best hyr yaf appel tho thus hope well yf goo wylle ordeyne matere pleyne shal haue come ageyne haue ye herd wold seyne saye ye stont youre auyse euery man tho said sondry cause recorde last acorde parys shall grece wende thus parlement took ende cassandre herd whiche parys suster anone gan wepe wayle said ala may v ayle fortune hir blynd whele ne wylle lete v stonde wele dare wel vndertake yf parys wey take seid shal doo ben euer fordoo mayden cassandre hyght al world bereth syght bookes men fynde wryte sybell whome ye wyte al men yet clepen sage whan wyst vyage parys shold grece fare woman myght werse fare ne sorowe dyde ryght stede ferd helenus whiche hir broder prophecy suche another al holde iape purpoos whiche shape hem leef hem lothe holde grece goth parys retenaunce felle vpon chaunce grece londeth yle hym told whyle folk whiche began freyne tho yle quene eleyne eke countrees aboute ladyes many lufty rowte mochel worthy peple also comen thedertho cause stood suche wyse worship sacryfyse venus wold make fore vndertake good wyll biheste hir hyhe feste within temple whiche whan parys wyst anone shope ordynaunce gone te done obeysaunce venus hir hooly day dyd vpon best aray grete rychesse hym behongeth suche lord longeth armed netheles londe pee thus gothe oute ship taketh hym felauship suche maner yow say vnto temple hold way tydyng whiche gothe oueral grete smal forth come quenes ere told parys come wold doo sacryfyce vnto venus whan herd telle thus thought euer wylle hym abyde see forth cometh parys glad vysage temple pylgremage vnto venus goddesse yeueth offreth grete rychesse prayeth hyr pray wold syde gan behold see lady stood forth fresshe mode goth made hyr chere wel couthe manere worldes suche plesaunce took al hir acqueyntaunce ferforth herte lay stale went away goth forth took leue thought anon eue wold done sacrylege many man shal abyge ayene ship come hym hath counceyll nome deuised matere suche wyse thou shalt within nyght al pryuely men warneth armed redy soone certeyn thyng done anon redy alle eche gan calle wente hem oute vpon stronde took purpoos londe thyng wold doo towards temple forth ther go fyl deuocion heleyn contemplaaon many another worthy wyght temple woke al nyght byd pray ymage venus vsage parys ryght hym lyst temple wyste came men al sodenly al one set skrye hem whiche temple fr tho moche peple bnt defence bote suffre suffre mote parys vnto quene went hir armes hent hym felauship forth bere ship vp goth sayle forth went suche wynd fortune hem sent till hauen troy caught oute ship anon strauyt gone hem forth toward toun whiche cam procession ayene parys sene pray euery man began say parys felauship al couthen worship none lytel man troye ne made myrthe ioye parys wonnen eleyn al nyght sorowe peyn helenus cassandre token shame sklaundre losse al comon grace parys oute hooly place stelthe hath take man wyfe wherof shall lose lyf many worthy man therto cyte doo whiche neuer shall made ayene felle ryght seyne sacrylege whiche wrought cause grekes sought vnto towne belay wolden neuer parte away tyl sleyght stregth wonnen brede length brent slayn therin sone suche syn sacrylege hooly stede beware therfore byd thy bede doo thyng holy chirche thou myght reson wyrche eke take hede achilles vnto loue chees polixena also hooly temple appollo whiche cause dyede al lust leyd asyde troylus vpon creseyde also first loue leyde hooly place ferde seyth al world herde forsake dyomede suche lust last mede thy sone wold rede ensample thou myght rede seche elles thou wylt thy grace ware wel hooly place thou loue speke aunter yf wreke ou hast herd telle fore take good hede also therfore vppon forme anaryce ony vyce haue deuyded partyes braunches whiche companyes oute world general lyke ye shall couetyse periurye fals brocage vsurye scarcenes vnkyndeship whiche neuer drough felouship robbery pryue stelthe whiche done worldes welth rauyn sacrylege whiche take conscyence grege al though may rychesse atteyne floureth bnt shal greyne vnto swete rightwysenesse wold doo largesse vpon reule yeue myght man thought leue toward god eke also toward world two largesse wayteth belongeth neyther parte wrongeth kepeth hym self kepeth frendes stonte sauf endes suche wyse sure excedeth mesure wherof sone thou shalt wyte philosophre hath wryte prodegus et parcus duo sunt extremum quam largus est horam medins pl ore bonus nota hic de virtute largitatis que ad oppositum auoricie inter duo extremum videlicet percimoniam et prodegalitem specialiter consistit e ix two extremytres vyce stont propyrtees v rtu pr ue take auaryce take also vyce prodegalyte betwix hem lyberalyte whiche vertu largesse stant gouerneth noblesse tho two vyces discord stant euer fynd record bitwene debate largesse ruleth estate suche wyse auaryce fore haue told vyce thorugh streyte holdyng scarsenesse stant contrarye largesse right prodegalyte reuers suche degree auaryce spareth kepe tresoure careth al owne ayene wysemans lore yeueth dispendeth hym retcheth neuer whyle may borugh wol dispende til last seith wende spoken al late pouerte yate taketh hym euen sleue rst wylle wysedom leue ryght auaryce synne wolde tresoure kepe wynne ryght yonre prodegalyte largesse degre whiche euen stant bitwene two hyghe god man also vertu eche hem commendeth hym seluen fyrst amendeth ouer al name spredeth al nedeth yaf good suche wyse maketh many man ryse whiche el shold falle lowe largesse may vnknowe lond regneth may ayle wyn deserte loue grace shall fayle place thus bitwene moche lyte large e whiche wyte holdeth euer forth myddel way wol torne way fro prodegalyte anone leueth propyrte vertu goth vyce suche wyse auaryce lefte scarsenes good name r g soo blame rgh wast mesure excedeth wote harme bedeth mochel ioye ther leueth largenesse herte gydeth sur gouerned par lerned god world also doth reson two poure folk almesse releued ben distresse thurst honger colde yeft hym neuer solde frely yeue netheles myghty god encrces reward hym double grace uen e doth hym purchace yeueth hym eke ye worldis good thus cete hoode orgesse taketh yet synne th bow euer wynne man hath horse men yeue hors none hath hym may foote goo e world hath euer stond loken twey man go syker wey better yeue take yeft man may frendes make yt taketh outher grete small taketh charge forth stant fre till quyte deme mannes wyt helpeth man haue owne good craue men make hym bonde el may stonde vnbonde seneca si re tue tibi non sufficiunt fac vt rebus tuis sufficias seneca counceyled wyse seyth yf thy good suffyce vnto lykyng thy wylle withdrawe thy lust hold stylle thy good suffysaunt thynge appertynaunt trouthe causeth fre rule charyte whiche first begynneth hym self thou richest twelf wherof thou shalt thy self pouer thonk thou myght recoue whyle man hath good ye e grete rente may leue hath frendes oneral eueryche hem telle shall whiche hath ful pak say good felawe iack whan foyleth last anone pryce ouercast none lawe iak good felawe whan hym poure nedy se lete hym passe fare wel al wende companye torned folye speke kynde loue man may suche fynde come euery row cast wast hir loue aboute tyl tyme ouergone haue loue none loueth oueral reson shal loue haue ony propyr e thy sone auyse thou loue hast ben large suche man charge yf thou hast dyspended al thy tyme wast set thy loue sondry place though thou substauce thy grace lese last wonder put hym seluen vnder saith comyn ouer alle leseth loue specialle ony one yf wyse loue shal bere pryse reson passeth one haue sene many one loue wel ese whiche felle grete dysese thorugh wast loue spent sondry place went ryght sone aske thou prodegalyte hast thy loue wasted fader nay haue tasted many place haue goo yet loue neuer one tho dryue forth day leueth well herte ay withouten mo euermore vpon one desyre hir loue allone make many pryue mone wel fele haue dispended long loue amended spede ought fynde yet wast youre wyt loue prodegalyte good fader demeth ye one thyng wyll shr shal loue thryue yf hir self wyl releue sone may wel leue netheles semeth ought thou bast yet mysdo tyme whiche thou hast myspendyd may grace amendyd thyng may worth co per chaunce newther wast ne lo thyng stont auenture worldes creature telle certeyne shall ende tyl may see ende note yet therfore thou sonne hast wonne lore oftyme sene whan somer hath lost al grene wynter wast bare hym left thyng spare al recouerd throwe cold wynter ouer blowe styl ben sharp showres sodenly ayenst flowres somer happeneth ryche per caas thy grace lyche sone though thou pouer loue yet thou myght recouer fader certes graunt mercy ye haue taught redyly euer whyle lyue shall better may beware thyng whiche ye haue said euermore toward shryft belongeth wyte poyntes longeth wherof ye wolden teche herte yow byseche explicit liber quintus sequitur liber sextus incipit iter sextus st gula quam nostr maculauit pama p tum ex veti pomo quo let omnis home hec agit vt corpus anime cont ana spirat quo cawsit crassa sp tuat r intus exterins si que vir tutis habentur potibus ebrietas conuia ta uit mersa sapore lebis que ba inebriat hospes indignata venus oscula caro premit hic sextu libro tractare intendit de illo capitali vicio quod gu la dicitur ne nen et eiusdem duabus solu modo speciebns videlicet ebrietate delicacia ex quibus humane concupis nae oblectamentum habudancius argumentatur grete synne orygenal whiche euery gouernal vpon byrthe hath enemyed paradys mystymed adam thylk appel bote swete morcelle hote whiche dedely made kynde bookes fynde vyce whiche oute rule hath set v al cleped gule whiche brauches ben grete hem wol irete touchyng two thynke speke mo wherof fyrst dronkeship whiche bereth cuppe felauship ful many wonder doth vyce wyseman make nyce foole hym shal seme al lawe deme yeue euery iugement whiche longeth fyrmament bothe sterre mone thus maketh gret clerk soone hym lewde man thyng ne whyle hath dronkeship honde knoweth see knoweth ye lode noble man armes yet strengthe armes strong ynowe fore dronkeship forlore al chaunged estate wexeth anone soo feble e may nether go ne come al geder benome power bothe honde foote algate abyde mote al wyttes foryete whiche hym suche lete note neuer doth ne whiche fals ne whiche sooth ne whiche day ne whiche nyght ye tyme knoweth wyyt ne wote moche maner thyng hym seluen man best hold ryght sory fest reson vnderstood sodenlyche wexe woode el lyche dede man whiche nother go ne speke thus oft bed brought lyeth reteheth nought tyl aryse vpon mow seith sorowe man drynkeles half dronke suche rees drye mouthe stert hym vppe sayth bayley sa cuppe made hym lese wytte ageyne morow al leyne cuppe al euer hym pleseth also moost hym dyseseth cuppe whome serueth whiche al care hym herueth al balys hym bryngeth ioye wepeth soro syngeth may whyle stont vers dronkenshyp dyuers drynketh wyn last wyn drynketh hym bynt hym fast leyth hym droke ye walle hym whiche bonde thrall al subiection lyche suche condycyon speke otherwyse falleth wyse b n whyle loue adoted bywhapped assoted dronken men neuer yet none whiche half lost wytt drynke suche thynges whiche cleped olyf wo wexen hir owne thought dr nk ne knewe nought reson lesse suche kynde sykenesse lack brayne loue grete mayne taketh herte honde may thyng myyt withstod whiche salamon nome strong sampson ouercome knyghtly dauyd hym ne myght rescue syght bersabe ne bestad yrgyly also ouerlad aristotiles put vnder thy sone wonder yf thou dronke loue amonge whiche aboue al strong yf thou telle thy shryft prynyte shame suche thewe yong man dronkelewe suche phisyk parte semeth arte thou sholdest phisonomye shapen melodye louedronke routhe holy fader trouthe ye telle beknowe loue bythrowe al herte thorugh sonkr verylyche dronke yet may bothe speke goo ouercome torned fro self clene oft wote mene excusen ne may herte fro first day lady hythe neuer yet sobre sythe hir see see hir musyng thought loue whiche herte assayleth dronk herte fayleth brayne ouertorned maner torned foryete stonde lyke mased man oft whan wold play maketh drawe oute way soleyn place self doth laborer delf whiche gentylmans chere el lewde frere put penaunce ryght lese contenaunce yf nedes vetyde company abyde must daunce synge houe daunce carolynge goo newe fote may wel heue vp foote way al myrthe away weye anone thought full wherof lymmes ben dull may vnnethes goo pa thns euer hit suche thoughtes muse lust myrth men vse whan see lady byme al foryete tyme ferforth wyttes chaungen al lustes fro straungen seyn al truly swore man whiche ofte drynketh wyn stomake synketh wexeth dronke wytles throwe right lust ouerthrowe myn owne thought mate wexe myn estate lyme wylle ser e dronk man swerue suffre suche passyon men haue grete compassyon eueriche self merueyleth thyng one eyleth suche maner wo whiche tyme hurte soo l efte ageyne hir see nycete telle yow fare whan may vpon hir stare hyr woman de hir gentylnesse herte ful suche gladnes ouerpasseth wyt wote nowhere syt dronken sight thynketh tyme myyt ryght streyte thorugh hole walle may wel yf shalle bothe synge daunce lepe aboute hold forth lusty rowte netheles falleth soo ful ofte fro hyr go ne may stake stonde auysement take loke vpon hir fayre face whyle oute place world ne myght wen e suche lust cometh mynde withoute mete drynke lustes thoughtes whiche thynke thynketh myght stonde euer leuer suche syght leue wel haue leue haue mochel wylle thus thynkyng stond stylle withoute blemysshyng myn eye ryght thought sye paradys moost ioy soo whyle reioy herte grete desyre whiche hoter fire al sodenlyche vpon renneth thought within brenneth ferforth ouercome note bycome soo amonge hertes strong stede drynke vnderfonge thought swete courage neuer pyement ne vernage half swete daynke wold thynke though myn aboue thorugh dronke loue soty demeth soothe semeth whyle may thoughtrs kepe thynketh though slepe goddes barme see myn owne harme sodenlyche awake oute thought hede take sooth stant dede sykernes drede ioye torneth woo soo hete al ago suche soty ynne inward begynne take loue newe thurst whiche greueth worst cometh blanche feuer chele make cheuer coldeth hert wonder asterte suche poynt ne deye certes neuer keye ne frosen vppon walle inly cold alle thus suffre hote chele whiche passeth poyntes fele cold brenne feese hete drynk bytter swete drye lyppe eyen wete loo thus tempre dyete take draught suche relees al wyt herteles al herte therin syt saith withoute wyt preue reson makyng comparyson may difference bytwyx dronke man al werst euerychone euer thurst one herte drynketh may thynketh thurst shall neuer acqueynte god sheld dreynte suche superfluyte wele fele degre al wyt ouercast wherof agast defante ladyship per chaunce suche dronkeship may cede beware certes fader dare beknowe thyrst telle draught haue welle whiche deth lyf ioye torned staf sobre shall neuer worthe dronken man worthe londe fare lust lore welfare may bote fynde thynketh wonder kynd dronk drynk thoughtes thynke whiche fynd relees yf myght netheles suche drynke coueyte soo lust haue one receyte shold assobre fare wele fortune vpon hir whele deyneth sette euermore fynd lette botyler frende whiche hath key bende may wysshe waste wel wote fresshe taste yf grace shall assay neuermore thus dronke see forcastyng forfendyd seluen staunche fader braunche gytlyf telle trouthe sone thynketh routhe loue dronke meschyef aboue moost chyef lusty thought assay whiche may sory thurst alay tyme lesseth hym whiche ioye mysseth thy sone aboue alle thynke well befalle kepe wyttes thou hast late hem dronke wast netheles wyght may withstonde loues myght cause fynde dyuerse kynde loue dronke men pleyneth coutrey whiche al ordeyneth wylle telle manere lyst sone thou shalt hic narrat secundu poetam qualiter suo cellario duo dolia jubiter hci bet quorum primum liquoris dulassimum secundum amarissimum plenu consistit ita quod ille cui portata est pro spenta de dula potabit alter bero cui adnersabitur poculum gustabit amarum fortune euery chace f r goddes purueaunce man groweth fro aboue spede euery loue shape befalle er abouen alle whiche goddes soueraynt hath seller men saynt two tonne ful loue drynke maketh many herte synke many herte also flete fowre swete one ful suche pyement whiche passeth al entendement eny man yf taste maketh ioylyf herte hast bytter galle whiche maketh mannes herte palle whoos dronkeship sykenesse thorugh felyng bytternesse cupyde boty r bothe whiche leefe lothe yeueth swete soure somme laugh somme loure moche blynde ful oftyme aoth amys badde good whiche hyndreth many man fode withoute cause fortheteth eke ben loue somme seke whiche ought reson ben hole somme comen dole e hem self lyst ynke vndeserueth best thus blynd botiler suche comen yeueth swetee stede truble l hertes trouble maketh dronke al vppon chauce withoute lawe gouernaunce drawe swete tonne thenne sorowe al ouercome loue drynke shall greue dronke euery eue ali game bytter tonne draweth suche dronkeshyp hert gnaweth febleth al man thought better haue drok nouyt brede haue eten drye leseth lusty wey dronkeship wote whyder go weyes ben slyder whiche may par caas falle shal breke wyttes alle wyse men ben dronke drynk haue droke men drynke lyke somme shall syng som shal sike thyng merueyleth sone loue assayleth el knowe thy tale thou hast dronke dwale whiche bitter til god sende suche grace thou myght amende sone thou shalt bydde pray suche wyse shal say thou thy lust wel atteyne thy woful thurstes restreyne loue mayst swetenesse bachus dyd distresse bodeliche thurst hym hent straunge londes went nota hic qualiter potus allquando scicienti precibus adquiritur et narrat exeplum quod cum bachus de quodam bello ad orientem repatrians quibusdam libie partibus alicuius generis potum non inuenit fusis ad ouem precibus aruit sic potum pe tenti peticio preualuit bachus sone ubiter hote went fer faders assignement make werre oryent grete power hym ladde hyher hond hadde vyctorye enemye torneth homethard pry suche countrey dreye meschyef felle vpon weye rode companye nygh strondes lumbardye myght drynk fynde water ne kynde hym self al hoost defaute drynk almost destwyed bachus prayd iubiter thus said hyghe fader seest alle whome reson shalle byseche pray euery nede byhold fader take hede woful thurst ben ynne stauche graute v wynne sauf vnto countrey fare oure lusty loues waytyng vpon home comyng voyce prayng whiche herd goddes heye sawe anone fore eye wether whiche ye groud hath spurned hath ouerturned sprong welle fresshe cleve wherof owne otylere lustes wylle yaue euery man drynk fylle ylke grete grace forth place ryche temple lete arere whiche euer shall sto de thursty men remembraunce thy sone thy chaunce syt well take hede pray vpon nede bachus prayd welle thynk thou hast herd grace grad grace foole fyrst radde elden gete domme man londe take prouerbe vnderstonde wordes ben vertues grete thy speke thou ne lete aske pray erly late thy thurst quenche thynk algate otyler whiche bereth keye blynde thou herest seye yf myght betyde vpon blynde syde er caas swete tonne raught shalt thou haue swete draught wexe loue dronke sobre thus rede thou assobre thyn herte hope suche grace dronkeship euery place whether side torne doth harme make man sporne falle suche wyse per caas may aryse hic de amoris ebrietate ponit exemplum qualiter ristrans ad potum que brangweyne manu ei porrexit de bello isolde inebriatus extitit loke euydence vpon sooth experyence hath befalle euery man mouthe rystram loue dronke beal isawde dronke drynk whiche brangueyn hym bytoke er ye kyng mark eme hir toke wyf knowe eke sone yf thou wylt knowe hath fallen euermore lones cause dronkeshyp afore drede whysome befelle dede wherof thou myght better eschewe dronken men thou sewe company manere grete e sample thou shalt hic e li ebrietatis causa amore contingentibus narrat quod cu pirotheus illa pulcherrimaa ypotaciam em duceret quosdam qui centari vocabantur inter alios vici o ad nupcias inuitauit qui vino br ati nupte formasitatem aspicien plici ebrietatis mensa ypotaciam irotheo marito suo impetu rapuerunt fynde wryte poe ye thylk fayre ipotasye whoos beaute spake euery man felle per ca pyrotheus hym spedde wyf hir shold wedde wherof grete ioye made wold loue glade ageyne day maryage mouthe bothe message frendes fest praid grete worship al men said hath yong lady spoused whan yt al day honsed set serued mete wyn may begete ne plente ynough bachus thylke tonne drough wherof way dronkeship gretest felauship oute reson ouertake venus whiche also hath take cause moost special hath yeue hem drynk forth al thylke cuppe whiche exciteth lust wherin man delyteth thus double wey dronke lust ylk yry fonke hath made hem seith half wod reson vnderstoode ne none thyng seyen hir whiche fore hir exen wedded thylk day fresshe wyf lusty may ir al thoughte ferforth lusstes sough whiche named centauri feste one assent one acord yong wyf maugre hir lorde suche rage forth ladden none insight hadden dronken fare many man hath made mysfare loue wel wey wherof yf shal sey vpon nature vyce customme excercyse mannes grace fordoth tale whiche whylome sooth fooles dronken shal reherce vnto thyn ere loquitur specialiter contra vicium illorum qui nimia potacione ex consuetudine chriosi efficiantur et narrat exemplum de gabba vitello qui potentes hispania principe fuerunt sed ipst cotidiane ebrietatis potibus assueti tanta vicinus intulerant enormia quod tandem toto conclamante populo pena setencie capitalis eos dicialiter diffinita est qui p usquam morerentur vt pena mortis alleuiarent spontanea vim ebrietate sopiti quasi porci semimort gladio perierunt rede cronycle thus gabba vi llus spayn grettest al bothe one condicion disposicion glotony dronkeship sory felauship thou myght wel vnderstonde man may wel long stonde whiche wyndronk comyn vse hath lore vertuse wherof reson shold hym clothe sene vpon hem lo ayn euydence wherof knowe difference bitwene dronk wode neuer neyther goode wyn doth wyt awey wysedom hath oft ryght wey maner vyce dredeth blynde man thredeth nedel sonne lyght reson myght dronkeship blent poynte shent gabba bothe eke lle vpon cause shall telle wherof good taken hede two hir dronkenhede wytles ex tacion oppresseden al acion spayne fowle vsaunce whiche done coutynuaunce hem whiche al day dronken wyf ne mayden fayre fowle ne wolden defoule wherof lond often wo ke thynges mo wroughten many sondry day longe derke nyght cometh los god wold sholden last shope lawe suche wyse dome iuyse dampned ben lore hadden fore encly ed al dronkenesse ande wytnesse hope aswage payne deth vppon rage lesse sholde fele wyn le e fulfylle mele ill bifalle th strengthes loften alle te wy ony brayne thus en dede holf slayne hem ne gr ueth lyde thou wyde ony poynt whiche haue seide wherof thy wyttes ben vntey rede clepe hem home ayene shal fader ye seyn ferforth may suffyse wel wote wyse dronkeship loue awey may remeue wyse stont vpon fortune yf thou lyst comune second glotonye whiche cleped delycacye wherof ye spak fore byseche wold therfore sone ylke vyce whiche noryce stant vpon retenue venus due propyrte fareth ook herafter declareth delicie cum diuicijs sunt ra pote um n quibus orta venus excitat os gule non sunt delicie tale quam corpus pascunt ex quibus impletus gau dia venter agit qui completus amor maiori munere gaudet cum data delicijs men amante fatur hic narrat super illa specie gule que delicacia nuncupatur cuius mo icijs voluptuose carni personis precipue potentibus que quam complacencia corporaliter ministrauit chapiter whiche trete yet one suche dyete power may al paast peindemayn sondry wyn sondry drynke wherof wyll ete drynke ben hym affayted body wayted hym shal lacke delyte ferforth appetyte suffyseth mete hote wherof lusty vyce hote gule delycacye whiche hole progenye lusty folk hath vndertake fele whyles may take rychesse wherof founde abstynence wote bounde proufyte shold serue yet ph sik conserue maketh many restauracion vnto recreacion whiche wold venus leef thus poynt releef cooke whiche shall mete aray better mouthe assay lordes thonk shall oft lese e serued chese ther may lacke soo lyte ne fynt anone wyte lust fully serued hath wyyt thonk deserued yet mannes sustenaunce kepe hold gouernaunce hym wylle hele gete none good comon mete loketh bookes seyth confexion cooke man hym shold wel auyse took wyse vseth knoweth ful seldom sykenes hym groweth vseth mete straunge though nature empayre chauge wonder lyef sonne whan doth ayene wonne sykenes fynde vsaunce second kynde philosophus consuetudo est alter natura right chaunged estat loue delycate though honde best wyf al londe fayrest loue alle yet wold herte falle thynk hem delycious hath owne hou men seyn ofte auyse hem wel speke way ful oftyme haue herd say whiche hath loue acheued hym thynkth releued though lady make hym chere may good manere hir honoure hir name saue yf surplus myght haue thyng withstondyng hir estate loue delycate set hir chere delyte haue appetyte sone yf telle hooly fader delycate suche wy loue ye deuyse ne neuer yet gyltyf yf suche wyfe ye speke shold wold neuermore lust ony womanhede herte vpon none fede yf dyd waste withoute suche repaste suche ye told aboue wyf yet loue faste may foode gete lack deynte mete whiche herte may fedde go fastyng bedde myght geten told mochel lady wold fede hir glad semblannt though lacke remenaunt yet shold somdele abesshed tyme wel refresshed certes fader ne doth good feyth tellen sooth trowe though shold ser ue wold eye swerue herte one goodely looke fede thus suche cooke may goo fastyng euer mo yf ony woo may fede man herte wele therof haue euery mele plente ynough hym self cough stomak may defye loo thus delycacye loue whiche herte fedeth thus haue lack nedeth al yet netheles sey gyltles somdele delycate el fully mate yf somme lusty stound comforte ese founde take loue somme repast though ful taste lust loue may stele honge otherwyse kele smale lustes whiche pyke tyme yet lyke ye wysten mene good sone shryue clene suche dayntees ben good wherof thou takest thyn hertes foode fader shall yow reherce foodes ben dyuerse fallen degre fedyng see another thyrd shalle telle groweth myn owne thought e e shold eue nought fayleth foode herde may wel deth asterte qualiter visus amore se co tinet de syght al fyrst foode tho ugh whiche eye al goode hath hym acordaunt lusty foode suffysaunt go toward place shall see ladyes face myn eye whiche loth fast begynneth hongre anon fast hym thynketh one houre thre tyll come hir see appetyte taketh foode suche delyte hym none deynte nedeth sondry sightes hym fedeth seeth hir face suche coloure fressher ony floure seeth hir fronte large pleyne withoute frouce ony greyne seeth hir eyen lyche heuen seeth nose streyte euen seeth hir rude vpon hir cheke seeth hir reed lyppes eke hyr chynne acordeth face seeth full grace seeth hir necke round whyte al thyng withoute wyte may see naked lest wel feste wel delycacye fedyng eye seeth hir shap forth hir body round hir myddel small wel bigone good array whiche passeth lust may moost soft showres ful clothed lusty floures suche sightes myn eye fedde fnll fynally porte manere seeth hir womanlyche chere hath suche delyte honde thynketh myght stylle stonde hath full suffysaunce lyue de sustenaunce parte euermo yf thought fro wold neuer wende vnto worldes ende wold abyde yf myght feden hym vpon syght though myght stonde ay tyme dome day looke vpon hir euer one yet whan shold fro hir gone myn eye wold though faste ben honger storuen also fast til efte ayene hir sye suche nature myn eye lust deyntefull whiche man shold full stomak vnderfongeth euer one myn eye longeth loke goushauk tyreth ryght doth whan pyreth tutyth hir womanhede may neuer fully fede lust euer lyche sore hym hongreth desyreth fedde algate thus eye made gate thugh ye deyntees thouy lust ben myn herte brought ryght eye look myn herte lusty cook loues fede delycate ryght ere estate eye may serue wel myn eres thonk deserue feden hym fro day day suche fode may thus oueral come special may lady pryce one sey wyse another seith good somme men seyn worthy blood one also fayre none soo preise hir goodly chere thus euery thyng may whiche sowneth lady good herte lusty foode eke ere hath ouer deynte feste maye hir selum speke anone fast breke suche wordes seyth ful trouthe ful feith ben good disporte ere grete comforte done ben delices al mete al spyce ony lumbard couthe make ne lusty take ne ferforth restauratif seye myn owne lif ben wordes hir mouthe wyndowes southe ben moost debonaire debonair hir lust speke faire vertu hir goodly speche verily hertes leche bifalle among carole vpon songe fedde fro lyf ledde though paradys certes myn auys hir vois steu thynketh blysse heu eke vois also ful oftyme falleth myn ere good petaunce fed redyng romaunce ydome amadas whilome ca eke many store loueden long bode hir loues redde myn ere tale fedde lust hir storye somtyme drewe memorye sorowe maye euer last cometh hope last none foode knowe endureth throwe right chery feste counten lest yet eseth somdele herte appeseth thyng ere spredeth whiche plesaunt somdele eseth wordes suche may gete lust stede mete loo thus fader sey lust whiche eye hath sey eke ere hath herd ful ofte haue better ferd two bryngen thyrd whiche hath herte amydde place take aray lusty foode whiche assay mete namelyche nyghtes lacketh al sightes heryng awey redy wey rere souper make whiche hertes fode take lusty cooke name hoote thought whiche hath euer pottes hote loue boylyng fyre fantasye desyre whiche full ofte fedde herte bedde set vppon lorde bothe euery sight euery word lust whiche haue herd seyn yet fest pleyn wordes fisshes therof haue full disshes felyng taste yet myght neuer haue one repaste thus ye haue herd forn lycke hony thorne seith vpon brydell chewe ydell effecte fode haue man wold hym saue syke medycyn ryght loue famyn fond euer may fede drynke forth day til may haue gretter feste whiche al honger myght areste loo suche ben lustes thre thynke see take loue fedyng withoute tastyng felyng poure doeth heyre lyue good espyer none suche delycacye trowe glotenye netheles youre auys hooly fader ben wy recommaunde myn estate haue ben delycate sone vnderstonde well thou hast told euerydele thynketh thy tale ben delytes wonder smale wherof thou takest thy loues foode sone yf thou vnderstood ben delycious thow woldest curyous vpon lust thyn estate ben fore delycate wherof thou reson excede bookes thou myght rede mannes wysedome shall shewed ought wel ben eschewed loue wel wey hooly bookes sey bodely delyces alle euery poynt falle vnto sowle done greuaunce take remembreunce tale acordaunt vnto wiche grete vnderstondyng man soule resonable thynke telle fable hic ponit exemplum contra istos de licatos et narrat de diuite et layaro quorum gestns euangelio lucasuidencius describit cristes worde wil rede yt vyce drede euangely telleth pleyne wiche must algate certeyne crist hym self bereth wytnesse though clerk clergesse latyn tong rede synge yet knowlechyng trouthe whiche good wyte shall declare wr te englys thus bigan crist seith ryche man myghty lord grete estate eke delycate clothyng euery day purpir bice made hym gay ete drank fylle lustes wylle whiche stood al delyce took hede thylk vyce shold betyde poure layar vpon tyde came gate axeth mete myght thyng gete dedely honger staunche whiche ful paunche lustes bord ne deyneth speke word onlyche cromme yeue wherof peure myght leue vpon yeft almesse thus lay poure grete distresse ac lde hongred gate whiche myght goo gate woful besene lay grene houndes comen fro halle sike man falle lay dye woundes maladye lyeken done hym ese full suche dysese may deth escape tyme shape wle fro body passeth whome thyng ouerpasseth hyghe god vp heuen hym took hath set hym euen abraham barme hyghe heuens ioyr sighe haue wold felle befalle shold ryche man throwe sodeyne deth ouerblowe forth withouten ony went helle streyght went fende fire hym drough peyne ynough flamme whiche euer brenneth eye aboute renneth toward heuen cast loke sawe hede tooke layar set see ferre euer myght see abraham prayde vnto patriarke sayde sende layar doune fro thylk sete doo fynger wete water may droppe vpon tonge stoppe grete hete whiche hrenne abraham auswerd thenne seid hym wyse sone thou myght auyse take thy remembraunce lalar grete penaunce whyles lyf thou al thy lusty iolyf bodely delytes soughtest thy thou wroughtest shalt thou take thy reward dedely payne herafter ward helle whiche shall ener last layar last worldes payne ouer ronn heuen hath lyf begonne ioye whiche endeles thou praydest neuertheles shal layar sende water fyngers ende thyne hote tonge kele thou shalt suche grace fele folble place synne euer whiche thou shalt ben inne cometh none place thidder ne none yow maye come hydder thus ye parted two ryche ayeneward cryed tho abraham sith hit soo layar may doo whiche haue axed place wold pray another grace haue yet bretheren fyue fader ben alyue geder dwellen one hows whome thou arte gracious pray thou woldest sende layar myght wende warne hem world wet afterward shent suche peynes drye loo pray crye may hem self amende patriarke anone sende prayer answer nay said hym euery day bretheren myght knowe moyses erthe prophetes mo hem best said yf myght man aryse deth lyf suche wyse tellen hem seyd thenne pure fere sholden beware therby quod abraham nay sikerly yf wylle obeye suche teche hem wey al day preche al day telle stont heuen helle wylle taken hede though befelle dede ony dede man arered ben hym better lered another man lyue thou sone canst descryue tale cryst hym self told thou shalt haue cause hold see grete euydence sooth experyence hath shewed openlyche eye bodely delycacye hym whiche yeueth almesse shal falle grete distresse sene vpon riche ne wold vnto lyche crome yeuen brede afterward dede droppe water hym werned thus may mannes wytte lerned hem delytes taken deth ben ouertaken erst swete sowre gouernoure worldes good yf wyse within herbe set pryce al world yet vseth good nothyng refuseth whiche lord thynges ouches ryche thynges clothe gold perrye taketh yet delycacye leueth though best mete eteth drynketh best drynke taketh none hede thynke delycacye put awaye whiche goth right waye fede clothe body sowle bothe taken otherwyse lustes ben none wyse whylome shewed eke thou old bookes seke wel reson kynde old ensamples men fynde hic loquitur de desicacia newnis qui corporalibus delicijs magi adherens spiritualia gaudia minus obtinuit man yt wold hym wel auise delycacye despyse whan kynde acordeth wherof ensample special new whylome may told whiche ayens kynde many fold lustes took till last god hym wold ouercast whome cronyke pleyne lust hym seyne netheles glotonye bodely delycacye knowe stomak ferd man fore herd whiche wythin hym self bethought wonder subtyle thyng wrought thre men vpon election age complexion lyche hym self al way toke wardes hym play ete drank wel therof dyersyte euery day whan ete tofore ne borde sete suche mete serued al though deserued token seruyce afterward thylk game woful ernest torned thus soiourned within tyme mete nero whiche foryete lustes freel estate whiche al delycate knowe thylke experyence men lete come presence one tyde courser shold ryde felde anone bad wherof man wonder glad goth pryke daunce aboute whyle oute leyd vpon bed slepe thyrd whiche wold kepe within chambre fayre softe gothe vp doune ful oft walkyng pace ne slepte tyl whiche courser lepte comen fro felde ageyne new bookes seyne men dyde done take al thre slewe hem wold see whoos stomake best defyed hath sooth tryed found whiche goth pa defyed best al whiche afterward vsed ay thus thyng vnto pay moost plesaunt left none ony lust bygone wherof body myght glade abstynence made moost al erthely thynges woman vnto lykynges nero set al hole herte lust shold hym asterte thurst loue hym caught hym lust take draught spareth neyther wyf ne mayde suche another men saide al world neuer yet dronke al wyt thorugh sondry lustes whiche toke euer whyle ther book new men shal rede synge vnto worldes knowlechyng good sone thou hast herd euer yet hath ferd delycacye loues ca withoute reson loue herte set hym thynketh myght bet though fully mete lust loue eure svete loo thus geder felauship delycacye dronkeship wherof reson stant oute herre haue made full many man erre loues cause moost alle euer falle wytte reson vnderstonde late gouernannce stonde wylle whiche wexeth wild hym self shyld fro perylle oute fere way secheth hym retcheth vppon fyde oftyme goth besyde doth suche thyng withoute drede wherof hym ought wel drede whan loue assoted sore passeth men lore lust ordeyneth ther mannes myght restreyneth god taketh none hede lawes withoute drede purpoos wol acheue ayenst poyntes byleue tempteth heuen erthe helle afterward shal telle dum stimulatur amor quicquid iubet ordo voluptas audet et aggredi tur nulla timenda timens omne quod astra quem herbarum siue potestas seu vigor inferni singula temptat amans quod nequit ipse deo mediante parare sinistrum demonis hec magica credulus arte parat sic sibi non curat ad opus que recia tendit dumodo nudatam prendere posset auem hic tractat qualiter ebrietas et deticacia onus pridicicic contrarium insti tantes inter alia ad carnalis concupiscencie promocionem sacrilegio magica requirunt dare thyng whiche loue ne dare loue euery lawe vnware lawes best fisshe fowle man beest al worldes kynde loutith loue whiche thyng douteth mannes herte sytte cometh toward wytte woo nomore wele hete chele wete drye lyue dye fore ne behynde seeth thyng blynde withoute insight courage doth mecuayles rage thyng hym draw god lawe whome taketh heede baiard blynde stede tille falle dyche mydde goth ther man wyll hym bydde stant ferforth oute rewle wytte may hym reule thus telle hym sooth ful many thyng doeth better laft among whiche suche craft somme men clepen sorcerye whiche wynue drewry many circumstaunce vseth poynte whiche refuseth craft whiche saturnus founde make prykes sounde geamaunce cleped ful ofte vseth amys flood idromaunce fyre romaunce question echone tho tempteth ofte eke also acremaunce iugement loue bryngeth assent craftes fynde man may doo wey kynde good entent goth al another went rather shold faile nygromancye wold assayle make incantacion hote subfumygacion thilk arte whiche spatula bote vsed comon rote among paine whiche craft eke whiche auctor thosey greke wercheth one one rowe rachell hym vnknowe ne salamon candarye ideote entonye figure howe balachame genball selle therupon chymage byth auauntage taketh somwhat gy ere whiche helpend matere babilla hir sonnes seuen whiche heth renounced heuen ceornes bothe square round grateth efte vpon grounde makyng inuocacion ful informacion ole whiche hono u wr te pursueth loo thus magyke vseth wyn ne loue spareth synne ouer soty ryght seeth sorcerye hem ben magycyens ryght naturyens vpon sterres aboue wey secheth vnto loue ferre hem vnderstondeth many sondry wyse fondeth maketh ymage maketh seulpture maketh writyng maketh figure maketh cala lacions maketh demonstracions houres astronomye kepeth partye whiche longeth inspectyon loue affection wold helle seche deuyll hym self byseche wyst spede gete loue lusty mede wherof hath herte set lede neuer fare bet ne wyte heuen sone yf thou suche lore hast ben thie rede leue amans holy fader youre leue al ye haue spoken whiche uchith vnto matere telle soothe right wene wote one word ye mene wille sey yf couthe nold lusty youthe binethe helle eke aboue wyn lady loue done al euer myght therof haue none insight afterward bycome wynne ouercome hir loue whiche coueyte sone gothe wonder streyte may wel telle soothe noman whiche doth al craft cast ne byeth last ofte wol begyle gyled gyle thus gylour begyled fynde book compyled matere old hystorye whiche cometh memorye grete ensamplerye ageynst vyce sorcerye wherof none ende may good whylome therof stood tale whiche good knowe sone shal beknowe nota hic contra istos ob amoris causam sortologos vbi narrat exemplum quod cum vlixes subuersione troie repatriare nanigio voluisset ipsum insula cilli vbi illa expertissima ga nomine cyrces regnauit cotigit applicuisse quem vt sui amoris concupiscenciam exardesceret circe onibus suis incatacionibus vincere conabatur vlixes tamen magica potencior ipsam amore subegit ex qua filium nomine thelogonum genuit qui postea patrem suum interfecit et sic contra fidei naturam ge tus contra generacionis naturam patricidium operatus est moges whiche troye vlixes syege one name special whome yet memoryall abydeth whyle ther mouthe euer name shal couthe worthy knyght kyng clerk knowyng euery thyng grete rethoryen grete magycyen tullius rethoryk kyng zorastes magyke tholome astronomye plato philosophye danyel slepy dremes neptune eke water stremes salamon prouerbis mater strengthe herbes phisike ypocras lyche vnto pyctagoras surgerye knewe cure somwhat auentures whiche mater shal acorde sone wylle recorde kyng whiche yu hast herd seyne troye goth home ageyne ship found see dyuerse many wyndy storme reuerse thorugh wysedom yt shapeth ful many grete perylle escapeth whiche thynk telle one mangre nedel stone wynde dryue al sodenly vpon strondes cylly must abyde whyle two quenes yle calypha named aud cyrces herd vlixes londed therupon ryue hym senden also blyue hym suche wold name courte hem came quen two goddess art magyke sorceress lord cometh ryuage make hym loue suche rage vpon hem assote soo wol haue go al hath worldes good lixes wel vnderstood couthe moche couthe shape cast ayenst hym sore wrought many subtyle wyle yet myght hym egy men nauye two forshope grete partye may none hem withstond hestes parte shopen beestes parte shopen fowles beres tygres ape oules el way myght thyng hem disobeye suche crafte aboue kynde arte couthe fynde whiche vlixes deceyued ne hath hem weyued broughte hem suche rote vpon hym assote thurgh scyences arte took hem wel parte bigate cyrces childe kept hym sobre made hym wyld set hym self aboue hir good hir loue therof leef lothe al quyte ship gothe cyrces swelle bothe side lefte wayted tydes streyght thorugh salt fome taketh cours cometh home fonde penelope better wyf may none yet ben ynowe good hir goodlyship vnderstood fro first wyfehode tooke many loues forsoke bare hir al aboute ther whyles hir lord oute e myght take grete auaunt amonges remenaunt one rest wel myght set herte rest kyng whan foud hir al bele couthe wysedom dele couthe womanhede sawe withoute drede hir lord vpon owne ground e come sauf sonude al world ne myght gladder woman fame whiche may hydde thorugh oute lond sone kydde ir kyng come home ageyne may man ful seyne al glade mech oye hem made euery day e newed gyftes al sewed peple hym glade ugh none hym bade ge vpon hem self sette pure dette ue goodes kyng glad welhome comyng thus vlyxes wold wyf suche sholde peple hym subiect shold withoute lette fortune suche sleyght whan man moost myght maketh hym rathest falle man wote shall befalle happes ouer mann hede b hanged tendre threde proued vlyxes whan moost p sone gan meke hym werre set hie welthe oute herre vpon day mery myyt hym thynge nyght come goth dde sl pe bothe yen fedde whyle slepte met sweuen hym thought sawe statue euen whiche bryghter sonne shen man semeth none fygure moost lyche mannes creature beaute henenlyche moost aungel lyche thus bytwene angel man beholden kyng began suche lust took syght fayne wold yf myght forme figure embrace goth hym forth toward place sawe ymage tho taketh armes two embraceth hym ageyne kyng thus gan seyne vlixes vnderstood wel th token oure acqueyntaunce afterward mochel tene loue v bitwene suche ioye make one v deth shal take deth cometh destyne may none wyse vlixes tho began praye figure wold hym saye wyght seyth hym wyght vpon spere tho pensel whyte wel bigone enbrowdred shewed hym anone thre fysshes one coloure manere toure vpon pensel wrought vlixes knewe token nought praid wyte somme party thyng myght ygnyfye signe whiche answered empyre forth ferd al sodenly said vlyxes oute slepe brayd ryght ayene day lenger slepen ne may ayene man hath knowlechyng saue hym self thyng owne chaunce man knoweth fortune hym throweth yet neuer wyse clerke whiche myght knowe al goddes werk ne secrete whiche god hath sette ayene man may lette vlyxes though wyse wytte auyse sweuen acounteth lesse wote amounteth calculacion seeth none demonstracion al pleynly knowe ende netheles wende drad hym owne sone maketh hym wel ye astone shope therof anone within castel walle thelamon sone shette tyl myght knowe bette sooth ne knewe til fortune hym ouerthrewe netheles sykernesse myght wyte gesse place strengest londe lete make lyme sonde strengthe wold dwelle neuer man yet herd telle suche another strengthe hym ca al onde sykerest seruanntes worthyest kepe hym within ward charged hem sholden harde make suche ordynaunce loue ne acqueyntaunce erly late shold bete yate mauer man betydde hym self bydde al myght hym auayl whome fortune wyll assayle may resistence whiche myght man make defence al shall must fal algate cyrces whiche spake tate whome vlyxes hath bigete childe though haue foryete tym came wonne delyuerd sonne whiche cleped thelogonus child bore thus aboute moder ful age reson langage good estate drawe forth mochel w th stonde mannes stede circe moder hath hym bede shall fader go told hym al geder tho man hym bega lelogonus herd ware ful knowlechyng fader kyng prayd moder fayre go fader hym graunted shall made hem redy forth tyme suche vsaunce euery man cong ysaunce countre bare honde went straunge londe thus euery man therfore well knowe bore espyall myst wynges dyde suche thynges euery man may knowe bifelle throwe thelogonus ca contre signe thre fisshes whiche sholde bere vpon pynon spere thus arrayd harneys assayd redy euerydele moder bad hym fare wele said hym shold ythe fader grete thousand ythe thelogonus moder ky took leue wyst fader way name til vnto nachare came whiche lond chyef cyte cleped asketh kyng ferde sooth herde kyng vlix alone vpon ho grete paas rood hym forth honde bare signall londe fisshes thre haue told thus went hold owne fader dwelleth cause came telleth vnto kepars gate wold haue cemen ther ate shortely hym said nay fayre euer may besought told hem kyng fader proude wordes grete biganne manace threte go fro gate fast wold hym take set fast fro wordes vnto stroke thus felle thelogonus sore hurte wel nyhe dede sharp speres hede maketh defence falle wan yate vpon hem alle hath slayne best fyue aseryeden belyue thorugh oute castel al aboute euery syde men came oute wherof kynges herte aflyght al hast yt myght spere caught oute goeth nyhe woode wroth sawe yates ful blood thelogonus stood sawe also ne knewe man hym threwe spere sterte oute asyde desteny whiche shold betyde befelle ylke tyme thelogonus knewe thyng tho man hym cast whyles owne spere last al signe therupon cast vnto kyng anone smote hym dedely woude vlix felle anone grounde tho euery man kyng kyng began crye thyng thelogonus whiche sawe caas knee felle seid ala haue myn owne fader slayn wold deye wonder fayn slee euer wylle certes right good skylle cryeth wepeth seid therfore ala euer bore vnhappy destyne wofully cometh kyng yet hath life ynoug herte ayene vnto hym drough voyce ere leyd vnderstood seid gan speke said hyghe bryng man whan syghe thelogonus thought set vpon sweuen whiche met axeth myght see spere whiche fysshes thre sawe vpon pensel wrought tho wyst wel faileth nought bad hym telle shold fro whens came wold thelogonus sorowe woo myght told tho vnto vlixes caas cyrces moder forth seid hym euery dele moder grete hym wele wyse hym sent tho wist vlixes ment tooke gym armes softe al bledyng kyst hym ofte said sone whyles lyue infortune foryeue sone hast sente bigan hym cam vnto fader ty e saw hym suche plyte wold haue ronnen vpon anone slayne owne broder ne ben vlixes bitwene hem made acord pe heyre thelamacus thelogonus al power shold kepe till woundes depe al hole shold hym londe vpon lyue thelamacus herde vnto fad answerd said wold done wylle dwellen geder stylle bretheren fader sterueth lo wherof sorcery serueth thorugh sorcerye lust wan thorugh sorcery wo bygan thorugh sorcerye loue chese thorugh sorcerye lyf lese child get sorcerye whiche dyd felonye thyng ayene kynde wroyt vnkyndely bought child owne fader slough vnkyndeship ynough thy take heede wynne loue amys whiche endeth l ioye wo al arte fynde also hath loues sake thou myght ensample take grete cronycle emperyall whiche euer memoryall among men wende shal dwelle vnto worldes ende hic n rr exemplum qu ter nectanabus ab egipt macedoniam fugiti olimpiadem philippi gi ibidem tunc absentis vxorem arte magi decip en c ipsa concubuit magnum quam ex ea alexandrum sortelogus genuit qui natus p stea cum ad erudiendum sub custodia nectanabi patrem suum ab altitudine cuiusdam turris fossam profundam percipiens interfecit et sic sortil gu ex suo sortilegio infortunij sortem sortitus est hye creatoure thynges whiche kyng al kynges ful many worldes chaunce l te slyde vnder sufferaunce wote noman cause whiche al myghty proued whilome thus kyng nectanabus whiche egypte lede sey dede thorugh magyke sorcerye wherof couthe grete partye enemyes hym comende fro whome myght hym defende oute owne londe fledde wyse hym dredde felle al wytchecraft egypte hym beraft desguysed fledde awey ship held ryght wey macedoyne ar yueth chyef cyte thre yomen chambre serue hym whiche trusteth wonder wele trewe ony stele hapneth hym lad parte best good toke lodgyng towne disposicioun hym thought best dwelle axeth herd telle kyng oute go vpon werre tho cyte quene whiche olympia hoote solempnyte feste hir natyuyte fell holde hir lust biholde prayd people aboute shope hir ryde oute mete al openly anone al men redy monethe may lusty quene good aray set vpon mule whyte sene grete delyte ioye eyte made fresshe thynges glade noble une al behonged euery wyght sore alonged e lusty lady ryde grete myrthe euery side passeth strete th full many tymbre bete many mayde carolyng thus thurgh yt un playeng quene vnto pleyne rode houed abode see dyuerse g pley lusty folk iust torney forth euery man whiche play couthe playe bigan plese noble quene nectanabus came grene amonges drough hym nyghe lady syghe hir beaute hede tooke uthe withdrawe loke see nought elles felde stood hir biheld clothyng chere al vnlyche hapneth last quene vpon hym hir eye cast knewe rauge anone biheld hir euer one withoute blemysshyng cheere took good ede h manere wondreth dyd bad men sheld hym goo came dyd hir reuerence axeth sylence whome came wold sobre wordes told seyth madame clerke yow message cam whiche may tellen yf lyke yow must said al pryuely none shal ye thus tyme tooke leue day goth forth till eue euery man mote lete werk thought euer vpon clerk thyng wold men wyse abode quene passeth ouer thylk nyght till moro lyght send hym came hym astrolahe name whiche fyne gold precious poyntes cercles merueylous eke heuenly fygures wronght book full peyntures took lady shewe told eche hem rewe cours condycyon grete affectyon sate stylle herd wold thus seeth tyme told feyneth wordes wyse tale seyth suche wyse madame whyle agoo egypte tho radde scole scyence felle conscyence temple went hole entent sacryfice dede one goddes hath ed yow warne pryuely ye make yow redy ye thyng agaste suche loue hath yow cast ye shall ben owne dere shall youre bedfere til ye conceyue child word wex al myld somdele bicame shame axrth hym goddes name whiche wol done companye seid amos luby said may leue yf see better preue madame quod nectanabus token shal thus nyght enformacion ye shall hane vysyon amos shall yow appere teche maner thyng shall afterward befalle ye oughten wel abouen alle make ioye suche lord ye one acord shall sone yow begete swerd shal wyn gete wyde world lengthe brede al erthely kynges shall hym drede suche wyse yow behote god erthe shall hote sooth tho quod quene nyght thou se st shall sene yf falle grace god amos purchace take hym grete worship wol doo suche ladyship wherof thou shalt euermo ryche thanked hyr tho took leue forth went wist lytel ment gyle sorcerye al took prophecye nectanabus thorugh oute day cam home lay chambre hym self tooke ouertorneth many book thorugh craft arte mage wex forgeth ymage loketh equacions eke constellacions loketh con unction loketh recepcions signes houre ascendent dr weth fortune assent name quene olimpias thylk ymage wryten myddes fronte aboue thus wyn lust loue nectanabus werk hath dyght whan came within nyght euery wyght falle slepe thought wold tyme kepe whiche hath houre apoynted first hath anoyn eed sond herbes figure therupon gan coniure thorugh enchauntement lady whiche innocent wyst thyng gyle mette slepte thylke whyle fro heuen cam lyght whiche al hir chambre made lyght loked fro sey hir thought dragon tho whoos scherdes shynen sonne hath soft paas begonne al chere may toward hed lay til cam beddes syde lay stylle thyng cryde al thynges fayre curtoys debonayre stoode hir fast forme thaunged sodenly figure man nome hir hir bedde come suche thyng ther loue wroyt wherof hir thought thorugh lykyng god amos childe anone hir wombe roos wonder glad alle nectanabus whiche causeth alle metred substaunce seeth tyme nygromance stynt thyng seide carecte abreyde oute hir slepe leueth wele sooth enery dele clerke hir told gladder many fold hope suche glad metrede whiche shalle befalle dede longeth sore day hir sweuen telle may gylour pryuete whiche knewe wel netheles morow soone lefte thynges done hym sent caas told hym pleynly said wel wyst wordes myght tryst fond hir auysyon ryght condycyon whiche hir told tofore prayd hym hertely therfore hir hold couuenaunt forth remenaunt may thorugh ordynaunce toward god doo suche plesaunce wakyng myght hym kepe suche wyse met slepe couthe gyle ynough herd ioye lough said madame shall doo warne yow therto nyyt cometh play lyf way shall lykynge ordeyne comyng ye ne shall hym fayle madame yow conusaile ye kepe pryue wyght el thre haue knowlechyng el myght fare amys ye dyd ought shold hym greue thus maketh hir bileue fayneth vnder gyle feyth netheles seyth troweth ayene nyght hath within hir chambre dyght gyloure fast vpon god shal pryuely awayte ye make hir wene thus noble gentyl quene moost trust deceyued nyyt cam chambre weyued nectanabus hath take place sawe tyme space thorugh deceyte magyke put hym oute man lyke dragon took forme whiche wold al conforme sawe sweuen thus chambre comen quene lay bed syghe hopeth euer cam nyghe god luby lesse fere wold hir assure yet efte chaunged figure wether lykenesse took fygure noblesse large horne none fyne gold precious stone corowne hede bare sodenlyche ware whiche gyle forme turneth man cam bed lay stylle suffred wylle whiche wende mysdo netheles hapned soo al though parte deceyued yet hath conceyued worthyest al kythe whiche euer fore sithe conquest chyualrye thorugh gyle sorcerye noble knyght begone whiche al world hath wone thus felle thyng falle shold nectanabus hath wold gyle hath loue spedde gyle cam bedde gyle goth hym oute ageyne shrewed chambyrlayne begyle worthy quene hym sene netheles thyng fals god soone goo deceyte helde hym cloos tyl morow cam aroos tho tyme leyser tho quene told hym al ca gyle none supposeth two poyntes hym opposeth one yf god nomore wyll come ayene euermore shal stonden acord kyng philip hir owne lord cometh home seeth hir grone madame seyth lete alone god vndertake whan lyketh yow take company ony throwe day fore knowe shall yow nyght wylle suche myght kepe yow al blame thy comforte yow madame shal none cause thus took leue forth goth tho began muse quene myght excuse toward kyng falle fonnd crafte amonges alle thurgh hath sefoul dasited magyke enchaunted flewe forth nyyt vnto kynges tent ryght lay amyddes hoost slepe moost sefoull hym brought another charme whiche wrought home within chambre stylle kyng turneth wylle maketh hym dreme see dragon pryuete whiche bytwene hym ye quene ouer made hym wene sweuen god amoo whan quene aroos toke forth rynge wherin stone set graue therupon sone whiche whan cam nyght lyon swerd syght prente tho mette vpon quenes womhe sette seall goth hym forth way sweuen went waye tho bygon kyng wake sighed wyues sake lay within tent hath greete woder ment hasted hym ryse anone sent wyse among whiche one clerk name amphyone kynges sweuen herd bytokeneth answerd said sykerly lyf god hath leyn thy wyf gete sone whiche shall wynne world al withynne lyon kyng beestes shalle world obeye heestes swerd shal wone ferre shyneth ony sonne kyng doutif dome netheles come ageyne owne londe wyf child grete founde myght hym self stere ne made hir heuy chere whiche couthe sorowe nectanabus vpon morow thorugh deceyte nygromaunce toke dragon semblaunce kyng sat halle came rampyng among hem alle suche noyse suche rore agast sore though shold deye anone netheles greueth none goth toward deyse hye quene nyghe stynt noyse wyse hir profered seruyce leyd honde vpon hir barme goodly chere hir arme aboute neck ayeneward leyde thus quene hym pleyde sight al men aboute last gan loute obeysaunce vnto hir make wold leue take sodenly lothely forme egle gan transforme flewe set hym rayle wherof kyng grete meruayle plumeth hym pyketh doeth hawke hym wel liketh self shoke wherof halle quoke terremote saiden alle god suche rees forth flygh kyng whiche al wonder sighe cam chambre alone vnto quene made mone foryeuenes hir prayd knewe wel said child god kyng withoute rod chastysed quene excused ben accused gretter euydence yet presence kyng philip mo whan roode feldes tho fesaunte came cye whiche anone hir seye fleyng lete egge doune falle brake among hem alle token therof kepe sawe oute shelle crepe lytel serpent oute ground whiche rampeth al aboute round ayene wol haue wonne brennyng sonne myght deyde therupon clerkes seide serpent oute went enuyroun shelle aboute myght torne ageyne shall falle certeyne child world shal enuyroune aboue bere crowne hym shalle befalle yong age shall desire courage world honde turne ageyne londe bore weye home ward shalle poyson deye kyng whiche al sawe herd fro day forth ferd ielousye hath foryete whiche hath child begete nectanabus pryuete tyme natyuyte vpon constellacion wayteth relacion maketh quene shalle euery houre appoynteth mynute therof lore due tyme bore child forth therupon fell wondres many one terremote vnyuersell sonne took coloure stele left lyght wyndes blewe many strengthes ouerthrewe see propre kynde chaunged al world forme chauged thonder fyry beuen cruel vpon heuen euery erthely creature tho thought lyf auenture tempest last seceth child kepte age encreceth alysaunder name hote whome calystre arystote techen hym philosophye endenden astronomye thynges whiche couthe also teche hym youthe nectanabus took vpon honde euery man may vnderstonde sorcerye wende wylle hym self proue ende namely begyle lady whiche withoute gyle supposeth hereth often euyll stereth ship dreynte therin mydde caas ryght betydde nectauabus vpon nyght fayre sterre bryght yong lord lad vpon hyghe aboue towre syghe sterres suche acounteth seeth eche hem amounteth though knewe al thynge yet hath knowlechyng shall vnto hym self befalle hath told wordes alle yong lord hym opposeth asketh yf supposeth deth shall hym self deye seith fortune aweye euery sterre hath lost wonne el myn owne sonne shall slayn may fle thought alysandre pryuyte herof old dotard lyeth ought aspyeth al sodenlyche old bone shoof ouer wal none seyth hym lye doune part wherof serueth al thyn art thou knowest al mennes chauce thy self hast ygnoraunce thou hast said amonges alle thy persone befalle neccanabus whiche hath deth yet whyles hym lasteth lyf brethe alysander spak seyd w th wrog blame hym leid fro poynt poynt al che ca told hie sonne tho whiche sory ynough oute dyche fader drough told moder ferde counceyl herd knew tokenes whiche told nyst sey shold stoode abasshed whyle magyke gyle thought deceyued hath man conceyued wend god netheles suche degree myght hir honoure saue shope body begraue thus nectanabus abought sorcery whiche wrought though vpon creature thorugh carectis figure maystry power creatour nought hym lad ageyne who law crafde vseth lust god refuseth tooke hym deuyls aft lo profyte hym belaft thyng thurgh wede haue stode first hym exiled londe whiche owne fro kyng made hym vnderlyng sythen deceyue quene torneth hym mochel ne thorugh lust loue gate hym hate ende couthe abate old sleyghtes whiche cast yong alisander hyn ouercast fader whiche hym mysbigat slewe grete myshappe one mys another mys yolde ful oft nectanabus craft myswent mysfell hym went note helpeth clergy whiche maketh man doo foly namelyche nygromaunce whiche stont vpon mysereaunce nota qualiter rex zorastes statim cu ab vtero matris sue nasceretur gaudio magno risit quo prenosticum doloris subsequentis signum figurabatur nam et ipse detestabilis artis magica primus fuit inuentor quem postea rex surrie dira morte trucidauit sic opus operarium consumpsit see euydence zorastes experyence arte magyke first forth drough anon bore lough whiche token woo sewyng owne contreuyng found magyke taught forth al hym lytell worth surry worthy kyng hym slewe endyng yet thurgh hym craft vsed thorugh world accused shal neuer wel acheue thei stont ryght byleue lyche wulle euyl sponne leseth hym self hath lytell wonne ende proueth euery thyng saul whiche yt iewes kyng vpon peyne deth forbede arte yet took therof parte phitonysse samary yafe hym counceyll sorcery whiche felle moche srowe slayn vpon morowe conne moche helpeth moche man yelpeth loke euery side magyk may wel betyde thy sone wol rede thou ensamples drede lust erthely loue thou seche come aboue wherof worldes wonder thou shalt euer put vnder good fader graunte mercy euer shall beware therby loue euer bifalle suche sorcery abouen alle fro day forth wyll eschewe ne wylle pursewe lust loue seche wold yow byseche eside stant periferijs thre deuyded suche degre bynethe one one amydde aboue set thyrdde whiche vpon deuysyons ben dyuerse oppression moyst eke drye also whiche sonne two ben drawe haled vpon hye maken clowdes knyghthode ldes make man drede shame honour desired thorugh beaute hem desyred dar e whiche cupide throweth wherof iolyf peyn groweth whiche worlde oth vnderfo woman manne ote lyf deth woo thyng may wed wymmen ben good kynde ensample thus fynde nota de fide tate coniugis qua te cesta vx ameti vt maritum su viuificaret seipsam ti spontance subegit duke ametus ay seke ed euery day men waiten whan shold day alcest hiswyf goth prey deuoutely pray g w sacryfyce vnto myn e wy answere goddesse h r lord sykenesse wherof soo isene recouer myght hele ne loo thus cryed thus praid tille last voys hir said yf wold sake malady suffre take dye hir self shalle lyue answere alceste hath yeue vnto mynerue grete thankyng hir deth lyuyng chese hir hoole entent thus acorded home went chambre came hir houshold anone name bothe hir armes hym kyst spak vnto hym lyst therupon within throwe lay doune seke ouerthrowe dyed hoole hast may n reson tast next god aboue trouthe woman loue whome al grace founde myghtyest vpon grounde moost behoue many fold loo thus zorobabel hath told tale oppynyon finall conclusion strengest erthely thynges wyn wymmen kynges seith trouthe aboue hem myghtyest euer falle trouthe euer come may nothyng ben ouercome may well suffre throwe last shall knowe prouerbe trewe shalle whyle neuer rewe cause wende trouthe shameles ende thyng troutheles may shameles shame hyndereth euery wyght pryuely myght withoute trouthe degre thus trouthe degre zorobabel moost commended wherof question ended receyued hath mede trouthe whiche mannes nede moost behouelyche ouer thy trouthe speciall first poynt obseruaunce take vnto gouernaunce alysander seid therupon grounde leyd euery kynges regyment thyng whiche moost conuenyent set kyng euen worldand eke heuen absit auaricia tangat regia corda cuius enim spolijs excoriatur humus fama colit largum voluntas per secu la regem dona tamen licitis suut moderanda modis hic tractat de regi magestatis secunda policia quam aristotiles largitate vocat cuius virtute non solum propulsata auaricia regis nomen magnificum extollatur sed et sui subicionum diuiciarum habundancia cundiores ef ficiuntur next trouthe second polycye found whiche serueth worldes fame worship kynges name largesse whoos pryuelege may auaryce abrege worldes good first comune afterward vpon fortune thylk comyn proufite cesed peple stode encresed lygnage en grete anone singuler beyete sacrefye vnto mynerue wyte answere goddesse hir lord sekenesse wherof woo bysene recouer myght hele ayene lo thus cryed lo thus prayed tyl last voys hir sayed yf wold sake maladye suffre take dye hir self shal lyue answer alcest hath yeue vnto mynerue grete thonkyng hir deth lyuyng al hole entente thus accorded home wente chambre wha came hir busbond anone name bothe hir armes hym kyste spake vnto hym hir liste vpon within thro good wyf ouerthrowe deyed hole haste may man reson taste nexte god aboue trouthe woman loue whome al grace founde myghtyest vpon grounde behouely many folde lo thus zorobabel hath tolde tale opynyon fynal conclusyon strengest erthely thynges wyne wymmen kynges seyth trouthe aboue hem alle myghtyest euer falle trouthe ener come may thynge ben ouercome may wel suffre throwe last shal knowe prouerhys trewe shal whyle neuer rewe cause wende trouthe shameles atte ende thynge trouthlesse may wel shamelesse shame hyndereth euery wyght pryuely myght trouthe degree thus trouthe degree zorobabel moste commended wherof questyon ended receyued hath mede trouth whiche mannes nede moste behouelyche ouer al thy trouthe specyal first poynte obseruaunce take vnto gouernaunce alysaunder sayed ther vpon groude layed euery kynges regymente thynge whiche moste conuenyente sette kynge euen bothe world eke heuen absit auaricia tangat regia corda cuius enim spolijs excoriatur humus fama colit largum voluntas per secula regem dona tames licitis sunt moderanda modis hic tractat de regie magestatis secunda policia quam aristotiles largita tem vocat cuius virtute non solum propulsata auaricia regie nomen magnificum extollatur sz et sui subditi om niu dunciarum habundancia iocundi ore efficiuntur nexte trouthe second polecye founde serueth worldes fame worshyp kynges name largesse who preuylege may auarice abrege worldes good first comune afterward vpon fortune thylke comyn prouffyt cesed whan peple stode encresed lygnages wexen grete anone synguler byy e drewe euery man partye wherof comyn fyrst enuye grete debate warees stronge laste emoge men longe tyl man wyst ne frende ne whiche foo whyl atte laste euery londe within hem self peple fonde good make kynge whiche myght appesen al thynge yeue ryght lignages partyng heritage eke al good thus aboue hem al stood kyng vpon regalye whiche hath iustefye worldes good couetyse syt wel al wyse kyng betwene lesse sette herte vpon largesse toward hym self eke also toward peple yf say yf toward self large free peple take pylle largesse weye skylle may said auarice kyng grete vyce kyng hehoueth eke flee vpce prodegalyte mesure expence kepe indygence may saufe fro nedeth al werke wers spedeth nota super hoc qued aristotilus ad alexandrium exemplificauit de exactionibus regis chaldeoru aristotle vpon caldee ensaumple grete auctorite vnto alisaunder taughte thylke folke vnsaughte toward hir kyng pyllage wherof hade corage vnto thre poyntes entende wold good dyspende fyrst shold loke stood al owne good yeftes whiche wold yeue myght better leue eke must taken hede yf canse ony nede whiche oughte deffended goodes ben dyspended mote eke befalle amonge thynges alle se decertes men ben ken estate meryte shal hem largely acquyte werre pea none honoure falle dyscreast whiche myght torne deffame kepe good name holde vnkynde cronycle tale fynde whiche speketh som dele matere afterward thou shalt hic secundum gesta iulij exemplu ponit qualiter rex suorum militum quos probos agnouerit indigenciam largitatis sue beneficijs releuare
