tenetur rome pursue right worthy poure knyght whiche came allone seyne cause courte pleyne iulyus presence hym lacketh dyspece hym none aduocate make plee estate though hym lacke plede hym lacketh nought manhede wist wel purse pouer yet thought right receuer penly pouerte aleyed emperour thus seyed iulyns lord lawe behelde counceyl withdrawe lacke golde thyn offyce lawe iustyce helpe counceyl vpon trouthe matere iulyus anone assygned hym worthy one hym self worde spake knyght wroth fonde lake emperour said thus thou vnkynde iulyus whan thou thy batayle vpon aufrik might rescue dyd man stede thou wotest woundes fynde bad ne list speke one worde thyn owne mowthe thy horde yeue floreyn helpe shold yelpe fro forth largesse whan suche grete vnkyndenesse founde suche lord thou iulyus knewe wel al sothe hym tolde wold ben holde vnkynde toke cause honde goddes sonde yaue hym good ynough spende euer vnto lyues ende thus shold euery worthy kyng take knyghtes knowlechyng whan sawe nede euery seruyce axeth mede whiche haue deserued thorugh vertu ape serued kyng shal deserue grace though large suche place hic ponit exemplum de rege antigo qualiter dona regia secundum mame et minus equa discrecione moderanda sunt sitteth wel euery kyng haue discressyon whan men hym craue may gyfte wyte wherof fynde tale wryte ciuichus power knyght somme whiche ouer myght prayed kyng antygonus kyng answerd hym thus said suche yefte passeth power estate lasseth axeth lytel peny yf kyng wold yeue hym ony kyng answerd smalle hym lord ryalle yeue man lytel thynge vnworshyp kyng ensaumple kyng may lere yeue manere yf kyng tresour lasseth without honoure thankelesse passeth whan hym self wyl begyle note shal compleyne whyle ne right hym shal releue nethelesse beleue nota hic qd regis status suis fideliby omni fauore supportandus est whiche owne londe behoueth euery mannes honde sette vpon necessyte eke kynges ryalte mote euery lyege man comforte good body supporte whan see cause resonable entendable holde vp right kynges name hym ought blame nota hic secundum aristotelem qua liter principum prodigalitas pauperta tem induat co nne polecye euer speke matere phylosophre tolde kyng rule holde modefye adresse yeftes vpon suche largesse seneca sit alijs benefacito vt tibi non g mesure excede yf kyng shal nede causeth ofte sendry thynges ben vngoodly kynges man wyl hym self mesure men secth ful ofte mesure hym hath forsake doth vseth prodygalite moder pouerte wherof londes ben deserte namely whan ylke vyce aboue kynge stante offyce hath holde partye cenetous flaterye many worthy kyng deceyueth fallace perceyueth hem seruen glose plese glose ben men tellen norice vnto fosteryng vyce wherof ful ofte netheles kyng blamed gyltles nota qualiter principum curijs adula tore triplice grauitate offendunt philosophre thou shalt spake kyng matere said hym wel flaterours coulpable thre errours one toward goddes hye wroth syghe myschyef whiche befalle shold fals flaterour tolde toward kyng another whan sleyght falla feyned wordes make hym wene blacke whyt blew grene touchyng condicion whan doeth extorcion many another vyce moo men shul fynde one tho grutche speke ageyn holden vp oyle sayn al wel euer doth thus fals maken soth kynges eye blente wote world went third errour harme comune peple mote comune wronges bryngen ynne aud thus werchen treble synne ben flaterours aboute kynge myght werse thynge aboute kynges regalye vyce flaterye nethelesse hath ben vsed neuer yet refused speke courte ryalle specialle many longe bore whan vyce hem bore shold vertuous forth brynge trouth torned lesynge sayth ageynst kynde wherof olde ensaumple fynde hic contra vanitates adulandum loquitur et narrat quod cum arisippus de cartagine philosophus scole studium relinquens sui principio obsequio magnis adulacionibus pre ceteris carior asistebat accidit vp ipse quodam die dioginem philosophum uuper socium suum virum tam moribus quam probatissimum herbas ad olera sua collectas lauantem ex casu ad ripam inuenerat cui ait diogene scito sicut et ego principi tuo placere scires huiusmodi herbas aut celligere aut non lauare indigeres arisippe certe si tu olera tua lauare scires blan icijs et adulacioni u principi tuo seruire non oporteret mouge olde tale wyse phylosophres wyse trde whilom two soole lere vnto athenis fro cartage frendes whan age hem sente stoden longe tyl suche lore haue vnderfonge tyme surmounte al men accounte hem two grete fame first hem right name drogenes hote founde ryote felowe arisippus hyght whiche moche coude myght atte last sothe sayne bothe torned home agayne vnto cartage soole lete dyogynes beyete worldes good lasse ne sought longe lore toke hym onely dwelle home bookes telle hows nygh ryuere besyde bridge thou shalt dwelled toke reste thought hym beste studye philosophye whiche wold defye worldes pompe euery syde arisippe bookes syde hath leyed courte wente many wyle many wente flaterye wordes softe caste hath compasse ofte prynce myght plese wyse gate hym ase veyne honour worldes good londes rule vpon hym stode kyng hym wonder glad al thynge bad bothe courte eke flaterye brought purpoos worldes werke ageyn state clerke philosophye lefte rich hym self vp lefte thus arisippe wylle dyogenes dwellyd stylle home loked boke sought worldes croke veyn honour ne richesse al herdes besynesse set vertuous thus within owne hows lyueth suffysaunce hauyng fyl perchaunce dyogynes vpon day monthe may whan herbes ben holsom walked gader som gardyn whiche iolytes thought haue thus aboutes wha hath gadred hym liketh set hym doun pyketh wysshe herbes flode vpon gardyn stode nygh bridge tolde ere happeneth whyle sitteth came arisippes strete many hors route grete streyght vnto bridge rode houed abode caste eye nygh felowe dyogenes syghe dyd sawe also wherof sayd hym tho diogenes god spede certes lytel nede sit wortes pyke thou thy prynce coudest lyke degree arisippe ageyn quod thou coudest thy wortes pyke truly lytel nede lesse thou yt worldly wold compasse flaterye serue wherof thou thynkest dysserue thy prynces thanke purchace thou myght stonde grace getyng lytel good thou wold take thy mood reson thou myght reson deme thy prynce queme reson accordaunt gretely discordaunte vnto sooles athene thus answerd diogene ageyn clerkes flaterye men seen assemplarye arisippe wel receyued thylke dyogene weyued offyce courte golde coffre men sayn philosophre whiche hath worshyp halle flaterye passeth alle chaubre courte uauceth vpon thylke lotte chaunceth byloued daye note yf ye nay dante poete answerde flaterour tale herde vpon stryf betwene two sayd hym ther ben many mo thy seruauntes myn poete couyne hath none wyl hym clothe fede flatour may rule lede kyng al londe aboute stante wyse man doute hem folye drawe suche comyn lawe comune boece telleth flaterye dwelleth ony londe vnder sonne ful many thynge begonne whiche better lefte hath shewed efte yf prynce wold hym rule romayns rule thylke tyme vsed vyce shold refused wherof poyntes ben assoted playn trouth noted may prynce wel conceyue hym self deceyue hereth wordes pleyne hym nought reson pleyne warned hym woo fully pre yd tho whan rome worldes chyef sooth sayer tho leef wold trouthe spare worde playn bare themperour sothes tolde cronyke yet withholde afterward thou shalt accordyng vnto matere hic narrat super eodem qualiter nuper romanorum imperator cum ipso triumphator hostes bello rome rediret tres sibi laudes signum sui triumphi precipue debebantur primo quatuor equi abbissimi currum quo sedebat veherent secundo tunica iouis pro tunc indueretur tercio sui captiui prope currum ad viriusque latus cathena ti deambularent set ne tanti honoris adulacio eius animum superbiam extolleret quidam scurra linguosus iuxta ipsum curru sedebat qui quasi contumatis vocibus improperando notheos hoc est noscete ipsum quia hodie fortunata sibi prospera sunt cras forte versa rota mutabilis aduersabitur see olde ensaumplerye whilom flaterye toward prynces wel fynde wherof cometh mynde sone tale vnto thyn ere worthy prince rome thynke tellen whan chaunces byfellen ony emperour tho victorye vpon foo came forth rome ageyn treble honour certeyne wherof magnefyed first specefyed whan came ylke tyde chare whiche shold ryde four whyt stedes shold drawe iubyter thilke lawe cote shold also prisoner eke shold goo endlonge chare eyther honde al noblesse londe fore hym come rydyng broughte hym rome token chyualrye none flaterye wed forth al satte chare ryalle besyde hym rybaud set worde beset themperour al glorye said take thy memorye al pompe al pride lete iustice goo syde knowe thy self befalle men seen oftymes falle thynges men wende siker stode though thou victorye haue honde fortune may stonde alwey whiche perchaunce another day may turne thou myght ouer throwe ther lasteth thynge throwe wordes moo ribaulde sat hym themperour hys tale tolde euermore wolde euyl good playnly trouth stood spareth speketh oute myght euery man aboute day solempnyte tale telle wel themperour al openly al cause stode noblesse shold vanyte represse suche wordes herde lo thylke tyme ferde toward hygh worthy lorde fynde eke recorde whiche cronycle hath auctorized emperour intronyzed hic eciam contra adulacionem narrat qd primo die quo nuper imperator intronisatus extitit latonij sui ab ipso constanter peterent de quali lapide sue sepulture tumulum fabricarent vt sic futuram mortem commemorans vani tate huius seculi transitonas facilius reprimeret first day corone ryal trone helde feste paleys sittyng vpon hye deys al lust may gete whan gladdest mete euery mynstral played euery gestour sayed moste plesaunt ere atte laste came mason shullen craue wold bygraue stone sepulture sholden make scripture wold ordeyne vpon tho flatrrye none worthy prynce beiape kyng otherwyso shape good counceyl wyse hem self wyse vnderstoden wel knewen whan suche softe wyndes hlewen flaterxe ere setten nought hertes whan herde wordes feyned pleyne trouthe hath disdeyned hem dyscrete toke flaterer beyete hym prynce tho proue tale fynde dede cronycle rome rede hic inter alia gesta cesaris narrat vnum exemplu precipue contra illos qui cum aspectu principis alijs sapi enciores apperere vellent quando que tamen similitate sapiencie talia comittunt per que ceteris stulciores fine comprobantur cesar vpon ryal trone satte persone hyest al pryse man whiche wold make hym wyse fyldoun knelyng presence dyd hym suche reuerence though hygh god men grete meruayle worshyp dede man aroos fro thylke stede forth withal tyde goeth hym vp syde set hym doun pere said yf thou sittest arte god whiche al thynges myght haue doo worshyp right god otherwyse yf thou thylke assyse bnt arte man suche may syt faste bothe one kynde cesar answerd said blynde thou arte fole wel sene vpon thy self yf thou wene god thou doest mys sit thou seest god man also thou hast grete foly whan thou suche one shal deye worshyp thy god alweye hast yeuen vnworthely thus may preue redely thou arte wyse herde wysely kyng answerde hem newe lore wherof dreden hym brought thynge ere bnt yf treuth reson ben many suche wyse faynen wordes wyse al veray flaterye hym whiche wel aspyr nota qualiter ista circa principem adultores potius curia expelli quam ad regie magestatis munera acceptan policia suadente delerent kynde flatour loue brynge hym self aboue euer mayster fare hym self stonde care retcheth nought thus ofte deceyueth wordes softe kynges ben innocent thastement wyse phylosophre seyed kyng tresour leyed vpon suche folke hath lesse yet doeth largesse nt harmeth owne honde hym self eke owne londe many sondry weye wherof yf man shal seye speke generalle suche thynge falleth ouer al ony kyng hym self mysrule phylosophre vpon rule speaal cause sette whiche euer hath bette gouernaunce aboute kyng vpon myselyef thyng seyth sla ye wherof fore partye vyce haue declared hath wytte bywared vpon flaterer beleue whan weneth best acheue god worde moste fro preuen exaumples ther ben many one whiche yf thou wylt knowe one behouely whylom fyl matere hic loquitur vlterius de consilio adusantum quorum fabulis principe aures organiyate veritatis auditum ca ere nequeunt et narrat exemplu de rege achab oui pro eo qd ipse prophe fidelis michee recu auit blandiaas oue adulantis yedechye adhesit rex sir e benedab campo bellator ipsum diuino iudicio deuictum interfecit monge kynges byble fynde tale credyble one whylom achab hyght whiche al israel ryght coude glose softe latre sette lofte arete estate made hem ryche wroten wordes lyche trouthe wold forbere hem none estate contre suche toke none tyl atte laste vpon nede benadab kyng surry israel grete partye ramoth coloath hote hath seced yote toke counceyl sondry wyse hem wyse nethelesse vpon caas strengthe hym iosaphas whiche thenne kyng iudee sende come whiche thorugh frendshyp alliauce nexte hym acqueyntaunce ioram sone iosaphath achabbes doughter wedded hath whiche hyght fayr goodelye thus came samerye kyng iosaphath founde kyng achab whan gyder spekyng thynge iosaphath saith kynge wold gladly somme trewe prophete matere counceyl myght yeue poynte shal dreue tyme befelle suche one israel whiche sette hym al flaterye cleped sedechye hym achab hath sente comaundement hym came sleyghte hath vpon heed heyght two large horne sette bra flaterour goeth rampyn lyon cast horne vp doun bad men ben good espeyre horne persen eyre saith withouten resistence wist wel science benadab discomfyte whan sedechye vpon plyte hath tolde tale vnto lord anone one accorde prophetes false many bere vp oyle altho affermed whiche hath tolde wherof kyng achab bolde yaue hem yeftes al aboute iosaphath grete doubte helde fantasme al herde prayeng achab ferde yf ony man whiche prophecye hym speke gone quod achab one brothel mycheas hyght ne cometh syght hath longe pryson leyen hym lyked neuer yet sayen goodely word plesaunce nethelesse thyn instauce shal come may say hath said many day yet said neuer wele tho iosaphath gan somme dele gladen hym hope trouthe bade hym withouten slouthe men hym shold f tte anone fro hym gone whan came tolden vnto mycheas manere sedechye declared hath prophecye therupon praye hym fayre wyl say contrayre wherof kyng may dysplese shal euery man esed may helpe hym self also mycheas vpon trouthe tho herte sette hem seyth al belongeth vnto feyth none feyned thynge wyl telle vnto kynge ferre god hath yeue hym grace thus came prophete ye place kynges wylle herde therto anone answerde vnto hym wyse lyege lord fernyse treuth stonde hath euer yet thou hast pason aquyt al shal glose trouthe suppose touchyng batayle thou shalt soth sayle yf lyke taught matere thou myght vnderstonde sone afterward done auyse seye tofore trone heye al world thought stode herde vnderstode voyce god wordes clere axyng said manere wyse may best begyl kyng achab whyle vpon poynte speke fast tho said spyrit atte last vndertake empryse god hym axeth wyse shal qd deceyue lye flateryng prophecye suche mowthes leueth whiche al thynge acheueth bad hym goo forth right ouer say also noble peple israel dispers sheep vpon hylle without kepar vn arayed wente aboute strayed herde voys vnto hem seyn goeth home hows ageyn tyl haue fetter ordeyned quod sedechye thou hast feyned tale angeryng kyng wrath vpon thynge smote mychee vpon cheke kyng hym hath rebuked eke euery man vpon hym cryed thus shente euery syde ageyn pryson ladde kyng hym self badde trouthe myght herde afterward hath ferde dede proueth entente achab batayle wente benadab al shelde hym slewe vpon felde peple goeth aboute straye god whiche al thynge may doth myschyef haue kyng deed saue home ageyn goddes pee wente al founde lee chye hath sayd tofore sit wel kyng therfore loue theym trewe mene atte laste wyl sene flaterye thynge worthe matere forth speken ouer phylosophers lore third poynte polecye thynke specefye propter transgressores leges statuuntur vt vn iusti regis honore v lex sine iusticia populum sub principis vmbra deuiat vt rectum nemo videbit r hic tractat de tercia principum legie policia que iusticia nominata est u condicio legibus incorupta vniuiaue qd suum est cquo pondere distribuit londe men none ben men allone without kynges gouernaunce kyng lygeaunce lawe londe take lawe honde yf iuges ben trewe olde worldes newe wyl take euydence may se experience thynge kepe lawe thorow wronges withdrawe rightwysnes stande comended wherof regnes ben amended lawe may commune lordes forth comune eche hath propre deute eke knyghtes ryalte bothe worshyp vnderfongeth estate bylongeth whiche worthynesse hath gouerne rightwysnesse whiche shal lawe guyde neuerthelesse vpon syde power stante aboue lawe yeue bothe drawe forset mannes lyf thynges whiche excessyf ageyn lawe shal doo loue ne hate also imperatoriam magestatem non solum armis sy eciam legibus oportet esse armatam b myghtes kyng grete yet worthy kyng shal et wronge done al myght whiche shal peple right yt sitteth wel regalye hym self fyrst iustefye toward god degree estate elles fre toward al persone saue onely god allone whiche wyl hym self kyng chastyse none may suffyse good taken hede fyrst kyng owne dede betwene vertu vyce redresse iustyce sette euen balaunce towardes gouernaunce powre ryche lawes myght stonde lyche shal excepte persone may al hym one sondry place iustyce shal ryal offyce wyse consyderacion ordeyne dysputacion suche iuges ben lerned peple gouerned hem trewe ben wyse yf lawe couetyse set vpon iuges honde woo peple thylke londe wronge may hym self hyde allas syde yf lawe stonde right peple glad stonte vp right lawe meuable comyn peple stante resonable yf lawe torne mys peple also mystorned nota hic iusticia maximinj imperato ri qui cum alicuius prouincie custode sibi constituere volebat primo de sui nominis sama proclamacione facta ipsius condicionem diligencius inuesti gabat ensaumple matere maxymyn man may rome whiche emperour whan made gouernour weye substytucion prouynce regyon wold fyrst acquyre name lete openlye proclame man euyl good vpon name stode enclyned vertu vyce wold sette hym offyce elli put hym al weye thus helde lawe right weye whiche fonde lette couetyse world stode vpon wyse ensaumple thou myght rede holde thy mynde rede hic ponit exemplum de iudicibus incorruptis narrat qualiter gaius fabricius nuper rome consul aurum sampnitibus sibi oblatum remi dicens qd nobilius est aurum possidentes domino subuigare quam ex auri cupidi tate dominij libertacem tere cronyque fynde thus gayus fabricius whiche whylom consul rome lawes yede come whan sampnytes hym brought somme golde hym besought done hym fauour lawe toward golde gan hym drawe wherof al mennes loke parte honde toke whiche mowthe al haste put smelle taste eye lere ne foude comforte began despyse tolde vnto hem wyse note wyth golde thryue whan none al wyttes fyue fynde sauour ne delyte therin nyce synne golde couetouse ryche gloriouse whiche hath subieccion tho men whiche pocessyon ben riche golde skylle may al day whan wylle hym lefe hym lothe iustyce doon vpon hem bothe lo thus said worde threwe tofore hym vpon borde golde honde anone said theym wold none kepte lyberte doo iustyce equyte lucre suche rychesse ther ben fewe suche gesse thylke tyme vsed euery iuge refused whiche frende comyn right wolden stonde vp right trouthe onely iustyce referred thylke offyce deme iuge comyn lawe whiche sayn al draw sett lawe kepe nought comune prouffyt sought abeue al nethelees lawe whiche made pee good kepe beste setteth al men reste hic n rrat de iusticia nuper conrar imperatoris cuius tempore alicuius reuerencia persone aliqua seu precum ruencione quacunqy vel auri redempcione legum statuta comutari seu r nullatenus potuerunt rightful emperour conr de kepe pee suche lawe made none within cyte dysturbaunce vnyte durst one meuen matere tyme thou myght poynte lawe sette sheld good lette persone brought comyn fere ony man lawe dradde ther none fauour nota exemplum de constancia judicis vbt narrat de carunidotiro rome nuper cosule aui cum sui statuti legem ne ciens offendisset romani que super hee penam sibi remittere noluisset ipe propria manu vbi nullns alius ipsum vnidex fuit sui criminis vindic tam ex cutus est olde lookes sayn fynde write romayn whiche consul pretoyre who name caromydot yre sette lawe pee euery man wepenlees came counceyl hows elles malicious shal ben lawe dede statute rede accorden al shal certeyn cause whiche tho fyl herafter sone consul done feldes ryden hym longe abyden lordes couuceyl bad hym come came swerde gyrde foryete tyl couuceyl sete none hom made speche tyl hym self wold seche fonde defaute hym self said vnto twelfe whiche senate wyse haue deseruyd juyse haste hym sayden al wel wyst vyce whan ne thought malyce onely lytel slouthe thus leften routhe justyce vpon gylte shold spylte whan maner wold hym saue made vowe manful herte thus sayed rome shold neuer abrayed heyres whan dawe auncetour brake lawe thy ware forthwyth swerde statute lawe kepte al rome deth wepte nota fals iudices mortis pen pu iendi sunt narrat enim qualiter cambices rex persarum quemdam iudicem coruptum excori viuum fecit eius que pelle cathedram iudicialem ope costituit ta qd filius suus supe pat pellem poste pro tribunali sessurus iudicij equitatem euiden ius oraretu n place also rede iuge hys owne dede ne wil venge lawe broke kyng hath hym self wroke grete kyng whiche cambises ho e juge lawles fonde remembraunce dyd vpon hym suche vengeaunce skyn befloyne al quycke wyse slayne skyn shape al met nayled vpon set sone shold sitte auyse hym yf e wold flitte lawe couetyse sawe redy juyse thus defaulte juge kyng mote inge holden vp right lawe speke olde dawe take ensaumple tho fynde tale wryten also worthy prynce hol lawes londe helde first hygh goddes sake hy betake peple guyde lede whiche charge kynghe hic ponit exemplum de principi u illis qui non solum legem statuentes illam conseruant set comune bonum adaugeant propriam fatultate diminuunt et narrat qd cum liguri u atheum princeps omni prosperitatis habundancia diues vnanimes congruis legibus stare fecisse volens ad vtilitatem reipub e leges il la firmius ob ruari pe gri prof ssi se fuixit set prius iuramentu solempne leges suis sub hac forma exegit qd ipsi vsque reditum suu leges suas milla enus infringerent quibus miratis pere g nacionem suam exiliu bsque redditu perpetuo delegauit cronycle rede thus rightful lygurgyus whiche athene prynce lawe euery wherof shold peple rule hath sette vpon good rule al world cite none lawe wel begone forthwith trouthe gouernauce emonge hem distannce euery man hath encrees without werre pee without enuye loue stood richesse vpon comune good vpon synguler ordeyned power hom estate sauf wherof vpon debate stode thynge reste myght euery man herre reste whan noble rightful kyng saw ferde al thynge wherof peple stode ese whiche euer wold plese hye god who thonke soughte wonder thynge bethought shope myght lawe cite myght afterward euer laste vpon witte caste thynge hym beste sayen purpoos myght atteyne parlemente thus sette wysdom sette audience grete smale wyse tolde tale god wote ye woten alle afterward falle yet wylle hath iustyce equyte ferderyng comyn proffyt suche hath ben euer delyte one thynge beknowe wh le wylle ye knowe l e whiche toke honde al gyder goddes sonde ynge myn owne wit mote nede endure yit shal lenger yf ye wyl wyl trlle skyl god mercurius man hath taught al suche lawes made wherof ye ben al glade god thynge dyd al thy hath comaunded grace shal come place whiche ferre yle moto tarye whyle wich hym speke hath bede saith thylke stede shal suche thynges telle euer ye world shal dwelle ne shal better fare fyrst thyder fare wold lawe amonges ne withdrawe while shal oute thy setten doubte bothe thus wil praye ye wold assure saye suche othe wyl take eche shal vndertake lawes kepe holde sayden al wold vpon swere theyr othe fro tyme gothe tyl hem come ageyn shullen lawe wel pleyne euery poynte kepe fulfille thus hath lygurius wylle toke leue forth wente wel entente rightwysnes dyd goo shope hym neuer founde athene whiche founde neuer shold releced ne thylke good lawe seced comune prouffyt souyt kyng owne estate ne rought prouffyt comune toke exyle fortune lefte pryuely thylke offyce onely loue justyce whiche thoughte yf yt myyt euer deth right cite hym betake wherof men ought ensaumple take hem whiche vnder gouernaunce good lawes auaunce wold take kepe lawes haue kepe hem first lawes founde ferre lasteth ony grounde londe name yet knowe yf lyke knowe name stonde herken thou shalt vnderstonde hic ad eorum laudem qui iusticie causa leges statuerunt aliquorum nomina specialius commemorat euery benefete meryte god hym self wyl acquyte eke ful ofte falleth world wyl acquyte also may euen syche god yeueth heuen ryche world yeueth onely name stante vpon good fame hem done good dede wyse double mede receyuen done wel wherof yf thou list fame blowe ther myght thou wel soth knowe thilke honest besynesse hem first rightwysnesse emonge men lawes made may neuer vpon erthe fade euer tonge name shal redde songe hole cronyke write men shullen wyte speke good wel oughten hem first lawes soughten forderyng worldes pee vnto thebrewes moyses first egypciens mercurius troiens first ne wma pompilius athene ligurius yaue first lawe vnto gregoys foroneus hath thylke voyce romulus romayns suche men ben vylayns lawe suche wyse ordeyneth man lawe pleyneth juge stonde vp right shal serued right ferforth befalle lawe comune emonge v alle god lene mo e wel holde euery kyng therto holde thynge whiche kynges sette kynges ought lette kyng lawe taketh kepe lawe may royame kepe lawe aweye kynge right ony thynge lawe londe ought kyng wel vnderstonde lawe sworne yf lawe forlorne withouten execusyoun hit maketh londe torne vp dou n vnto kyng sclaundre thy vnto kyng alisaundre wyse philosophre hadde hym self first ladde lawe forth alle doo justyse generalle al wyde londe aboute iustyce lawe doubte shal stonde reste therto lawe one beste aboue al erthely thynge make liege drede kynge kyng shal gete hym loue toward hygh god aboue eke man erthe nexte poynte whiche ferthe aristotle lore techeth wherof soole secheth polecye book reherceth nil racionis habens vbi vel tirani regna stringit amor populi transiet exul ibi set pieta regnum que conseruabit euum non tantum po pulo set placet illa deo hic tractat de quarta principum giminis policia que pietatis dictum est per quam principe erga populum mi serioordes effecti misericordiam altissimi consecuntur nedeth debate prynce preised algate hath ben euer euer shal wherof speke special vertu pyte thorough hye mageste sterred whan sone alyght pyte world right toke mayde flesshe blood pyte cause thylke good wherof ben saue wel oughte man pyte haue vertu sette price whan hym self al wyse hath shewed shal preysed pyte may counterpeysed tyrannye peyse pyte maketh man curteyse bothe worde dede sit wel euery liege drede kyng heste obeye right weye sit kyng pytous toward peple gracious vpon rule gouernaunce worche vengeauuce whiche may cleped cruelte iustyce doth equyte dredeful man spareth l nde pyte fareth kyng may neuer fayle loue pyte thorough grace aboue phylosophre affermeth reygne good estate confermeth appostle iames wyse yth man shold iuyse hath pyte forth wyth dome hym whiche demeth may hym self ful sore drede hym shal lacke vpon nede fynde pyte whan wolde pyte wyl beholde poynte cristes love loken ouermore behouely fynde reson lawe kynde tassyodre aprise telleth royame sauf pite dwelleth tullyus tale auoweth saith kyng pite boweth pyte stonte ouercome hath shelde grace nome vnto kynges yeueth victory alisannder hystorye rede worthy knyght sodeyn wrath right foriuged bath appeleth yt word kyng quareleth said none aboue wote wel lord ad fro thy lordshyp appele nought fro thy wrath al thouyt thy pyte stante myn appele kyng vnderstode hym wele pure pyte gaue hym grace eke rede another place constantinus imperator ait vere se dominum esse comprobat qui seruum pietatis se facit thus said whilom constantyne emperour enclyne pyte seruaunte al worldes remenaunte worthy ben lorde olde bookes recorde trai nu ait qd cum ipse subditos suos solite pietatis fauore magi qua austeritatis rigore regere corum que neuolenciam pocius quam timorem penis se attractare proponebat fynde write ensauplayr traian worthy debonayr whome rome stode gouerned vpon tyme lerned famulyer said vnto counceller emperour wylle veyne honour ne yet reddour iustyce yf myght offyce lord peple plese hym thought grete ease loue hertes hym drawe drede ony lawe wha thynge done doubte ful ofte cometh wers aboute kynge pytous gracious mykel thrist hym shal leiyde whiche elli shold torne syde qualiter iudeus predester cum pa gaue equitante itinerauit per desertum et ipsum de fide sua interrogauit pite supporte grace phi sophre vpon place writyng dayes olde tale grete ensaumble tolde vnto kyng macedoyne bytwene cayr babyloyne whan comen somer hete happened two men mete shold entre paas wyldernes wente forth spekende vnder large wodes ende one man axeth man art thou lyef broder thy creaunce thy feyth paynym seyth lawe vse shal feyth refuse louen al men liche poure bothe eke riche whan glad shal glad sory whan ben bestad shal lyue vnyte euery man degre right self wolde right toward al sholde gracious debonayr thus haue tolde softe f feyth lawe creaunce yf lyst acqueyntaunce telle manere man thou art answerd vpon part iewe lawe shal man felawe kepe hym trouth worde ne dde yf without drede veray iewe right elli may truly bereue hym bothe lyf good paynym herde vnderstood thought wonder lawe thus vpon sondry sawe talkyng bothe forth wente day hote sonne brente paynym rode vpon asse catel lasse hym riche trusse ladde iewe al vntrouth hadde went vpon foot besyde bethought hym myght ryde wordes slye wyse vnto paynym wyse said shal sene thou woltest mene yf thy lawe certeyn thou hast tolde darwel seyn thou wylt beholde distresse ful werynesse ne may vnnethe goo lete ryde myle two may body ese paynym wold hym dysplese spake pytee list hym knowe see pleynte whiche made wold herte glade light made hym thyng strauge thus ther made newe chauge paynym iewe lofte sette vpon asse softe soo goon forth carpend faste tyl laste paynym myght goo nomore prayed vnto iewe therfore suffre hym ryde lytel whyle iewe thouyt hym begyle anone rode forth grete paas paynym caas seid thou hast thy right thou haddest behyght socour vpon nede accordeth dede thou arte lawe holde suche wyse tolde thynke also partye vpon lawe iewrye werche duete thyn asse shal goo forth al thy good whiche haue sesed wote thou arte dysesed right glad myspayed whan hath wordes sayed al haste rode aweye p nym wote none weye grounde kneleth euen hondes vp vnto heuen said hye sothfastnes louest al rightwysnes vnto thy dome lord appele beholde deme quarele humble herte beseche mercy bothe wreche set al thy iugement thus vpon marrement paynym hath made prayere thenne drery chere goeth hym forth gate e caste eye aboute algate iewe yf myght see tyme may bee tyl atte last ageyn nyght god wold wente right whiche helde hye weye thene sawe valeye iewe liggend al blody deed vpon gras strangeled leon boked vp doun fonde asse fast forthwith harneys redely al hool sounde lefte whan iewe hym byrefte wherof thanked god knelende thus man may knowe ende pytous pyte deserueth man pyte serueth aristotle bereth wytnesse god shal foomen represse shal ay stonde vnderfote pyte men sayn thylke rote wherof vertues spryngen alle infortune befalle ony londe lacke pyte cause thylke aduersite alday may shewe eye world discretely syhe good euery man therfore take hede said tofore tale nowe noble prince whylom drowe euydence appryse men may fynde many wyse olde bookes rede though ben erthe dede good name may deye pyte wold obeye doo dedes mercy tale redely remembre aristotle tolde may wylle god beholde vpon poynte ended wherof pyte stood comended charite felawe kepen bothe one lawe nota hic de pietate principis erga populum vbi narrat quod odius rex atheuis contra dorences bellum gere deberet consulto prius appoline respo sum accepit quod vnum de duobus v e cet seipsum preli interfeci et populum saluari aut seipsum saluum fi ri populum interfeci eligere oport ret super quo rex pietate mot plebis que sui magi qua proprij corporis salutem affectans mortem sibi preelegit et sic bellum aggrediece provita multorum solus incerijt pyte speke playne mercy wel besayn fuf ofte hym self wold peyne kepe another fro peyne charite moder pyte thynge mys suffre yf may amende sitteth euery man lyuende pytons none wel kyng whele fortune hath set abouen alle kyng yf befalle pyte ferme stable al londe vaylable onely thorugh grace persone pyte hym allone may al large royame saue sit wel kyng haue pyte valere tolde said dayes olde godrus hys degree kyng athene cyte werre ageynst dorrence take euydence shal lefalle batayle thouyt shold hym self counceyl appollo triste thorough who answer thus wyste two poyntes myght chese wold body lese batayle hym self deye elli second weye seen peple dyscomfyte pyte hath persyte vpon poynte byleue peple thought releue chese hym self dede suche another hede wold lymmes deye nethelesse somme parteye ought kynges herte stere lyege men forbere eke toward enemyes ful ofte may deserue prise take pyte remembraunce myght vengeaunce whan hath victorye drawe memorye pyte stede wreche may fayle thylke speche wherof ariseth worldes fame yeue prynce worthy name hic ponit exeplum de victoriosi principis pietate erga aduersarios suos et narrat qd cum pompeiu rom noru imperator regem armonie aduersariu suum bello victum cepisset captum quam vinculis alligatum rome tenuisset tirannidis iracundie stumilos post ponens pietatis masuetudine operatus est dixit enim qd nobilius regem facere quam deponere su quo dictum regem ab quam ulla redempcione non solum vinculis abso luitsz ad sui regni culmen gratuita uoluntate coronatum restituit irede whylom pompey rome must obey werre iupartye ageynste kynge ermonye long tyme hym greued atte last acheued kyng dyscomfyte hadde forth hym rome ladde prisoner many day sory plyte power laye crowne heed deposed within walles faste enclosed ful grete humylete suffreth aduersite pompeye sawe pacyence toke pyte conscience vpon hygh deys tofore al rome paleys wolde vpon hym rewe lete yeue hym corone newe estate ful playn restored reygne ageyn said goodely thyng make vndone kyng hym power bothe thus longe wrothe accorden hem fynal pres yet iustyce nethelees kepte thynge offended wherof pompeye commended may kyng hym self excuse yf iustyce kepte vse esch cruelte mote attempre pyte cruelte felonye engendred tyrannye ageyn who condycion god hym self champyon who strengthe may man withstode euer yet hath stonde god tyraunt ouer ladde pyte reygne ladde ther myght fortune laste greuous atte laste god hym self hath redressed pyte thylke v rtu blessed neuer lete maister falle cruelte though befalle may reyne throlbe god wold shold ouerthrowe wherof ensaumples ben nowe hem thylke mer drowe hic loquitur contra illos qui tirani potestate principatum optinentes ini uitatis sue mal cia gloriatur et narrat exemplum qualiter leoncins tira nu pium iuscinianum non solum sl ima orie magestatis fraudulentur expulit sed vt ipe inhabilis ad reg nu aspectu plebis efficiretur aso et labris absasis ipm tiranice mutilauit deus tamen qui su omia pius est tibe io suueniente via cu adiutorio terbel bulgarie regis iustianinum inter fecto leoncio ad imperium restitui mise ricorditer proturauit f cruelte rede thus whan tyraunt leoncyus thempyre rome aryued fro hath strength priued pyt u iustynian cruel man nose lyppes bothe ut wold hym bothe vnto peple make hym vnable al merciable hygh god ordeyneth within tyme also whan strengest yre shouen empyre tyberius power hadde rome power ladde leonce suche wyse ordeyneth toke iuyse nose lyppes bothe two dyd another worthy lo falle hath cruelte pyte sette vp ageyn bookes yn terbellis kyng bulgarye helpe chyualrye iustynyan hath vnprisonned thempyre ageyn coroned hic boquitur ulterius de rude f te situly necnon et de berillo eiusdem consiario qui ad tormentu populi qu dam taurum eneum tiranic coniectura fabritari constituit quo tamen ipse prior prio crie illud exigente vsqy ad sui interitus expiracionem iudicia iter torquebatur cronycle fynde also siculus eke cruel kyng lyke tempest pyte myght areste first bokes ye vpon see fonde galeye ete hem make werre al herre fro pyte mysericorde therto coude accorde myght een slough therof glad nough counceyl many one emonge one name brillus hyght bythought hym myyt vnto tyrannt lykyng owne ymagenyng lete forge make tonne bra syde cast dore man may payne shal begyn fyre men putten vnder al dyd wonder whan man payne cryed bull bra gapeth wyde shal seme though al belewyng mannys ere cryeng man al sleyghtes deuyl lyeth helle faste hym made hath ouercaste trespace dede put stede hym self fyrst alle whiche peyne falle men ordeyneth ther man yt hym compleyneth tyrannye cruelte ensaumple kyng may see hym self eke counceyl bothe mankynde bothe god abhomynable ensaumples ben couenable fynde prynces moo thou shalt tyme ago nota hic de diomisio tirano qui mire crude atis seueritate eciam hospites suos ad deuoradu equis suis tribuit cui hercules tandem super venientes victum impium impietate sua pari morte conclusit grete tyraunt dyonys mane lyf set pry vnto hors ful te yafe men stede corne chafe h r thylke stode deuoureden maunes bloode tyl fortune atte laste came hercules hym ouercame right wyse tyraunt toke iuyse tyl hath deth deyed also pyte hym hath socoured tyl lyf deuoured nota hic de consimil lichaontis tirania qui carnes hoim hoiby suo hospicio ad vescendum dedit cuius formam condicioni similem qualiter coequas ipm lupum transformauit lychaan also fynde ageyn law kynde hoost slewe mete made bodyes e e men within hows iubyter glorious meued thynge vengeaunce vpon cruel kyng toke fro mane forme wolf lete transforme thus cruelte kyd longe tyme hyd wolfe openlye who nature pryuelye condycion vnto conclusion tyraunt dyspryse fynde ensaumple sondry wyfe namelyche hem ful ofte fortune hath set ofte vpon warres wynne wronge begynne tyrannye may laste suche done atte laste men suche hem falleth ageyn suche pyte calleth vengeaunce god aboue hath tender loue sauyng mannys lyfe shal founde gyltyfe whan wold mercy craue tyme nede shal none haue nota qualiter beo homiby stratis cit nature thus fynde fiers lyon kynde goeth rampyng praye yf e man fynde waye wil hym slee yf withstonde yf man coude vnderstonde falle anone tofore face signe mercy grace lyon shal nature restreyne yre suche mesure though beste tamed torne aweye halfyng ashamed man shal thyng greue shold prynce acheue th worldes grace yf wold r ye n whan yolde stante vpon mercy alle speken specialle haue suche suche tyrauntes who hertes ne pyte may poynte mercy plye vpon tyrannye ne gladen hem men slee ractes see ben vnpytous tempeste right may pyte reste cruelte grete vltrage tyraunt corage engendreth hath wherof fynde tale cometh mynde hic loquitur contra tiranos illos qui cu bello vicere possut huani saguinis effusio saturare nequeut et narrat exemplu de quodam sa rege cui nomen stachus erat qui pre ceberis tuc oriente bellicosus victoriosus quoscuqy gladio vincere poterat absqy pietate interfeci costituit set tandem sub manu thamaris marsegittaru regine bello captus quam diu quesiuit seueritatem seueritate final inuenit nam ipa quoddm de sanguine saru plenu ante se offerre decreuit quo capud tiranni vsqy ad morte mergens dixit tiranaru crude ssime semper esuriens sanguinem sicisti ecceiam ad saturitatem sanguinem bibe rede olde bokes thus ther due spertachus men cleped wetrour cruel man conquerour stronge power ladde condicion hadde hym happeneth victorye lust al glorye slee saue rauson wold good haue sauyng manys lyfe al goeth swerde knyfe beef hym mannys blood nethelesse thus stod fortune aboute wente fyl right heyre dyssent pers crowned kynge wha worship ynge falle kyng pers fyrst dyuers hath shape vpon tyde whan hyest pryde rancour hete ageyn quene mersagete thamaris tyme hyght made werre al myght wolde hir londe defede hir owue sone ageyn hym sende deffence hath vndertake dyscomfyte take wha kyng hym honde wold mercy vnderstonde dyd hym slee presence kyng vyolence whan came moders ere sende one ay wyde suche frendes grete power tyl lad sondre wyse tho caste kyng may ouercaste atte last accorded daunger paas thorugh tyraut shold pa shope power compas strengthe men suche weye shal escape aweye whan thus ordeyned hath hir owne body feyned fere though wold flee hir londe hath herde thys lady fledde fast chase spedde founde araye betyd vpon day paas whan falle enbusshementes breke alle hym beclypte euery syde fle ne myght syde dede take two hondred thousand sake hym hoost thus leyed grete boost hym tyrannye hit helpeth mercy crye hym whilom dyd none vnto quene anone brought hym sye word spake leyed hye man mannes kynde reson man hath lefte behynde lyued wors beste pyte myght areste mannys blode shede spylle thou haddest neuer yet thy fylle last tyme come thy malyce ouercome thou tyl hast mys shal right tho bad lady men shold vessel brynge wolde see vengeaunce iuyse began anone deuyse toke prince whiche ladde chyef counceyl hadde hem lefte ony brethe made hem blede dethe vessel stode whan fulfilled blode caste tyraunte therin said thus myght thou wynne lustre thyn appetyte blode whylom thy delyte thou shalt drynke al thy fylle thus onely goddes wylle wold hym self sirauge pyte fonde mercy straunge without grace bore may wel shelbe therfore cruelte hath good ende pyte wende maketh god merciable cause resonable kyng shal pytous ellys yf doubtous sleen cause rightwysnesse may sayd pytousnesse pusillanymyte euery prynce shold flee yf pyte mesure excede kynghode may alwey procede iustyse vpon right belongeth knyght gladly fyght reste sette liege peple reste whan warre vpon hem falleth mote befalleth knyghthode lyon peple champyon without vny pyte fayned yf manhode restreyned pee werre iustyce goeth herre knyghthode set behynde aristotle lore fynde kyng shal ke good vysage man knowe corage al honour worthynesse yf kyng shal vpon gesse without v r cause drede may lyke rede though lyke fable ensaumple good resonable hic loquitur secundum philosophu di n ad sicut non decet principe ti ania esse c deles ita nec mo osa pusillamitate esse vecor olde dayes felle rede whylom helle vp n lo de arc de wonder dredeful noyse made fyl ylke day hylle chyldyng lay th wes hym come oyse like day dome fereful mannys thought thynges see nouyt wel herden al aboute oyse doute wenden lore thynge thene vubore nere hylle vpon chaunce taken delyueraunce vnbuxumlyche cryed euery man fledde syde drede lefte owne holbs atte laste molbs lore notice bytake tho helde hem nyce withouten cause dradde thus yf kyng herte ladde euery thynge shal ful ofte shold chaunge chere vpon fantasye drede whan ther cause drede nota hic secundum oracium de mag nanimo de pusillanime thersite orace prynce tolde hym l uer wold vpon knyghthede achylles sewe tyme warre eschewe thersites dyd troye chilles al hole ioye set vpon armes fyght thersytes sought al myggt vnarmed stonde reste two beste achilles vpon nede hath wherof knyghthede yet commended ouer alle kyng salamon specialle saith tyme pee tyme nethelees werre prynce algate shal comyn right debate h owne worshyp eke behoueth seke onely werre worshyp right lordship holde deffende mote euery worthy prynce entende betwene symplyesse pyte fole hast cruelte stante hardynesse therupon kyng herte adresse whan tyme forsake whan tyme also take godely werres vpon honde shal drede wonde rightwisnes withal god myghty ouer al forther euery mane trouthe le thorugh owne slouthe namely kynges nede may fayle spede stante one hem alle mote wel better falle wel god fauoureth comune right socoureth see soth dede beholde byble thou myght rede grete ensaumples many one wherof wyl telle one hic dicit qd princeps iusticie causa bellum modo timere debet et narrat qualiter dux gedeon cum solis ercentis viris quinque reges scilicet madianitharum amalichitarum amortanrum amor orum buseorum cum eoru excercitu qui nonaginta milium numeratus est gracia cooperante diuina victoriose infugam conuertit upon tyme byfelle ayenst iude israelle whan sondry kynges come purpoos destroye e peple whiche god kepte tho stode thylke dayes gedeon shold lede goddes folke toke hym rede sende al londe aboute tyl assembled hath route xxx thousand deffence fyght make resystence ageyn wold assayle nethelesse one batayle thre enemyes double al wherof gedeon hym drad litel peple al thynge may helpe ther lacketh mane helpe gedeon aungel sente bad forther wente al openlye crye euery man partye wold owne wylle delyte abyde stylle home ony maner wyse purchace couetyse lust loue lacke te shold aboute sterte holde hym stylle pee wherof vpon morowe lee wel xx thousand men mo crye ben goo thus hym onely lefte thyrd parte yet god efte aungel sende said gedeon yf thyn helpe shal vndertake thou shalt yet lesse pexle take wyl thou spede thy morowe take good hede vnto flode whan ye come man hath water nome vpon hande lappeth thy parte chese al hym wery swynke vpon wombe lyeth drynke forsake put hem al albeye myghty al weye lyse helpe sewe good men though fewe gedeon wayteth welle vpon morowe euery delle god hym bade right dede thus laften stede hym thre hondred moo remenaunte al goo wherof gedeon merueyleth therupon god counceylleth pleynyng ferforth dare god wold e ware shal spede vpon right hath bede hym goo nyght toke man hym shal spoke matere amonge hethen enemyes may wyse afterward hym shal befalle gedeon monges alle phara tryst moste nyght toke toward thylke hooste whiche lodged valeye wolden seye vpon fote ferde two sareyyns spekyng herde quod one arede sweuen right met sweuen nyght thought sawe barley cake fro hyll weye hath take came rollyng doun one none forth cours ran kynges tente madyan amalech amareye amon iebuseye many another tente mo grete ioye thought tho threwe grounde ouercaste al hoost sore agaste woke pure drede sweuen wel arede qd sareyyn anone barly cake gedeon fro hylle doun sodeynlye shal come set suche skrye vpon kynges v bothe shal v al lothe suche drede shal v brynge yf hadden flight wynge weye fote dyspayre shul leue flee ayre ther shal thyng hym withstode whan gedeon hath vnderstonde tale thanked god alle pryuelye ageyn stalle lyf hym bath perceyued hath fully conceyued shal spede vpon nyght sewyng shope gone multitude assayle shalt thou grete meruayle wysdom wrought lytel peple brought none hem ne hath potte erthe tath light brennyng cresset eche hem eke trompet bare honde eke besyde thus vpon nyghtes tyde du gedeon whan derke ordeyneth hym vnto werke parted folke thre chargeth ne fle taught hem shold askrye al one wyse par companye word shold eke speke shold pottes breke eche one whan herde hym self first ferde whan came stede bad hem right dede thus stalkyng forth pa noble duc whan tyme pot brake loude ascryed tho brake euery syde trompe tho seke blewe blewen eke suche noyse emonge hem alle though heuen shold falle hylle vnto voys auswerde hoste valey herde saith hylle light heryng syght caught suche sodeyn fere none hem lefte tentes hooly forsoke none good toke onely body bare fledde doeth wylde hare euer vpon hylle blewe tyl sawe tyme knewe fled vpon rage whan wyst th ir auautage fyl anone vnto chace thus myyt thou see goddes grace vnto good auayleth elli oftyme faylleth suche wel disposed tale nedeth glosed openlye shewed god hem ben wel thewed hath yeue grauted victorye thensaumple hystarye good euery kyng holde first hym self beholde good lyuyng yt folke shal brynge good also may glad many mery day euer hath done sitte aboue mone al thynge may spylle spede euery caas euery nede good kyng wel dresseth al foo men represseth ther may man hym dere also wel forbere suffre wicked kyng falle handes foon alle hic dicit qd vbi et quando causa tempus requirunt princeps illos sub potestate sua quos iusticie aduersarios suo agnouerit occidere de iure tenetur et narrat exemplum qualiter pro eo qd saul regem agag bello deuincit iuxta samuelis consiliu occidere nolu ipse diuino iudicio non sosum regno israel priuatus set heredes sui pro perpetuo exhereditati sunt n ow ferthermore yf shal seyn mater torne ageyn speke iustyce pyte rule ryalte may kyng wel vnderstonde enyghthode mote take honde whan stonte vpon nede shal rightful cause drede werre pee wyl stonde blameles suche cause kyng may haue better slee saue wherof thou myght ensaumple fynde hygh maker mankynde samuel saul bade shal thyng ad ad ageyn kyng agag fyght godhede hym behyght agag shal ouercome whan ferforth come saul hym hath dyscomfyte god bad make respyte ne shold hym slee anone saul lete ouer gone dyd goddes heste agag made grete beheste raunsom wold gyu kyng saul suffreth hym lyue fayneth pyte forth withal sawe knewe alle hye god feyneth samuel vpon hym pleyneth sende hym worde l f e agag ne refte lyf shal onely deye hym self fro regalye shal put euer mo nought eke eyre also shal neuer come ageyn thus myght thou see sothe pleyne hic narrat vl erius super eodem qualiter dauid extremis iusticie caus vt ioab occideretur absque vlla remissione filio suo salamoni iniunxit moche ly vpon prynces stante ye wy euer kynges right dedes knyght hondes kynge deth lyf al thynge lawes iustyce sl en dedely vyce yf man deth deserne yf kyng lyf preserue hym ought deye sh weth ensaumplerye byble euydente yd te amente whan lenger myght leue vnto sone cherge hath geue ioab sheld slee algace whan dauyd gone gate yonge wyse salamone hi ders heste dyd anone slewe ioab suche wyse herden iuyse euer dredden hym god eke wel payed therfore wold herte plye lawes iustefye yet kepte forth al yt prynce shal ne tyrannye wrought fonde wysdom sought rightful nethelees al lyf e ode pee dedely warres hadde euery man wysdom dradde hym self wyse right worthy men pryse hath counceyl withholde euery prynces holde make suche retenue wyse ben renewe fooles thynge may better aboute kynge tha oc ceyl substauce al bynges gouernaunce hic dicit qd pepulum sibi comissu bene ere super omnia principi laudabilius est et narrat exemplum qualiter pro eo qd salamon vt populu bene regeret ab altissimo sapienciam specialius postulauit omma bona pariter cum illa sibi habundancius aduerunt salamon man may see thynge moste necessyte vnto worthy kynge bylongeth whan kyngdom vnderfengeth god bad hym chese wolde said hym haue sholde wold aske thynge noble kynge ther vpon bone prayed god wyse sayed thynge whome shal regne yeue wisdom regne forth peple haue thyn honour may kepe saue whan salamon loue hath taxed god hath axed ryght wel payed graunted sone al onely bone shal haue richesse bele pee hye noblenesse wysdomes axynges stant aboue al erthly thynges hic dicit secundum salamonem qd regie magestatis imperium ante omia sano consilio dirigendum est vt kyng wil reygne saue first hym behoueth haue thy god beleue snche counceyl byleue fulfilled trouth rightwysnes aboue al noblenes bytwene reddour pyte kyng shal suche equyte set balaunce euen hygh god heuen al peple nobleye longe vnto name seye moste aboue al erthely good kyng hym self good hel th weye yf kyng forsueye quidquid delirant reges plectuntur achiui vl hath seyn comyn peple ouerleyn hath kynges synne abought al though peple agylte nought kyng god mysserueth peple taketh deserueth world elli note shal stonde thy good kynge triste first hym self ne wyste none helpe god allone shal rule persone within hym self thorugh prouidence ben better conscience fynde ensaumple tale fynde soth hic de lucio imperatore exemplum ponit qualiter princeps sui nominis famam secretis consiliarijs sapienter inuestigare debet et siquid ea sinistru inuenerit prouisa discrecione ad dexteram conuertat cronycle telleth thus kyng rome lucyus within chambre vpon nyght steuard hows knyght forthwith chamberleyn also counceyl bothe two stoden chymne gyder spekyng al thre happeth kynges fole sat fyre vpon stole bable played yet herde al sayed therfore toke hede kyng hem axeth rede suche matere came mowthe hym tolde couthe whan al spoke ment kyng al hole entente thenne atte laste hem axeth kyng men tellen emong folke touchyng name pris blame right herde sayn bad hem telle playne peynte soth forbere thylke feyth hym bere stuard first vpon thynge gafe answer vnto kynge thought glose matere said ferre name good honourable thus steward fauourable trouth p yne ne tolde kyng axeth sholde chamberleyn auyse subtyl wyse somdele thouyt vpon feythe hym tolde al peple seyth yf counceyl trewe wyst wel knewe hym self shold worthy kyng degree thus counceyl accuseth partye kyng excuseth fole herde al caas tyme goddes wylle se th sayden ynough hem scorne bothe lough kyng sayd tho syr kyng yf wysdom thyn owne mode thou thy self good thy counceyl shold bad kyng therof merueyle whan fole wysely spacke hym self fonde lacke within owne conscience thus felith euydence goddes grace nspyred maketh yt good counceyl desired put awey vycious toke hym vertuous wrongful lawes ben amended londes good wel dyspended peple nomore opressed thus stood euery thyng redressed kyng propre wyse hath suche hym self counceyl may fayle euery thynge shal anayle vyces goeth aweye euery thynge holdeth waye wherof hye god plesed al londes folke esed yf comyn peple crye kyng list plye clamor wolde otherwyse shold ayneth done hem grace hath seen many place hath falle grete contrarye fynde ensaumplerye hic dicit qd seniores magi experti ad principis cousilium admittendi poci u e istuut et narrat qualiter pro co qd roboas salomonis filius here senium sermouibus renuncians dictum iunenum preelegit de duodecim tribus israel domino sud decem penitus ami sit sic cum duabus tautumodo il usus postea regnauit eth salamone whan wise kyng gone n roboas persone ryue shold corone peple vpon parlement auysed one assent al vnto kyng preyden comune voys thus seyd hege lord byseche thou receyue humble speche graunte v whiche ye reson wyl thy grace thy skyl thy fader whyle lyue myght bothe graunte pryue vpon werkes whiche comyn peple streyte ladde whan temple made newe thyng men neuer tofore knewe brought vp llage al vnder vsage werkes whiche made tho befalle al made right seyed riche whan deyd nomore nede thou therof wylt taken hede pillen peple longe hath greued sore wyse seye tender herte preye thou relese thylke det vpon v thy fader sette yf lyke done ben thy men euer mo gone comen thyn e kyng herde requeste saith wyl ben aduysed hath therof tyme assysed hym thouyt vpon thynge counceyl sought first wyse knyghtes olde tale tolde counceyllen hym manere loue glad chere foryeue graunte al axed fader taxed may reygne acheue thyng shal hym litel greue kyng hem herde ouer passeth wit copasseth yonge thynge wyse olde men despys saiden sit shal shame euer vnto thy worthy name thou ne kepe thy right thou arte thy yonge myght thyn olde fader gate say vnto peple plate whyle thou lyuest thy londe leste fynger thyn honde shal strenger ouer al thy fader body alle thus also shal thy tale hem smote roddes smale scorpyons thou shalt hem smyte thy fader toke lite thou thynkest take mychel thus shalt thou make hem drede sore grete herte thy corage holde hem seruage yong kyng hym hath coformed done laste enformed hym vndoyng whan came spekyng hath yonge counceyl holde wordes tolde al peple audyence whan herde sentence malyce manace anone tofore owne face haue hym entyerly refused ful grete reproue accused began raue hym self fayne saue wylde wode rage wyndes maketh see sauage yt calme bryngeth wawe defaute grace lawe peple stered al one forth goo wones lignage twelfe two tribus onely hem selfe hym abyden moo euer moo retorne without espryre departed fro rightful heyre al israel comyn voyce kyng vpon owne choyce amonge hem self anone make haue yonge lord forsake polber knyght jeroboas toke lefte roboas rightful heyre dyssent thus yonge cause wente counceyl good reygne fro rightful blood euer afterward deuyded may prouen caas yonge couceyl warme men ware dothe ofte harme olde age counceyl serueth lusty yongth thonke deserueth vpon traueyle dothe bothe say sothe sondry cause haue wyl wygne saue kyng behoueth euery day one may kyng bothe rule ellys al goeth rule nota questionem cuiusdam philosophi vtrum regno conueniencius foret principem optare sapientem quam cum sano consilio ipsum eligere insipientem vpon matere also questyon betwene two thus writen book fonde whether better londe kyng hym self wyse bere owne pryse counceyl good kse yf stode kyng yf vycious counceyl vertuous answered suche wyse better wyse counceyl shold gone many one rather shal onely man f l counceyl ought wysdem made falle allone shold hem alle fro vyces vnto vertues chaunge wel straunge thy onde may wel glad wh kyng good couceyl lad sette hym vnto rightwysnes hygh worthynes betwene reddeur pyte th mercy forth equyte kyng holden ouer alle pyte specialle moste beholde thy shold pite beholde b n ge onde ben euer vnder honde f r go de ordenaunce stonde vnder gouernaunce nota ad u precipue de principis ga suos subditos debita pietate legitur nim ouabter anthonius scipion exemplificatus dixit quod mallet vnum de populo sibi commisso viru sa uare uam centum ex hostibus enigenis lo perdere emperour anthonyus fynde h w sayd thus leuer hym saue one lieg haue enemyes hundred dede thus lerned rede cypyo consul rome thus see dru r ensaumples stonde kyng hath charge honde comyn peple gou rne wyl may wel lerne none good plesaunce god good gouerna e euery gouernaunce due pyte thus may argue pyte foundemente euery kynges reygnemente medlyd wyth iustyce two remeu n al vyce vertu moste vaylable make kynges royame stable lo thus foure poyntes tofore gouernaunce bore trouth first laregsse pyte forth rightwisnesse haue hem tolde ouer first poynte set rule polecye wherof kyng shal modefye flesshly lu e nature thynke telle suche mesure bothe kynde shal serued eke lawe god obserued corporis et mentis regem decet omnis honestas nominis vt famam nulla libido r omne qd est hominis effe minat illa voluptas sit n si magnanimi cordis vt obstat ei hic tractat secundum aristotilem de quinta principum xegiminis pol cia quam castitatem concernit cuius honestas im pudicicie motus obtemporans tam cor poris quam anime mundiciciam specialius pres rnat male made femele one desyreth fele nedeth weye kynde whan man may redy fynde owne wyf shold che straunge place beseche borowe another mane plough hath grete good yuough affayted owne heste hym wel honeste thynge vnknowe thy shold euery good man knowe thynke maryage trouth plyte lyeth morgage yf breke falsehede discordeth manhede namely toward grete wherof bookes al trete phylosophre techeth alysaunder hym bytecheth lore shal mesure body mesure flesshly lust shal excede thus forth shal procede first poynte sayd ere chastyte selde cometh dayes place nethelesse grace aboue al specialle none chaste may ben alle yet knyghtes hygh estate order prelate shal enoynted scifyed mote magnefyed dygnyte corone shold another lowe persone hygh empryse therfore prynce hym shold aduyse falle suche ryote namely ne assote chaunge womanhede worthynesse manhede nota de doctriua aristotiles quasi ter princeps vt animi sui iocundita prouocet mulieres formosa c bro aspicere debet caueat tamen ne men vo luptuosa torpesceus ex carnis fragilita te vicium dilabatur f aristotle haue wel radde alysaunder badde gladen corage shold beholden vysage wymmen ben fayre yet set exaumplayre body guyde rule ne passe mote rule wherof hym self begyle wymmen gyle man hym self bywapeth whan owne wytte iapeth woman wel excuse man wyl vpon hym muse folyssh impressyon ymagynacion within hym self fyre bloweth ye woman thyng knoweth may thynge wyte yf man hym self excite drenche wyl forbere water shal blame bere may ye golde though men coueite yf man wyl lyue streyte woman hath hym thyng boude yf owne herte wounde may lette folye though fyl companye myght ony thynge purchace yet maketh man first chace woman fleeth purseweth weye skyl sueth man cause befalle ful ofte sythe falle may wel aryse netheles ful many wyse befooled hath hem self dayes yet emonge men euer ronge febelest caas syt man kynde loue kynde man loue wyt lese yf month iuyle shal frese decembre shal hote yere mystorneth wel wow seen man fro estate thorugh soty eff mynate leue man shal hose aboue shoo man ought vsed yet world hath ofte accused ful grete prynces dede loue hem self myslede wherof manhode stode behynde olde ensaumples fynde hic ponit exemplum qualiter pro sardanapallus assirioru prin p eri oblectamento effeminat f e concupiscencie torp rem quasi ex c nsuetudine adhibebat barboro rege doru super h c insidiante sui feruo ri maiori voluptate subitis mutacioni bus ext nctus est olde gestes tellen thus whylom sordanapallus helde al hole empyre grete kyngdom assyre thorugh slouth corage falle ylke fyry rage loue man assoteth hym self ryot th wexeth ferforth womannysshe ageyn kynde fysshe byde wolde vpon londe wymmen suche luste fonde dwelt euer chambre stylle onely wrought wylle wymmen bede seldom whan stede wolde wenden oute seen stod aboute kyste played taughten hym lace ayed weue purs enfyle perle fyl thylke whyle one barbar prynce mede seeth kyng womanhede falle fro chyualrye gate hym helpe companye wrought atte laste kynge reygne caste vndoon euer moo yet men speken hym shame thy loue manere nota qualiter dauid amans muli propter hoc probitat armorum non minus excercuit kyng dauid many loue nethelesse alweye aboue knyghthode kepte suche wyse flesshly couetyse luste lygge lady armes lefte luste armes prynce lu sueth werre purseweth whan tyme armed contre stante ful ofte harmed whan enemyes wexe bolde deffence none beholde ful many londe hath lore men may rede ofte tyme tofore hem as soughten ful dere aboughten hic locuit r qualiter regnum lasa ui voluptatibus deditum de facili vin r et ponit exemplum de ciro rege persarum qui cum ddo miru probita ti strenuissimos sibiqy llo aduer sant nullo modo vincere potuit cum ipsis tandem pacis tractatum dissimilans ordiam finalem stabilre finx superquo ddi postea per aliquod mpus armis insoluti sub pacis tempore voluptatibus intendebant quod cir percipiens eos armatus subito irruit ipsos que indefensibiles vincens sub imperio tri tarios subiugauit mochel ease thynge worth setteth euery vyce forth euery vertu put backe wherof price torneth lacke cronyke may reherce telleth kyng pers cyrus hyght werre hadde geynst people dradd courte lyddos hyght yet ought myght batayle vpon werre hem alwey werre whan sawe wyst wele strengthe wan dele thenne atte laste caste wyle worthy peple begyle toke hem fayned p e shold laste endelees sayd wordes wyse thought al otherwyse btyd vpon caas whan peple reste token ese many folde worldes se tolde waye kynde noryce euery luste toucheth vyce thus whan lustes falle werres ben forgeten alle none wold worshyp arme ydelshyp putten besynesse aweye toke hem daunce pleye moste aboue al thynges token hem lykynges flesshly lustes chastyte receyued degree euery man doth hym lyste whan kyng pers wyste vnto folye entenden power wha leste weden sodeynly doeth thonder came put hem vnder thus hath lecherye lore londe tofore beste hem tho byble fynde also nota hic qualiter facta belli luxus infortunat et narrat qd cum rex amolech hebreis sibi insultantibus resis tere nequijt consilio balaam mulieres regni sui pulcherimas castro hebre orum misit qui ab ipsis conta inath graciam statim iserunt et c ab amalech deuicti magna multituine gladio aderunt tale lyke vnto thynge amalech payen kynge whan myght weyr defende londe put albeyr veray peple israel sarasyn byfelle thorough counceyl balaam rowte fayre woman nam lusty yonge age bad hem goo lynage ebrewes forth wente eyen greye brolbes bente wel arayed euery chone whan comen anone emong brethes none syght catche catche myght eche hem sustes sought ful dere bought grace anone began fayle whan men batayle se plyte take dyscomfyte wythin l tel throwe myght hem ouerthrowe whylom wonte stonde tyl ph nces cause honde hath take vengeaunce laste c sed atte laste god poyed dede fonde vpon stede mysferred te hem bothe two ge mennys eye hem sye ensaumyled hem vpon dede ra ed vnto godhede olde synnes amende wold mercy sende ed hem newe grace may shewe sondry place chas yte clennesse accordeth worthynesse men armes ouer alle moste alle specialle verta yng ylongeth vpon fortune hongeth bonde shal spede spylle thy yf kyng wylle fro ustes flesshe restreyne ageynst hym self maketh treyne yf slyde hym better goo besyde eurye man may vnderstonde tyme stonde sory luste lyke wh ende maketh man syke torneth ioyes sorowe r ght sonne morowe beshyueth derke nyght lusey yongthe mannes myght age stonde e mystorneth al laste whe e hic boquitur qualiter principum irre gulat voluptas eos et semita rectum multociens deuiare compellit et narrat exemplum de salamone qui ex sue carnis concupiscencia victus mu ierum blandimentis sui scandalum deos enos colore presumebat euery worthy prynce holde within hym self hym self beholde see state persone thynke ther ioyes none vpon erthe made laste flessh shal atte laste lustes lyf forsake hym ought grete ensaumple take salamon who appetyte hooly set vpon delyte take wymmen plesaunce vpon ygnor unce wyde world meruayleth yet al mennes wyt thylke tyme hath ouerpassed flesshly lustes cassed vnder lawe peple god hym self withdrawe hath fro god suche wyse worshyp sacrefyse sondry loue sondry stede vnto false goddes dede wyse ecclesiaste fame whome shal euer laste myghty god forsoke ageyn lawe whan toke wyues concubynes hem sarazyns dyd ydolatrye rede sotye sydone hym ladde knelyng fader spradde strat h n grete humblesse bonde goddesse moabyte ferforth made hym delyte thorugh lust al wyt deuou reth chamos hir god honou reth amonyt also loue hym hath assoted hir god moloche wyth encence sacreth doeth reuerence suche wyse hym badde thus wysest ouerladde blynde lustes sought afterward abought nota hic qualit achias pheta fig nu qd regna pest mortem sabomonis ob ei peccatum suo herede dimuneretur pallu suum duodecim partes scidit vnde dece partes ieroboe filio nabul qui regnaturus postea successit precep dei tribuit achyas soleuytes prophete deces whyle lustes alle betokeneth shal falle day mette ieroboam knyght grette bad hym shold abyde hym shal betyde forth al achyas caste mantel also faste cut py ce twelfe wherof two partyes toward hym selfe kepte al remenaunte od hath sette couenaunte toke vnto ioroboas nab l sone ynges courte knyyt said hym suche goddes myyt thou hast seen departed mantel suche manere deth salamon god hath ordeyned therupon reygne shal deuyde tyme thou shalt eke abyde vpon dyuysyon thy reygne proporcion thou hast mantel take thou shalt receyue vndertake thus sone shal abye lustes lecherye hym fader taken hede sit kyng wel chaste ellys may lighlly waste hym self eke reygne bothe ought euery kyng bothe one synne vyolente wherof kyng shente vengeannce persone inough take alone afterward whan passed hath heritage assed openly tofore tale tolde thus tofore phylosophre vpon thynge write counseyld kynge forfete luxure shal tempre rule suche mesure kynde suffyciaunte eke reson accordaunte lustes ygnoraunce cause mysgouernance thorugh ouerthrowe wyl reson knowe yf manys wyt swerued whan kynde dulyche serued ought reson suffyse yf fyl hym otherwyse may lustes sore drede anthony thus rede seuerus sone lyf comune wone yaue holy vnto thylle vyce ofte tyme nyce wherof nature hath hir compleyned vnto god hath disdeyued werkes anthony wrouyt lustes ful sore abought god forfete hath wroke cron ke yet spoke toke r men r unce specyal mysg uernaunce thorugh c uetyse niustyce forth remenaunt vyce namesye lecherye fynde write grete partye tale thou shalt saumple matere hic b quitur de tarquino nuper rome patore necno de eiusdem filio noie arr u oim vicieru vari ta repleti ta h e quam muli re innumera sc le ra petrauit set specialif su hijs oue contra gabinos fraudulenter operati sunt tractare intendit olde gestes seyn proude tyrauntee romayn rquynus thene kynge wrouyt many wrogful thyng ne many one emenge arrous one e fader maners within fewe yeres treson tyrannye wonne londe grete partye token hede iustyce dewe offyce vpon rule gouernaunce al euer lesaunce vnto flesshes luste toke fyl vndertoke werre acheued ofte tyme hem greued eyn folke hyght gabyens al nyght thus arrous whan home rome pryup place nome within chaumbre bete hym selfe made hym woudes x twelfe vpon bakke sce forth hurtes grene al haste may rode came daye vnto gabye cyte wente whan know anone yates shet lordes al vpon hym set drawen swerdes honde arrous wold hem withstonde said wylle lecf ye spylle yf myn owne fader dede forth within stede prayed hem wold see tolde hem degre fader bredern bothe said wrothe hym beten reuyled rome euer exyl thus made hem beleue said yf myght heue purpoos shal wel yolde hym helpe wolde whan lordes herde sayn wooful besayn toke pyte greue yet hem wonder eue rome hym exyled gabyens coun yl tho vpon goddes made hym swere shold hen trouthe bere strengthe hem al myght also hym hath b hyght helpen hem ouar le shopen thenne h le bathed anoynte tyl lusty poynte wold hadde al hole cyte ladde right wold hym self deuyse thought hym ye whse myght tyrannye shewe toke counceyl shrewe fader forth sente message tho wente prayed fader saye auyse fynde weye myght cite wynne whyle stode wel therin whan messenger come rome hath counceyl nome kyng felle perchaunce gardyn tho messager forth kyng whan tolde thyng maner stode turquynus vnderstode message ferde anone toke honde yerde gardyn gone lyly croppes one one sprongen oute smote stode aboute said vnto messengere lo thynge shal stede thyn answere wyse bere thou shall vnto sone telle lenger wold dwelle toke leue goeth alle vnto lorde tolde hym alle fader whan arrous herde hym telle anone wyst mente therto set al entente tyl thorugh fraude trechery prynces h edes gabye hath smyten al wonne fader came fore sonne towne romeyns toke slewe cyteseyns without reson pyce spareth degre spede conqueste lete make ryche feste solempne sacrefyse phebus temple wyse whan romayns assembled presence hem al vpon auter al dygkt fyres lyght vnder auter sodeynly hydous serpent openlye came hath deuoured alle sacrefyse eke alle fyres queynte forth anone came gone depe grounde ageyn euery man began yn lord may sygnefye therupon praye crye phebus myyt knowe cause throwe gastely voys al herde romayns wyse answerde said wickednesse pride vnrightwysnesse tarquyne sone hath sacrefyse wasted myght ben axceptable vpon suche synne abhomynable ouer yet hem wysseth saith hem first kysseth moder shal take wreche vpon wronge speche ben within hertes glade though semblaunce made ther knyyt buit hyght al haste myght groude fyl kyste none hem cause wyste wende sporned perchauce torned brutus al another mente knewe wel entente therthe euery mane kynde moder blynde sawe ferre whan leften cyte comen home rome ageyn euery man romeyn moder hath hir bende kyst eche hem wende first vpon chaunce torquyne vengeaunce herden phelus seyn euery tyme hath certeyn must nedes thenne abyde tyl afterward vpon tyde hic narrat qd cum tarquinus obsidione ciuitatis ardee vt eam destru eret intentus fuit arrous filius eius romam secreto adies domo collatini hespitatus est vbi de nocte illam castis simam dominam secrete lucreciam yma ginata fraude vi oppressit vnde illa pre dolore mortua ipse cum tarquino patri suo tota clamante rom impm exilium delegati sunt tarquinus made vnskylfully werre fast ageyn towne walles stronge ardea cleped longe caste sege aboute may man passe befyl vpon nyght arrous souper dyght parte chyualrye hym sowpe companye hath bede whan comen sette sowper emonge wordes glade arrous grete spekyng made tho beste wyf rome began stryf arrous saith hath beste iangle withouten reste tyl atte laste one collatyne worthy knyght cosyne arrous said hym wyse qd none emprise speke word dede therof take hede anone thy tyde lepe thy hors lete v ryde may knowe bothe two vnwarely wyues shal trewe assaye arrous saith one nay horsbacke anone lepte suche manere thynge slepte rydyng forth tyl come al pryuelye within rome strauge place doun lyght toke chambre syght ben dysgysyd throwe lyfe shold hem knowe paleys first souyt see thynge lady wrouyt arrous made vaunte hir sawe al glad semblaut al ful myrthes bordes emonge al wordes spake hir husbond whan al vnderstonde thylke place hem lyste gone hem forth none wist besyde thylke yate bra collacea cleped collatyn hath dwellyng founden home sittyng lncrece wyf al enuyronned woman abandoned werche wrought also al bade hem haste sayth shal husbondes swerde spere lyeth siege grete dysese yf shold hym dysplese wold god hym certes tyl may good tydyng estate herte euer vpon debate al men wytnesse suche hardynesse hecan hym self spare al moste care whan walles shold assayle yf wysshes myght auayle wold groundeles pytte siege vnknytte husbond sye water eye aroos ne myght stoppe men seen dewe bedroppe leues floures eke right vpon whyt cheke wooful salte teeris felle whan collatyn hath herde hir telle menyng trewe herte none hir sterte said loo good dere come yon ye bouen ye sayn goodely chere ageyn byclypte hym armes smale colour erste pale beaute restored myght mored kynges sone nyghe lady herde syghe thynges ben befalle reson wyttes alle hath loste loue vpon parte came fyry darte suche woude hym hath smyte must nedes fele wyte thylke blynde maladye cure surgerye helpe yet nethelees thylke tyme helde pee countenaunce made openlye wordes glade coude manere spake made frendely chere tyl tyme goe collatyne hym also leue toke nyght al haste myght ryden syege ageyn arous woo byseyn thouytes vpon hym rone al brode sonne bedde goeth reste thenke vpon beste fayrest forth alle euer sawe euer shalle hym thought corage portreyed ymage fyrst fetures hir face nature al grace womanlye bewte bysette myght bette hir yelow tressed hir atyre wel adressed wepte al thouyt spake wrouyt foryeten hath dele al aketh hym wele worde dede hir lacked nouyt womanhede thus tyranysshe knyght soupled halfe right none hede toke myght somme croke al though ageyn hir wylle lustes flessh fulfylle loue resonable honour remeuable ought wel ben aduysed hath luste assysed wyth medlyd loue tyranye hath founde vpon trecherye weye thynketh holde saith fortune vnto bolde fauourable helpe thus within hym self yelpe wylde man vpon treson began vp sterte forth wente horsbacke entente knewe wyglt name nexte day tyl came vnto cellocea yate rome yt somdele late right euen vpon sonne sette shape nette hir innocence berrappe shold myshappe pryu lye euer myght rode hors alyght tofere cellatynes inne al frendeliche goeth hym cosyn house good sponse lucrece hym syghe goodely chere drewe hym nyghe al honour supposeth hym dare opposeth stode hir busbond tho dyd hir vnderstonde tale feyned wyse right wold hym self deuyse wherof myght hir herte glade better chere made whan glad wordes herde hir busbond ferde thus trouthe deceyued shye treson perayued hir mente al good festes stode souper right wel arayed yet hath worde assayed speke loue degre couert subtylte frendely speches affayteth tygre tyme awayteth hope catche raye herdes aweye whan haue souped halle sayth slepe hym falle prayeth mote goo bedde al haste spedde hir thought done euery thynge redy sone brought hym chambre tho ann toke hir liue forth goo hir owne chambre wende certeynly frende foo wherof fyl mochel woo tyraunt though lye softe bedde roos ful ofte goeth aboute leyed ere herken tyl al bedde goon sleped faste vpon hym self caste mantel swerde al naked toke honde vnwaked bedde laye mette god wote dore vnshette pryue lye none herde softe paas forth ferde vnto bedde slepte al sodeynlye crepte hir bothe armes toke worthy wyf awoke tendernesse womanhede hir voyce hath loste pure drede one worde speke ne dare eke bad hir ware yf made noyse crye sayd swerde laye fast bye slee hir hir folke aboute thus brought hir doubte lyke lambe whan cesed wolues mowth sesed lucrece naked fonde wherof swouned honde saith laye dede oppressed al hym adressed lust toke hym lyste goeth none wist owne chambre ageyn cleped chamberleyn made hym redy ryde thus lecherous pryde hors lepte forth rode bedde abode whan wyst gone cleped lyght anone vp aroos longe day kyst aweye hir fresshe araye hath world fors toke vpon clothes blake euer vpon contynueng right men see welle sprynge eyen ful wooful treas hir hangyng aboute hir eerys wepte man wyst whye yet emonge ful pytouslye prayed nolden dretche hir husbond fetche forthwyth hir fader eke also thus comen bothe two brutus came collatyne lucrece cosyne wenten al thre chambre myght see woofullest vpon molde wepte water sholde chambre dore anone stoke haue ought vnto spoke see hir clothes al dysgysed hath hir self despysed hir heer hangyng vnkempt aboute nethelesse gan lowte knele vnto hir husbonde wold fayne haue vnderstonde cause fared soo softe wordes axeth tho may good swete thouyt hir self vnmete leste worthe wymmen alle wooful chere lete doun falle shame coude vnnethes loke therof good hede toke prayden hir al weye ne spare saye vnto hir frendes hir ayleth sore hir self bewayleth sothe wold mene hath hir sorowe grene hir woo telle thenne assayeth tendre shame worde delayeth sondry tymes mente speke vpon poynte stente hir beden euer one telle forth vpon whan sawe moste nede hir tale bytwene shame drede tolde without peyne wold hir wo restreyne hir husbond sory man comforteth hir al swore eke hir fader bothe hir wrothe ageynst hir wylle prayden hir stylle hir hane al foryeue thought leue hem wyl foryeuenesse said thylke vnkyndenesse hir body wrought al myght nonght afterward world ne shalle reprouen hir forth alle ony man therof ware naked knyf bare within mantel priuelye betwene hir hondes sodaynlye toke thorugh hir herte throge fyl groude euer amonge whan fyl myght hir clothes hir honde right man dounward fro knes shold ony thynge hir see thus laye wyf honestlye al though deyed woofullye tho sorowe seke hir husbond hir fader eke swoune vpon body felle may mannes tonge telle anguysshe brut hem toward hym self herte kepte successe anone lep blody swerde pulleth swere goddes al aboute therof shal venge unce tho made c untenaunce h b dely eye atte loste th kyng vp caste helde hym wyse boke may suffyse brutus manly herte hir husbond hath made vp stert forthwyth hyr fader eke also al haste said th anone without lette bere body fet uc ce vpon bledyng l forth without cryeng goeth vnto market place rome litel space thorugh crye cyte assembled euery mane herte trembled whan soth herde ca vpon counceyl take grete smale brutus tolde hem al tale thus came remembraunce synne contynnaunce arrous tofore eke longe tyme low f fader ronge came place th comyn clamour tolde newe shame synnes olde al towne began crye aweye aweye tyrannye lecherye couetyse atte laste suche wyse fader whyle forthwith sone exyle taken better gouernaunce yet another remembraunce rightwisnes lecherye accorden companye hym hath ye lawe honde may man wel vnderstonde tale thou shalt wy e olde ensaumple write hic ponit exemplum super eod ua ter huius virginen dux ex tus remanc vnicam fikam pulcherimam habens cum quodam neb vi nomine cio vt vxorem du ret fina ter concord uit set interim apius claudius tune n perator virginis formesitatem vt eam violaret concupiscens occasiones qui matrimonij impedire ipsam que ad sui um apprehendere posset bdola censpiracione fieri coniect uit et cum propositum sui desiderij productis falsis stibus udicio mperator habere de uisset pater tunc ibide presens exi e gladio filie sue pectus mortali vulnere per medium transfobit dicens michi de filia mea virginem habere mortuam quam scandalum meretri cem reseruare uiuentem rome whan apyus who name claudius gouerrnour cyte fyl wonder se touchyng gentyl mayde thus lyuyus vyrgyneus begeten vpon wyfe men sayden fayre lyfe al towne fame goeth vp doune claudius came ere wherof thought anone al
