herte hath sette fyre began flo e desyre longeth vnto mayden de sent yf myght spede blynde lustes wylle thynge myght fulfil stode vpon maryage knyght ful grete gnage ilyaus hyght accordeth hir faders syght shold douyter wedde cause fully spedde hir fader romanye leder chyualrye gouernaunce hath vndertake vpon werre take goeth al ye strengthe men armes mariage lefte stode vpon accorde tyl efte kyng herde telle mayde ordeyned mariage thought another thylke tyme broder marcus claudius hote man grete ryote right kyng hym self two gyder vpon caas couceyl founden weye marcus claudius shal saye weye couenaunte seruyce apurtenaunte hool none man vpon saith euery poynte wytnesse take sy e al forsake whan shape lawe tho hir fader absent somned assent come presence kynge stode answer thynge hir frendes wysten al wele falsehede euery dele comen kyng sayden pon comune lawe prayden noble worthy knyght hir fader comune right thylk tyme falle lay profit alle vpon wilde feldes armed shold harmed ne shamed oute thus preyden al aboute al clamour herde kyng vpon luste answerde yaue hem onely dayes two respyte wente tho orte tyme appere hir fader myght manere therof deceyued lyuyus al conceyued purpoos kynge tofore thought therfore al haste came rydyng lefte vpon felde lyggyng ooste tyl came ageyn thus worthy capteyn appered redy daye al euer reson maye lawe audyence doth doughter vpon soth marcus hir accused hath tofore courte excused kyng saw purpose faile sleyght myyt auayle combred lustes blynde lawe torned kynde half wrath though presence hem al deceyued concupiscence yaue broder sentence bad hym shold cese doughter make hym wel ese al within owne entent wyst cause went broder hath wyte hym self wyte thus mayden wronge whiche vpon kynge alonge ageyn hym none appele fader wyst wele wherof vpon tyrannye luste lecherye doughter shold dysceyued illicius weyued vntaily fro mariage right lyon fro rage drede sette counte note pyte shold amounte naked e de ulled oute amonges al route th ste thorugh doughter syde al alowde thus cryed lo take hir ye wrongful kynge leuer vpon thynge e fader mayde though de men sayde lyf shamed therof euyl named tho bade kyng men shold ste body thylke heste lyke chaced wylde h houndes whan feleth sore proueth goeth forth weye suche wyse saye worthy knyyt swerd hode weye made hym wonde none hem stroke kepte thus vpon hors bylepte swerd droppyng blode within doughter stode came power rome tolde hem al caas said hem myght vpon wronge matere better redresse home grete vnright isnesse warre straunge place lefte home hir owne grace thus stant euery mannys lyf partye wyf doughter yf passyng another beute meruayle sy apurtenaunte afore hir eye kyng hath hym mysbor othes haue al sw wyl stonde ryght thus one acorde vp right rome one home ag n torne shortely sayn tyrannye came mowthe euery man saith couthe pryuy trecherye set vpon lecherye came openlye mannes ere brought comyn fire euery man perylle dradde hym hem euerladde thy worse falle thorugh comyn counceyl h alle haue wronge kyng deposed hem supposed counceyl stode ledynge lawe vnto brynge yuen penaunce longeth suche gouernaunce thus vnchaste chastised wherof myght ben aduysed shold afterward gouerne euydence lerne good kyng eschewe luste vyce vertu sewe hic inter al castitatis regimen con rnencia loquitur quomodo matromonium cuius status sacramentum uasi continenciam equirerans eciam honeste delectacionis regimine moderari decet et narrat exemplum ualiter p eo quod illi septem viri qui sat e raguelis fille magi propter concupis teciam quam propter matrimonium voluptuose nups unt vnus post um omnes prima nocte demone asmodeo singillatim ingulati interierunt make partye toucheth polecye chasty e specialle f conclusion fynalle euery luste eschewe grete ensaumple may argewe age towne mede ther mayde rede sarra hyght raguelle hir fader byfelle body bothe vysage none fayre lygnage seche emonge hem al wherof ryche cyte lusty folke couden loue assot vpon hir loue axen hir wedde one laste spedde lykyng haue luste weddyng within herte caste hym repenteth atte laste fyl fyrst nyght whan bedde dyght thynge god esecheth al onely lustes secheth bedde fully warme toke hir arme asmode fende helle serueth bookes telle mpte man suche wyse redy thylke empryse hath set suche delyte vengeth suche plyte nec e hath wronge two yonge wyf woo tho wyst thynge men nethelesse yet thus wente onely fyrst man th began syx hir husbondes asmode take hondes al bedde deyden whan yt hande toward hir leyde nought lawe maryage ylke fyryrage n wyl lawe excede wyl take hede fyl matere ther myght wel sothe whan wedded thobye raphael companye taught hym honeste asmode wan nought thylke fe te yet th wylle h luste goddely ladde bothe lawe kynde serued wherof hath hym self preserued fyl sentence another euydence ensaumple man may see whan lykyng degre mariage may forsuey wel ought weye lust better aduysed god lawe hath ysed wel reson kynde bestes wold bynde onely lawes nature mannes creature god gaue hym reson forth alle wherof nature shalle vpon cause modefye shal lecherye yet shal lustes haue ben lawes bothe saue euery thyng put sclaudre whilom kyng al sanndre wyse phylosophre taughte whan first bore caughte onely vpon chastyte onely vpon al honeste wherof kyng hym self may taste trewe large iust chast hym ought reson forthwyth vertu pyte thorugh whiche thonke deserue toward god preserue hym peple al welthe richesse henour helthe world elli eke sone tofore speke shrifte thou saydest thyn ese thou preydest thy louethro be asse wold telle wysse forme aristotiles lore haue sayd somdele ensaumples assaye yf thy paynes myght laye thorugh ony thynge say weye fader praye ye haue tolde thanke thousand folde tale founden myn ere yet herte elly may self restreyne nam euer loues peyne suche lore coude neuer gete myght make foryete nte yf slepte tydes ay ne kepte thynke loue lalbe erte withdrawe thy good fader dere ue speke matere uc yng loue begonne yf ther ought ouer ronne ought foryete lefte behynde falleth vnto loues kynde wherof nedeth shryue axeth whyle lyue myght amende amys good dere sone yi thy shryfte make pleyne ie yet nomore sayne loue vnaduysed thou shalt wel aduysed vnto thy shryfte bylongeth poynte vpon loue hongeth laste al tho wyl slewe ho explicit liber septimus incipit liber octau que fauet ad vicium vetus modo regula coufert nec non econtra qui docet ordo placet ce u amor dudum non dum sua lumen cepit quo venus impos tu deuia fallit iter post quam ad instanciam amantis confessi confessor genius suy hijs que aristotiles regem aloxandrum edocint vna cum aliarum cronicaru exemplis seriose tractauit iam vltimo isto oc cauo voluminead confessionem amoris causa regrediens tracttare ponit super hoc qd non vlli premordia nature ad ibitum voluptuose consequentes nullo humane racionis arbitrio sen ecclesie legum imposicione suis excessi bus debite resrenantur vnde quatenus amorem conceruit amantis consciencia pro finali sui confessionis materia genius rimari conatur myyty god vnbegon stante hym self hath begon al thynges wylle heuen lyste fulfille al ioye syt entronysed see hath aungels hym serue suche hym lyketh preserue note forueye lucyfer put albeye al route apostasyed ben hym alyed heuen helle aungels fendes felle ny ioye light derke ony nyght paynes shal endelesse yet paynes nethelesse plente ben blake wherof syght may take thus whan thynges ben falle lucyfers courte falle dedely pryde hem hath conceyued none forthwyth purueyed thorugh hym al thynges may made adam sixt day paradyse make hym lyketh one also make bade hem crece multeplye mannes progenye woman shal ore nobre augels lore whan fro blysse felle thought restore felle hauen thylke holy place stode tho wyde vpon grace wel wyst knowe adam eue throwe shold hem betyde paradyse thylke tyde ne dwelten cause wryte book genesye al men haue herde raphael fyry swerde honde toke droue hem gete lyues foode aboute vpon wooful erthe metodre saith matere truelacion vpon vysyon adam ue also vyrgynes comen bothe two world ashamed tyl nature hem hath reclamed loue taught hem thylke lore fyrst kyst ouermore done kynde dewe wherof fayr yssue sone fyrst alle caym name hym calle bell seconde geste fonde nature cause ladde two doughters eue fyrst cleped calmona delbora thus mankynde begynne thy tyme synne suster take broder whan choyce none caym calmana bytake delbora hath abel take gete nethelees worldes fyrst encrees men sayn nede hath lawe thylke dawe laste vnto second age tyl grete water rage noe said flode world synne stode hath dreynte take lyues eyght tho mankynde litel weyght sem cam iaph thyse thre ben sone noe world mannes nacion multiplicacion tho restored newe ageyn ferforth bookes seyn hem yssue ther large retynue nacyons seuenty two sondry place eche one tho wyde world haue e h byted nature hath excyted toke litel hede broder suster yede wedde wyues tyl came tyme abraham whan third age bygonne nede ouer ronne ther peple ynough londe thenne alte fyrst came honde systerhode mariage torned cosynage right lyne syn wedded cosyne abraham deyed charge vpon seruaunt leyed hym wyse spake sone ysaak wedde worldes good onely owne blood wherof seruaunt adde whan dede sone hath ladde ba huel rebecke hath wedded whyt necke wyst wel syghe chylde syn nyghe thus abraham taught whan ysaak god bysette mote afterward repente sore euery man lore befyl tyme present tyme may enformed stode take hym thynke good leue loke tyme goo lust loue excedeth lawe ought withdrawe euery man shold drede namelyche sybrede torneth ofte vengeauuce wherof tale remembraunce longe processe thynke tellen omnibus est communis amor sed et immoderatus qui facit excessus non reputatur amans sors tamen vnde venus attractat corda videre que rationis erunt non ratione sinit hic loquitur adhuc contra incestuosos amantum coitus et narrat mirabile exemplum de gno rege antiocho qui vxore mortua propriam filiam violauit et quia filie matrimonium penis alios impedire voluit tale ab eo exiit edictum quod si quis eam vxorem peterit nisi quoddam proble nia questionis quam ipse rex proposu erat veraciter solueret capitali sentencia puniretur super quo veniens tadem discretus iuuenis princeps tiri appolinus questionem soluit nec tamen filiam habere potuit sed rex indignatus ipsum propter hec mortis odium took first name saith bock coupled noble quene doughter bytwene fortune came honde dethe kyng may stonde euery lyf mote obeye worthy quene toke aweye kyng made mochel mone tho stode saith hym allone without wyf nethelees doughter peerlees bewete dwelte aboute hym stylle whan man hath welth wyl flesshe freel falleth ofte mayde tendre softe hir faders chambre dwelte within tyme wyst felte lykyng concupiscence withouten insyght conscyence fader lustes blente caste al entente owne doughter spylle kyng hath leyser wylle strengthe whan tyme seye yonge mayden forleye tendre ful drede coude hir maydenhede defende thus hath forlore floure whiche hath longe bore helpeth though wepe shold hir body kepe wymmen absent thus mayden goeth man wylde fader thus deuoureth owne flessh none secoureth cause mochel care vnkynde fare chambre goeth kynge laye styl thynge within hir self suche sorowe made ther nouyt myght hir glade fere thylke horryble vyce came norice fro chyldehode hir kepte axed hir yf slepte hir chere vnglad hath ouer lad myght wreke shame coude vnnethys speke nethesse mercy prayed wepyng eye thus sayed ala suster wel away euer sawe ylke day thyng body firsst begat world onelych worldes worshyp hath byrefte swowneth efte euer wissheth deth welny lacketh breth hir wordes herde comfortyng hir answerde lete hir faders foule desyre wyst recouryre whan thynge ther lote suffren suffren mote ther none hym wist hath kynge al lyste lykyng plesaunce last suche contynuunce suche delyte toke hym thought syn durst hym thyng withsey fame goeth euery wey sondry royames aboute grete bewte telleth suche mayde hye parage loue mariage worthy prince come sende al honour wende knew thyng stode fader whan vnderstode doughter thus lysought al wyt caste sought myght fynde lette suche statute thenne sette wyse lawe taxeth man doughter axeth coude questyon assoyle vpon sugestyon certeyn thynges byfelle wold vnto hem telle shold certeyn lese hede thus many dede hedes stondyng gate eke wyf herof inquysytyf tale saue al quyte shal doughter haue answer yf fayle shal deed without fayle thy sone qd kyng wel aduysed thie thyng hath lyf ieopartye appol ynus partye ou yon herde vnto kyng hath answerde hath reherced one one poyntes said therupon questyon thou hast spoke yf thou wylt vnl ke toucheth al pryuyte betwyxte thyn owne chylde stante al vpon two kyng wonder sor tho theuyt yf said oute thenne shamed al aboute sly wordes felle said sone shal telle though thou lytel wytte meruayle yet thyn age may suffyse loke wel thou despyse thyn owne lyf grace thyrty dayes ful space graunte ben aduysed thus loue tyme assysed yonge prynce forth wente vnderstood wel mente within herte lered make hym afered kyng tyme hath deloyed wherof drad amayed treson deye shold kyng trouth tolde sodeynly nyght tyde morowe wold abyde al pryuelye barge hente home ageyn tyre wente owne witte sayed drede yf kyng bewrayed knewe wel kynges herte deth ne shold asterte kyng wold hym pursewe wold deth eschewe knewe al tofore honde forsake thought owne londe wold abyde wel knewe somme syde tyraunt felonye somme manere trecherye greue body wyl leue thy outen takyng leue pryuelyche ashe ther dauce euery myrthe melodye thenne maladye vnlust auenture ther man toke tonsure dredeful clothes clothe bathe stewes bothe shyt euery weye ther lyf lust pleye ne take ony ioye kepe hir liege lord wepe euery wyght saith couthe ala lusty floure youthe prynce hede gouernoure thorugh stonden honoure without conoune assent thus sodeynly v went suche clamour hem alle see befalle qualiter thaliartus mile vt appolinum veneno intoxicaret ab anti oche tirum missus ipse ibidem non inuento antiochiam rediit vpon fyst tale playn torne thereto agayn antiochus grete syre ful rancour yre herte bereth qualiter appollinus cum rege pro filia sua erudienda retentus est appollynus mene tho toke leue kyng quene worthy mayde also prayed vnto hir fader tho myght yonge man tho science lore haue wyse kyng hir graunteth hir apprise hym self therto assent thus accorded went al euer may yonge fayr fresshe may coude shold enforme ful assented forme qualiter filia regis appolinum ornato apparatu vestiri fyl day rode kyng quene al route pleye hem vpon seconde seen toward londe shyp saylyng grete araye knowe mene may tyl come abyde sawe stonde euery syde endlong shyppes borde shewe penonnes ryche rewe wyte fire lyghtenyng al smyte doughter hath chaunce ben bothe one balaunce thy lyege lord seye name al londe preye lefte al thynge done lyke come sone see owne lyege men ben ken lyuen longyng desyre appollino cum vxore sua imprignata pentapoli versus tyrum nauiganti contigit vxorem mortis artia angustiatam naui filiam que postea thaysies vocabatur patere tthus goeth tydyng ouer al nede must nede shal appollynus leue took god al bonde bytook al peple longe brode lenger abode kyng quene sorow made yet somdele glade suche thynge herde tho thus bytwene wele woo shyp goeth wyf childe euer meke mylde wold departe hym fro suche loue bytwene hem two lycho rida hir offyce take norice wende yonge wyf shape wooful lyf within tyme betyd see amyd northe see cloude storme awos wyndes loud blewen many dredesul blaste welken al ouer caste derke nyght sonne hath vnder ther grete tempest thondre mone eke sterres bothe blacke clowdes hem clothe wherof bright loke hyde yonge lady wepte cryde comforte myght auayle chylde began trauayle laye caban choos wooful lord fro hir awos longe ony morowe anguysshe sorowe delyuerd al nyght dede euery mannes syght nethelesse al woo mayde chylde boren tho qualiter appollinus mortem vxoris sue planxit appollynus thys kuewe swowne hym self ouerthrewe man wyst hym lyf woke said wyf ioye lust desyre welth recoueryre shal lyue thou shalt dye ha thou fortune defye hast thou thy werste herte ne wyl thou breste forth hir myght passe paynes moche lasse suche wepyng suche crye dede wyf laye hym bye thousand sythes hir kyste neuer man sawe ne wyste sorowe sorowe lyche euer emonge vpon lyche fyl swownyng thouyt owne deth besought vnto goddes al aboue many pytous worde loue suche wordes tho herde neuer mannes eere onely thylke sayed mayster shypman came prayed suche ben therin sayn may thyng wyn ageyn deth hym rede wel ware take hede see weye nature receyue may creature within hym self holde dede thy wolde counceyllen al aboute deed body casten oute better sayden alle hir byfalle yf sholden al spylle kyng vnderstode wylle knewe counceyl trewe began ageyn sorowe newe pytous herte thus seye al reson ye preye qualiter suadentibu nautis corpus vxoris sue mortue quadam cista plumbo et ferro obtusa circumligata apoolinus cum magno thesauro vna cu quadam littera sub eius capite scripta reludi mari proiti fecit iam ad one allone wold persone fel suche aduersite whan may better doth thus vpon worde ete make coofere stronge borde fyrme lede pytche anone made coofre suche al redy brought vnto honde whan sawe redy fonde cooffre made wel englued deed body besewed cloth golde leyed therin wold vnto hir wyn vpon somme coste sepulture vnder hir heed aduenture golde leyed somme grete iuels stronge byyete copia littere capiti vxoris sue supposite forthwith lettre said thus kyng tyre appollynus doeth al men wyte heereth seeth lettre wryte helpeles without rede l eth kynges doughter dede happeth hir fynde charite take mynde begraue tresour haue thus whan lettre ful spoke none haue coofre oke bounden yron faste may wawes laste stoppen suche wey shal within dreye water myght greue thus hope good beleue corp l n l ary e caste ouer clerkes cowthe couereth atte laste first hir eyen vp caste whan strengthe cauyt hir armes bothe forth straught helde vp hir honde pytouslye spake sayd lorde onde wote cerymon worthy leche answerd anone vpon hir speche said madame b n ye saue ye shal afterward thy counceyl comforteth trysteth wel without fayle ther nothyng shal faile ought reson thus passen day two qualiter vxor appolini sanata domu religionis peciit vbi sacro velamine munitam cast omni tempore se vouit speke nought ende tyl began somdele amende wyst hir self mente tho knowe hir hole entente mayster axeth al caas came came chastyte myyt emonge wymmen dwell whan tale herde tell riyt glad made hir knowen doughter owen hath wyl vnto hir yeue serue whyle bothe lyue stede hath loste al onely owne coste shal rendred forth hyr sayth graunte mercy leue syr god quyte ne may thus dryue forth day tyl tyme hole tho toke counceyl hole shape vpon good gouernaunce made worthy purueaunce ageyn day whan veyled thus whan counceylled ord stode ynne sayleth tyl may wynne hauen tharse sayd ere whan aryued qualiur appolinus tharsim nauigas filiam suam thaysim strangulioni dionisie vxori sue edu n comen uit dein de tirum adijt vbi cum e imabi gaudio suis receptus est tho thorugh cyte knowe men myght see within throwe saith al towne attones come ageyn none yeuen hym reuerence glad resonce though rage ysesed yet glad vysage made h ynne whylom soiorneth goeth hym reyte ceyued whan ye pr e peple weyued toke hoost vnto hym tho saith nde rangulyo thus thus byfalle thou thy self arte one alle forthwith thy wyf must trist thy yf bothe lyste doughter thayse leue thynke shal bleue tyme thus praye kepte al weye whan hath age set book ere thys au god make shal ueuer ir sake berde lykyng sh ue yl befa le haue coueuable tyme age beset hir vnto mar age thus accorden wylle resten hym somdele whyle ther soiourneth taketh leue torneth shyp goeth hym home tyre euery man grete desyre wayteth vpon comyng whan shyp came saylyng perceyuen neuer yet n cite suche ioye made tho made herte also began glade seeth peple glad lo th fortune happe hath ladd sondry wyse traueyled euer assayled latter ende shal good speke stood thayse enemye thorugh pure treson enuye al sorowe tho spake vnto hir bondeman c eped theo phylus made hym swere couceyl thus suche tyme hym sette shal come thayse fette lede hir al syght man hir helpe myght dionise hath bede thou shalt murdred stede mayde tho sere shryght e god al myght pr th litel stouude myy knele vpon grounde toward heuen c aue hir wooful sow saue noyse crye barge fast hyd scomer fare men sterten ware fe goo began crye tho mercy helpe goddes sa e barge hir take theues shold forth wente vpon se wynde hem hente malgre wold none tofore weder forth gone ther helpe sayle ther helpe none take grete k pe hym lyst better wepe cught llys game thus kept hir self fro shame knelyd doun therthe prayed vnto man thus sayed yf thy mayster wold golde encrece shold may falle thys weye suffre goo weye hows shal hym wyn somme place towne relygyowne honest wymmen dwelle thus thou myyt thy mayster telle whan haue chambre lete hym crye al wyde bord hath doughter dere wylle shal lere suche scole trewe shal hir che thynges newe none woman al londe tho man hir tale hath herde goeth ageyn tolde vnto mayster pleyn hath said therupon whan sawe byyete noon bordel bycause hir bad man g spyr place myght abyde may wynne vpon somme syde atte leste thus saufe tempeste qualiter thaisis lupanari virgo liberata inter sacras mulieres hospiciu habens scie cia quib edocta fuit nobiles regni puellas ageyn therin nolde come hath bynethe place nome wepyng allone lay sawe lyght day thus tofore wynde dryue tyl longe late arryue grete distresse sene vpon towne mytelene noble cite tho happeneth thylke tyme lordes bothe commune hygh festes neptune vpon stronde atte ryuage custome vsage sole pnely syghe straunge vessel syghe comen hath sayle aualed one therof hath spoke tal qualiter athana goras vrbis metelene princeps nauim appolini iuestigans ipsu sic contr statum nichil que respodente consola satage lorde cyte who name nagoras said wold see shyp ben therin sone whan sawe done large hym hym vp ageyn qualiter precepto principis ut appollnu consolaretur thaisis cu cithe sua ad ipsum obscuro nauis vbi iacebat producta est thus spoke many wyse emongest hem wyse atte laste wysdom towne thus caste yonge thayse assent yf ther mendement glad wooful kynge whiche moche euery thynge shal glade hym anone messager hir gone came hir harpe honde said hem wold fonde al weyes glad wyth sory man bur wyst nought al shyp hir hath bysought hir wytte hym dyspende aunter yf myght amende sayn shal wel aquyt whan hath vnderstonden goeth hir doun laye wher harpeth many laye lyke aungel songe alle nomore walle toke hede ony thynge herde whan sawe ferde falleth hym vnto wordes telleth hym sondry lordes axeth hym demaundes straunge wherof made herte chaunge hir speche erre leyde hath meruayle seyde prouerbe probleme spake bad shold deme many subtyl questyon subiestyon toward hym coude sterr wold one word answere mad man otte laste heed wepyng aweye caste halfe wrath bad hir goo yet wold shyp al fayre felawshyp qualiter appolliuus vna cum vxere fi ia sua tirum applicuit kyng hath desire sayth wold holde co r tyre h dden wynde atte wylle tho topsayle cool forth goo stryken neuer tyl qualiter appollinus tiro mare versus tharsim iter axipiens vindictam contra strangulionem et dionisiam vx orem suam pro inuiria quam ipi thaysi filie sue intuler nt iudicialiter assecutus est astronge purueaunce doth mercy iustyce slayn mordrer mor thorugh trouth rightwysnesse thorugh mercy saue symplenesse hir mercy preserueth thus hath wel wel deserueth qualiter artestrate pentapolim rege mortuo ipsi de regno epistolas su hoc appolino direxerunt vnde appolinus vna cum vxore sua ibidem aduenientes ad decus imperij cum magno gaudio coronati sunt al thyng goo ended kyng loued frended letter hath came hym shyp fro pentapolym londe hath hym write wyl vnderstonde wyte good mynde good pee deed kyng arestrates wherof al one accorde hym prayden lyege borde letter wyl conceyue come reygne receyue god hath yeue hym fortune thus besought hym comune forth grete lordes alle kyng sawe befalle fro tharse prosperyte toke l ue cyte goeth hym shyp ageyn wynde good yt see pleyn hem nede ryff slake tyl pentapolym haue take londe herde tydyng wonder glad comyng resteth hym day two toke counceyl hym tho set tyme parlement al londe one assent forthwith wyf hath hym c roned al good hym forsoned lo wel grounded hath first loue founded honestlye wedde honestly loue spedde chyldren wyf hym lyst ledde lyf ensaumple lyf wryte al louers myghten wyte atte last shal sene loue wolden mene see syde antyochus al lewde pryde sette loue vnkyndely ende sodeynly set ageyn kynde vpon vengeaunce lust hath penaunce confessor ad amantem procedendo lo thus sone thou myght lere loue good manere loue wyse mede aryseth seruyse fortune though stable yet somtyme fauourable hem ben loue trewe certes rewe see loue ageyn kynde falle maketh man sore falle thou myght tofore rede thy sone wyl rede lete al loue aweye yf suche weye loue reson wyl accorde elli yf thou discorde take luste doeth leste thy loue may honeste skyl fynde suche luste loues kynde confessio amantis vnde pro finali conclusione consiliu confessoris impetrat fader stonde tale herde vnderstonde thynge worthy grete ensaumple grete matere wherof fader god quyte poynte self acquyte may right wel neuer yet assoted wyt onely worthy place al luste al grace set yf daunger ne al moste fere note fortune acounte thyng daunger may amou te wote wel haue assayed whan herte beste arayed haue al wyt thorugh souyt loue beseche hir ought al euer syke may concluded nay one syllable hath ouerthrowe thousand wordes rowe suche best speke u l ude man fader ye ben clerke loue matere derke euer lenger lasse yet may lete passe hole counceyl beseche ye somme weye teche beste ende ne vnto trouthe wende wel loue te al tryfles hic super amoris causa finita confessione confessor genius ea que sibi salubrius expediunt sano cousilio finaliter iniungit nede hye nedeth slye hym hath nede honde haue wel herde vnderstonde sone al thou hast yed eke thou hast prayed tyme shal conclusyon fynal counceyl vpon nede sette thynke fynally knette thy cause ke make ende spoke ehyght gyfte first whan yu come vnder shryfte though toward venus yet spake suche wordes preesthode haue myn ordre myn estate saue said wold myn offyce vertu vyce enclyne teche lore thy speken ouermore loue may auayle take loue may auayle thou arte thou seest synne synne may pryce deserue without pryce shal serue note prouffyt myght auayle foloweth yf thou trauayle thou prouffyt hast pryce thou arte toward thy self vnwyce sythe thou myghtest lust atteyne euery lust ende peyne euery peyne good flce wonder thynge see suche thynge shal desyred stocke fyred rather asshes torneth fote weye sporneth fuf ofte heed hath ouerthrowe thus loue blynde knowe goeth tyl falle thy yf byfalle good counceyl ladde hym ought le n dradde counceyl passeth al thynge hym thynketh kynge aud euery man partye kyngdom hath iustyfye sayn owne dome mys ule kyngdome leseth hym self yf lost shyp ore al worldes good alle man specialle hath hym self hath ellys perles shelles al hym one valewe though retynewe wyde world right wolde whan herte hath withholde toward hym self al veyne thus sone wold seyne sayd thou aryse thou falle suche wyse thou ne myght thy self recouer loue blynde euer maketh al seruautes blynde also sone yf thou haue ben yet tyme withdrawe set thy herte vnder lawe reson gouerned wylle lerned ensaumple thou hast many one eke tyme gone euery lust whyle wyl hym self begyle may rather dysceyued sone thou hast conceyued somme wold mene afterward shal sene yf thou leue vpon ore che th right weye chese yf thou wylt lyue deye hic quitur de contrauersia que inter confessorem amantem fine confessiomis versabatur fader haue herde tale yf answerde mochel blame wo yow game feleth fele felyng mannys hele may likened herte note though wold asterte ye fre al peyne loue wherof compleyne right easy commaunde herte whiche free goeth ye laude oxe hym ey eth falleth ofte manmerueyleth seeth another fa yf knewe hym self fare felte sothe shold done right dothe elli wors degree wel wote ye loue hath euer ben yet vsed mote nede ben excused fader yf ye wold thus vnto cupyde venus ben frendel toward quarele herte hele loue breste wote wel better preste neuer made behoue al whyle houe none certeyn betwene two note wele wo shal torne al drede note rede fynal conclusyon thynke supplicacion pleyne wordes expresse wryte vnto venus goddesse praye bere brynge ageyn good answere tho betwene preest debate grete perplexyte reson vnderstood hym wele knewe soth euery dele hath said thy wylle hath thynge set therby towchyng vnto wyse aporte vnto loue dysporte yet myght neuer man beholde esen loue withholde one gouernaunce thus fellen dystaunce preest spake fayre thorugh wordes debonayre atte laste accorden sayth wyl accorden speke stonde syde venus bothe cupyde bad wryte wolde said truly shold letter l vnto quene sat doun vpon grene fulfilled loues fantasye erys myn eye stede ynke gan wryte wordes wold end te vnto pyde venus letter said thus hic tractat formam cuiusdam supp oni quam ex parte amantis genij rdot sui venus sibi porrectam acceptabat wooful payn leues maladye ag yn physyke anayle te hath wapped soty reste trauayle fynde euer redy assayle reson hym deffende th che helpe wherof myyt amede first nature yf compleyn fynde euery creature sotyme yere hath loue demeyn btel wrenne mesure haue kynde loue vnder cure ut one desyre mys ut hath euery kynde blys reson wytte ouerpasseth nature techeth weye loue yet certeyn compasseth shal spede th betwene yt tw stode note shal lyue dey though reso ageyn wyl debate may flee yt ne loue algate vpon self ylke tale come whilo pan god kynde ue wrestled euercome euer wrasile euer behynde strengthe al herte fynde wherof may ston den ony trowe soo ferre wytte loue ouerthrowe nedeth helpe mote helpe craue helpeles shal nede spylle pleynly thorugh sought wyttes al haue none hem helpe wylle also wel myght sitte stylle praye vnto lady ony helpe thus wote wherof self helpe vnto grete ioue yf byd grace thylke swete tonne vnder key lere yd lyeth couched yt fortune ouercome bitter cuppe haue begene note ofte thus fynde game euer aske ye see world stodeth vpo schauge wynde lowde ow weder softe may see eke grete mone chaunge thynge whiche lowe fto ofte dredeful wer re pee ful ofte torne euer daunger one place whiche wil chauge wil grace vpon grete clerke ouyde loue maketh remembrauce saith ther blynde cupide hath loue vnder gouernaunce hande many fyry launce woundeth ofte wyl h e somdele cause quarele ouyde sayth eke yt loue parfourme stante ye ho de venus ye goddesse whan taketh hir counceyl satourne grace tyme gesse began loue myn heuynesse euer shal spede wote self rede thy cupyde venus bothe al hertes obeysaunce praye ye atte fyrst tyme wrothe whan began loue say stynte thilke fortune away daunger whiche stondeth retynewe wyth alle lady hys place may renewe thou cupyde god loues lawe thy darte brennyng hast sette fyre herte wounde wythdrawe yeue salue suche desyre seruyce thy courte wythouten hyre whiche euer yet hath kepte thyn heste may neuer loues lawe honeste thou gentyl venus loues kynde quene without gylte thou doest thy wreche thou wotest peyn euer elyche grene loue yet may areche thus wolde laste word byseche thou loue acquyte deserue ellys playnly sterue hic loquitur qualiter venus accepta amantis supplicacione indilate ad singula respondit thys supplicacion good deliberacion suche wyse ye wyte myn enteute wryte vnto cupyde venus preest hyght genyus toke honde presente message forth wente venus wyte hir wylle bode place stylle bode lytel whyle fully mountenauce myle behelde sodeynly sawe venus stode myght vnder tree grounde felle vpon kne preyed hir grace cast hir chere vpon face haluyng game axeth name madame said iohan gower iohan qd power thou must thy loue stonde thy wylle haue vnderstonde cupyde somdele thou hast compleyned somdele nature also shal stonde emonge ye two therof haue done nature vnder mone maystresse euery lyues kynde yf may fynde holy man wil withdrawe kyndely lust ageyn lawe selde whan falleth fewe men ther ben tho thyse ynough owne nycete ageyn nature hir offyce delyten hem sondry wyse wh rof ful ofte hath pleyned eke courte hath dysdeyned euer shal rec yueth none suche kynde dysceyueth al onely genty loue court stont al courtes aboue taketh retinewe thynge whiche kynde delbe ellys shal refused wherof holde excused many dayes gone thou emonge hem oue courte hast withholde beholde thy dyscase comune renewe fortune many dayes hath greued counceyl may leued thou shalt esed thou goo thylke vnsely ioly woo wherof sayest thyn herte fyred thou hast desyred sentence thy bylle th u must therof wylle therof wyl aduyse thou hole shal suffyse medecyn seke holsem seke al perchaunce ye wolde ye reson sholde accordaunt vnto loues kynde plyte fynde courte hath awarded thou shalt duely rewarded yf thou woldest craue right thou haue qui cupit id quod habere nequit sua tempora perdit est decrepita senium iuuenile vo luptas floret obsequium quod venus ipsa petit coueniens igitur foret nec qd ua senectus attigit veterius corpus casta col nt hic cotra quoscuqy viros inue teratos amoris concupiscenciam affectans loq tur venus huius qy amantis confessi suppstcationem quasi deridens ipsum eo qd senexit debilis est multis exortutionibus insufficientem redargu ven stonte lawe none certeyn men drawe ragman vpon chaunce leyeth peyse balaunce hir lyketh weye trewe man ful ofte alle weye put hath hir grace bede sette vntrewe stede lo thus blyndely ye world demeth loues cause semeth note men shold seyn algate beseyn stonde one emongest alle grace falle nedeth take wytnesse said goddesse whether parte loue de hath set fynal ende poynte wherto shal holde whan hath wel beholde haluyng scorne sayd thus thenne wyst thou venus al onely lustes seche wel wote though thou beseche loue lustes ben none may take thy persone loues lust locke hore chambre accorden neuer though thou feyn yonge corage sheweth wel thy vysage olde grysel foole ther ben ful many yerys stole suche moo outeward thought beth within power assaye herte wold ne maye nought loued dayes thou make ony suche assayes loue falle vppn fete better make beaw retrete though thou myytest lone atteyne yet ydel peyne whan thou arte suffysaunte helde loue couenaunte thy take home thy h rte ageyn thou traueyle veyn wherof courte may dysceyued wote haue wel conceyued thy wylle good ynough behoueth plough wherof lacketh trowe wel thou knowe feble estate thou begyn thyng yu myght none ende wyn bargeyn shold man assayr whan hym lacketh paye sone yf thou wel bethought toucheth foryete nought thynge torned whylom grene gras elowed hey tyme thy counceyl thou remembre wel thou arte olde whan venus hath hir tale tolde qualiter super derisoriam veneris exhortacione cotristatus amans quasi mortuus terram corru vbi vt sibi videbatur cupidinem cum numera multitudine nuper amantum varijs turmis assistenaum conspicicbat whan bethought al abowte wyst wel withouten doubte ther recouyre man blase fyre water quencheth fare colde caught sodeynly sorowe herte made dedely fare pale fade bycome swowne fyl grounde laye stounde ne fully quycke ne fully deed thought sawe tofore myn heed cupyde bowe bente lyke vnto parlement ordeyned none hym arme al ye world attones gentyl folke whylom louers sawe hem al floure somme grete perles newe guyse beme sondry thynges wel deuysed see wherof quentysed al lust ferde ther songe ne herde loue loue touchyng pan al lykyng pypyng melodye herde thylke companye loude hast wryte wel wyte yf thou thyn hele wil purchace thou myght make suche chace game prouable thynge vnresonable ouerseye thy take hede seye lawe commune shapen comune thy self neuer haue seyd al loue day ferth take reste nomore loue make many horte hath ouertake ouertorned blynde fro reson salbe kynde wysdem goeth aweye see right weye gouerne owne estate euery day stante debate within hym self leue thus thy synal leue take euermore without makyng ony loue dedely hele physycyen hele nature dyuers hath euer somme trauers moche lyte playnly may man delyte hym fayleth thylke loue within mannes herte affermed stante charyte conformed suche loue goodly haue suche loue may body saue suche loue may selvle amende hyghe god suche loue v sende forthwith remenaunte grace aboue thylke place resteth loue al pee ioye may endelees amen explicit iste liber qui transeat obsecro liber ut sine liuore vigeat lectoris ore qui sedet scannis celi det ut ista iohannis perpetuis annis stet pagina grata britannie derbie comiti recolunt auem laude periti vade liber prius sub eo requiesce suturus epistola super huius operis vet opusculi sui complementum iohanni golver quoda philosopho transmissa quam anxere freta golber tua carmina leta per loca discreta canit anglia laude replita carminis leta satirus tibi siue poeta sit laus completa quo gloria siat sine meta quia vnusquisa que prout deo acoepit alijs impartire tenetur iohes gow er super hijs que deus sibi intellectua liter donauit villicacionis sue racionem dum tempus instat scundum aliquid allemare cupiens inter labores et ocia ad aliorum noti iam tres libros doctrine causa forma subsequenti propterea composuit primus liber galico sermone editus decem diuiditur partes tractans de viais et virtutibus necnon de bariis huius seculi gradibus nama que qui peccator trausgressus ad sui creatoris agnicionem redire debet recto tramite docere conatur titulus libelli istius speculu hominis nuncupatus est scandus enim liber sermone latino versibus exame tri compositus tractat super illo mirabi euentu qui anglia tempore regis ricardi secundi anno regni sui quarto contigit quando seruiles rustici impetuose contra nobiles et ingenuos regni insurrexerut innocenciam tamen dicti domini regis tune iunioris etatis causam inde excusabilem pronuncians culpas abunde et quibus et non fortuna talia inter homines contingunt enormia euidencius declarat titulus que voluminus huius cuius ordo septem continet paginas vox clamantis nominatur tercius iste liber ang co sermone octo partes diuisus qui ad instanciam serenissimi principis dc domini regis anglie ricardi secundi conficitur secu dum dauic propheciam su huius modi regnorum mutaciene tempore regis godonosor vsqy nunc tempora distinguit tractat eciam secundum nectanabum et aristotilem super hijs quibus rex alexander tam sui regimine quam aliter super amorem et amantum condiciones fundamentum habet vbi variarum cronicarum historiarum qy finem necnon poetarum philosophorum qy scripture ad exemplum distinctius inseruntur nomen qy presentis opuscuk confessio amantis specia tre nuncu patur carmen quod quidam philosophus memoriam iohannis golber super consummacione suorum tuum brorum forma sub sequenti composuit et eitem gratanter transmisit eneidos bucoks que georgi ra perhennis virgi laudis certe dedere soo hijs tribus ille brie prefertur honore poetis rom qy precipuis laudiby instat eis golber sic que tuio tribus est dotata libellis anglia morigeris quo tua scripta seris ille que latinis tantum sua tra loque scripsit vt italicis sint recolenda notis te tua set trinis tria scribere carmina linguis constat vt inde viris sit scola lata magi gallica ngua prius latina secunda set ortus lingua tui pocius angli complet opus ille quidem vanis ro manas obstupet aures ludit et studijs musa pagana suis set tua xpristicolis fulget scriptum renatis quo tibi licolis laus sit hab da locis quis sit vel qualies sacer ordo conubia scripsi mentalis sit amor qd ordine talis exemplo veteri poterunt ventura timeri cras caro sicut heri leuiter valet illa moueri non ita gaudebit sibi qui de carne placebit quin corpus flebit aut spus inde dolebit carne refrenatus qui se regit inmaculatus omnes quoque status precellet e beatus ille deo gratus splendet ad omne latus carmen qd iohannes golber super amoris multiplici varietate sub compen dio metrice composuit est amor glosa pax bellica pietosa accio famosa vaga sors vi imperiosa pugna quietosa victoria pe niciosa regula discosa soola deui uia lex capitosa cura molestosa grauis ar virtu viciosa gloria damp nosa flens risus et ira iocosa musa dolorosa mors leca febris preciosa esca venenosa fel dulce fame animosa vitis acetosa sitis ebria men furiosa flamma pu inosa nox clara dy enebrosa re dedignosa soci ali et ambiciosa garrula verbosa se creta silene studiosa fabula formosa sapiencia prestigiosa causa ruinosa rota versa quies operosa vrticata rosa spes stulta fides que dolosa magnus exiguis variatus vt est tibi clamor fixus ambiguis motibus errat amor instruat audit tibi leccio sit repetita mors amor et bita participantur ita lex docet aucto rum quod iter carnole norum tucius est quorum sunt federa coniugiorum fragrat vt ortorum rosa plus quam german agroa qrdo moriteru caput e et finis amoru hec est nuptorum carnis quasi regula morum que saluandorum sacratur orbe virorum hinc vetus anerum eolber sub spe meritorum ordine sponsorum tutu adhibeo thorum orate pro anima iohannis golber quiacunque enim pro anima ipsius iohannis golber orauerit ciens quo en mi
